## **167: Submission and the Catastrophe Decisive Battle**

**AN:** Updated on 2/30.

I said in the activity report that I would spoil it, but in the end I never did. The effects of the special ability are finally revealed.

I was planning to write it, but my inner Koda said, “If you’re going to waste time on that, move the main story forward”, so I didn’t. Sorry to anyone who was looking forward to it, if there was anyone.

---

“I have one thing I want to ask. Do you want to quit being the ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’? Or do you want to continue?”

“What are you talking about? Don’t tell me you’re saying you’ll make Yuria the next ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’ after me?”

Yurisuzu gives Claude a suspicious look at his question.

“No. I’m asking whether it’s all right to defeat the Disaster Dragon, if we can.”

“Huh? I understand even less now. Defeat a Disaster Dragon? That’s impossible. It’s not something you can defeat in the first place.”

The suspicion on Yurisuzu’s face deepens even further.

“I also thought about whether there was something I could do long ago, and that’s why I founded the Adventurers Guild. I gathered a hundred people equivalent to S-rank adventurers at the time and challenged it, but the result was total annihilation.”

Ah, so Yurisuzu herself founded the Adventurers Guild.

The goal was to defeat the Disaster Dragon… Yeah, that was never going to work.

“Our master, my master, has already defeated one Disaster Dragon.”

“That’s enough of the jokes! No, even as a joke, that’s far too cruel!”

Yurisuzu explodes in anger, but Claude remains calm.

“It’s not a joke. The reason we know so much about Disaster Dragons is because our master, who defeated one, heard the circumstances from a ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’. The person he spoke to was Ulysses, the ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’ of the ‘Earth Disaster Dragon: Earthquake’, which was sealed in the Regalia Beastman Kingdom.”

“The location matches, and both the Disaster Dragon’s name and the ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’s’ name are correct… No, even so, I can’t believe that a Disaster Dragon was defeated.”

There are members of the Earth clan in the Sky Castle, so it wouldn’t be strange for them to have heard about it.

“You don’t have to believe it. All we need is for you to send our master to the space where the Disaster Dragon is.”

“Thinking about it normally, that’s like sending someone to their death. Are you serious…?”

“Yes. Completely serious.”

Seeing the earnest expressions on Claude and the others’ faces, Yurisuzu thinks deeply.

“All right. I said I would follow your decision. If that’s what you want, I’ll make it happen. So then, where is this master of yours? Is he here in the city?”

“Yes… or rather, he’s just beyond the door of this office.”

“W-when did he get there…!?”

“Master, please come in.”

Nott, who was standing near the door, opens the office door.

“Yo. I’m Jin, Claude and the others’ master. Nice to meet you.”

Since it was our first meeting, I tried to greet her as friendly as possible.

However, Yurisuzu remains unresponsive, still sitting in her luxurious chair in the office.

-Pichan, pichan-

From somewhere, I hear a sound like water droplets falling.

What’s that sound?

A: The sound of Yurisuzu fainting, losing bladder control, and wetting the floor.

“Excuse me for a moment.”

I approach Yurisuzu.

Yurisuzu is slumped in the chair, unconscious, eyes rolled back and foam coming from her mouth.

Her crotch is thoroughly soaked, and the overflowing liquid runs down the chair and drips onto the floor.

“Whoa…”

Just what in the world happened here?

A: Yurisuzu looked directly at master with \<Spiritual Rank Perception> and couldn’t withstand the shock.

Ah, so I’m that dangerous when seen through \<Spiritual Rank Perception>.

Thirty minutes pass after Yurisuzu loses consciousness.

“Huh!?”

Yurisuzu wakes up, still seated in the chair.

“Just what happened to me… That’s right, I saw Yuria and the others’ master and the shock made me… ugh!”

It seems recalling it gave her a headache, as Yurisuzu holds her head in pain.

“Are you all right? You were unconscious for about thirty minutes.”

“Y-yeah, I’m fine. …My clothes don’t seem to be, though.”

Since no one bothered to cast ‘Purify’, Yurisuzu’s crotch is still wet.

“More importantly, where is that person now?”

“That person…? If you mean our master, he stepped out for a bit.”

“I see. That’s good. I can’t afford to be rude to that person again.”

Hasn’t Yurisuzu’s reaction changed?

Just to add, he stepped out, but he’s still watching.

“Why are you being so deferential to our master?”

“Even I have no choice but to submit to someone on such a completely different level.”

She answers Claude’s question with a look of resignation.

“When I saw a Disaster Dragon long ago, its sheer overwhelming existence nearly made me lose consciousness. But if you steel your heart, you can stay conscious even before a Disaster Dragon. That person was different. The instant I saw him, all resistance was ignored and I was swallowed by a torrent of power. In the brief moment before I lost consciousness, it was engraved into my soul. Never oppose this person. Just remembering it makes my body tremble…”

Yurisuzu really is trembling.

“I said earlier that I would follow your decision, but I’ll have to revise that. I’ll accept any and all demands from your master. Total surrender.”

A man who, simply by showing himself, subjugated and forced the complete surrender of the head of the Adventurers Guild, which holds influence across the world. That’s Shindo Jin. Nice to meet you.

I don’t really know what I’m saying myself.

“Then, as we asked earlier, please send our master to the subspace where the Disaster Dragon is.”

“Ah, of course. Understood. …So it really was true that you defeated a Disaster Dragon.”

She murmurs quietly and Yurisuzu begins preparing to go out.

First, she seems to be changing her wet clothes, so Claude and the others step outside for now.

The area around the office had been cleared of people by Yurisuzu beforehand, so a fair bit happened, but no one came near.

It seems the effect of the clearing will continue until Yurisuzu declares the end of her scheduled work.

“I’m going to the volcano for a bit.”

Since she couldn’t just go out without reporting it, Yurisuzu, having finished her preparations, informs the reception desk that she will be going out.

“Huh? Didn’t you just go to the volcano earlier this month?”

“The plans changed. Well, I’ll be with S-rank adventurers, so no escort is needed.”

Apparently, Yurisuzu visited the volcano once a month to maintain the seal of the ‘Fire Disaster Dragon: Volcano.’

To maintain the seal of a Disaster Dragon, the ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’ needs to periodically approach the Disaster Dragon’s body.

Even just approaching it regularly places a great mental burden on them, and eventually they will wish for a next-generation ‘Princess Shrine Maiden.’ One can only imagine the hardships Ulysses endured, bearing that burden for so long.

“Understood. Please take care, and have a safe trip.”

Seeing them off, Claude and the others head for Volcan Volcano with Yurisuzu.

“So this is a Lesser Wind Dragon. What a fine view.”

Yurisuzu mutters as she rides along on Claude’s Lesser Wind Dragon.

“So then, is that person not coming along?”

“There’s no problem as long as we call our master once we arrive.”

“…I may have lived a long time, but it seems there are still countless things in this world that I don’t know. Truly astonishing.”

She speaks in a tone that could be either exasperated or impressed.

After flying a bit longer, Claude and the others arrive at Volcan Volcano.

“We’ve been waiting!”

“We have been awaiting your arrival!”

“Maids? Why are there maids in a place like this?”

Waiting for Claude and the others after they dismount the Lesser Wind Dragon are two girls.

As you know, they are my subordinates and Heroes: the human Hero from the Estea Labyrinth group, and the dwarf Hero who is a maid. Both of their default outfits are maid uniforms.

It’s only natural that Yurisuzu, who doesn’t know their background, would be confused.

“We’d like you to send them to the subspace together with our master as well.”

“Huh? I understand that person, but these two don’t have such strong auras. Are they really all right? Well, if you tell me to do it, I won’t refuse, but still…”

“Yes, it’s fine. This is also at our master’s instruction.”

Claude explains to the doubtful Yurisuzu.

The reason for bringing the two this time is that when we defeated the ‘Earth Disaster Dragon: Earthquake’ before, Maria’s \<Hero> skill leveled up while she was in the subspace, so I thought other Heroes might be able to do the same.

Since the \<Hero> skill had a bad feeling, she hasn’t touched it with her skill points, so she doesn’t want to miss this valuable opportunity to level up.

“Besides that person and these two, is there anyone else you want me to send to the subspace?”

“Yes. We’d like you to send about ten people in total. Is that all right?”

Apparently, it seems levels won’t increase unless you’re in the subspace, so we’re also bringing the dragonkin. There’s precedent for \<Dragon Magic> leveling up.

“That’s no problem, but that’s quite a lot. Are you going as well?”

“No, we’ll be staying behind.”

Claude and the others don’t have any skills that look like they’ll level up.

Also, the Disaster Dragon’s subspace is dangerous after all, so we’ll keep the numbers to a minimum.

“I guess there will be more new faces again… Sorry, but I’ll have to do the work blindfolded. If I see that person again, I’ll probably faint again.”

“Please do. As long as you don’t look directly, you’ll be fine, right?”

“Yeah, probably. I think I can at least stay conscious…”

She doesn’t sound entirely confident.

After that, guided by Yurisuzu, we proceed through Volcan Volcano.

At the destination Yurisuzu is heading toward… there is a hidden passage, and beyond it lies the body of the ‘Fire Disaster Dragon: Volcano.’

“This is it. If you do this here…”

When Yurisuzu manipulates what looks like nothing more than rock, the hidden passage opens with a clunking sound.

“It’s hidden with a specially made magical tool, but you all don’t seem surprised at all.”

That’s because you’re allowing map usage. Everyone knows.

“Normally, when you get this close to a Disaster Dragon, you start to feel sick, but…”

As she says that, Yurisuzu looks a bit unwell.

“It’s no problem.”

“Yes, please don’t worry about Rico and the others.”

“This is it… My common sense seems to have completely fallen apart.”

All thanks to \<Multiple Existence>.

We walk on for a bit longer and reach an open space at the end of the hidden passage.

Part of the wall is glowing red, its brightness changing periodically like the beating of a heart.

I don’t need to say it, but that’s part of the ‘Fire Disaster Dragon: Volcano.’

“It’s hot, as expected.”

“Of course it is. This is the main heat source of the volcano. Though this isn’t actually the hottest spot.”

Yurisuzu replies to Claude, who is wiping away sweat.

If you look at the whole body, you’ll see the bottom.

“From here, I can send you to the ‘Fire Disaster Dragon: Volcano’ subspace. Will you call that person?”

“Yes, that’s the plan.”

“Then, would you mind waiting just a moment? It won’t take long.”

“That’s fine, but…”

“Thanks.”

Saying that, Yurisuzu takes out a blindfold and covers her eyes.

Then she kneels down on the spot and moves into a full prostration.

“U-um, what are you doing…?”

“I’ll show my will of submission through prostration. …To show that I have no will to resist, it might be better to strip completely naked.”

Saying that, Yurisuzu, still prostrating, stores her clothes and underwear in her item box. …It’s been a while since I’ve seen a naked woman prostrating herself.

“H-hey!?”

Claude, Nott, and Adel, the male members, turn their faces away. It seems it’s too stimulating for youths.

…Since I was borrowing Claude’s vision, I can no longer see Yurisuzu naked.

I quickly transfer to the ‘Portal’ Claude and the others prepared.

“I accept your will of submission.”

“Eek!?”

When I speak, Yurisuzu twitches.

“A-ah… Even without looking directly… just the aftereffects…”

Yurisuzu trembles violently. It seems she leaked again, and the ground is wet.

Naked prostration with incontinence… that’s really throwing away all human dignity.

I consciously suppress my presence.

Still not good enough… a bit more…

Ah, Yurisuzu’s trembling has subsided a little. How about this?

“Hah, hah… The aura got weaker…?”

“I intentionally suppressed it.”

“Th-thank you very much…”

Yurisuzu is already completely exhausted, but she still has work to do after this.

Following me, the five members of the main party transfer in.

Then I use ‘Summon’ to call the dragonkin Blue, Mikazuki, and Leaf.

“A-again, such a strong light…!?”

As expected, when Sakura transferred in, Yurisuzu trembled and lost bladder control again.

It seems the strength of the aura Yurisuzu perceives is not unrelated to the Special Powers.

However, unlike with me, it doesn’t seem to be unbearable (though she still wets herself).

I give everyone instructions and begin preparing for the transfer, and once preparations are complete, I call out to Yurisuzu.

“Yurisuzu, Claude and the others are standing behind you from your perspective. Transfer the nine people within ten meters in front of you to the subspace. Keep your distance from the Disaster Dragon.”

“Y-yes! As you command!”

And so, we transfer into the subspace.

“So, here we are in the subspace.”

“You make it sound so casual, but this isn’t a place you can talk about lightly.”

When I speak casually, Mio responds in exasperation.

“There’s an incredible noise coming from far away…”

《Loud!》

As Sakura says, a tremendous roar echoes from the distance.

It’s probably the sound of the ‘Fire Disaster Dragon: Volcano’ erupting.

I checked the map, but even though it’s over 100 kilometers away, is it still having an effect?

Just to add, the subspace is large, but on the map it’s treated as a single area, so the whole thing can be grasped.

“Not only that, but it’s quite hot.”

“It seems lava is constantly flowing from ‘Volcano’.”

《Hot!》

Maria reports after checking the map (subspace-compatible version).

“What should we do? Ride our dragon mounts and approach? If Master wishes it, I’ll do my best.”

“I’m not good with heat…”

“I’m not fond of it either. Also, in terms of numbers, we’d need each of us to carry two people. Would we be able to move quickly…?”

The three dragonkin girls each speak up, but I shake my head in denial.

“No, this time I only brought you for leveling up. The dragonkin group and the Hero group don’t need to do anything.”

“It’s a shame. I wanted to fight such a big target…”

The headlong-charging Hero, Cynthia, doesn’t flinch even when the opponent is a Disaster Dragon.

“Cynthia-san, were you planning to challenge that thing?”

“Yes.”

Rico looks aghast, but Cynthia is serious.

No, even Cynthia can’t take on a Disaster Dragon. She’d just die.

Maybe I should have brought Kate, the stopper…

“Master, getting back to the topic, how are you planning to fight the Disaster Dragon? Are you going to punch it like usual?”

Mio said “like usual.”

Do I punch things that much? …Ah, I do.

“It wouldn’t be impossible, but getting close would make it even hotter. Since we’re here anyway, let’s try that.”

“That?”

“Yeah, my new skill… or rather, what should I call it, a new ability?”

“An ability that’s not a skill?”

In terms of classification, it would probably be considered a trait?

It’s an ability, a trait, obtained through a Special Power.

“It’ll be faster to show you.”

Saying that, I take a single step toward the direction where ‘Volcano’ is.

The next moment, the ground ahead of my stepping foot splits.

With a sound that rivals the roar of the eruption, the fissure spreads.

The crack continues to spread endlessly, eventually reaching the ‘Fire Disaster Dragon: Volcano’ and greatly disrupting its posture. The roar echoes once more.

“Eh? What was that just now?”

Mio barely manages to say that much, while the others are dumbfounded.

“As you can see, it’s the ability of the ‘Earth Disaster Dragon: Earthquake.’”

“…You said you didn’t get any skills from ‘Earthquake’, right?”

“Yeah. This isn’t a skill, but a unique trait of ‘Earthquake’. When I defeated ‘Earthquake’, I directly absorbed its soul using a combo of \<Life and Death Authority LV9> and \<Multiple Existence LV7>.”

“Ah, that crazy one…”

The effect of \<Life and Death Authority LV9> is ‘contact with the soul.’

I became able to touch souls with the same ease as touching another person’s body.

And the effect of \<Multiple Existence LV7> is ‘manipulation of the soul.’

\<Life and Death Authority> is just contact, \<Multiple Existence> is just manipulation, but when the two are combined, ‘contact and manipulation of the soul’ becomes possible.

This allowed me to erase hostility from Feather Dragons toward dragonkin, or directly obtain information from souls.

No, it was so godlike it was honestly just scary.

These powers were obtained when I defeated ‘Earthquake.’

With \<Life and Death Authority LV8>, by absorbing the corpse and soul of a defeated opponent, I can use that target’s skills.

However, ‘Earthquake’ existed as a soul-only entity in the subspace, so it couldn’t be absorbed as-is. Or rather, it would be more accurate to say it would have been meaningless.

So I used \<Life and Death Authority LV9> and \<Multiple Existence LV7> to alter it into a state that could be more easily absorbed.

As a result, I can now use ‘Earthquake’s’ abilities and traits almost as they are.

Just to be clear, I usually keep it sealed so I don’t accidentally use it.

“Conversely, I can do things like this too.”

I say that and take another step.

Nothing happens.

“Nothing happened…”

《Is it over?》

“No, not yet. There should be an impact coming, so make sure you don’t bite your tongue.”

《Okay》

After a while, a tremendous impact strikes the ground.

“Kyah! An earthquake!?”

“W-what is this!?”

“I think a rock pillar thrust up ‘Volcano’, lifted it, and the impact was when it fell back down.”

I lightly take another step.

With a thump, the ground bulges, and a rock pillar about two meters high and one meter in diameter shoots up.

“I made a giant version of this come out from under ‘Volcano’. That’s how it floated.”

‘Volcano’ probably floated in the air for the first time in its life.

A good experience, right? …Though I’m going to kill it after this.

“This is also ‘Earthquake’s’ ability. I saw it too.”

Blue, who accompanied us during the ‘Earthquake’ battle, says.

“Master, is this free location targeting?”

“Yeah. At least anywhere within the range I can confirm on the map. Since it’s a trait, not magic, MP consumption is naturally zero.”

I answer Mio’s question.

“Zero MP to lift a mountain-sized monster like that? Isn’t that insane?”

“Yeah, it’s insane. By the way, the stepping action isn’t required. I just do it because it makes it easier to imagine the activation.”

It seems ‘Earthquake’ couldn’t turn its ability off and was constantly growing rocks, but I can turn the ability on and off.

When using it, I need to activate the ability and strongly imagine the effect. It’s to prevent accidental activation.

“I could have a serious battle one-on-one, but since we have a lot of people this time, let’s prioritize safety and cheese it from a distance. We’ll rapid-fire those rock pillars… rock spears.”

“That’s brutal. Cruel.”

“I’m glad Jin-sama chose a safe method.”

Mio gives a sympathetic look toward the unseen ‘Volcano’, while Maria is happy with my choice.

“So, in other words, die!”

I stomp with all my might on the spot.

-Gogogogogogogogogo-

In sync with the stomping, a roar echoes from the distance.

-Gogogogogogogogogo-

Before, it was rock pillars and the goal was lifting it, but this time they’re rock spears, with sharp tips. The damage should clearly be greater.

-Gogogogogogogogogo-

“Somehow, this feels surreal.”

“From just here, it looks like Jin-kun is just stomping…”

《Go, Master!》

Encouraged by Dora, I speed up a little.

-Gogogogogogogogogo-

“‘Volcano’s’ volume is decreasing! It’s at an incredible rate!”

“When we’re with master, it’s hard to get a sense of how strong the opponent is. It’s troubling.”

Hearing Rico’s report, Cynthia has a complicated expression.

-Gogogogogogogogogo-

“So we really did just come along.”

“Easy work, huh.”

“If possible, I’d like to work as a dragon mount, though.”

Blue is diligent.

-Gogogogogogogogogo-

“All right, done.”

I stop stomping.

When I check the map, the ‘Fire Disaster Dragon: Volcano’ in the distance has lost its power and is disappearing into particles.

“Ab-sorb!”

Those particles gush toward me and are absorbed into my body.

Following the same flow as with the ‘Earth Disaster Dragon: Earthquake’, I can now use the abilities of the ‘Fire Disaster Dragon: Volcano’ as well.

And then, a large-scale skill level-up.

Each of the Hero group leveled up by one. Maria is now \<Hero LV8>, Cynthia is \<Hero LV6>, and Rico is \<Hero LV4>.

Among the dragonkin, Dora leveled up by one to \<Dragon Magic LV9>. The other three leveled up by two: Blue is now \<Dragon Magic LV6>, Leaf is \<Dragon Magic LV3>, and Mikazuki is \<Dragon Magic LV5>.

Additionally, Sera also leveled up to \<Proof of Hero LV8>.

Come to think of it, \<Proof of Hero> was a skill with levels. What changes when it levels up?

A: The multiplier for physical enhancement changes.

Plain.

Well, it’s strong and effective, but plain.

Multiple Existence has reached LV8.

A new ability has been unlocked.

\<Multiple Existence LV8>

Adds a subspace management function. Owned subspaces are reassigned directly under \<Multiple Existence>.

And then, the long-awaited Special Power level-up.

…..

\<Life and Death Authority> didn’t level up…?

W-well, just \<Multiple Existence> leveling up is enough, right?

So then, what kind of effect does the new \<Multiple Existence> have?

A: You can now manage subspaces where Disaster Dragons have been defeated. Currently, you own the subspaces of the ‘Earth Disaster Dragon: Earthquake’ and the ‘Fire Disaster Dragon: Volcano.’

Hmm, so what can I actually do with that?

A: You have obtained administrator privileges over the subspaces. In a sense, it’s close to being a labyrinth ruler. In managed subspaces, you can use almost all functions, such as two-way transfer, setting environmental information like temperature and room temperature, and so on.

Simply put, it’s an effect that lets me privatize those subspaces.

Right now, the only large areas of land I can freely use are the 50th-floor range of the labyrinth and the green space at the center of the Brown Wall Kingdom.

Now, ‘subspaces’ will be added to that.

They might be suitable for things that can’t be done in the other two, like practicing new techniques or work that could cause collateral damage. Practicing abilities absorbed from Disaster Dragons, for example.

---

At last, boss-class enemies are starting to die off-screen.

Meanwhile, the protagonist is just stomping his feet. What an image.

By the way, please imagine ‘Volcano’ as something like Godzilla or Groudon, with a volcano on its back. There was no description, so just in case.

Next time: “Seizing the Guild and the Collapse of the Sky Castle.” Look forward to it.

+++

## **168: Taking Control of the Guild and the Fall of the Sky Castle**

**AN:** I finished writing the April Fool’s joke.

This year, it’s a normal IF story. It’s not an different story.

---

“By the way, what kind of skill did Maria get from \<Hero LV8>?”

\<Hero> skills don’t have effects on their own, and you gain a new skill with each level up.

From a certain level onward, you start obtaining unique-class skills, so by level 8, you would expect to gain something appropriately powerful.

That said, I already had a pretty good idea of the name.

“Yes. The skill I obtained is called \<Yata Mirror>. It nullifies all status ailments and grants resistance to elemental attacks.”

“The name was exactly what I expected, and it’s simply strong. It’s basically a natural enemy to opponents who rely on magic or status effects. That said, it’s a shame that it mostly strengthens areas you weren’t really struggling with…”

She already has resistance to status ailments, so the effects overlap.

And as for magic resistance, we have someone with complete immunity, so it doesn’t stand out.

“It seems this effect can be applied to all party members, so normally it should greatly stabilize a party’s combat power.”

“All party members? That’s impressive.”

It was stronger than I expected.

The entire party becomes immune to status ailments and gains resistance to elemental attacks.

It really is power befitting a hero’s party.

“\<Hero> skills are strong! I want one too! Cynthia wants to level up quickly!”

“It’s nice that it works solo as well, but since I don’t form parties, the additional effect doesn’t really matter to me.”

Cynthia, who forms parties, was excited, while Rico, who mainly works alone as a maid, showed little interest.

“I’ll call you when we fight another disaster dragon, so you can expect a chance to level up then.”

“Yay!”

“When that time comes, I look forward to it.”

Hopefully, \<Life and Death Authority> will level up too.

《Master! Dora’s breath got stronger too!》

Dora fires her breath toward an empty area.

Blue, Leaf, and Mikazuki are also test-firing.

Since Dora’s \<Dragon Magic> skill level is high, her breath stands out above the rest.

“My base stats were already too high, so it’s hard to really feel the effect of \<Proof of the Hero>…”

Sera says this with an unconvinced look while moving her body.

“Ugh, everyone is so lucky! Mio wants an innate special skill too!”

Watching everyone test their newly leveled skills, Mio says this enviously.

If you count my and Sakura’s Powers as innate, then Mio is the only one without an innate special skill. That’s kind of sad.

“I don’t think there’s anything you can do about innate abilities at this point…”

“Try again in your next life.”

“Master, that’s way too soon! I’m going to live at least another hundred years!”

“You’re surprisingly greedy.”

In a medieval-level civilization, living past 100 seems like a bit much for a human, doesn’t it?

“Being by your side, Master, I don’t think it’s that hard… By the way, what kind of Power did you have? Was it convenient? Strong? Crazy?”

Mio switches topics quickly and asks about my Power.

What do you mean by “crazy”? …Ah, \<Life and Death Authority LV9>.

“It’s just conveniently useful. Like the previous labyrinth, I can now manage a subspace. I can move in and out freely, so I don’t need a ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’ anymore.”

“Oh! Then this can become a training ground just for us?”

“Yeah, that’s the plan. It’s perfect for practicing big moves.”

Looks like Mio arrived at the same idea I did.

Having land where you don’t need to worry about collateral damage is important.

Until now, we used the ‘Gray World’ for that, but that place has a lot of restrictions.

“…You’re right, it’s definitely convenient, but compared to the combination of \<Life and Death Authority LV8> and \<Multiple Existence LV7>, it feels kind of plain.”

“I can’t really argue with that.”

Having the effect of two abilities is no joke.

As for \<Multiple Existence>, it doesn’t necessarily get stronger just because the level is higher.

Basically, it gives you the effects you need at the time.

“Alright, let’s head out of the subspace with this plain ability. If you want to do test firing, you can come back anytime.”

“Okay!” x many

Come to think of it, I haven’t seen the ‘Disaster Dragon of Fire: Volcano’ in person even once.

When we exited the subspace, Yurisuzu was lying upside down, had wet herself, and was unconscious.

She was also completely naked. Naked, flipped over, legs spread wide.

Yeah, that pose is bad in a lot of ways.

“…Ah, I completely forgot.”

“Master, please notify us if you’re coming back.”

Claude clutches his head when he notices Yurisuzu’s miserable state.

“Sorry. I was too focused on stomping the fire dragon to death, so Yurisuzu slipped my mind.”

“Stomping to death?” x8

The adventurers who stayed behind didn’t seem to understand what I was saying.

Claude and the others turn their eyes to Mio, apparently recognizing her as the designated explainer.

“Master’s new technique was linked to stomping.”

“I see… I see?”

It sounds like they kind of understand, but also refuse to understand anything beyond that.

“It’ll be faster if you just see it. I’ll show you someday.”

“Please do.”

Claude and the others are diligent about combat, so they don’t seem hesitant to see a new technique, but I doubt it will be useful for their own fighting.

It just looks like I’m stomping the ground from far away. Getting killed by that would feel pretty unfair.

“Jin-sama, what shall we do about her?”

Maria asks while casting ‘Purify’ on Yurisuzu.

“My objective is complete, so Claude, sorry, but could you take her back?”

“Yes, that’s fine. What will you do after this, Master?”

“The hero group and dragonkin group will disband here. We didn’t come here by legitimate means, so we’ll sneak back using a ‘Portal’. Then we’ll enjoy the hot springs again.”

With the threat of the ‘Disaster Dragon of Fire: Volcano’ gone, there’s no need to rush enjoying the hot springs.

That said, since we’re already here, it’s true that we want to enjoy them as much as possible.

We can sightsee today and head back tomorrow.

“We’ll do a bit of sightseeing too. We need to buy souvenirs for acquaintances…”

“I recommend hot spring buns.”

A man who doesn’t try to be fancy with souvenirs. That’s Shindo Jin.

“I’ll keep that in mind.”

“Oh, Claude. By the way, what happens to our request?”

Coco from the adventurer group asks Claude.

“I forgot to ask… Technically, the request was completed when we met and talked, so I think it’s considered fulfilled, but we’ll ask Yurisuzu when she wakes up.”

“We also need to think about whether to continue being adventurers.”

At Yuria’s words, the adventurer group’s expressions darken.

This request was a trap to lure Yuria.

Yurisuzu abused her position as guild master, devaluing the very existence of the Adventurers Guild. If being an adventurer loses its appeal, there’s no reason to continue.

Yurisuzu’s actions have not yet been forgiven.

“You don’t need to force yourselves to keep being adventurers. You’ve already carried out my orders.”

“Understood. We’ll discuss it among ourselves.”

I told them to become S-rank adventurers, but I never said they had to remain S-rank adventurers.

If they have reasons to quit, it can’t be helped.

“That aside, I’m also curious about the Sky Castle.”

“Are you referring to the ‘Disaster Dragon of Wind: Tempest’?”

I shake my head at Sera’s question.

“No, I don’t really care about that. What’s important is the Sky Castle itself. A floating island in the sky is nothing but a tourist attraction!”

“Master, you really never waver. Well, Mio understands how you feel. Honestly, I really want to go too. I wouldn’t call it a tourist spot, but it ranks high on my list of places I want to visit.”

To be blunt, I don’t care about the ‘Disaster Dragon of Wind: Tempest’.

I want to go to the Sky Castle. I want to treat people on the ground like trash.

In fact, as Yurisuzu said, the Sky Castle is the least problematic of the disaster dragons.

Unlike with the Earth Disaster Dragon and Ulysses, she’s not sealed and suffering.

Unlike the Fire Disaster Dragon and Yurisuzu, it’s not openly active and at risk of being killed.

The Sky Castle is ideal for a ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’ to live on with minimal suffering.

Yuriela isn’t particularly troubled, and the risk of breaking the seal is low. So if you ask whether I want to go out of my way to defeat it, the answer is NO.

“I want to go to the Sky Castle, but I don’t want to get involved with the elves. That’s the problem.”

“We wouldn’t be welcomed even if we went…”

“I’ve already had Claude and the others place a ‘Portal’, so going there is easy.”

During the mess with Yuriela, I secretly had them set up a ‘Portal’.

We can teleport there anytime.

“If it comes to it, we can turn invisible with \<Non-Attribute Magic> and sneak in for sightseeing.”

The unique-class skill \<Non-Attribute Magic> includes a spell that makes you invisible.

“So you’re really just going to look.”

“If Jin-sama goes, I’ll accompany you.”

《Dora too!》

Even if we go, we should finish sightseeing the Guild Union District first.

I’m the type who prefers to fully enjoy one tourist spot at a time rather than juggling several.

That night, after thoroughly sightseeing the city of Bolken.

There was a naked woman in front of me.

“Please, make me your slave.”

Yurisuzu visited our inn during our post-dinner relaxation time and begged us with a naked dogeza.

For the record, she didn’t come here naked.

Also, aside from Maria, the women had gone to the bath.

“What are you suddenly saying?”

“I swear absolute loyalty to you, so please show mercy.”

“Claude, explain.”

Yurisuzu didn’t come alone. She was accompanied by Claude and the others.

I couldn’t understand just from Yurisuzu’s words, so I asked Claude, who was averting his eyes from the naked body.

“In short, she’s saying she’ll become your slave if you spare her life. Yurisuzu is terrified of you from the bottom of her heart. She thought that if she became your slave and property, she wouldn’t risk unknowingly displeasing you and getting killed.”

Sure enough, Yurisuzu is trembling even now.

I can understand her reasoning, but she’s extreme.

…Come to think of it, most high elves are extreme people. Yuria is probably the exception.

“What about your position as guild master of the Adventurers Guild?”

“If you wish it, I’ll resign immediately!”

An instant reply.

Since the organization relies heavily on the magic tools Yurisuzu creates, there’s a high chance it wouldn’t function properly if she quit.

Even though Yurisuzu herself devalued the Adventurers Guild, completely collapsing it would cause chaos everywhere.

It’s safer to have her continue running the guild.

“I’ll make you my slave, so continue the Adventurers Guild. I basically won’t interfere.”

“Thank you very much! Thank you very much!”

It’s not so much that I won’t interfere, it’s that I’ve already lost interest…

So with that, I promptly enslaved Yurisuzu using \<Slave Arts>.

“By the way, what happened with Claude and the others?”

“Our request was considered completed the moment we entered the guild master’s room, and going to the volcano was also treated as a request from the guild master. In exchange for money and a large number of magic tools, we agreed to keep quiet about this incident and… to act as intermediaries to you, Master.”

So that’s why Claude and the others came here with Yurisuzu.

“I’m grateful to Claude and the others. They haven’t fully forgiven me, but at least they agreed in a way that won’t cause further harm. They took all the magic tools I’d gathered, though…”

Yurisuzu, saying lines like that while doing a naked dogeza, really doesn’t look cool.

“This incident made us distrust the Adventurers Guild, but we decided that destroying it or weakening its influence wasn’t a good idea. We obtained the magic tools in case Yurisuzu wasn’t able to become your slave. Either way, we intended to give them to you, so please accept them.”

It seems Claude and the others weren’t planning to do anything drastic to the guild.

And apparently, they acquired Yurisuzu’s magic tools for me.

“I’ll gratefully accept them.”

“Are you interested in magic tools?”

Yurisuzu asks with an expectant tone.

“Yeah. Collecting magic tools is one of my hobbies.”

“In that case! If you leave it to me, I can create many magic tools for you!”

Ah, she saw this as a chance to sell herself.

“I’d be happy about that, but I already have someone in charge of that.”

“I’m a ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’, so I can make higher-performance magic tools than ordinary humans!”

“No, like I said, the other person in charge is also a ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’. The Earth Disaster Dragon’s ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’, Ulysses, is also my slave. She can probably make higher-performance tools than you.”

The innate skill of a ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’ strengthens production skills.

“…Huh?”

“At least make magic tools that don’t overlap with what Ulysses makes.”

“Y-yes…”

She proposed something thinking it was something only she could do, only to find someone even better was already there.

Yurisuzu slumps her shoulders dejectedly.

Incidentally, Yuria is not a ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’, so she doesn’t have magic tool creation skills.

…Come to think of it, Yuria, Ulysses, Yurisuzu. The names of ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’ are confusing.

Especially Ulysses and Yurisuzu sound too similar. In cases like this, it’s first come, first served.

“Yurisuzu, your name is too similar to Ulysses, so change it.”

“Eh?”

“Right. ‘Yuri’ is confusing, so let’s remove it and go with ‘Suzu’. Yurisuzu, from today on, your name is Suzu. Got it?”

“Y-yes! From today on, I’m Suzu!”

And so, Yurisuzu, now Suzu, joined my subordinates.

She’ll continue acting as guild master as usual, and in her spare time, she’ll make magic tools for me.

Since there’s still a lack of trust after this incident, I won’t tell her the details of my ability just yet.

“M-Master has finally taken control of the Adventurers Guild…”

After her bath, Mio says this upon seeing Suzu, who is still naked and doing a dogeza as a slave.

No, I told you, I’m not interested. Especially in management. I’m 100% not touching that.

The next day, we left the Guild Union District in the morning.

And in the afternoon, Maria and I began the Sky Castle infiltration operation.

Though we called it an infiltration operation, it was really just sightseeing while invisible using \<Non-Attribute Magic>.

Bringing a whole group felt excessive, so it ended up just being me, who wanted to go the most, and Maria as my guard.

Mio also wanted to come, but since we decided to go this morning and she had already made plans yesterday, she couldn’t participate.

“Master, can’t we go tomorrow?”

“I feel like today is better, so rejected.”

“Seriously…”

I feel bad for Mio as she slumps her shoulders, but it’s a case of strike while the iron is hot.

If there’s a next time, I’ll bring Mio along.

《Looks like there are no residential areas around here.》

《Given the proximity to a disaster dragon, it’s likely unbearable for elves.》

We teleported via ‘Portal’ to the point where Claude and the others were teleported by Yuriela. In other words, a location close to the physical body of the ‘Disaster Dragon of Wind: Tempest’.

Since normal elves can’t withstand the miasma of a disaster dragon, there are no people around here.

《Approaching densely populated residential areas is risky.》

Even if invisible, you can’t erase all traces of your existence.

That’s why we’re communicating entirely via telepathy.

《The central castle is even riskier.》

The Sky Castle is a floating island with a diameter of about 15 km.

At its center stands a massive Western-style castle befitting its name, with residential areas spreading outward from it.

The population is around 1,000. All are elves except Yuriela. There are no half-elves.

There also seems to be an agricultural district outside the residential area, supplying food from its crops. Water is produced by magic, so there are no ponds or rivers.

This area would normally be considered agricultural based on its distance from the castle, but as mentioned earlier, it’s close to the disaster dragon and thus abandoned.

As an aside, the reason it’s close to the disaster dragon is that the wind disaster dragon’s head is around here, tilted slightly upward.

《Even if we look around the outer perimeter, the scenery isn’t that great.》

As is common with castles in the sky, the Sky Castle is surrounded by clouds.

It’s a disappointing design that prevents you from enjoying the view from the perimeter.

《It can’t be helped. Let’s wander around the perimeter and agricultural district.》

《I will accompany you.》

We came here without really thinking about what we wanted to do. The act of ‘coming’ itself was the goal.

If only we could stroll openly through populated areas…

Let’s start with the perimeter.

《Yup, it’s nothing but clouds.》

《The underside is also covered in clouds.》

We step over the token fence and look out over the surroundings from the very edge.

The clouds surrounding the Sky Castle envelop it entirely.

Only the upper part that takes in sunlight is open, and you can’t see into the Sky Castle from any direction except above.

《It doesn’t look like thunderclouds. If we wanted to, could we enter from outside?》

A: The clouds are rotating at extremely high wind speeds, making it difficult to break through by normal means. While there are no clouds above, the wind speed is also high, so entry from above is not possible either.

It seems there is a defensive mechanism in place. Let’s call it the ‘Windcloud Barrier’. Sounds cool.

《Despite the strong winds around it, the Sky Castle itself is completely windless.》

As Maria says, the land area is almost perfectly windless.

Otherwise, we wouldn’t be doing things like stepping over fences and peering over the edge. Well, I’d be fine even if I fell, but mentally…

《No wind, no rain, no change in climate. It’s an elven, closed-off, stagnant space.》

I won’t say that not changing is bad.

If you see change as a risk, then keeping the land guarding the disaster dragon’s seal unchanged could be considered a form of safety.

Though personally, I’d get bored in less than three days.

Staring at clouds forever isn’t interesting, so we move to the agricultural district.

Except for the areas close to the disaster dragon, various crops are grown in the ring-shaped farmlands.

The body of a disaster dragon holds tremendous energy, and just like crops grown on the Earth Disaster Dragon Earthquake, those grown on the Wind Disaster Dragon Tempest are highly nutritious.

And not just that…

A: Many species that have gone extinct on the ground still exist here.

So that’s how it is.

Preserving extinct species, it’s like Noah’s Ark.

Though the ark itself being a mass of disaster is the twist…

《Jin-sama, since we’re here, shall we secure some?》

《No, that’s not acceptable. Taking from someone who isn’t an enemy and who hasn’t wronged us isn’t my style. And that doesn’t just apply to skills. Yuriela acted semi-hostile, but that doesn’t mean stealing crops is right.》

《Understood.》

I hate crop thieves.

Stealing crops that someone put their heart and soul into growing without compensation is despicable.

What? When is it okay to steal crops someone put their heart and soul into growing?

That’s why I only take everything from enemies. Looting enemies is normal and not a problem.

When I take from someone who owes me, I take one point and return two, so I’m fine mentally.

While actually looking over the crops, I notice something on the map and ask Alta about it.

《There are crops, but no livestock. Are there even any living creatures other than elves and high elves in the Sky Castle?》

A: There are none. It is not an environment ordinary creatures can adapt to, and small creatures cannot survive due to the disaster dragon’s miasma.

In fiction, elves are often portrayed as vegetarians, but in this world, elves normally eat meat and fish.

However, the elves of the Sky Castle have no meat, making them completely vegetarian.

Exclusive, reclusive, vegetarian, and magic users. The elves here perfectly match the stereotypical image of elves!

Just learning that makes the trip worthwhile.

A: When she was interacting with Yurisuzu, or rather Suzu, it seems meat was imported from the ground.

…

《Let’s go home…》

《Understood. ‘Portal’.》

My enthusiasm plummets to rock bottom, so we decide to return via the ‘Portal’ Maria set up.

A: Please wait a moment.

Alta stops me.

If Alta stops me, it means an event occurred. What happened?

A: Someone has teleported into the Sky Castle. That person’s name is ‘Gired’.

…Who?

《Jin-sama, he’s the high elf who sealed Ulysses in a crystal.》

《Oh!》

Right. I had categorized him as a person to watch out for.

Forgetting about someone I marked as dangerous is pretty pathetic.

Still, what is this Gired doing in the Sky Castle?

Come to think of it, there are clans here connected to Ulysses. So maybe Gired has a home here?

A: It doesn’t seem to be a simple homecoming. I will replay the conversation between the two.

Alta can grasp all audio within the map. Reproducing past conversations is trivial.

(Hehehehehe, Princess Yuriela, it’s been a while.)

The replay is sped up to catch up to the present, making the voice slightly higher-pitched.

It’s hard to distinguish gender at that pitch, but this is probably Gired’s voice.

(Gired, you still have that disgusting laugh.)

(Hehehe, you’re as harsh as ever, Princess. I’ve brought the latest version of the promised sealing crystal. So, where is Lady Yuria?)

The sealing crystal, is that the one that trapped Ulysses?

A: Yes.

From the conversation, it seems Yuriela intended to seal Yuria.

（Yuria is not here. We failed to capture her due to Yurisuzu’s incompetence.）

（Heh? That’s troublesome. I’ve finally completed the 78th-generation sealing crystal, but without the key ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’, it’s meaningless.）

（…Since you were able to come here, the disaster dragon’s seal hasn’t been broken? It seems Yurisuzu wasn’t killed. Which means Yuria is also alive.）

（Heh, Princess? Is something wrong?）

（It’s nothing. Gired, next time, you will also assist in capturing Yuria.）

（Heh? I don’t mind, but is that okay? Even if I make contact with Lady Yuria? She was extremely wary of me, you know?）

（Yes, it’s fine. Yuria had amnesia. …Isn’t that a flaw in the previous sealing crystal?）

（Heh! Heh! Ah! Ah! So it really did happen! When I analyzed the 77th, I found there was a possibility it could destroy memories!）

（If you knew that, you should have told me beforehand.）

（Heh, sorry. I only realized recently. I never imagined the sealing crystal would go berserk and activate teleportation magic, so I was focused on analyzing that. I guess combining your magic tools as-is was a bad idea.）

（Don’t blame me. This was your mistake.）

（Heh, my apologies.）

（Teleportation and amnesia… No wonder she couldn’t be found. There are no such defects this time, correct?）

（Hehehe! Of course. This time, my theory should be flawless. Just as you wished, it allows the sealed ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’ ability to be used externally.）

（To protect the seal, sealing the ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’ is essential. However, letting the abilities she possesses remain locked away unused is wasteful. With this, I should have been able to retire without regrets.）

（Hehehehe. Yes, yes, my research progressed as well. I can only be grateful to Lady Yuria, who became the human pillar, and to Lady Yurina, who was sacrificed as a failed prototype with the 50th-generation sealing crystal.）

（Yurina… Ah yes, there was someone like that. A human pillar candidate who died without being useful to me has no value.）

The audio stopped here.

The replay must have caught up to the present.

To summarize:

What they intended to use on Yuria was not the same sealing crystal as Ulysses, but an improved version that allows the ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’ ability to be used externally.

Yuria disappearing from the Sky Castle and losing her memories was due to an accident caused by Gired’s incomplete improved sealing crystal going berserk.

Yuria’s predecessor as a ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’ candidate died in a sealing crystal accident.

What a bunch of irredeemable trash…

Ah, right. I promised to let Ulysses punch Gired once.

He’s the type you could beat to death without remorse.

A: Master. A problem has occurred.

…Let’s hear it.

A: Yuriela was attacked by one of the elves and will die shortly. …She has died.

What?

A: The father of Yurina, mentioned in the conversation with Gired, overheard the discussion. In a fit of despair over his daughter’s death, he launched a magical attack on Yuriela, and the surprise attack succeeded. Gired escaped using a teleportation magic tool made by Yuriela.

Wow…

That’s completely self-inflicted.

This means the seal on the ‘Disaster Dragon of Wind: Tempest’ will be broken and the Sky Castle will collapse, right?

A: It will.

…

Ah, right. There is just one thing I need to say…

“Balls.”

---

**AN:** It wouldn’t be an exaggeration to say this entire chapter existed just for that final line.

I couldn’t come up with a reason for Jin to kill Yuriela, so she died by the consequences of her own actions.

And as usual, the truth is revealed carelessly.

Gired survived by sheer luck, so he’ll get one more chance to do something before he dies.

## **169: The Liberation of the Wind Disaster Dragon and the Spoils**

**AN:** Jealous of the popularity of the spell of destruction.

---

—Gogogogogogo—

Because I cast the spell of destruction, the Sky Castle began to collapse (some exaggeration included).

For now it is only shaking, but with Yuriela dead, its eventual collapse is a certainty.

Looking at the map, I can see the elves running around in confusion in the distance.

“Jin-sama, we should escape.”

When I look, the “Storm Barrier” that had protected the Sky Castle is gone.

At this point, it looks like we could escape even without using a ‘Portal’.

“No, we can’t just leave this place as it is. Alta, organize a recovery team.”

A: Understood.

The Sky Castle is land formed around the ‘Wind Disaster Dragon: Tempest’ as its core.

With Yuriela’s death, the sealing of the ‘Priestess Princess’ is released, and when the ‘Wind Disaster Dragon: Tempest’ revives, the Sky Castle will collapse.

In other words, fragments of the Sky Castle will rain down on the surface from high altitude. The Sky Castle is over the sea, but it would be strange to say there will be zero impact elsewhere.

So I decided to deploy my subordinates riding dragonkin and Lesser Wind Dragons to recover falling debris and the resident elves.

“‘Summon’, ‘Summon’, ‘Summon’…”

We repeatedly cast ‘Summon’, calling forth dragon knight maids who were ready to act.

After using ‘Summon’ a certain number, those who had been called with ‘Summon’ began calling others with ‘Summon’ in turn.

In the blink of an eye, more than a hundred pairs of dragon knights had assembled.

I raised my voice and issued instructions to them.

“This Sky Castle is about to fall! I want you to collect falling debris with \<Infinite Storage> so it doesn’t cause damage! And if you have the capacity, collect the elves too!”

To be honest, I have no obligation or emotional attachment to the elves here, so if they died, it wouldn’t really matter. However, for certain reasons, some of them need to be kept alive.

“Yes!” ×100+

The dragon knights who received my orders descended one after another from the Sky Castle.

Since we don’t know what will happen when ‘Tempest’ awakens, I have them keep some distance at first and wait.

Once the number of dragon knights had thinned out, I summoned Sakura and the rest of the main party, Blue, Leaf, the three dragonkin girls Mikazuki included, and the Hero pair Cynthia and Rico.

“I’m going to defeat the ‘Wind Disaster Dragon: Tempest’ now.”

“If it’s an aerial battle, it’s my turn!”

“I’ll accompany you as well.”

“No.”

Blue and Maria asserted themselves, but I cut them down decisively.

“Blue, do you have confidence you can fly in that wind?”

“Huh? Ah, um, honestly speaking, that would be tough, I think.”

No matter how flight-specialized a Sky Dragon is, flying through that storm would be difficult.

“Maria, can you keep up with me without riding Blue?”

“…No, that would be difficult.”

Basically, Maria has no means of flight.

She can move through the air, but like Blue, she wouldn’t be able to act properly in that gale.

“It’s so I can fight ‘Tempest’ without worry. Give up this time.”

It’s not the same as fighting under overwhelmingly advantageous conditions in subspace.

Considering the impact on the surroundings, the only option is for me to go all out alone and seal it.

“All right, I’ll endure it this time too. Master, do your best. And then, later, ride me, okay?”

Knowing the power of Disaster Dragons, Blue realized that she couldn’t casually talk about an “aerial battle” against one.

“…”

On the other hand, Maria, her face pale, struggled internally for a while before letting her shoulders slump.

“…I resent my own lack of strength compared to a Disaster Dragon. Jin-sama, please be careful.”

Even Maria can’t do anything without a means of movement.

Judging that she couldn’t stop me through persuasion, she seemed to give up.

“Sakura, do the same as the dragon knights and handle the debris.”

“Understood… Jin-kun, please don’t overdo it…”

“Leave things on the ground to us.”

《Dora will do her best too!》

Sakura and the others are used to acting while riding dragonkin, so I entrust them with debris handling.

The Hero pair are for leveling up their \<Hero> skills, just like with the ‘Fire Disaster Dragon’.

Cynthia does have a Lesser Wind Dragon, so she can work as well.

As for Rico, I’m counting on her precognition for danger avoidance. Hopefully it won’t be needed.

“By the way, Master, if you’re not riding Blue-chan, how are you going to fight?”

Mio asks, as if she just thought of it.

“If it’s another means of flight… is it the ‘Undead Wings’?”

“No, this time I’m going completely serious… Rain, I’m counting on you.”

Rain, my contracted spirit, enters my body.

The secret art of merging with a spirit to enhance one’s abilities, ‘Spiritization’.

‘Spiritization’ with Rain has the secondary effect of granting flight capability.

This is the safest way to fly. In the worst case, no one else will be hurt.

“So you’re really serious, Master. Is it that kind of opponent?”

“Yeah. …It’s about to collapse. Everyone, prepare to evacuate!”

At my command, everyone mounts dragonkin or Lesser Wind Dragons and leaves the Sky Castle.

After everyone had evacuated, the landmass of the Sky Castle began to crumble apart.

The dragon knight maids on standby begin recovering the debris. And as a bonus, the falling elves too.

‘Tempest’ probably hasn’t fully awakened yet.

It feels like someone half-asleep, squirming around in bed.

“Master, wouldn’t it be better to attack now, while it’s not awake yet?”

“I don’t intend to attack ‘Tempest’ until it’s fully awakened. There are two reasons.”

I reject Mio’s suggestion from atop Mikazuki and explain.

This collapse of the Sky Castle and ‘Tempest’s’ awakening, while Yuri and Claude and the others are somewhat involved, is fundamentally caused by Yuriela and Gired.

If ‘Tempest’ causes damage, responsibility can be said to lie with Yuriela and Gired.

If we attack before ‘Tempest’ fully awakens, we can no longer say it was unrelated to its awakening.

We want to be in the position of benevolent third parties who suppress ‘Tempest’s’ damage.

I have no intention of taking responsibility for cleaning up after someone else. Even if that means damage occurs.

“Master, you really have a troublesome personality…”

“I’m aware of that. It sounds like an excuse, but what’s important is the justification… or rather, whether I can accept it myself.”

What’s important isn’t whether others see it, but whether I myself am satisfied.

I’m the type who puts principles first.

In other words, like this.

My principles > An insurmountable wall > Damage to the surroundings > > > Falling elves

“So what’s the other reason?”

“I have a bad feeling. My intuition is telling me that attacking in a half-baked state is a bad idea.”

“Isn’t that reason alone enough?”

“I can’t deny that.”

To be a bit more specific, it feels like a lot of things might go out of control.

If I were confident I could finish it in one blow, that would be different, but otherwise, it feels better not to.

Except for Maria, who wanted to stay as close as possible, my companions headed off to collect falling debris.

“It looks like it’s about to fully awaken.”

Most of the land that had been above ‘Tempest’ had collapsed.

Perhaps because awakening is near, the winds blowing around us feel like they’re gradually getting stronger.

The ‘Wind Disaster Dragon: Tempest’, unlike the ‘Earth Disaster Dragon: Earthquake’, was a Western-style dragon.

Jade-like scales, bat-like wings, and a long tail are its defining features.

Like ‘Earthquake’, it’s probably about 10 km long.

And then, at last, ‘Tempest’ fully awakened.

The moment ‘Tempest’s’ jade-colored eyes opened, it opened its mouth wide and roared.

“AAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAA!!!”

I called it a roar, but in reality, almost no sound came out.

It was just a shockwave.

“Crap.”

If it had only been the shockwave, that would have been fine, but it also scattered the remaining Sky Castle debris.

Large chunks of debris flew off in all directions at tremendous speed.

…If that fell on populated areas, the damage would be catastrophic!

“Maria!”

“Yes!”

Maria and I repeatedly use ‘Visual Transfer’ to recover the flying debris.

“As expected of a Disaster Dragon. It brings calamity just by waking up…”

Naturally, it seems it will continue to bring calamity even after waking.

In the brief moment I looked away, tornadoes had formed around ‘Tempest’.

No, tornadoes over 10 km in diameter, that’s basically something like a typhoon (lack of vocabulary).

Naturally, the surrounding winds are even stronger.

Of the dragon knight maids waiting below, those riding dragonkin are barely able to act without being overwhelmed by the wind, but those riding Lesser Wind Dragons are forced to retreat.

The power of Lesser Wind Dragons can’t withstand ‘Tempest’s’ gale.

And that wasn’t all.

Before I knew it, my clothes were soaked.

“It’s not just wind, it’s a rainstorm too?”

Even above the clouds, the wind is mixed with rain.

…No, that’s not rain, it’s seawater.

The tornado surrounding ‘Tempest’ is drawing up seawater from the ocean far below.

That mixes with the wind, turning it into something like a rainstorm.

No good.

Disaster Dragons really are beings that should not exist in this world.

In every way, they interfere with my goals.

“Jin-sama, please be careful.”

“Yeah.”

Seeing me off by Maria, I head toward the ‘Wind Disaster Dragon: Tempest’.

First and foremost, the priority is to suppress damage to the surroundings.

Even if the ‘Wind Disaster Dragon: Tempest’ stays above the clouds, there’s a high chance it will cause damage in various places.

Then we just need to go even higher.

Maintaining ‘Spiritization’, I approach ‘Tempest’.

It’s covered in a tornado, but if I fly in with enough momentum, I can punch right through without any problem.

Inside the tornado, the gale is even more intense than outside, but it’s not so bad that I can’t act alone.

For a Sky Dragon, it would be just barely possible to act, I think.

To move ‘Tempest’, I kicked it upward from directly below, right in the ass.

-Dogon!!!-

That impact raises ‘Tempest’s’ altitude.

-Dogon!!!-

-Dogon!!!-

-Dogon!!!-

-Dogon!!!-

Again and again, I kick ‘Tempest’s’ ass upward.

More and more, ‘Tempest’ rises higher into the sky.

Naturally, ‘Tempest’ resists.

It directs an even more powerful gale at me alone.

“Wap!”

The gale slams into my face, contorting it.

For example, if this gale directly hit the royal capital of Castal, it would have enough power to flip the land itself upside down. Naturally, the capital would be annihilated.

(Why are you using Castal as an example!?)

I feel like I heard the queen shouting something in my head.

It’s the place I’m most familiar with, and the scale is easiest to imagine, okay?

Anyway, we really can’t let this thing get close to the ground.

At least for me alone, it’s within tolerable limits.

I’m really glad I didn’t bring Maria or Blue along.

Ignoring ‘Tempest’s’ resistance, I keep kicking it upward, and eventually we cross the stratosphere and step into the realm called space.

“Without air, even a ‘Wind Disaster Dragon’ can’t avoid being weakened, right?”

When I look, the tornado that had surrounded ‘Tempest’ at some point has vanished.

Looking more closely, ‘Tempest’ seems kind of listless.

“All right, let’s start the fight. Here, even if I go all out, there won’t be any damage to the surroundings.”

Even if it can’t hear my voice, there’s no doubt that ‘Tempest’ recognizes me and is staring straight at me.

It’s strange, but it feels like ‘Tempest’ is backing off. That’s just my imagination, right?

‘Tempest’ roars and charges at me.

The wind?

I dodge ‘Tempest’s’ charge and punch it hard in the side of the face.

‘Tempest’ is sent flying.

I then mercilessly continue my combo.

Uppercut! Jab! Jab! Straight! Knife-hand kick! Piercing palm! Kung fu!

To prevent ‘Tempest’ from doing anything unnecessary, I attack mercilessly, truly mercilessly.

I can feel ‘Tempest’ gradually weakening.

“Time to finish this.”

I clench my fist and pour all my strength into it.

“Dieeeeeeeee!!!”

I close in with all my might, draw back with all my might, and swing with all my might.

That blow sinks into ‘Tempest’s’ abdomen, and strength drains from ‘Tempest’s’ body.

I touch ‘Tempest’s’ soul and confirm its death.

I absorb ‘Tempest’s’ soul with \<Life and Death Authority>, and store its body in \<Infinite Storage>.

Now I should be able to absorb its traits just like the other Disaster Dragons.

The body itself has various uses as well.

“Hm?”

When I look, there’s something where ‘Tempest’s’ head had been.

A: There appears to be something like a crystal. Inside is a human girl. It seems to be a being created by ‘Tempest’, and it appears to retain its consciousness.

I defeated a calamity god, and a little girl came out.

Well, that happens fairly often.

From a distance, I don’t feel any threat at all.

Can that even fight?

A: That seems unlikely. It only possesses combat ability appropriate to its appearance.

I don’t know ‘Tempest’s’ true intentions, but I can’t just leave it alone.

I tuck the not very large crystal under my arm and return to my companions.

Ah, this crystal can go into \<Infinite Storage>.

“Everyone, thank you for waiting. It’s time to announce the battle results!”

“Yay, clap clap clap.”

《Clap clap clap!》

Thanks to Mio and Dora playing along, I managed not to completely fall flat.

Our main party is currently in a hidden area of the Estea Labyrinth (51st floor).

There were various things obtained from defeating the ‘Wind Disaster Dragon: Tempest’, and we needed a highly confidential space to announce and examine them.

Let’s roughly go over what we got.

“First up, skills.”

Maria \<Hero LV9>, Cynthia \<Hero LV7>, Rico \<Hero LV5>.

“Maria, later explain the skills you got from Hero.”

“Yes.”

Blue \<Dragon Magic LV7>, Leaf \<Dragon Magic LV5>, Mikazuki \<Dragon Magic LV6>.

“Dora’s Dragon Magic didn’t go up this time. It would have been LV10 next.”

《That’s too bad…》

Sera \<Proof of Hero LV9>.

“As usual, the effects are pretty understated.”

“There’s still LV10. I believe something will happen then.”

Basically the same lineup as last time (the Fire Disaster Dragon).

Skill levels have shot up dramatically in a short period of time.

“Maria, please explain.”

“Yes. The skill obtained by Hero reaching level 9 is called \<Yasakani no Magatama>. Like the previous ones, it has no skill level.”

“The name was as expected.”

“Yeah.”

Just as Mio and I predicted, it’s one of the Three Sacred Treasures.

“When this skill is activated, MP is continuously consumed. In exchange, the body temporarily approaches being magical… closer to a spirit, and stats increase. In addition, like a spirit, it becomes possible to move through the air.”

“That’s self ‘Spiritization’!”

Simply put, it’s “Spiritization usable without a contracted spirit”.

“If I had obtained it a little earlier, I could have followed Jin-sama…”

Maria says regretfully.

During the fight with ‘Tempest’, even Maria couldn’t keep up.

Normal Spiritization doesn’t grant flight, but \<Yasakani no Magatama> does. That means she could have followed me.

The timing was unfortunate.

“So that I won’t be left behind by Jin-sama, I intend to train intensively.”

“It seems like a very useful skill for Maria-chan…”

“It certainly does. Compared to \<Proof of Hero>, it’s flashy. I’m jealous.”

“Since Mio-chan doesn’t have an innate rare skill to begin with, there was never an opening… sigh…”

For now, that means we have all three of the Three Sacred Treasures skills.

Let’s organize them a bit.

\<Kusanagi Sword LV >

Obtained at \<Hero> skill LV7.

Creates swords made of light (indestructible, effective against demons and monsters). Unlimited number, but they disappear if not held by the user. Can also be activated layered over normal weapons, in which case attack power increases and demon and monster effectiveness is added.

\<Yata Mirror LV >

Obtained at \<Hero> skill LV8.

Negates all status ailments for the owner and all party members, and reduces damage from various elemental attacks. Reduction rate is 50% for the owner, 30% for party members. Additionally, light-attribute attacks are nullified.

\<Yasakani no Magatama LV >

Obtained at \<Hero> skill LV9.

While MP is continuously consumed, the body approaches that of a spirit and stats increase. While in use, HP automatically recovers, but MP cannot be recovered. When MP runs out, the effect ends. Also allows movement through the air like a spirit.

Lined up like this, they’re quite powerful skills.

As expected of a Hero.

That makes me look forward to the skill obtained at LV10.

“Maria, would you mind aiming to level up your Hero skill?”

“Understood. If Jin-sama desires it, I will raise the level by any means necessary.”

“No, choose your means.”

When Maria says that, it sounds like she really wouldn’t choose her means, which is scary.

I’d like her to raise it through proper methods.

“That’s about it for skills.”

“Are we good on Special Powers?”

Mio, was that a pun? That is… allowed.

“Yeah, Special Powers are later.”

“Because they’re dangerous again?”

“No. Because it’s a bit of a hassle.”

This time, they’re not that dangerous.

“So next are the acquired items. First, the soul of the ‘Wind Disaster Dragon: Tempest’.”

“Is that considered an item?”

I ignore Sera’s question.

“With this, I can manipulate wind like ‘Tempest’. I can flip skirts as much as I want.”

“You can do the same with magic, can’t you?”

“Unlike magic, there’s no MP consumption. It can be adjusted more delicately than magic. There are plenty of advantages.”

If I wanted to, I could not only flip skirts, but even use wind to pull down panties.

Freely manipulable wind. That is practically tentacles (absurd argument).

“Master, if you want to see panties, you can just ask, you know?”

《Do you want to see panties?》

Dora lifts her skirt without hesitation. White and light blue stripes.

No. I don’t want to see panties, I want to flip skirts.

It’s not enough to just see panties. It’s the result of flipping the skirt and then seeing panties that makes me happy. What am I even passionately talking about…?

“Dora, that’s improper, stop it.”

《Okay.》

“Huh? You’re the one saying that, Master!?”

Mio is fidgeting, holding her crotch.

“Then Mio, will you show me your panties?”

“Not right now! Give me a break!”

Even Mio has her limits, it seems.

“It’s a convenient ability, but since I can’t think of a use for it right away, let’s move on.”

When I said manipulating wind, the only thing that came to mind was perverted stuff.

“Next is likewise the body of the ‘Wind Disaster Dragon: Tempest’… you could call it a corpse.”

“Calling a corpse an item feels a bit wrong…”

Sakura gives a wry smile.

“Materials from monsters are basically corpses, so what’s the difference now?”

“When you put it that way, you’re right…”

Meat and horns are also parts of a corpse.

If we call materials items, then calling a corpse an item is the same thing.

“I defeated ‘Tempest’ without damaging it, so it’s almost exactly as it was in life. Of course, I can’t take it out here…”

“It was about 10 km long, right…? It fits in \<Infinite Storage>…”

“The name Infinite isn’t just for show.”

I can’t take it out here, but if I wanted to, it would be instant.

“Since Master is calling it an item, does that corpse have some kind of effect too?”

“Actually, this corpse floats in midair, just like when it was sealed.”

“Does that mean…?”

“Yeah, we can build our own Sky Castle!”

“All right!”

Mio pumps her fist with all her might.

“And on top of that, we’ve also recovered rare plants that the elves were cultivating, which are extinct on the ground. If they can’t be grown on the ground, we’ll have them grown in the Sky Castle.”

In the collapsing Sky Castle, I had the dragon knight maids prioritize recovering rare plants.

I don’t intend to steal fields, but there’s nothing to complain about if we recover them from a place that’s falling apart.

“That’s why we recovered the elves too.”

“So the elf rescue was for that… Master, aren’t you a bit too ruthless?”

This time, I had the dragon knight maids rescue the falling elves.

At that time, I gave the elves a choice: fall and die, or become my slaves and live. Given our less-than-friendly relationship including the matter with Claude and the others, I showed no mercy.

Those who died while falling, those who looked down on humans even when on the brink of death, those with arrogant attitudes, I ignored anyone not worth saving and only saved those who obediently complied.

In the end, about 30%, several hundred individuals, were saved.

“If it’s elf fields, then as master of elf slaves, there’s no problem with them becoming mine, right?”

“Yes, there is no problem. A slave’s belongings are their master’s belongings.”

I got Maria’s seal of approval.

I saved the elves from the collapse of the Sky Castle in order to seize ownership of their fields. That’s why I thought it was fine not to save them all.

“By the same logic, the magical tools in the Sky Castle are also mine.”

“Huh? Weren’t those made by Yuriela, the ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’?”

“Yeah, but I’ve also revived Yuriela and made her a slave, so there’s no problem.”

We recovered Yuriela’s falling corpse and revived her using ‘Resurrection’ (by a maid).

To be honest, there was no benefit to reviving Yuriela, but at Alta’s request, I decided to revive her. More precisely, I permitted the revival.

The reason Alta said that was because she wanted to confirm something.

That was what happens when you revive a dead ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’.

The conclusion was that the title of ‘Human Pillar’ and the unique skill of ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’ had disappeared.

Such a shame about the unique skill… well, there was a form of salvation there too.

“The skills remained, which was good, but apparently the revived Yuriela had lost most of her memories. Not much time should have passed, but the memory loss happened faster than expected.”

If time passes between death and revival, memory loss occurs.

This time, due to the collapse of the Sky Castle, it took some time to recover Yuriela’s body.

Normally, it wouldn’t be enough time for such severe memory loss. However, Yuriela lost most of her memories in that short time.

Whether this is specific to Yuriela, to High Elves, or to ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’ is unknown.

“Elves have a high rate of memory loss, huh. So what’s her condition?”

“She can do simple things if ordered, but otherwise she does nothing.”

Memory can be said to be everything that makes a person who they are.

Losing most of it, it’s no wonder a proper ego doesn’t remain.

“She doesn’t say anything on her own, so she needs help even with basic care, and is currently in diapers.”

“Why did you look at Mio-chan when you said that!?”

Because Mio is a pioneer on that path?

I haven’t forgotten that she wore diapers in the labyrinth.

So anyway, Yuriela is currently in a state like an elderly person requiring care.

“Right now, I’m thinking about how to make use of her.”

“As usual, you show not a shred of mercy.”

“This is the fate of those who weren’t included in Master’s definition of ‘decent’.”

It’s not normal, but there’s no changing the fact that I made Yuriela a slave.

Which means Yuriela’s magical tools also become mine.

What’s yours is mine.

“So in effect, everything related to the Sky Castle has become mine.”

“Please, please, let Mio-chan be involved in building the Sky Castle!”

Mio prostrates herself enthusiastically.

“Mio should be able to make something close to the Sky Castle I envision. Can I leave it to you?”

“Of course! Leave it to me!”

Since I have no design sense anyway, leaving it to someone else was inevitable.

It wouldn’t do any good for me to get involved, but I do have an ideal form for a Sky Castle.

Then it’s only natural to involve someone who knows that ideal form just as well.

By the way, let me declare here that there is no clear objective to building a Sky Castle.

I’m just building it because I want to.

Anyway, back on topic.

“The last spoils… or rather, the drop item, is this.”

Saying that, I take the crystal out of \<Infinite Storage>.

Inside the crystal, a little girl about four or five years old (naturally naked) is sleeping.

Her jade-green hair with a luster like a Disaster Dragon’s scales reaches her shoulders. She looks about four or five, but is it my imagination that her chest is slightly developed?

“This child has the consciousness of the ‘Wind Disaster Dragon: Tempest’…?”

“It’s hard to believe.”

《This kid isn’t a dragon.》

“Yeah, she might become a Disaster Dragon we can communicate with.”

Until now, I never considered the possibility of communicating with Disaster Dragons.

If this little girl understands human language, that would mean Disaster Dragons have ego and will.

“But why a little girl? Master’s tastes?”

That’s something I wonder about too.

And it’s not my taste.

---

**AN:** It’s the author’s taste.

## **169.5 – Lost Legend, Episode 3: Wind Disaster Dragon**

**AN:** I wrote down the future schedule, and then suddenly did a surprise update (work on the main story already).

It is a fairly short piece, but this is the first Lost Legend in a long time (over 100 episodes).

---

I was having a long dream.

There was no one there, and a barren land stretched out endlessly.

I was just flying around the sky there without end.

With no purpose, just flying around.

Why am I alive, I wonder? No one answered me.

Just how much time had passed?

With no day or night, and nothing to compare against, the endless days simply continued in that dream.

…or so I thought.

Celebration! This time, I have woken up from the dream!

Well, to be honest, I am still sleepy.

Also, somehow the futon is heavy.

Since the futon is way too heavy, I sway my body back and forth, shaking it to push the annoying futon away.

Ah, it got a little lighter.

Sway, sway, sway, sway, sway, sway.

Yeah, it is getting quite a bit lighter.

While pushing the futon away, my sleepiness started to fade.

It cannot be helped, I guess it is about time to get up.

And then, I opened my eyes.

“Faaa…”

At the same time, a yawn slipped out from the lingering sleepiness.

On top of that, it seems the remaining futon is gone too, so I feel refreshed.

Huh? Is someone nearby?

Wait a second! I just woke up! Do not look at my just-woke-up face!

I hastily wrapped myself in a tornado so my face would not be seen.

Phew, that surprised me.

That is bad for my heart…

Since I am thirsty after waking up, I will drink a cup of water and wash my face too.

I use a tornado to scoop up seawater, gulping it down while also washing my face.

Ahh, I am revived.

-Dogon!!!-

Ouch! That hurts!

I leap up with tears in my eyes from the sudden pain attacking my butt.

Did you kick me!? Someone kicked my butt!? Huh? A human!?

-Dogon!!!-

-Dogon!!!-

-Dogon!!!-

-Dogon!!!-

Ouch!? Hey!? Wait!? Stop it!? It hurts!?

I keep taking unceasing impacts to my butt, writhing in agony.

I finally get fed up, so I pour my heart and soul into a full-power attack against the human who is kicking my butt.

Huh? The wind is not working at all…

-Dogon!!!-

-Dogon!!!-

-Dogon!!!-

Realizing my counterattack is meaningless, I resign myself and accept the kicks in a state of surrender.

Fine, do whatever you want.

And then, at last, we arrive near the region called space.

Finally, finally it is over… ugh, my butt hurts so bad…

The human who kept kicking my butt is saying something.

“Now then, shall we begin the fight? Up here, even if I go all out, there will be no damage to the surroundings.”

Seriously!?

After tormenting me so thoroughly up to now, you say that only now!?

I was already going all out in that pointless counterattack earlier, you know?

I am confident in my power, but I do not have a lot of attack variety, you know?

At this altitude, I can barely produce any wind at all, so my means of attack are reduced even further, you know?

If wind does not work, then I am left with only primitive attack methods like ramming.

I do not really want to say it, but I am quite heavy. My weight is a secret.

If my tackle actually lands, a human would not stand a chance.

I will do it, dammit!!!

-Bago!!!-

It hurts!!!

Ugh, I got punched right in the face with full force.

After that, I got beaten up terribly.

I-I am going to die…

“About time I finish you off”,

Saying that, the human clenched his fist.

Th-that is bad. Somehow, the killing intent is incredible. I will probably die if I take that.

My body is weakened, and I do not feel like I can dodge it.

Ah, this is it, I am dead.

No, wait, do not give up, me.

Beg for your life. Somehow, beg for your life.

“Dieeeeeeeeeee!!!”

There is no time to begggggg!!!

I-if it comes to this, the last resort!

I have no choice but to separate my consciousness from my body.

I will be discarding this body, but it is better than dying completely.

Since I am about to be punched in the stomach, I create a crystal near my head and put my body into it.

If I stay as a dragon, I might get killed, so a human form is better.

To raise my survival rate even a little, I should make it the form of a little girl.

If I am seen as a threat, it would be dangerous, so I need to make myself as weak-looking as possible.

I have to flatter with everything I have!

All right, I made it in time! Just barely safe! I can do it if I try!

Now, at the same time I die, my consciousness will transfer to the little girl.

The human clenches his fist and approaches.

Ah, please do not make it hurt too much, okay?

Guhf!

---

**AN:** Please try comparing these actions with those of the previous episode.

There are probably many points you are wondering about, but they will be explained to some extent next time, so please wait until then.

Also, there are no Lost Legends for the other Disaster Dragons.
