## **170: Interrogation and a Fragment of Truth**

**AN:** This marks the end of Volume 11. The number of chapters per volume has been gradually decreasing.

The peak was Volume 3, the Labyrinth arc. That one was exhausting. And I was writing at my absolute best then.

---

According to Alta, the young girl inside the crystal is in a state of suspended animation.

And if the crystal is broken, she will awaken almost simultaneously.

The crystal itself is not particularly sturdy. It is something that would break if struck with a hammer.

Incidentally, if I swing a hammer seriously, most things will break. The contents would die.

Also, while the Calamity Dragon had no status, the young girl did.

It looked like this.

Name: –

LV 1

Gender: Female

Age: 65535

Race: Human (Manifestation)

Skill: \<Mind of the Gale LV >

Title: Manifestation of the Calamity Dragon

She has no name, and the title she had as a Calamity Dragon is gone.

Her level looks like an initial value, and her stats are low, appropriate for that level.

Also, that age… it looks like a value I have seen somewhere before. What was it again?

She possessed \<Mind of the Gale>, the unique skill that Yuliera lost.

Did it transfer to the ‘Wind Calamity Dragon: Tempest’ when Yuliera died? And then transfer again to this one?

“I do not think there is any danger, so I want to wake her up and ask her some questions. …No, that is wrong. I will wake her up and question her. By force, if necessary.”

Even if she looks like a young girl, I will show no mercy.

Due to certain conditions it cannot be used anyway, but just in case, I disable the teleportation skill \<Mind of the Gale>.

“Oh! Master, you are unusually aggressive today!”

“It is rare to see Jin-kun take such a hard-line stance… Is there some reason for it…?”

“Of course there is. …I am getting tired of information being deliberately withheld.”

Until now, there has been a persistent situation where certain information could not be obtained.

Specifically, information about the Goddess. This was information that even Alta could not acquire, and neither the long-lived Final Trials nor the gatekeepers of the Goddess-created ‘Gray World’ knew anything about it.

There is even suspicion that the information is being deliberately concealed.

It is not that I absolutely need to know about the Goddess.

If information had been revealed little by little, I probably would not have cared that much. But when it is concealed this thoroughly, it makes me want to know instead.

And this is probably one of the few chances.

Most likely, the Calamity Dragons are connected to the Goddess.

If communication with a Calamity Dragon is possible, we might be able to gather information about the Goddess.

Unlike the Final Trials, whose role is essentially to be defeated, Calamity Dragons are not meant to be defeated, and there is a chance that information has not been suppressed.

“Now that you mention it, it really is unnatural how we cannot obtain any information about the Goddess…”

“It is more natural to assume it is intentional.”

When I finished explaining, Sakura nodded in understanding.

“They hid it so carefully that they ended up piquing Master’s interest. My condolences.”

“You make it sound like drawing Master’s interest is some kind of misfortune.”

“Huh? If you get involved with Master, there is no way things will end peacefully, right?”

“I cannot deny that…”

I really wanted you to try harder to deny it.

Though the fact that it requires effort to deny says it all…

“This is a rare opportunity. I will have this girl tell us everything. If she refuses, I will not hesitate to use coercive measures.”

First, do XX to OO, then do △△ to □□.

After that, if you ◇◇ ☆☆, it should become ▽▽.

“Alright then, shall we break the crystal?”

“Lord Jin, please leave that task to me.”

“Very well. Maria, do not damage the contents.”

“Yes, understood. Hah.”

Maria drew her sword and, in an instant, sliced the crystal into fragments.

With its support gone, the young girl collapsed.

-GON!-

The young girl fell and hit the back of the head.

The young girl’s eyes flew open.

“NUOOO!!! UGOAAAAA!!!”

《That looks painful…》

The young girl rolled around, writhing in agony. It must have hurt badly.

Since I do not yet know her stance, I do not bother doing something like casting Heal, and simply observe.

“Ugh, it hurts… That is definitely going to be a bump…”

After a while, the young girl stopped rolling and rubbed her head with tear-filled eyes.

“…Ah.”

Then, the same jade-green eyes as the Calamity Dragon locked onto me.

Immediately, the young girl clasped her hands in front of her chest and forced a full smile.

Her cheeks were twitching slightly.

“Please do not kill me! I will do anything!”

A manifestation of a being called the God of Calamity.

The first thing she did upon waking was “roll around”, and the second was “beg for her life by ingratiating herself.”

She is already a complete gag character.

Well then, let us begin interrogation time.

“You are the ‘Wind Calamity Dragon: Tempest’ that was fighting me, correct?”

“Huh? Ah, yeah. If you mean the one that fought you and could not do anything, then yes, that is me.”

At the very least, she seems to retain her memories up until death.

“From now on, I will ask you several questions. If you answer honestly, I will give you a chance to survive. If you lie or show hostility, I cannot guarantee that.”

“O-Okay! Ask me anything!”

As an aside, the reason I am bothering to threaten her is because \<Slave Art> and \<Monster Taming> did not work on this girl.

I tried them for the sake of ‘smooth communication’, but they did not work.

“Then my first question. What is that form? Why did you transfer your consciousness and take that shape?”

“Huh? That is because I did not want to die. I thought you were going to kill me, so I created this body to let at least my consciousness escape. To show I was not resisting, I left almost no power behind. I die easily, so please do not hit me.”

This time she is begging with a full prostration.

So it was like an escape pod.

She made herself weak so as not to be perceived as a threat. And the immediate begging for her life was also to increase her survival chances. …She is thorough.

“Next question. Do you have memories from when you were a Calamity Dragon? Are there any missing parts?”

“I have all of my memories as a Calamity Dragon. But when I was rampaging in subspace, there was so little change that I might not remember the finer details.”

“That is good. If you had told me you had no memories, your value would have dropped sharply. There was even a chance I would not have guaranteed your life.”

“Eek!”

Good. She is terrified.

“What I want to ask about is the Goddess. Do you have any knowledge about her? …And why do you have such a clear consciousness? Do the other Calamity Dragons have it too?”

“I-I will answer in order. I do have knowledge about the Goddess. When I was born, various knowledge flowed into me, and I also remember her speaking to us.”

Good. It looks like she has the most important information.

“My consciousness became clear about a year ago. Before that, I do not think I had anything that could be called a sense of self. So I do not know about the other Calamity Dragons.”

“A year ago…”

“Lord Jin, is that not around the same time Lady Yuria went missing?”

As Maria said, it overlaps with the time Yuria went missing and lost her memory.

I have not heard of anything else related to Calamity Dragons happening around that time.

“…Could the rampage of the sealing crystal have affected something?”

At the time, Yuria was not a sacrifice for the ‘Wind Calamity Dragon: Tempest’, so there should not have been a direct connection.

However, it is possible that the sealing crystal created by Gired was influencing Tempest in some way.

And during the rampage of the sealing crystal, it may have caused a change in Tempest.

“Or did Yuria’s memories or consciousness flow into ‘Tempest’? …Do you have any memories other than those of a Calamity Dragon?”

“Um, yes, I do. Memories other than the Calamity Dragon… a little bit of memories of a High Elf girl. These are not complete, just fragments…”

“So that is it. …If they have already flowed elsewhere, recovering Yuria’s memories will be difficult.”

If Yuria merely forgot, that would be one thing. But if her memories flowed elsewhere, and not even all of them, then recovery or restoration seems difficult.

If the possibility is not zero, I want to try, though.

A: We will try.

Alta will do her best.

“For now, considering a way to extract consciousness and memories from this one might be an option.”

“Eek! Eeeek!?”

Not understanding the details but sensing danger, the young girl trembles.

“Master, you are being rather harsh on that child.”

“She is not a subordinate, and if anything, she is an enemy, is she not? Even if they were originally enemies, once they become subordinates, you are relatively kind to them afterward…”

“! I-I will become a subordinate! I will do anything you say! I swear loyalty, so please do not kill me!”

Seeing hope in Mio and Sera’s conversation, the young girl begs again with a full prostration.

While I cannot make her a slave or tamed monster, I can make her a subordinate through \<Bond of Contract>.

Sakura is also not my slave, but a subordinate through \<Bond of Contract>.

That said, is this young girl eligible for \<Bond of Contract>?

A: There is no problem. She can become a subordinate as a valid target.

“Will you really do anything?”

“I-I will! I will do anything except an order to die!”

It does not seem like a lie.

For the sake of ‘smooth communication’, making her a subordinate is fine.

“If you are willing to go that far, I will make you my subordinate. Hold out your finger.”

“Y-You are going to cut it off!?”

Trembling, the young girl holds out her finger.

“No, that is not it.”

Why does ‘hold out your finger’ immediately lead to the idea of cutting it off?

And stop accepting it as better than death.

We safely did the pinky promise and made the young girl a subordinate.

In a sense, a finger was cut, though…

“Now then, it is fine for a stranger to be nameless, but once you are a subordinate, you need a name. Do you have one?”

“Um, I think I did not have one besides ‘Tempest’.”

If she is no longer treated as the original Calamity Dragon, using Tempest as-is is out.

“Then, I will take it from ‘Tempest’ and call you ‘Pes’. From today on, you are Pes!”

“That is a dog’s name!”

Mio’s lightning-fast retort!

“Or ‘Pest’.”

“That is the name of a pathogen!”

“Alternatively, ‘Test’, ‘Tent’.”

“Those are not even names! And why is a dog’s name the best option!?”

And so, the best option, ‘Pes’, was chosen.

Pes herself did not seem dissatisfied with the name, so I asked why.

“Huh? If you give me a name, that proves you do not intend to kill me, right? So I am happy.”

She was more pleased about her increased chances of survival than being given a strange name.

Thorough, as expected.

By the way, because a storm is a violent wind, ‘Ran’ was also a candidate, but it was not interesting, so I did not mention it.

Now that she is a subordinate, we cannot just leave her naked forever.

“Now then, tell me about the Goddess. Or should I ask about your birth first?”

“Yeah, I think that will be easier to understand.”

Pes, wearing nothing but children’s underwear (blue stripes, sold at Advance Trading Company for a list price of 500G), agrees.

“You are not going to dress her, are you…”

“Master sometimes makes unbelievable choices, does he not?”

I gracefully ignore Sakura and Mio.

Pes herself does not care at all…

“I was born a very long time ago. I do not remember exactly how many years ago.”

“That cannot be helped.”

She said she had no sense of self at the time, so I did not expect her to remember.

And what matters is the reason for her birth, not the exact date.

“I was in subspace from the moment I was born. At the same time I was born, many kinds of knowledge flowed into me. Among them was the reason for my birth.”

“Tell me.”

“First, what is attached to our names are disasters that do not occur in this world.”

“Do not occur? Earthquakes, eruptions, violent storms do not happen in this world?”

Indeed, I have never heard of such disasters occurring.

“Wait, are you perhaps from another world?”

Now that she mentions it, I had not talked about that.

“Yeah. I am. Not a Hero, though.”

“I see. Then this will be quick. When the Goddess created this world, she made it so that disasters that threaten people would not occur. But disasters are things that are meant to occur. By twisting that, a backlash happened. …That is the birth of us Calamity Dragons.”

This goes all the way back to the creation myth of the world.

The backlash from sealing disasters. That must be the reason for the Calamity Dragons’ title, ‘Anti-Existence’.

“In exchange for sealing disasters, Calamity Dragons like us, embodiments of disasters, were born. Subspace and the ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’ are stoppers created by the Goddess, who understood our danger. Elves and High Elves were also born because long-lived races were needed to prevent extinction by lifespan.”

The truth of the elves is revealed here.

It is not that there are High Elves, ‘Princess Shrine Maidens’, among elves, but that elves were born to sustain the ‘Princess Shrine Maidens’.

“From what I hear, the Goddess does not seem that omnipotent.”

“I think so too. It seems the Goddess cannot ignore rules either. And when I was born and thrown into subspace, I heard her voice.”

This is the closest we have ever gotten to information about the Goddess.

“‘We bear you no grudge, but for the sake of this world, please remain sealed forever.’ …Thinking back, her tone sounded a little apologetic.”

“That is more serious than I expected…”

From my past experiences, I thought the possibility of the Goddess being serious was extremely low.

I will not judge from just one sentence, but at least the possibility is no longer zero.

Though forcing sacrifices on the ‘Princess Shrine Maidens’ still disqualifies her from being completely serious…

“Do you have any other information about the Goddess? Even secrets of the world are fine.”

I feel like I have at least heard the minimum I wanted.

Compared to the near-zero information before, this is excellent.

“This is not about the Goddess, but earlier you mentioned earthquakes, eruptions, and violent storms, right? There is one more Calamity Dragon. A tsunami, the ‘Water Calamity Dragon: Tidal Wave’.”

“I thought so…”

I had a feeling.

Earth, fire, wind. There is no way water would be missing. And when it comes to water disasters, tsunamis are the obvious one.

“There is no direct connection between us, but I can vaguely tell that it is alive. …Huh? The other two are dead… D-Do not tell me…”

Pes looks at me fearfully.

“Oh, those? I killed them.”

“Eek!? I knew it!”

That is strange.

Pes has been frightened so many times, yet she has not once wet herself.

A: There is no moisture in her body, so there is nothing to expel.

“Pes, are you not thirsty?”

“I-I’m fine. I look human, but I am not human, so eating and drinking are not necessary. I can eat and drink, but that just means I will need to excrete, so there is not much benefit.”

I see. She looks human, but she is not a normal human.

She probably will not grow either.

“For now, drink a cup of water.”

“? Okay.”

Pes gulps down the cup of water I took out.

Now, if I threaten her next time, she should wet herself.

“I sense Master’s evil plotting.”

“Mio-chan, I think it would be better not to say unnecessary things…”

If Mio wants to wet herself, I can make her do so anytime.

“I am zipping my mouth shut.”

Mio makes an X in front of her mouth with her fingers.

It seems she does not want to wet herself right now.

“So then, Pes. Is there any other noteworthy information?”

“Hmm… Sorry, nothing comes to mind right away. If I remember something else, I will tell you later. Can you forgive me for now?”

“Very well. There was quite a lot of useful information.”

“Phew…”

Pes exhales in relief from the bottom of her heart.

She was apparently quite frightened inside.

“Pes, do you have knowledge about the current state of this world?”

“No. The Calamity Dragon information is too old to be useful, and the High Elf knowledge is limited to the Sky Castle and fragmentary, so it is not helpful.”

Yuria was apparently a sheltered young lady to begin with.

She would not have much knowledge of the outside world.

“Then we will start with education as usual. Honestly, what should I have Pes do?”

“As I said before, I will do anything.”

Even if her motivation is fear of me, she seems highly motivated.

That is fine, but the problem is what to have Pes do.

A maid, as usual? But unlike a normal child, she likely will not physically grow, making handling difficult.

“Leave it to me.”

“Yes, please do.”

“Huh? Who is this person? When did they get here? Hey, wait, do not pull my hand!?”

《Bye-bye》

For now, I decided to call a maid and leave education to her.

If she is surprised by a maid appearing out of nowhere, the road ahead is long.

With that, there is only one remaining result from the battle with the ‘Wind Calamity Dragon: Tempest’.

“Now then, what you have all been waiting for. The introduction of the effects of the new Special Power!”

“So, did \<Life and Death Authority> go up?”

“Gh…!”

Mio’s merciless question strikes me.

Yes, \<Life and Death Authority> did not level up again.

It reached LV 9 and is still being stingy.

With this level-up, \<Multiple Existence> reached LV 9, meaning it finally caught up. Try harder!

\<Multiple Existence LV 9>

Can extract souls from corpses. Souls can be stored in \<Infinite Storage>.

“Are you some kind of demon? You said it was not dangerous, that was a lie.”

Mio’s first comment upon seeing the effect.

“Do not say rude things. …Well, I had a similar impression when I first saw it.”

“Extract the soul of someone you killed and store it.” In a story, it would be an ability used by a demon.

Let us call this ability ‘Soul Collector’. It sounds unnecessarily cool.

“However, this effect itself is not that meaningful. At best, you can extract information from the collected souls.”

“That is still amazing…”

“I could do similar things before, though. This has its own advantages, but…”

With \<Life and Death Authority LV 8>, absorbing a corpse along with its soul allowed me to use the target’s exclusive skills and read information.

However, this ability has several drawbacks.

For example, “I do not want to absorb someone I truly hate”, and “once absorbed, the body disappears.”

With ‘Soul Collector’, I can manipulate the soul while leaving the corpse intact, eliminating the drawbacks of \<Life and Death Authority LV 8>.

“Is it just my imagination? The high-level abilities of Master’s \<Life and Death Authority> and \<Multiple Existence> seem to focus on souls and information.”

“Probably because the essence of those two abilities lies in souls and information.”

As Sera said, many of the high-level abilities of \<Life and Death Authority> and \<Multiple Existence> are related to souls and information.

Until now, many abilities seemed to appear as needed at the time of leveling up.

However, at higher levels, that tendency fades, and it starts to look like abilities that were predetermined are manifesting.

Perhaps the essence of these two abilities lies in souls and information, and they are gradually approaching that essence.

I have started thinking that way.

“Then the ability that manifests at LV 10 is probably the true form of the ability.”

“Honestly, the effect of \<Multiple Existence LV 9> feels a bit half-baked.”

I was thinking the same thing as Mio.

“Yeah. Even though it has advantages, having another similar effect appear is unnatural. My guess is that this is preparation for the manifestation of the essence of \<Multiple Existence>.”

The ability to read information is like a bonus. The truly important part is probably the effect of separating corpses and souls, or the effect of storing souls.

“So that means what comes at level 10 will be really dangerous.”

“Probably. Unlike \<Expanded Interpretation>, which just increases numbers, \<Life and Death Authority> and \<Multiple Existence> have had a lot going on, so I think the final level 10 will be quite flashy.”

《Flashy!》

Honestly, I am really looking forward to it.

To be honest, I even wonder if \<Life and Death Authority> not leveling up was because it was waiting for \<Multiple Existence> to catch up?

Maybe it wants to show the greatest ‘essence’ together?

I cannot help but feel that way.

Now we have truly introduced all of the results.

“Ah, battles with Calamity Dragons really are rewarding.”

There is so much to gain that it requires serious discussion.

This makes me want to defeat the ‘Water Calamity Dragon: Tidal Wave’ as well.

“It was a huge crisis for the world, though.”

《Ah, that is Sakuya》

The one who picked up my muttering was Sakuya, who had teleported in at some point.

She looks exhausted.

“Sakuya-chan… Are you tired…?”

Sakuya nodded at Sakura’s question.

“…Yeah. That Calamity Dragon my big brother defeated? The gusts it created reached Castal… I was completely worn out dealing with the aftermath.”

“‘Tempest’s’ wind reached Castal…”

The land where the ‘Sky Castle’ was is quite far from the Kingdom of Castal.

I understood ‘Tempest’s’ winds were powerful, but I did not think it was to that extent.

“Fortunately, Castal did not suffer major damage, but I hear some other countries took quite a hit. Officially, it is information I should not know, though.”

Information obtained not as a queen, but through my subordinate network.

Alta, were there any countries I am involved with that suffered damage from ‘Tempest’s’ revival?

A: The Elgant Theocracy suffered the greatest damage. It was because they were in the middle of reconstruction.

Oh. That place does not matter.

Even though I have connections, I have no obligation or interest..

A: Other countries you are involved with did not suffer major damage. Some countries you are not involved with did suffer damage.

Why does being involved with me reduce damage?

A: Subordinate mages worked to counteract the wind. However, they did not completely negate it to avoid making it unnatural.

So they were doing things behind the scenes.

“In Castal, human casualties were almost zero. The biggest damage was elderly people getting knocked over by the wind and suffering minor injuries. Crops did take a very small amount of damage. It was only about one minute, but it seems the impact spread everywhere.”

“I am glad Castal is safe.”

From ‘Tempest’s’ complete awakening to me kicking it up and nullifying its influence was about one minute.

In just one minute, it scattered violent winds that affected the entire world.

Perhaps Tempest had the widest area of influence among the Calamity Dragons.

Conversely, one could say that for short-term manifestation, it causes the least damage. Earthquakes and eruptions cause tremendous damage in an instant.

Even though I decided not to attack until complete awakening, hearing that damage actually occurred makes me think a little.

However, it is too late now, but if I had attacked before awakening, the damage would have been even greater.

According to Alta, if you attack a half-awakened Calamity Dragon and fail to kill it in one blow, a wide-area indiscriminate counterattack automatically activates.

Even I could not defeat ‘Tempest’ in one blow.

If an indiscriminate attack had activated, the damage would have been far greater, and my actions would have increased casualties (though casualties would have increased regardless if I did not defeat it).

In that sense, I did my best in dealing with ‘Tempest’, and the result should be close to the best possible.

I will not let anyone complain.

“Yeah, thanks. …Even though no one knows it, this world was saved by you, big brother.”

Ah, I suppose that is true.

Once awakened, a single Calamity Dragon could destroy the world.

Defeating one could be considered saving the world.

…It does not feel real at all.

---

Settings

– About disasters

In this world, natural disasters such as earthquakes, tsunamis, typhoons, and eruptions are prevented from occurring.

Strictly speaking, they do occur, but their effects do not spread.

As a law of this world, only for disasters, the attenuation rate against change is set extremely high, which is the reason.

Earthquakes and tsunamis propagate as waves (changes in amplitude). In most cases, these changes attenuate with distance, like how seismic intensity decreases the further you are from the epicenter.

In this world, this distance attenuation is set extremely high, so earthquakes barely shake outside the epicenter, and even a 10-meter-class tsunami becomes something no longer treated as a wave within one kilometer.

This attenuation rate also applies to pressure changes and heat conduction, resulting in disasters not causing large-scale damage.

Note that this law is adjusted specifically for disasters and does not directly affect phenomena caused by magic.

Also, this law does not apply to disasters caused by Calamity Dragons.

If a Calamity Dragon revives, it is recommended to promptly escape beyond the affected area.

Since it would not be appropriate to impose the author’s tastes onto Jin, it was revised to children’s underwear. Now it is safe.

That aside, it will soon be April 1st. What should I do next year…?

## **170.1 Side Story: Shindo Rin**

**AN:** This is a what-if story: “What if Jin had a younger sister?”

It is a story about the little sister who appeared previously in an unrevealed-character introduction.

The gimmick is explained in the afterword.

Revised on 2019/04/10:

The subtitle was changed from “False Tale” to “Side Story.”

---

This happened while we were lazing around in the mansion.

“Come to think of it, I’ve heard about Master and the others’ school life, but I realize I hardly know anything about Master’s own past, don’t I?”

The trigger was Mio’s casual remark.

“Now that you mention it, that’s true. We hear quite a lot about Sakura-sama… though not many of them are good stories, but we hear them often. On the other hand, we hear very little about Master.”

“I’m very interested.”

“So am I…”

《Dora too!》

At Mio’s words, all four members of the main party present showed interest.

Indeed, ever since I came to this world, I had hardly talked about my own background.

“Master, is there some reason you don’t want to talk about it?”

“No. It’s not like there’s anything I can’t talk about, but it’s not something I’d bring up myself, right? It’s not like I have any interesting stories…”

“No, if it’s about Master’s past, it’s guaranteed to be interesting. I can say that with confidence, even just from the fragments I’ve heard so far.”

Mio looked utterly convinced.

“You really want to hear that badly?”

When I asked, everyone nodded.

It’s not something I’d volunteer to talk about, but if they want to hear it, I don’t really mind.

“Alright. Then I’ll take questions from everyone. I’ll answer them.”

Being told, “Explain yourself in a free talk”, is way too high-difficulty.

Answering questions is probably the easiest way.

“Then the first question is from Mio-chan. Please tell us about your family structure, Master.”

Since it was the first question, a harmless, ordinary one came flying in.

Which also meant that I hadn’t even talked about something this basic until now.

“I live with my younger sister. It’s just the two of us. Our parents passed away quite a long time ago.”

“Eh? Master, you had a little sister? You’ve never mentioned her even once…”

“That’s exactly not something I’d bring up on my own, right? Oh, and to clarify, she’s my step-sister.”

“A light novel protagonist!”

Mio fired off a full-power tsukkomi.

“Were you able to manage living together as just siblings…?”

Sakura asked, looking puzzled.

“Yeah. Our parents left us a pretty sizable inheritance, so we never had trouble living.”

“A light novel protagonist!!”

Mio’s full-power tsukkomi (second time).

“Given Master’s cooking skills, I imagine your sister did most of the cooking, didn’t she?”

Don’t call someone’s cooking ‘that.’

For the record, the most complex dish I can make is a whole roast of meat.

“Yeah, my sister cooked most of the time. When she didn’t, our next-door childhood friend would bring food over.”

“A light novel protagonist!!!”

Mio’s full-power tsukkomi (third time).

“Even though your sister is still back there, is it really fine for you not to prioritize returning to your original world…?”

“Now that you mention it, she’s your only family, yet you don’t seem worried at all?”

Sakura and Mio asked.

Incidentally, Maria was busy taking notes of my story and didn’t join the conversation.

“Well, there’s nothing to worry about. My sister’s very capable at taking care of herself, cooking included. I don’t think she’ll have much trouble even without me. And recently, she finally started to grow out of her brother complex. In a way, you could say this is good timing.”

《”””B-Brother complex?”””》

Everyone except Maria spoke in unison.

“Yeah. She’s been attached to me since she was little… extremely attached.”

“So ‘attached’ that you have to emphasize it…”

“Yeah, extremely. I only started trying to make her grow out of it about a year before my transfer, but before that, she’d even come into the bath with me.”

To be precise, it’s not ‘we went in together’, but rather, ‘when I went in, she came in afterward.’

“…How old is your sister?”

“She’s three years younger than me, so she was in her second year of middle school at the time of the transfer. Which means she kept coming into the bath with me until her first year of middle school.”

“That definitely qualifies as ‘extremely attached’.”

“I share some blame for not realizing how abnormal it was until my friend pointed it out…”

If Asai, who has a sister the same age, hadn’t said something, I might never have tried to make her grow out of it.

“I figured it was a problem, so I spent a year trying to get her to grow out of it. Over the last few months, I finally thought things were fine. And then I ended up getting transferred. In a way, the timing was perfect, right? Also, the reason she never came up in conversation before is probably just the leftover effect of me consciously keeping my distance.”

I had deliberately kept my distance to encourage her independence.

Since I transferred in that state, I probably unconsciously avoided bringing her up.

“Well, like I’ve said before, I haven’t given up on returning to my original world. Luckily, time seems to pass faster in this world, so there’s no need to rush too much. Even if I end up living in this world permanently, I’ll absolutely return to my original world at least once.”

I’m not actively pursuing a way back, but I haven’t abandoned the idea.

Right now, sightseeing this world is my main focus, but I have no intention of throwing away my original world.

More than anything, if my best friends Azuma and Asai are dead, I want to at least bring their belongings back and hold a proper memorial for them.

《Dora wants to go to Master’s house too!》

“Don’t forget me either, Mio-chan!”

“I will, of course, accompany you.”

If I return to, or go to, my original world, I’d probably bring Dora, Mio, and Maria with me.

The difference in the flow of time worries me a bit, but I’m sure it can be dealt with somehow.

“Come to think of it, I haven’t asked Sera yet. What would you do if I returned to my original world?”

The last time returning to my original world came up was shortly before Sera joined us.

“It depends on whether magic can be used in Master’s world. If magic cannot be used there, then I would be unable to use ‘Ration balls’, which means I would starve to death without question.”

《Not very tasty…》

“Even if they aren’t tasty, they are my staple food. This world has ‘Ration balls’, and monsters exist, so the food situation is stable.”

Satisfying Sera’s appetite in my original world would be an enormous burden.

In this world, for better or worse (at least around me), the food situation is stable.

“‘Ration balls’ probably can’t be used there.”

“Then I will remain in this world.”

Sera has decided to stay.

For her, food supply is directly tied to life and death.

“Back to the topic, what’s your sister’s name?”

“Shindo Rin.”

If you fit it into a status screen, it would look like this.

Name: Shindo Rin

Gender: Female

Age: 13

Race: Human

“She sounds similar to Jin.”

“Yeah. I named her. That was idea number three.”

“What about ideas one and two?”

“Everyone opposed them with full force.”

Adjusted to the current format, it was like this.

Name her ‘Jinnie’

Name her ‘Jinko’

Name her ‘Rin’

“A wise decision.”

I personally recommended ‘Jinko’, though…

“Jin-kun, may I ask one question…?”

“Not just one, you can ask as many as you like.”

I don’t recall ever limiting the number of questions.

I think Sakura could stand to assert herself more.

“You said you named her earlier, but isn’t it strange to name your step-sister…?”

“Now that you mention it, that is strange, isn’t it? Master, what exactly did you do?”

Mio is already convinced I’ve done something reckless.

“No, even though I say step-sister, she was originally my cousin.”

“So you are related by blood, at least…”

Her parents died, and my parents took her in. That’s how she became my sister.

“Yeah. I was close with her parents, so I went to see her right after she was born. A lot happened then, and I ended up naming her.”

“What do you mean, ‘a lot happened’?”

“She was already very attached to me, so her parents asked me to name her.”

Thinking back on it now, that’s a pretty outrageous thing to ask.

“She was already attached to you even before you named her?”

“Yeah. She was more attached to me than to her real parents.”

“At that point, she’s truly hardcore. Are you really sure she’s grown out of her brother complex?”

Mio tilted her head in confusion.

“Probably. She used to call me ‘big brother’, but now it’s ‘brother.’ She doesn’t barge into the bath anymore. And she doesn’t crawl into my bed when I wake up in the morning either.”

As an aside, when Sakuya called me ‘big brother’ in Castal, it was the first time in about half a year, so I felt nostalgic and a little moved.

“That’s all too normal to be useful as a reference. Hmm…”

Mio pressed her hand to her forehead and groaned.

“Master, please, put a bit more effort into searching for a way back to your original world.”

“Why?”

“Because your sister probably hasn’t actually grown out of it.”

“She’ll be fine, right?”

“Just do it! Please!”

“Well, if Mio insists that much, alright, I get it.”

If Mio is pushing this hard, then there’s probably a chance my sister hasn’t really grown out of it.

A way back to my original world, huh… Asking the goddess would probably be the fastest route.

After that, we talked about various other things here and there.

When time passed and it became time to eat, we decided to end the question session.

“It feels like we talked about your sister the whole time.”

“That’s because you suddenly dropped such a strong topic, Master. Of course we had to ask questions.”

Was it really that strong a topic?

Having siblings isn’t that strange, is it?

My friend Asai also has a sister, the same age as mine, and they got along well.

Only my other friend, Azuma, was an only child, so he sometimes got left out of sister talk.

Nostalgic memories.

Time rewinds a bit, to before Shindo Jin and the others were transferred, to an incident at Asai Yoshinobu’s house.

“Holy… I’m about to die…”

“There, there. I think Rin is doing her best. But that’s not a face a middle school girl should be making, okay?”

Asai Yoshinobu’s sister, Asai Hijiri, patted the head of Shindo Rin, who had clung to her, and comforted her.

On this day, Rin had reached the limit of her stress from trying to grow out of her brother complex, and had come to vent to her best friend Hijiri.

“Is my face really that bad?”

“Yeah. If a kid saw you in the middle of the night, they’d definitely cry.”

“That bad…?”

Rin’s face is well-shaped enough that ten out of ten people would agree she’s pretty.

Yet now, she’s terribly worn down. Her complexion is bad, and combined with her long hair, she has a certain horror-like presence. Children would cry.

“If it’s really too much, you should tell Jin-nii, you know? Even Jin-nii wouldn’t push you if he knew it was that hard on you.”

“No. I understand that my brother is saying this for my sake. That’s why I want to meet his expectations. So I can still endure it… even if I’m about to die.”

“Rin really is so earnest…”

As she praised Rin, Hijiri thought to herself.

(That doesn’t look like she’s grown out of her ‘brother complex’ at all, does it? She’s just pretending she has.)

Hijiri gets along normally with her own brother, Yoshinobu, but not to the extent that she’d need to grow out of it.

When she heard that Rin had been bathing together with Jin until recently, she was simply shocked.

“But if you go home like this, Jin-nii will worry, so maybe you should come up with something.”

“That bad…?”

“Yeah.”

Children would cry.

“Well then, want to do something to take your mind off it?”

“That’s true. Tests are coming up, so shall we study? Hijiri, you said you were worried about history, right? I’ll teach you.”

“Really!? That helps so much! What you really need in life is a genius friend!”

Hijiri is a bit bad at memorization subjects.

“I’m not a genius. I’m just an ordinary girl you can find anywhere. My test scores and report cards were average, weren’t they?”

“Rin insists she’s ordinary, but I don’t think consistently hitting the exact class average in every subject counts as ordinary.”

Rin’s grades are exactly the class average in every subject. That is the entirety of her academic record.

“I’m ordinary. And besides, the word ‘genius’ applies to people like Azuma-san.”

“Ah, Azuma-san. Yeah, he’s definitely in a class of his own.”

Both of them call Azuma Akira, the best friend of Jin and Yoshinobu, ‘Azuma-san.’

Azuma is the only one without siblings, so there’s a slight distance between him and Rin and Hijiri, who are close siblings.

“You say that like it’s someone else’s problem, but Yoshinobu-san is also in that exceptional category, you know?”

Since ‘Asai-san’ wouldn’t distinguish him, Rin calls Asai Yoshinobu ‘Yoshinobu-san.’

“Jin-nii too, right?”

“Of course. My brother is amazing.”

Rin’s trust in Jin has neither limit nor basis. That is precisely why it is so strong.

“Well, Jin-nii aside, my brother’s just got good eyesight, that’s all…”

Of course, that’s not true.

Hijiri, for her part, is somewhat numb because the people around her are all too exceptional.

“I’m home.”

“Speak of the devil, looks like he’s back. Welcome home.”

As they were talking about Yoshinobu, he came home.

“Oh, Rin-chan, long time no see.”

“Thank you for having me.”

Rin comes over to the Asai household fairly often, but rarely runs into Yoshinobu, who is often out.

“…Looks like Mom’s not here. Just hijiki, huh.”

“Don’t call me hijiki, you idiot brother!”

One of Hijiri’s forbidden words is ‘hijiki.’

The enraged hijiki jammed her hand into her pocket and threw what she pulled out at Yoshinobu.

“You missed!”

With his excellent dynamic vision, Yoshinobu easily dodged the ball flying at his face.

-Gon!-

“Guh!”

The next moment, Yoshinobu clutched the back of his head and collapsed.

The super ball had hit the wall behind him, bounced back, and struck him in the back of the head.

Yoshinobu’s eyes are indeed excellent.

Unfortunately for him, he only has two, and they’re on his face.

Therefore, he cannot see behind himself.

…Strictly speaking, he could perceive what’s behind him from reflections, but his own head blocked the view, so he couldn’t predict the ball’s trajectory.

Yes, hijiki had planned this far ahead. Her anti-brother measures were perfect.

“W-Wait… That seriously hurts!?”

Yoshinobu has tears in his eyes for real.

“It’s a special super ball made from a heavy, highly elastic material. I asked Azuma-san to make it for me as a decisive weapon against idiot brothers.”

Throwing a heavy super ball made by her brother’s friend at her actual brother.

The anger at being called hijiki runs that deep.

“Toooooomeeeeee!!!”

Yoshinobu screamed at his best friend’s cruel betrayal.

‘Toomei’ is Yoshinobu’s nickname for Azuma. Azuma himself doesn’t like it very much.

“He gladly agreed when I said I’d use it if you called me hijiki.”

Apparently, being asked by a younger girl wasn’t entirely unpleasant.

“That bastard. Giving hijiki something unnecessary…”

“Want to take another hit?”

“Seriously, stop! Ow… There’s no bump, right?”

It seems to have really hurt, as Yoshinobu keeps touching his head to check.

“…Huh? Rin-chan, have you lost weight or something? Your complexion’s bad.”

Only then did Yoshinobu finally notice Rin’s ghost-like pallor.

In truth, since Yoshinobu has good eyesight, he often notices even small changes.

But in Rin’s case, it’s obvious to anyone.

You could even say he noticed late this time.

“Yes. I’ve been keeping my distance from my brother, but it’s been painful…”

“You’re distancing yourself from Jin? …Could it be about that talk the other day?”

“Did something happen?”

Neither Rin nor Hijiri had told Yoshinobu about the growing out of her ‘brother complex’ talk.

“The other day, Jin and I were talking about sister stuff.”

“Eh, big brother, gross.”

Hijiri immediately insults Yoshinobu without hesitation.

“Shut up! Anyway, during that talk, I teased him about the distance between him and Rin-chan… and it turns out Jin seriously hadn’t noticed at all. He was completely shocked. In the end, I had to teach him what an appropriate distance looks like.”

Even Yoshinobu was left speechless when he heard they were bathing together.

Jin is also somewhat dense about personal boundaries, so he apparently didn’t think it was unnatural until someone pointed it out.

“So this was Yoshinobu-san’s doing… How unnecessary…”

“Seriously, he always does unnecessary things.”

“Huh…? Is this really my fault…?”

Suddenly blamed by both of them, Yoshinobu couldn’t accept it.

From his perspective, he acted out of kindness, and he never thought it would be a burden on Rin.

By common sense, Yoshinobu is not at fault.

“Yoshinobu-san, could you tell me what ‘appropriate distance’ you taught my brother?”

“Ah, I see. You’re checking the minimum conditions. You’re sharp.”

Understanding Rin’s intent, Hijiri gave a wry smile.

Rin thought that Yoshinobu’s ‘appropriate distance’ was the essential requirement for growing out of her ‘brother complex’.

Conversely, she saw hope that there was room for compromise in anything not listed there.

“Please.”

Rin pulled out a memo pad, fully prepared.

“Sure, that’s fine. …First off, bathing together is impossible.”

“I see. That can’t be helped. It was our main form of skinship…”

Rin looked genuinely regretful.

“Oh, so you were washing each other’s backs.”

Yoshinobu nodded in understanding, but imagining a high school boy (his best friend) and a middle school girl (his best friend’s sister) washing each other’s backs left him with mixed feelings.

“Back?”

Rin tilted her head.

“”Eh?””

“Eh?”

The Asai siblings were shocked by Rin’s remark, and Rin was shocked by their reaction.

Yoshinobu and Hijiri decided it was better not to probe further.

There are things in this world you don’t need to know.

After that, Yoshinobu told Rin the other things he had told Jin.

“That’s about it.”

“Thank you very much. This was helpful.”

Rin was inwardly delighted that the conditions had more holes than she expected, but she didn’t show it on her face.

“And to claim success in growing out of your ‘brother complex’, changing how you address him is also an option. ‘Brother’ should be fine.”

“That really is helpful.”

Rin added a note to her memo.

“Of course, calling him ‘bro’ is out. A sister like that isn’t cute.”

“And what’s wrong with not being cute!”

Incidentally, while Hijiri has a boyish vibe, she isn’t unattractive (at least in appearance).

“Hey, hey, I never said anything about hijiki.”

“I’ll hit you!”

Hijiri pulled out the special super ball.

“W-Well then, I’m heading out. Take it easy, Rin-chan!”

“Thank you very much.”

And so Yoshinobu retreated.

“You get along well.”

“Don’t be ridiculous! He keeps calling me hijiki.”

“Then why don’t you try giving Yoshinobu-san a nickname too?”

“…Yoshi?”

“That’s very normal.”

The top candidate for Yoshinobu’s nickname.

After that, as planned, they began studying for tests in Hijiri’s room.

“Break time!”

“Quite a bit of time has passed, so let’s do that.”

Hijiri stretched energetically, while Rin didn’t look tired at all.

“By the way… is Jin-nii popular?”

“Why would you ask that all of a sudden?!”

If you want to shake Rin’s calm composure, just bring up Jin.

“Well, my brother is actually pretty popular, you know. So I was curious how it was for Jin-nii, who’s also in the exceptional group.”

Yoshinobu has a good eye for people and a wide social circle. Naturally, he’s popular.

Though at the moment, he values hanging out with his best friends over getting a girlfriend…

“Well… my brother isn’t popular.”

“Huh? What about his childhood friend Mizuhara-san, or those girls who follow him around sometimes?”

Mizuhara Saki. Jin’s next-door neighbor and childhood friend, the same age as him.

“You mean Saki-oneechan?”

Being Jin’s childhood friend also means she’s been around Rin for a long time.

“Saki-oneechan’s feelings toward my brother are completely different from normal romantic love.”

“That, of all things!?”

“Yes. If you watch closely, you’ll understand.”

Both of them love Jin dearly, but their feelings are completely different in nature, so they don’t compete, and their relationship remains good.

She’s even called ‘Saki-oneechan’. You wouldn’t use that unless you were very close.

“I know about the girls who follow him too, but they don’t seem to intend to get involved with my brother. So they probably haven’t even considered confessing to him.”

“I see. Jin-nii just doesn’t register as a normal romantic interest…”

Despite having girls around him, it never turns into a clear romantic story. That is Shindo Jin.

“What about you, Hijiri? Do you like my brother?”

“I like him, but not romantically. I don’t think I could handle him, anyway…”

Hijiri is, for better or worse, a normal girl.

Unlike Rin, who is a pseudo-normal girl.

“What about you, Rin? Could your affection for Jin-nii turn into romantic love? You’re actually cousins, right? Ethically, that’s safe, right?”

“If my brother wanted it, I wouldn’t say no. I’d do anything for him. But my feelings are affection, nothing more. That will never change.”

“You wouldn’t say no… you’d do anything for him…”

Hijiri was thoroughly taken aback.

“Well, Jin-nii only sees Rin as a little sister anyway, so I don’t think it’ll turn into anything weird…”

“Yes, I think so too. And that’s fine. As cousins… as siblings, no matter what happens, our bond can never be cut.”

A husband-and-wife relationship is contractual in nature, and that relationship isn’t eternal.

As the phrase goes, ’till death do us part’, they are separated by death.

But cousins… siblings are bound by blood.

That relationship doesn’t require anyone’s approval, and not even death can sever it.

It can be called an eternal, unchanging relationship.

“You’re really a hardcore ‘little sister’.”

No matter how you look at it, she doesn’t seem capable of growing out of her ‘brother complex’.

“Yes. I will always be my brother’s little sister. Forever.”

---

**AN:** Whether Jin has a sister or not. The answer has not actually been decided yet.

The word ‘if’ has no power to determine which is true.

It states neither ‘he does’ nor ‘he doesn’t’.

If there is enough support (feedback) from everyone, it might become ‘he does’. Or depending on the needs of future stories.

And if the answer becomes ‘he does’, then an Answer (A) is added to False Tale (Giden), making it Side Story (Gaiden).

If the answer is ‘he doesn’t’, then the Girl (G) disappears, and False Tale (Giden) becomes Another Tale (Iden).

If neither is decided, then False Tale remains False Tale forever.

Revised on 2019/04/10:

Based on the responses, we decided to go with A.

+++

## **170.5: About the Soul**

**AN:** This is the first of two chapters posted together.

It is a short piece, but it explains some fairly important elements that I failed to include in the main story.

These may come up abruptly in the future, so if possible, please take a look.

---

This takes place after Jin’s Special Power levels increased, with \<Life and Death Authority> reaching LV9 and \<Multiple Existence> reaching LV7.

“As a side effect of gaining the ability to ‘make contact with souls’ and ‘manipulate souls’, I became able to access a concept called ‘Personality’.”

“Can you explain that in a bit more detail?”

Faced with Jin’s extremely rough explanation, that was all Mio could say.

Not just Mio, but all of the main members had question marks floating over their heads.

“In fact, humans and monsters possess individual traits and characteristics separate from Skills. This time, for clarity, I’ve decided to call those things ‘Personality’.”

“Still not detailed enough.”

Prompted by Mio’s interjection, Jin continued.

“This ‘Personality’ is information engraved into the soul, and it does not change as easily as Skills do. …Right. To make this easier to understand, let me give you an analogy.”

Jin organized his thoughts on the difference between ‘Personality’ and ‘Skills.’

“Imagine our souls as a single lump of clay.”

“Oil clay? Paper clay? Which one? That actually matters.”

“It really changes the impression, doesn’t it…”

The Japanese members gave wry smiles.

“Oil clay. In terms of being able to work it over repeatedly, oil clay is closer.”

“Okay. I can picture it.”

“Our souls are like shelves made of oil clay. Skills are the small items placed on those shelves. Skills that grow can be thought of as potted tomato plants.”

“A supreme salad.”

“That isn’t a salad.”

Mio made a reference that only some people understood.

“Back to the point. ‘Personality’ is different from Skills. It is something mixed directly into the oil clay itself. It is strongly connected to, and blended into, the oil clay, the soul itself. And once mixed in, it is almost irreversible.”

“How much influence does this ‘Personality’ have? Is it comparable to Skills?”

Maria asked because, as Jin’s guard, she was concerned about how much of a threat ‘Personality’ could pose.

“No. Most ‘Personalities’ do not have as much influence as Skills. But some of them are surprisingly important.”

Jin’s expression grew slightly serious.

“The easiest example is one of my own ‘Personalities’.”

“Master, you can’t learn Skills, but you do have this ‘Personality’ thing, huh?”

Mio said teasingly.

“That’s it. \<Unable to Acquire Skills>. That’s the clearest example of a ‘Personality.’”

“Yeah! Super important!”

Mio was completely convinced.

“There are quite a few ‘Personalities’ related to Skills. In my case, there’s \<Creation-Type Skill Inhibition (Large)> and \<Cooking-Type Skill Inhibition (Extra Large)>.”

At last, the reason for Jin’s negative traits was revealed.

“So it was because of ‘Personality’. Could it be that Dora-chan’s \<Pharmacy> is also…?”

“Yeah. She has \<Pharmaceutical Skill Support (Medium)>. And Maria and the others with \<Hero> Skills have \<Skill Acquisition Support (Large)>.”

“Even Maria-chan only has (Large), but Master’s \<Cooking> is negative at (Extra Large).”

“Please don’t say that.”

Jin had not avoided cooking until now.

He had tried, and failed. “Grilling meat” was the maximum level of cooking Jin was allowed.

“‘Personality’ cannot be checked via Status like Skills can. You can look at a shelf and see what’s on it, but you can’t tell what’s mixed into the shelf itself, right?”

“But, Master, you said earlier that you can access ‘Personality’, didn’t you? That means there are exceptions, correct?”

What Sera pointed out was Jin’s initial statement. He had indeed said that.

“Yeah. Thanks to ‘contact with souls’ gained from leveling up my Special Power, I can now tell what’s mixed into the shelf. …However, unless I touch the other person’s body, in other words, truly touch their soul, I can’t see someone else’s ‘Personality’.”

Even with \<Clairvoyance>, you can’t see inside a soul.

Without scanning through contact, you can’t obtain soul information.

“Is it possible to take or give them like Skills? Using the other Special Power, ‘Soul Manipulation’, couldn’t you do it?”

“At present, it’s impossible. The best I can do right now is delete ‘Personality’.”

Jin answered Maria’s question immediately.

“Isn’t that enough? At least you can delete \<Unable to Acquire Skills>… So now Master can finally learn Skills… right? You can’t?”

Midway through the conversation, Jin’s expression turned bitter, so Mio asked hesitantly.

“There are stages to how strongly a ‘Personality’ is bound to the soul. As far as I know, there are five stages. Right now, I can only delete the lowest, the first-stage ‘Personalities’.”

“What stage is \<Unable to Acquire Skills>?”

“The fifth stage.”

“_Oh_!”

Mio clutched her head with native pronunciation.

As an aside, while Maria’s \<Skill Acquisition Support (Large)> is fourth stage, both \<Creation-Type Skill Inhibition (Large)> and \<Cooking-Type Skill Inhibition (Extra Large)> are fifth stage.

The world is harsh on Jin (other factors aside).

“Then, what kinds of things are first-stage ‘Personalities’…?”

This time, Sakura asked.

“According to Alta, it’s \<Dragonkin Aversion (Extra Large)> possessed by dragons.”

“So that’s also a ‘Personality’…”

“Incidentally, dragonkin do not possess \<Dragon Aversion>.”

Even without directly touching them, Jin could already confirm all ‘Personalities’ of those who had become his subordinates.

Not a single dragonkin had \<Dragon Aversion>.

“I always assumed dragon behavior was a racial trait.”

Removing \<Dragonkin Aversion (Extra Large)> from the feathered dragon Mio was planning to tame would be a story for another time.

“By the way, racial traits are handled separately from ‘Personality’.”

Species-specific traits generally do not appear as ‘Personality’.

“They really are traits attached to the individual.”

“That’s why it’s called Personality, right?”

For Jin, it was surprisingly sensible naming.

“For now, only Master can see ‘Personality’, right?”

“It doesn’t appear in Status. But I could probably add known ‘Personalities’ to the Status screen.”

“Show me! Show me the hidden parameters!”

Mio was thinking like a gamer.

To be fair, Jin had thought the same thing before.

“Then for now, I’ll show you my ‘Personality’.”

Shindo Jin

Personality:

Aptitude

\<Unable to Acquire Skills Rank5> \<Creation-Type Skill Inhibition (Large) Rank5> \<Cooking-Type Skill Inhibition (Extra Large) Rank5> etc

Constitution

\<Primordial Divine Dragon Aptitude Rank2> \<Oni God Aptitude Rank2> \<Demon God Aptitude Rank2> etc

Other

\<Calamity Dragon Authority Rank4> etc

*For story convenience, some Personalities are not disclosed.

“The ‘Rank’ written there is what you meant by stages earlier, right?”

“Yeah. I didn’t have anywhere else appropriate to put it, so I wrote it where Levels usually go.”

The higher the Rank, the harder it is to be influenced by external factors. In other words, it indicates a stronger bond with the soul.

Without a point of comparison it’s hard to tell, but Jin’s ‘Personality’ Ranks are extremely high.

“What’s with ‘Aptitude’ and the like? Is that a classification like Skills?”

“Yeah. I decided those on the fly this time. Aptitude affects Skill acquisition and use. Constitution relates to physical traits. Other is other.”

Things that can’t be categorized are grouped under ‘Other.’

“So calamity dragon abilities are also ‘Personality’. I wondered where they were reflected since they weren’t Skills…”

‘Personality’ is basically self-contained within an individual.

However, calamity dragon-related ‘Personalities’ are exceptional in that they have a major external impact.

And since ‘Personality’ generally requires no cost, it does not consume MP or the like.

That alone should convey how abnormal calamity dragon abilities are.

“Most of my Constitution and Other ones were acquired later. The traits of souls absorbed through \<Life and Death Authority> must be getting tied to ‘Personality’.”

“So that clears up the parts that didn’t quite make sense before.”

“Yeah.”

Up until now, there were things that couldn’t be explained by Skills or Special Powers.

Those can now generally be explained by ‘Personality’.

In fact, Alta also had knowledge about ‘Personality’.

However, at the time, it was information she could not access, and since nothing could be stated definitively, she deliberately chose not to tell Jin.

“By the way, are Special Powers related to ‘Personality’?”

“Special Powers are Special Powers. They’re not Skills, Blessings, Curse Marks, or ‘Personality’. They’re something completely different.”

“I knew it, but Special Powers are still the most incomprehensible…”

‘Personality’ is information that became accessible through Special Powers, and Special Powers can sometimes increase ‘Personality’.

However, there was nothing on the ‘Personality’ side that affected Special Powers.

This can be seen as proof that Special Powers exist on a higher level than ‘Personality’.

So while understanding this new logic called ‘Personality’ was good, the situation of the most familiar Special Powers remaining incomprehensible had not changed.

---

**AN:** I put a lot of work into the soul-related settings.

Since explanations can get long-winded, I want to keep them as mild as possible.

## **Volume 11 Characters**

**AN:** Second part of a two-episode post.

This is the character introduction at the end of the volume.

There are not many newly introduced characters.

Also, there is a younger sister.

---

Basically, only characters whose names are shown in the main story are included. Skills are excluded.

Information that is not explicitly stated is excluded.

**Protagonist Side**

Name: Ange (Shion)

Gender: Female

Age: 5

Race: Angel

Titles: Jin’s Slave, Jin’s Familiar, Progenitor of Angels

Notes: A girl whose race was altered due to \<Branch of the System Tree>. She is a rare existence in many senses, as both \<Slave Arts> and \<Monster Taming> contracts are simultaneously valid. She is attached to Jin, and is pleased with the dual contracts as proof of the strength of her bond with him. She possesses a special effectiveness against “Evil” and is one of the candidates for an ultimate strongest character. Also, having become an angel (treated as a monster), her lifespan exceeds that of humans.

Name: Bran

Gender: Female

Age: 0

Race: Feather Dragon

Titles: Mio’s Familiar

Notes: A female Feather Dragon whose soul was tampered with by Jin, erasing her hostility toward the Dragonkin race, after which she was tamed by Mio. She recognizes Mio as her master, but submits even more completely to Jin. No expectations are placed on her combat ability, and her main role is essentially that of a body pillow. She has a rivalry with Dora’s fur, but at the same time understands that Dora is a distant and overwhelmingly powerful opponent.

Name: Londrine

Gender: Female

Age: 16

Race: Demon

Titles: Jin’s Slave

Notes: One of the Demon King’s Army Four Heavenly Kings, “Londrine of Phantoms.” She was captured by the fake heroes who serve under Jin. Stealth-type curse seals are ineffective against maps. In front of Jin she does nothing but scream, but she is a taciturn and duty-bound girl (her personality as a reincarnated demon). Her name before reincarnation was Kaho Hoshino. She was an energetic sports girl, but died in a traffic accident and was reincarnated. This will probably never be touched upon in the main story.

Name: Suzu (Yurisuzu)

Gender: Female

Age: 3110

Race: High Elf

Titles: Elf Princess Shrine Maiden, Elf Royalty, Living Sacrifice, Adventurers Guild Headquarters Guildmaster, Jin’s Slave

Notes: The “Princess Shrine Maiden” who continued to seal the “Fire Disaster Dragon: Volcano.” She is the founder and highest authority of the Adventurers Guild, and also possesses high combat ability (within a general range). This was based on the idea that “if she herself became stronger and harder to kill, it would be better for protecting the seal of the disaster dragon.” As a result, it is probably not just imagination that she ended up inviting unnecessary danger as well. At Yuriela’s request, she lures Claude and the others and attempts to abduct Yuria, but fails. Overwhelmed by Jin’s presence, she becomes his slave.

Name: Yuriela

Gender: Female

Age: 7569

Race: High Elf

Titles: Elf Princess Shrine Maiden, Elf Royalty, Living Sacrifice, Jin’s Slave

Notes: The “Princess Shrine Maiden” who continued to seal the “Wind Disaster Dragon: Tempest.” Because she lived in the safe Sky Castle, her abilities are low for her age. She has a spirit contract with the Great Spirit “Ilminea”, but this is a spirit inherited by successive “Princess Shrine Maidens” of the Wind Disaster Dragon, not an achievement of her own. She is killed by a mob, then revived but loses all her memories, and is currently in a doll-like state with no sense of self (in training). Later she becomes the public highest authority of a certain religion, but that is another story.

Name: Pes

Gender: Female

Age: 65535

Race: Human (Incarnation)

Titles: Incarnation of a Disaster Dragon

Notes: An incarnation into which the “Wind Disaster Dragon: Tempest” transferred its personality before dying. She looks like a girl of about five years old. By deliberately making her a powerless existence, it became possible for her to beg Jin for her life. She has only the abilities her appearance suggests, so she ends up working hard as a maid-in-training. Originally, disaster dragons have no ego, but due to an accident involving a sealing crystal, Yuria’s personality flowed in, allowing her to acquire a sense of self. Her personality base is Yuria as she was before losing her memories.

Yuria: “Was I really like that before I lost my memories…?”

Slave Elves x300

Race: Elf

Titles: Jin’s Slaves

Notes: Elves who lived in the Sky Castle and bore the mission of sealing disaster dragons. In addition to the clan that sealed the “Wind Disaster Dragon”, there are also clans for the “Fire Disaster Dragon” and the “Earth Disaster Dragon.” Of the 1000 elves, 30 percent, or 300, became slaves. The rest refused to become slaves and became sea mozuku. Mozuku?

**Guild Union District**

Name: George

Gender: Male

Age: 38

Titles: One of the S-rank adventurers, and one of those who did not try to capture Claude and the others.

Notes: A tough-looking macho man who also has a side as a philanthropist. Among the S-rank adventurers, he is one of the more cooperative ones.

Name: Reinhardt

Gender: Male

Notes: An S-rank adventurer known by the alias “Reinhardt of the Silver Flash.” He sided with those trying to capture Claude, so he ended up groaning in the toilet. The laxatives worked beyond the maids expectations, and because he went to the toilet frequently, he came to be called “Reinhardt of Frequent Bowel Movements.” He looks like he is about to cry.

Name: Unknown (Reinhardt’s Sister)

Gender: Female

Notes: After engaging in a (completely naked) battle with an S-rank female adventurer in the hot springs, she was knocked out in a single blow by Jin. Silver hair on both top and bottom.

Name: Unknown (S-rank Female Adventurer)

Gender: Female

Notes: After engaging in a (completely naked) battle with Reinhardt’s sister in the hot springs, she was knocked out in a single blow by Jin. Red hair on both top and bottom.

**Sky Castle**

Name: Gired

Gender: Male

Race: High Elf

Notes: A man of the elf clan that seals the “Earth Disaster Dragon: Earthquake.” He is the creator of the sealing crystal that sealed Ulysses, and also the cause of Yuria’s transfer and memory loss. When he appears next time, Jin will show no mercy. He will die.

Name: Unknown (Yurina’s Father)

Gender: Male

Race: Elf

Titles: The father of Yurina, a High Elf girl who became a victim of the sealing crystal before Yuria.

Notes: He was not aware that Yurina had died due to the rampage of the sealing crystal, and was told that she had run away because she did not want to become a “Princess Shrine Maiden.” Though he felt something was off, he could not say anything due to his position. Upon learning the truth, he snapped. He killed Yuriela and landed a blow on Gired as well. After that, he took his own life and followed after his daughter.

Depending on the situation, it may become the Crimson Empire arc (Part One).

Posts will continue on days ending in 0 as usual. Weekly posting has been abandoned.
