## **171: Rebuilding the Sky Castle and Future Plans**

**AN:** At last. Finally. It is here. The Crimson Empire arc.

There will be no detours. Really. The Volume title is not “???” either. It is “Crimson Empire Arc” right from the start.

---

That day, I received a message from Mio, who had been holed up for several days.

“Master, it is finally finished!”

“Oh, it is done at last? Sky Castle ver 2.0. Let us go right away.”

I had asked Mio to create a new Sky Castle, Sky Castle ver 2.0, using the remains of the ‘Wind Calamity Dragon: Tempest’ and the wreckage of the former Sky Castle as materials.

Mio, who has a surprisingly obsessive side, seemed to have gotten far more engrossed than expected. Aside from cooking and eating, she had not left her room at all.

This is just my own speculation, but was it not a goddess who created the original Sky Castle?

After all, burying ‘Tempest’ in the ground to create land is not something people of that era could have done under normal circumstances.

If a goddess sealed the calamity dragon soul in a subspace, then it would not be strange for her to also handle the remaining body.

This time, the one who accomplished such a goddess-like feat was, as you know, my Special Power.

The disassembly and synthesis functions of \<Infinite Storage>.

Frankly speaking, I lack all sense for crafting things, and if I want something, I usually ask someone else to make it. Because of that, I had not used it in a long time.

Apparently, my subordinates use it normally.

“‘Portal’.”

Without delay, we (excluding the food-obsessed Sera and Dora) transferred to Sky Castle ver 2.0.

“This is magnificent.”

“It really is exactly that…”

Sakura and I voiced our admiration.

Mio had drastically changed the exterior from the previous Sky Castle, bringing it much closer to the sky castle I knew.

Rather than the flat, land-like structure from before, it now had a vertical, layered structure like an egg when seen from afar.

There were no residents yet, but there were buildings that looked like living quarters, and there seemed to be fields as well. Rare plants were probably being grown there.

“It was hard work, you know. Since it was such an old memory, digging it out was quite a task.”

“Ah, right. Since you reincarnated, there is a time lag compared to us.”

Sakura and I transferred here, but Mio came to this world through reincarnation.

Since she lived time in this world, the memories were at least close to ten years old.

“Because I took my time, I am satisfied with the finished result. Oh, the construction parts were handled by the construction maids.”

“There they are. The construction maids…”

The construction maids that come up from time to time.

They built the Advance Trading Company building in a single night and even constructed a luxury cruise ship. A highly active group.

A: We are extremely pleased to be called highly active by Master.

Praise them… no, I am praising them.

I am praising them, but somehow it feels like they are directly denying the very concept of a maid…

Yes, yes. Do not say “it is a bit late for that.”

“When I told them it was your castle, Master, they really put their hearts into it.”

“Indeed. Anyone who would not do so would be unfit to be one of Lord Jin’s subordinates.”

“They were happy that they could finally build a base for you, Master. For now, both Castal and Estea are ready-made mansions, after all…”

Ah, I see.

Despite being called construction maids, they were not involved in building where I live.

Well, that makes sense. When I established bases in Castal and Estea, it was long before the maid corps reached its current scale.

And since then, I stopped preparing new mansions.

“I appreciate the effort they put into it, but I do not intend to stay here permanently.”

This Sky Castle is nothing more than a hobby.

It is at the level of a vacation home I would visit occasionally. I have no intention of using it frequently.

“They seem to understand that. They said that was fine. Such devoted girls.”

“If anything, it makes me feel sorry…”

You are saying we had them put their all into something I do not even plan to use properly, right?

A: They say that with even a single word of praise from Master, they can work as hard as needed.

…Later, I should go praise them directly. Maybe I should prepare a reward as well.

“I told them to focus on the exterior and not put too much effort into the interior, but… judging by this, they must have worked hard anyway. I have not even seen the inside yet, so I am looking forward to it.”

With that said, we entered the most luxurious building, what Mio called “My castle”.

“It is luxurious.”

“It is luxurious.”

“It is luxurious…”

“Considering Lord Jin’s status, this might still be insufficient, but it seems to be well made. I am relieved.”

It was a royal castle, plain and simple.

Also, Maria apparently thinks it should be even more.

Later, I invited Sakuya, Cattleya, and other royal women to see it. Most of them felt, “Ah, our castles lose”.

Barely, Castal, which had involvement from a Hero during its construction, was considered roughly equal.

The Estea royal family, though connected to the East, had no involvement in the castle construction and thus lost.

As for the Izumo Wa Country, there is a past where the construction maids repaired the royal castle. There is no way it could surpass the greatest work of the construction maids.

“They put so much effort into it that it actually makes me uncomfortable.”

“Only a real king would feel comfortable here.”

There is no “becoming a king” in my life plan.

I have no hobby of sitting on a throne in a royal castle when I am not a king.

If it is just for living, a normal mansion is fine.

After that, since it was just about lunchtime, we decided to have lunch in the royal castle while discussing future plans.

Dora and Sera, who had gone out eating, also joined us, and we called Ulysses as well, the Earth Calamity Dragon’s ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’.

“Sera and Dora, you were eating around until now, right? Are you eating lunch too?”

I asked, looking at the two who naturally demanded food.

“Lunch is a separate stomach.”

《Separate stomach!》

“That logic is wrong.”

If the main lunch is a separate stomach, how many stomachs do you need?

…Dora, or rather, dragonkin or dragons only have one stomach, right? They do not have multiple stomachs like cows, right?

A: One.

Good.

I do not know what exactly is good, but good.

“By the way, Jin-san, why was I called here? Of course, I am very happy to be invited to a meal by you, but you did not call me just to eat for no reason, right? Oh, if it is a confession of love, I am always ready, so feel free.”

Ulysses asked with a smile.

The joke in the latter half sounded like a joke, but it was not a joke at all. Her eyes were serious.

“Sorry, but it is not a love confession. The Sky Castle is finished, and I thought it was about time to decide what to do with the elves. I wanted to hear your opinion too, Ulysses.”

“Right now, they are being educated, correct?”

“Yeah.”

About 300 elves who lived in the Sky Castle were trained in a residential area on the 50-plus floors of the labyrinth.

This time, “training” is correct.

Most of the elves did not know common sense of the surface world, and to make matters worse, they had an elitist mindset.

They thought pure elves like themselves were superior and looked down on other races, including humans and half-elves.

Those with full-fledged elitism died when the Sky Castle fell, but the survivors still retained some of it.

The maids who dealt with them judged that they could not be brought before me.

Thus, they trained them without mercy and rewrote their thinking at the ideological level.

While Mio was building the Sky Castle, the training was completed, and the elves had apparently become obedient livestock.

After breaking them once and making them obedient, they are now slowly being educated in common sense and manners.

Because their memory is good, they are learning reasonably well.

“First, a question for you, Ulysses. Your relatives, the Earth clan, have joined my subordinates. What do you want to do? If you have any thoughts, I will prioritize your opinion.”

I asked Ulysses.

“Considering the lifespan of elves, there is no one alive who lived in the era when I was sealed. I have no desire to take out resentment toward ancestors on their descendants, so I will not demand anything. …Ah, of course, the only exception is the high elf Gired who is still alive. I will never forgive him.”

The Earth clan high elf Gired.

The man who sealed Ulysses underground and tried to steal Yuria’s memories and seal her as well.

For now, it is confirmed that Ulysses and Yuria will each punch him once. I will also let Sharon and Faron from the Regalia Beastman Kingdom punch him once each.

So, he is someone we want alive.

“Sorry. I should have captured him when he appeared at the Sky Castle.”

The span from Gired’s appearance to Yuriela’s death was so short that capturing Gired slipped my mind.

Even trying to investigate further, there were no elves directly involved, and Yuriela, the only one confirmed to have been involved, is now in a state requiring full-time care.

Rarely for me, there was “no connection.”

“Do not worry about it. But one day, I will absolutely make him atone for his sins.”

“I will fully cooperate.”

“Please do.”

If we see him next time, we capture him first.

“Then, let us talk about the future. The Earth clan will be treated the same as Fire and Wind. First, where to have the elves live and what to have them do.”

“Not the Sky Castle…?”

“It is not necessarily so.”

I shook my head in response to Sakura’s question. Until now, the elves lived in the Sky Castle and mainly farmed.

However, the current Sky Castle is no longer under the elves’ control and is completely my property.

Just because the elves lived there before does not mean I must let them live there from now on. At least, not without a clear benefit.

“To begin with, we have not decided how to handle the Sky Castle itself.”

“We made it on impulse, but we did not think at all about how to use it.”

“I acted a bit too impulsively. I should reflect on that.”

“Yeah…”

Mio and I got excited just by the words sky castle and barely thought about what comes after.

“If there are no plans to use it, maybe we should just put it back into \<Infinite Storage>.”

“It really would be a waste. But right now, we can only use it to grow plants.”

“Which can be substituted by the labyrinth.”

In Sky Castle ver 1.0, rare plants that had gone extinct on the surface were being cultivated.

Sky Castle ver 2.0 also has fields, so it is possible to continue growing them. However, they are not plants that can only be grown in the Sky Castle, and the maids have already started cultivating them in the labyrinth.

The labyrinth’s environment settings have a high degree of freedom, and there should not be many plants that cannot be grown there.

“The more I think about it, the more questionable the Sky Castle’s reason for existence becomes.”

Placing a heavy object in the sky is, in itself, a serious risk.

And there is nothing that can only be done in a Sky Castle.

In other words, we would be taking a completely unnecessary risk. That is undesirable.

“Unfortunately, it seems we cannot leave the Sky Castle unattended. When it is not in use, we will store it in \<Infinite Storage>.”

“It is treated like some kind of simple tent. The scale is incomparable, though.”

“Well, it is similar.”

Normally, it can be stored away, and when needed, you can stay there with minimal effort.

Yeah, similar enough.

Thus, Mio’s masterpiece, Sky Castle ver 2.0, was officially decided to be stored in \<Infinite Storage>.

“It is a shame, but it cannot be helped. Well, making it was fun. And it is not like we will never use it, right?”

“Yeah. We will use it if the opportunity arises. It is well made. It would be a waste not to use it.”

We can use it for large-scale parties, for example.

As a third option following mansions and the labyrinth. …Let us ignore the fact that everything other than mansions is not normal.

Now then, we strayed far from the main topic, which was the treatment of the elves.

“Back on topic. Since the Sky Castle will be stored, the elves will have to live on the ground.”

“Come to think of it, you called me, but was it fine not to call the other elves, the parties involved?”

Ulysses was called here, but no other elves were.

…Ah, excluding the elves among the serving maids. There are no Sky Castle elves here.

“I have no intention of calling them. At present, I do not feel much value in the Sky Castle elves.”

“That is harsh…”

“Well, they were not exactly friendly, and if their value is low in Master’s eyes, this is how they will be treated.”

“It is somewhat similar to how you feel about the citizens of Eldia.”

Simply put, I have no interest and no desire to treat them well.

Also, even if I asked the trained elves for opinions, I doubt anything useful would come out.

“Then why did you call me? To ask the earlier question?”

“That was a big part of it, but I also wanted to ask what elves can do. Even if I do not feel value in them, they do have numbers. If we use that many elves, maybe there is something they can do.”

The maids were also troubled by how to handle the elves.

To be frank, the elves’ specs are too low.

The Sky Castle elves did not hunt, and they handled farming with magic, so they only have some magic skill levels. They have none of the skills needed as my subordinates.

On top of that, as a result of training, their thinking ability has declined, making them even less useful.

Apparently, they do not meet the standards to become maids or butlers.

I have no interest. I truly do not.

But they are, at least nominally, people who became my subordinates by my instruction.

I thought I should at least come up with some idea.

“I debated between asking you or Suzu, but I decided to ask you, Ulysses, because of your connection.”

“That makes me honestly happy.”

As a clarification, Suzu is the Fire ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’.

With the “Yuri” gone from her name, her defining feature feels diminished.

“So, can you think of anything?”

“Hmm… They look good, so how about making them do night work?”

“You went straight for it…”

It is apparently common among half-elves.

It is a job where experience and appearance matter.

“Rejected. I will not have Advance Trading Company engage in shady business.”

I do not even have them run slave trading.

…If I let them do slave trading, I am afraid of how far they would go.

“Oh? In that case, I cannot think of anything else.”

“You gave up fast!”

“Because from what you say, nothing has changed since my era. Elitist, arrogant, but actually not very capable. I think it is a waste of time for you to think about it, Jin-san.”

Ulysses holds very little regard for the clan that guarded the calamity dragon seal, including her own kin.

“…It is a shameful truth, but the purpose of the ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’ clan was survival and leaving descendants. To never let the calamity dragon’s seal die out, to continue forever. Leave children and, if high elves, make them a ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’. A simple job. Individual aptitude had no meaning. It was like that even when we lived on the surface. Elves who lived in the Sky Castle, free from external enemies and living in peace, could not possibly do anything, could they?”

The low specs of the Sky Castle elves exist because there was no reason to raise them.

“…Yuri… no, Suzu seemed to have trained herself quite a bit, though?”

She had skills like a seasoned warrior, not something she was born with.

“The Fire ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’. She is an exception. I talked with her too. For the purpose of ‘surviving’, she chose to train herself so she would not die easily.”

“That is a bold choice. Elves are not particularly blessed physically, are they?”

If you become stronger, you become harder to kill. That is truth.

However, even with a long lifespan, it is not an easy path to choose.

Well, she clearly produced results…

“In a way, the Fire ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’ had the foundation. Her \<Will of Conflagration> is combat-oriented. Using that power, it was easy for her to become strong. But it seems no other ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’, no one in the sealing clan, ever thought of becoming strong. That is why there were no elves with high combat ability in the Sky Castle, right?”

Suzu sought strength, exceptional even among ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’s’.

The other elves never trained themselves.

…They are too weak to comfortably put into the adventurer group.

“They really cannot do anything…”

“I told you. It is a waste of time. …If you consider that night work also requires conversational ability, that might be impossible too.”

Maids, I am sorry.

It seems this is beyond what can be fixed with a small idea.

My motto is right person, right place. Then what should be done with those who have no place?

That is a future issue.

Later, I heard that by the maids decision, the assignment of the Sky Castle elves was postponed, and they decided to train them thoroughly from scratch.

Since they were already trained and obedient to orders, they were put through training up to the very limit before their bodies would break.

In about a month, they managed to raise them to a barely usable level. Apparently, that is still slow.

Since it is still unsettling to have them do important work, they will continue training while doing backstage work for now.

Q: What should be done with those who have no place?

A: Train them thoroughly for now. If that still does not work, train them more.

That is how it is.

After the meal, we called additional people and gathered in a conference room in the royal castle.

“Through the calamity dragon of the Sky Castle, we learned a bit about the goddess and this world. Important information in this world seems unnaturally hidden and cannot be accessed normally. It may be time to stop putting it off.”

“Master, what are you planning to do this time? Something weird again, pi!”

I silenced Mio with pressure.

“We are heading to the Crimson Empire, and beyond that, to the elf village.”

“I thought you had completely forgotten about the Crimson Empire, but you did remember.”

In this conference room were the main members, Rouge of the Crimson Empire royal family and her attendant Minerva, and…

“So that is why you called us, who have ties to the Crimson Empire, or rather, to Emperor Scarlet.”

“That makes sense.”

We had called Tsukiyo and Tokoyo, the golden fox mother and daughter whose friend or parents were killed by the Crimson Empire emperor Scarlet Crimson.

“Before, you said you would not go because you had no connection, but did you form a connection with the Crimson Empire after that?”

“Yeah. At the summit, I formed a connection with Scarlet of the Crimson Empire. I also gained a reason to go to the elf village regarding the goddess. Rather, now is the only time.”

Previously, when Rouge asked why ‘I would not go to the Crimson Empire’, I answered that due to bad timing, I had repeatedly been in situations where I could not go, so I had no connection.

However, now that I have a connection with the emperor himself and one of my destinations is there, it is fair to say there is no longer a reason not to go.

“So, I gathered everyone to decide how to enter the Crimson Empire and who will accompany us. By ‘how to enter’, I mean in what capacity. ‘Queen’s Knight Gene’, ‘Adventurer Jin’, or ‘Rouge’s companion’ are the candidates.”

“Ah, you mean taking me along as a guide. …I feel like I heard that a long time ago.”

Rouge seemed to remember and nodded.

It has been so long since that conversation that there was a chance she had forgotten.

“The primary purpose of going to the Crimson Empire is to stop the war they plan to wage against Estea. Being ‘Rouge’s companion’ would help avoid trouble and go smoothly.”

My impression of Scarlet when I saw him once was that he seemed serious.

However, Rouge says he plans to start a war against Estea.

Confirming the facts and, if true, stopping it is the objective.

Since there is an objective, I have no intention of enjoying trouble along the way.

Using royalty, which gives free passage in the Crimson Empire, would be the quickest.

“In the worst case, after removing my brother, we can just install me.”

“That is also an option.”

If persuasion fails, removal is also on the table.

After that, Rouge would become emperor (a puppet), so having her accompany us is convenient in every way.

“So, Rouge and the others will be going home for a visit.”

“That is quite a dangerous homecoming.”

“Do you have a complaint?”

I do not deny it is dangerous, but…

“No, I do not. Estea has taken care of me, and I have become close with the princess. If my brother is thinking of war, I am not unwilling to stop it.”

“Then it is settled. We will accompany you as guards.”

“That is a reassuring escort…”

“Yes, Lady Rouge. There is no greater peace of mind than this.”

Rouge gave a wry smile, and Minerva agreed.

“Now then, next is the matter of companions.”

This time, I turned to the golden fox mother and daughter.

“Tsukiyo, Tokoyo. It has been some time since I last asked, so I will ask again. Do you have any intention of retaliating against the Crimson Empire emperor Scarlet Crimson? If you have changed your mind, say so now. You may accompany us on this matter.”

About ten years ago, Tsukiyo’s friend and Tokoyo’s parents were killed by Scarlet.

When they became familiars, they said they would not seek revenge against Scarlet.

Because those who were killed did not wish for retaliation.

Since time has passed, there was a possibility of a change of heart, so I gathered everyone to ask again, just in case.

“Accompanying you on your journey is tempting, but we do not intend to retaliate against Scarlet. Please be assured.”

“Tsukiyo does not intend to either.”

Both answered without hesitation.

There was no sense of them enduring or suppressing anything.

“Are you really sure?”

“Yes.”

“Yeah.”

At this point, there is no mistake.

“Understood. If you are fine with it, I will not say anything more.”

“Thank you for your consideration.”

“Thanks.”

“Do not worry about it.”

It is a delicate issue, and I want to avoid excessive interference.

If they are fine with it, I should respect their will and refrain from unnecessary actions.

“My brother killed Tokoyo’s parents ten years ago, correct?”

At that point, Rouge joined the conversation.

“Yes. Her mother was also my close friend.”

“Hmm. Around that time, my brother was in a rough period. I believe it was due to the death of our other brother, Vermilion.”

“What is that information? That is the first I have heard of it.”

It is a bit late, but I had not been actively gathering information about Scarlet from Rouge.

So Scarlet had another sibling.

“Did I not say it? If you did not ask, I might not have mentioned it.”

“…It is Rouge, so I guess it cannot be helped. Continue.”

My evaluation of Rouge dropped slightly.

“S-should I have said it…?”

“We will know after hearing the story. If it is important information, punishment.”

“Hii…”

Ah, a little leaked out.

“F-fine. The two brothers, Scarlet and Vermilion, were twins who called each other Let and Leon. Scarlet was the genius type, Vermilion the hard-working type, and they competed and improved together.”

“‘They say’? What do you mean?”

“It is something I heard. By the time I was aware of things, the two rarely competed anymore. Scarlet had pulled far ahead of Vermilion. It seems Scarlet was almost decided as the next emperor.”

Come to think of it, there is a considerable age gap between Rouge and Scarlet.

She is closer in age to Scarlet’s daughter, if anything.

“Although Vermilion was a hard worker, he did not seem to have much talent. It was like he was trying to fill the gap from a negative start through effort.”

“Does that mean he could not obtain skill points?”

“In hindsight, that is probably the case. Vermilion likely had a constitution that could not gain skill points. In a way, he might be similar to Lord Jin.”

He would not be a complete zero like me, but there are people in the world who are disadvantaged and have difficulty gaining skill points.

“…Right. Talking about it reminded me of something. That was shortly before Vermilion died. Scarlet said, ‘I can lift Leon’s curse’. I did not ask for details, but shortly after that, Vermilion died.”

That is quite interesting. A curse?

“What was the cause of death?”

“Sorry. I did not hear that much. It seems it was announced as death by illness to the outside…”

“There is no less reliable information than a royal death by illness.”

When royals are in trouble, they tend to conveniently ‘die of illness’, right?

“That is true. There is something we can infer, at least.”

“Let us hear it.”

“The day after I heard my brother had died, part of the castle was badly damaged. Now I understand. That was the aftermath of a battle.”

“So he fought something and was killed?”

There is also a non-zero chance that Scarlet and Vermilion fought.

“After that, Scarlet was unruly for a while. I heard he went around hunting monsters.”

“That timing…”

Tsukiyo murmured with her eyes downcast.

“Yes, probably. And then, about ten years ago, my brother returned in tatters. Even I was shocked when I greeted him. After that, he calmed down, and a little later, he became emperor.”

Rouge looked at me as if asking.

“What do you think? Will I be punished?”

She seemed very concerned about punishment.

“No. I think it was good to hear, but it is not a story that changes anything, so there will be no punishment.”

“Haaaaa… Thank goodness…”

She let out a deep sigh of relief from the bottom of her heart.

“May I ask one thing?”

Maria raised her hand.

“What is it? It is rare for you to speak up in a setting like this, Maria.”

When I am talking, Maria usually listens quietly.

“Yes, there is something that concerns me. …Rouge-san’s brother, Vermilion-san, might he have possessed the \<Hero> skill?”

“…So his lack of talent was because of \<Seal>.”

“This is only speculation…”

When Maria said that and I organized the information, many things made sense if he had the \<Hero> skill.

Due to \<Seal>, he could not gain skill points, but aside from that, he had excellent qualities. Scarlet’s word ‘curse’ fits perfectly.

“It is possible.”

“Wait a moment. Vermilion-san was human, right?”

“Yes, human.”

Rouge answered Mio’s question.

“The ‘Human Hero’ is Cynthia-chan. Cynthia-chan is eleven years old. When did Vermilion-san die?”

“It was twelve years ago, I believe.”

“Do \<Hero> skills transfer to another person of the same race when the holder dies!?”

The \<Hero> skill turned out to have a parasitic attribute.

“At least call it inheritance!”

**AN:** The Crimson Empire arc is not a lie, but I never said we would depart in this chapter.

Next time, we start at the border right away.

## **172: On the Road and Arrival at the First City**

**AN:** We start from around the point where we entered the Crimson Empire.

For the most part, the Crimson Empire will be the stage until nearly the end.

---

After a journey in Advance Trading Company’s ultra-luxury carriage (the horses are our own), we finally arrived at the Crimson Empire.

“It brings back memories. Has it really been over three years since I left the Crimson Empire?”

“It will be almost four years soon. Lady Rouge has changed quite a bit as well.”

“I hope it has been for the better.”

Our companions include eight people from the Crimson Empire, counting Rouge and Minerva.

There are two carriages. The main party, along with Rouge and Minerva, rides in the higher-grade one, while the remaining six ride in the other carriage. That one is a rank lower.

There was no way I felt like steadily driving a carriage all the way from the Kingdom of Estea.

So instead, we chose a route that starts from the royal capital of the Kingdom of Narunka in the Atto Confederation (already fully under control), the closest point to the Crimson Empire, and heads east for one day before entering the Empire.

If I had really wanted to, I could have entered the Empire from an even closer location, but…

“In terms of distance, it is close. Master was stubborn about not going that way, though.”

“And the maids of Advance Trading Company are also instructed not to enter the Crimson Empire, right?”

My map \<Clairvoyance> currently shows the present area and the three adjacent areas.

If they got too close to the Crimson Empire, it could end up being spoilers, so I have instructed the Advance Trading Company maids not to approach the eastern part of the Kingdom of Narunka too closely.

“There is no way they would do anything that would rob Jin-sama of his enjoyment. …To be honest, for the sake of avoiding danger, I would like to thoroughly confirm Jin-sama’s destination.”

Apparently, Maria and the maids are always torn between wanting to ensure my safety and wanting to protect my enjoyment.

“In exchange, we will protect Jin-sama with everything we have.”

And that is where the final conclusion always lands.

Maria tends to be a bit overbearing because she wants to keep me away from danger.

…I appreciate the sentiment, I really do, but sometimes it is a bit of a hassle. Yeah…

“I brought the Great Spirit and the Progenitor Divine Dragon with me, and Tamo-san is attached as my guard too. If that is still not enough, then it is a lost cause anyway.”

You cannot tell by looking, but right now I am in a state of complete defense.

I can enter ‘Spiritization’ with Rain at any time, and if something happens, El and Tamo-san will automatically defend me.

L: I’ll do my best!

I cannot see her and she is not saying anything, but I can feel Rain is full of motivation too.

《Protect》

Come to think of it, Tamo-san has gotten quite fluent lately.

《I worked hard》

Yeah, the responses are fluent too.

Did you absorb all kinds of things? You did not absorb any people, right?

A: It did not.

Then all good.

“Technically, the ones being guarded are supposed to be us…”

As Rouge says, we are accompanying them as guards while Rouge and the others make a temporary return home.

The guards are more heavily defended than the people being guarded.

“It cannot be helped. Ever since I fought a calamity dragon alone, everyone has been more overprotective than usual.”

“Thank you for accepting our wishes.”

Personally, I do not think it is necessary to protect me to this extent.

However, because I took the risk of fighting the calamity dragon alone not long ago, Maria and the maids have become more sensitive than ever.

I obediently accepted Maria and the maids’ pleas. I mean, if more than a hundred people kneel and beg you, there is no way you can refuse.

Seeing all those maids lined up kneeling in the grand hall of the Sky Castle was something else.

“Even I do not think of myself as more important than Jin-sama. I understand that.”

“You are still royalty, Lady Rouge, at least technically.”

“Minerva, what do you mean by ‘at least technically’?”

Rouge is apparently royalty. Technically.

“Perhaps because you rarely leave the capital, the border soldiers did not recognize you.”

“Do not say that…”

Rouge slumps.

In fact, when we crossed the border between the Kingdom of Narunka and the Crimson Empire, Rouge showed her face to the soldiers.

She thought things would go smoothly if a member of the imperial family showed up. However, the soldiers tilted their heads and produced a ‘?’ expression.

Rouge cursed them as ‘country bumpkins,’ but Minerva looked like she had expected this, so it was probably natural that they did not recognize her.

“Well, they did send a courier, so it should be fine.”

In the end, Rouge showed her identification and the soldiers realized she was royalty, which changed their attitude.

Since this is a sudden return home, they asked the soldiers to send word ahead to Scarlet.

“Still, was it really okay to tell my brother that we are returning? Jin-sama’s presence will be conveyed to him as well.”

“That is fine. This time, I am not Gene.”

If I were acting as Queen’s Knight Gene, that would be one thing, but right now I am just Shindo Jin.

I am not hiding my identity, and there is no particular reason to move in secret.

“Originally, part of the reason I hid my identity and restricted flashy actions was because I had no foothold to operate from in this world.”

“Eh? Master, you were restricting yourself with that?”

“You hid your identity, but it did not look like you were restricting your actions.”

Mio and Sera look shocked.

That kind of opinion exists too, I see.

“Now that I have a somewhat stable foothold and the situation has changed quite a bit, it might be fine to stand out a little more. Or rather, to gain fame…”

“A foothold? More like you are stepping on multiple countries by putting them under your control. It is basically the same thing, though…”

Nice way of putting it, Mio.

But since I am only putting royalty under my control and not forcing anything on the countries themselves, it is safe (mysterious logic).

“Countries whose top leaders are under you, countries you economically control, countries whose foundations you control, countries under the control of countries you control. …Quite the selection.”

As an aside, my map treats locations where my subordinates are present as ‘current location’.

In other words, I can check information for lands where my maids are stationed as if they were my current location. And the maids are dispatched all over the world.

Before long, more than half the countries end up being under my control.

“I cannot make the whole ‘under my control’ thing public, but after I stand out for other reasons, I might even reveal that I am Gene. Of course, a lame reveal is not allowed.”

If my personal name becomes known and I gain fame, then revealing that Gene and Jin were actually the same person would not be so bad.

“…The moment the name ‘Jin’ starts spreading, people will probably suspect a connection with ‘Gene,’ you know?”

“Mio! Why!?”

“Because the names are similar.”

“Ah!?”

A fatal mistake!

It is fine if I say it myself, but being deduced and exposed is lame, so that is not allowed.

But just by Jin becoming famous, people will suspect a connection with the already-famous Gene. Why? Because the names are similar!

…I should have picked a more elaborate alias.

“Shindo Jin’s major debut project might be frozen… If the relationship between Jin and Gene became clear, I could ride my beloved dragon openly without worrying about anything, though…”

This time as well, my dragon mount, the Sky Dragon, is staying behind.

When acting as ‘Jin’, I cannot ride Blue, who is ‘Gene’s’ dragon.

Being exposed because the mount is the same would be lame. It is like being found out to be the same person because the voice actor is the same.

“Blue-chan looked lonely…”

《A little pitiful》

Sakura and Dora, who were watching Blue, say so.

“I rode her around before departure, so her mood should have improved.”

Of course, I followed up.

I flew around the Sky Castle where there were no onlookers. Around and around. Around and around…

“That is good to hear…”

《Master is so sweet to Blue》

Since Dora looks a bit jealous, I put her on my lap and pet her.

《Ehehe》

Dora’s mood improves.

Cheering her up is easier than cheering up Blue.

“Now that I think about it, this does not look like a guard at all.”

“Now you notice, Lady Rouge.”

A boy who is almost unarmed, petting a little girl on his lap.

Does he look like a guard? No, he does not.

After that, we spent some time traveling through the Crimson Empire by carriage.

“Still, there are no monsters at all.”

“Now that you mention it… I only see a few on the map…”

Picking up my muttering, Sakura also checks the map, but it seems she only found a few.

Seeking the reason, I look at Rouge.

“Indeed. In the Crimson Empire, the Imperial army periodically conducts monster extermination. Compared to surrounding countries, the damage caused by monsters is clearly lower.”

“The army exterminates monsters? What about adventurers?”

“There is no Adventurers’ Guild in this country. By the policy set by the first emperor, relying on unstable forces is not considered good. It is said he believed that maintaining national security should be done by those belonging to the state.”

Rouge answers my question confidently.

“That is surprising.”

“Right? I take pride in it being a policy without parallel.”

“No, that too, but I am surprised that you can actually explain things about your own country, Rouge.”

I did not expect such a proper answer.

I was sure the right to answer would be handed over to Minerva.

“Wait! How do you see me, Jin-sama!?”

“An airhead. You could not even use polite speech properly at first, right?”

“Ugh!”

Right after she became my subordinate, Rouge could barely use polite speech.

Now I allow her not to use it, but apparently she can use it if needed.

“Master’s evaluation of Rouge-san is harsh.”

“I want to defend her, but there are parts I cannot deny.”

Minerva agrees with Mio.

“I-I have still received sufficient education as royalty!”

“Really?”

Instead of asking Rouge, I confirm with Minerva.

“Yes. Lady Rouge is not unintelligent. In fact, I have heard she was an excellent student when it came to geography and history.”

“Oh…”

“Could you not look at me like you are seeing something completely unexpected?”

No, it really is unexpected.

My first impression set the bar low. Cannot be helped.

“Then what about common sense?”

When I ask, Minerva silently shakes her head.

“Lady Rouge basically never leaves the castle. All her studies and training are done inside the castle.”

“I cannot deny that, but when it comes to domestic affairs, I am confident.”

Apparently, Rouge was a shut-in at the imperial capital castle.

She says she is confident in knowledge that can be understood through documents.

“The Crimson Empire seems to have a lot of clueless noble ladies, does it not?”

“…Ah, Jin-sama has also met my niece… Strawberry, after all.”

Rouge’s niece, Strawberry, also lacked common sense.

“It is fairly well-known that many princesses of the Crimson Empire are single-focus types who lack common sense. It is standard for their attendants to handle common sense for them.”

“That is a pretty wild country.”

In other words, they have given up on teaching them common sense…

“There is a niece who is so absorbed in research that she barely leaves her room, and another who loved monsters, but since there are no monsters in the country, she ran away because of it. A few people followed the latter, though.”

The Scarlet family has a lot of amusing princesses.

“Even aside from the princesses, the Crimson Empire has many unique characteristics. There is even a theory that a certain Hero was involved in its founding.”

“Another Hero, huh… In this world, it feels like whenever something happens, a Hero is involved.”

“Rather than that, maybe the influence of Heroes is just too strong. Or it lingers too much…”

As Mio says, rather than ‘a Hero was involved’, it might be more accurate to say ‘the Hero’s influence is strong and keeps lingering’.

“I have experienced it several times, but there is this atmosphere of ‘what the Hero says is correct’.”

I think it is wrong to expect ‘correctness’ from just a high school student…

“That is the basic way of thinking of the Goddess Faith. For the record, our country bans the worship of the Goddess.”

“Even though a Hero was involved in the founding?”

A Hero rejecting a Goddess? Is that possible?

Ah, there were the former Heroes of the Kingdom of Sanokia, and Orihara as well. There seem to be exceptions.

“The reason for that is unclear, but ever since the first emperor, the basic policy of this country has been ‘self-reliance’. It does not consider over-reliance on anything good. Food self-sufficiency is at 100 percent, and it does not rely on uncertain forces like adventurers. This country can live on its own.”

In many ways, I think the Crimson Empire is a ‘solid’ country.

I do not feel the ‘fragility’ that I have often felt since coming to this world. That applies to both systems and human resources.

Speaking of human resources, even the border soldiers were as strong as elite soldiers from other countries.

“What you say sounds admirable, but that admirable content does not apply to you, does it? In the labyrinth, you brute-forced things relying on items, and it was a forced march with seven attendants…”

“”…..””

Rouge and Minerva avert their eyes.

“Come to think of it, Strawberry only had one maid attending her, right?”

It should have been a two-person journey, just the princess and her maid.

“I do not think that maid alone equals seven Minervas. If the number increases according to how inadequate the master is, then…”

“Enough… Please stop… I have turned over a new leaf now…”

Rouge gives up.

I might have teased her a bit too much, but the old Rouge really was terrible.

That said, as she herself says, Rouge has become quite decent lately.

This too is thanks to Alta’s training. Rouge is now a loyal female dog. …Decent?

A: Shall I train her to perform tricks like one of the former Heroes, Igarashi?

No, I am not hoping for that.

The ‘female dog’ thing is just a metaphor. I have no intention of putting Rouge in the pet category.

“We will arrive at the first city soon.”

Prompted by Rouge, I check the map, and it seems we will reach the first city in about ten minutes.

It is just about the time when the sun will start to set. I am glad we can arrive before nightfall.

“Please explain the first city.”

“Hmm, let us see. Being a city near the border, there are quite a few people from other countries.”

“That is normal, right?”

When Mio asks, Rouge nods and continues.

“That is true, but in our country, there is another aspect. In the Crimson Empire, rankings exist even among commoners, and the closer you get to the center… the imperial capital, the higher the rank. It is difficult for those of lower rank to enter higher-ranked cities, and the same goes for foreigners. In other words, people from other countries cannot approach the center, so they stay in the outer cities.”

“…Other countries are just way too lax about letting people in and out.”

I have always thought the security of the countries in this world was an issue.

“With just an adventurer’s qualification, you can easily enter even the capital.”

“Our country does not give adventurers special treatment, so they cannot approach the center just because of a high rank.”

“Since you do not receive the benefits of the Adventurers’ Guild, there is no reason to give them preferential treatment. That makes sense.”

Sera nods in agreement with Minerva’s explanation.

“To put it simply, this is the city with the most spies from other countries. If you stand out here, information will spread to other countries. …Though those other countries might be under Jin-sama’s control.”

What percentage?

A: About ten percent.

“So about ten percent seem to be from countries under my control.”

“The map can even tell that…”

“At first, it could not.”

By using \<Expanded Interpretation> with \<Clairvoyance>, I can now obtain more detailed information than before, so I can tell which country someone belongs to at a glance.

However, since it is not particularly important information, I usually do not display it.

“This is kind of irrelevant, but apparently, countries under Master’s control do not engage in information warfare against each other. Through Master’s residence, they can obtain as much national information as they want anyway, and being under Master means they are closer than a flimsy alliance.”

“That is impressive in its own way…”

Mio’s irrelevant supplement.

“Since we are acting together with Rouge, it is impossible not to stand out domestically, so let us not worry about it too much.”

“She is royalty, after all. Of course she stands out.”

“At least technically…”

Rouge takes damage from Mio’s casual remark.

As a policy, ‘having fun’ > > > ‘not standing out.’

It would be a waste if we could not enjoy sightseeing because we were too conscious of not standing out.

Even if we do stand out, there is a lightning rod, so I personally will not stand out.

And with that, we arrive at the first city.

The city’s name is ‘Tokiwa City’. …Where is the red!?

Given that the country name includes a color, it would not be strange for city names to include colors too.

But I did not expect a color completely unrelated to the country name.

Being close to the border, it is fairly large.

It is a city of tens of thousands, protected by solid walls.

Just because it is a lower-ranked city does not mean it is not prosperous.

Humans make up a relatively large portion of the residents, but there are also beastkin, half-elves, and other races.

At a glance, there does not seem to be much discrimination based on race.

Our carriage heads toward the VIP gate.

There is a gate for ordinary people some distance away, but the construction is clearly different.

“T-this certificate is!?”

I hear a voice while Minerva is dealing with the soldiers outside the carriage.

Why is Minerva doing something so template-like…?

Then, guided by soldiers who are excessively polite, we enter Tokiwa City.

We leave the carriage at the VIP depot near the gate, and finally get out ourselves.

“Alright, time for sightseeing.”

“Of course, I will accompany Jin-sama.”

“Master and Maria-chan really never waver.”

“That is because he is Jin-kun…”

《Because he is!》

“At this point, I am used to it. That aside, I hope the food is good.”

《Looking forward to it!》

“You never waver either. Well, I am also interested in the Crimson Empire’s cuisine.”

In a way, Mio is as usual too.

The main party is completely in sightseeing mode.

“We will go greet the city lord, so we will split up here.”

“We will take our leave. Please enjoy your sightseeing.”

Rouge, Minerva, and their six attendants are apparently going to greet the city lord.

Since they used the VIP certificate, they cannot just skip the greeting.

I often forget, but Rouge is an important person.

“Yeah, I will.”

We part ways with Rouge and the others, and head out sightseeing ourselves.

“For now, food.”

《Fooood!》

“I have been waiting for this!”

Since no one here knows the city, and we have no hints, I ask Alta for recommendations. I am counting on you, Alta.

A: Leave it to me. I will extract all dining establishments in this city from the map and display five recommended shops selected based on 15 criteria, including cuisine tendency, number of customers, safety, and cleanliness.

Yep, as always, Alta’s work is perfect.

I nod in satisfaction while looking at the Alta-recommended shops displayed on the map.

“This city, or rather the Crimson Empire’s main cuisine, looks like Chinese food.”

“Yeah. Now that you mention it, we have not seen much of it so far.”

The Crimson Empire’s culinary tendency is ‘Chinese food’.

To be precise, there are many things that call themselves ‘Chinese food commonly seen in Japan’. I do not know what people from the mainland would think.

“This gets my blood pumping. Mio-chan avoided strong flavors for health reasons in the previous world, so she hardly ate… or made Chinese food, and only knows general recipes. This is a good opportunity, so I will properly learn them.”

“I leave it to you.”

《Do your best!》

It is easy to forget in this world, but Mio was originally sickly.

Even after becoming reasonably healthy, she probably refrained from strongly flavored dishes for the sake of her body.

“Now that I think about it, Rouge wore a china dress before.”

That was at a tea party gathering royal women, where she wore a dress similar to a china dress, saying it was traditional attire of the Crimson Empire.

“Was that a Hero?”

“Yeah, a Hero.”

“Thought so.”

Apparently, a Hero passed it down long ago, but if they had a say in ‘clothing’, there is no way they did not have a say in ‘food’. I do not know if it was the same person, but the Crimson Empire clearly has a Chinese taste.

By the way, for ‘housing’, the buildings are mostly general Western-style ones.

“I thought this before, but it is Chinese-style at best, and the one who passed it down feels Japanese.”

“Somehow… it does not have the authentic atmosphere…”

“I have never been to the mainland, but I understand what Master and Sakura-sama are saying.”

Sakura and Mio seem to have similar impressions.

“…Why do they specifically summon Heroes from Japan, I wonder?”

Most of the summoned Heroes so far are probably Japanese.

There are almost no traces that look like they were left by foreigners.

Besides, the common language of this world is Japanese…

“There might be some reason.”

I have no idea who to ask about that reason, though.

If I could ask the Goddess, I would like to.

“Alright, let us stop thinking about things we cannot do anything about right now, and get back to dinner. Mio, pick one shop from Alta’s recommendations.”

“Okaaay.”

Alta’s choice, then Mio’s choice.

A shop chosen that way has never been a miss. Impossible.

So we enter a Chinese restaurant. Since it is relatively high-end, it does not seem to be full.

It reminds me of a Chinatown I have visited before.

“Welcome-al, ne.”

That is a line from a female server wearing a simple china dress.

“Seriously…”

It feels even more like a knockoff now.

Even though it is supposed to be a high-end Chinese-style restaurant…

It is definitely the Hero’s fault. And one hundred percent Japanese.

It is fine. The server’s speech will not make the food taste bad.

I steel my heart.

For now, we order all the dishes that catch our interest, in large platters.

Thankfully, money is not an issue, and since Sera and Dora are here, there is no worry about leftovers.

It is not particularly praiseworthy, but in the worst case, there is also \<Infinite Storage>.

“Yeah, this is good.”

Munching on fried rice that Maria served onto a small plate, I mutter.

The shumai that Maria also divided onto a small plate is delicious as well.

As expected from a shop chosen by Alta and Mio, the food is naturally good.

We also ordered shumai, spring rolls, and gyoza in large platters, so everyone can eat at least one of each. If we like something, we take more, and if it is not enough, we order more.

“Another large platter of fried rice, please!”

《Extra large!》

“Coming right up-al (what is that kid saying?)”

The special ankake fried rice in particular is delicious, and this is already the second refill.

Most of it goes into Sera and Dora’s stomachs, though…

“I am already full…”

“I think Mio-chan has tried everything too, so I am good.”

The light eaters, Sakura and Mio, are having almond tofu for dessert.

It is a Japanese-style Chinese restaurant through and through.

“Maria, are you eating properly?”

“Yes, I am eating whenever I can.”

Maria has been busy serving my portions onto small plates.

…I did not ask her to do that.

And when the fourth refill of fried rice is finished…

“I am satisfied!”

《Full! Dessert goes in a separate stomach!》

Satisfied, Sera and Dora are also eating almond tofu.

“I might have eaten a bit too much.”

It was delicious, and it has been a while since I had Chinese food, so I might have overdone it a bit.

“Mio-chan ate a bit too much too. But now I have grasped most of the recipes.”

“Then can we eat it at the residence too?”

“Yes, at the very least, I can recreate it.”

“Alright. Good job, Mio.”

We enjoyed the long-awaited cuisine, and Mio’s repertoire increases.

Heroes getting carried away is nothing new, and while there are some issues, we end up benefiting overall, so I cannot complain too much.

## **173: Haniwa and Proof of Strength**

After eating, we wandered around ‘Tokiwa Town’ to work off the meal.

Tokiwa Town has a strong Chinese flavor, but not everything is that way.

The buildings are Western-style, and clothing other than cheongsams is basically no different from other countries.

The fact that only cheongsams have spread probably comes down to the Hero’s personal taste.

…I am not saying that is bad. I am definitely not saying it is bad.

“There really aren’t many places you would call tourist attractions.”

“They probably do not rely on tourism revenue. It may not suit Jin-sama’s tastes, but…”

When I muttered with slight disappointment, Maria tried to guess the reason.

They said their principle was ‘self-reliance’, so that seems likely.

“Well, it is best to enjoy it for what it is.”

“Master, you are surprisingly positive about tourism.”

“Since we are visiting as tourists, I want to respect the local customs and characteristics as much as possible.”

I am not going to complain just because there are no tourist attractions. Probably.

“That said, there are exceptions. For example, things that impose unreasonable disadvantages.”

《Dora’s hometown?》

“Yeah.”

The ‘Dragonkin Sanctuary’ had a rule along the lines of ‘Kill all intruders’.

I have no intention of respecting rules that unreasonable.

In the end, since there were no notable sights, we decided to look around the stalls.

Because it is a town near the border, there are many people, and a great number of shops line the streets.

In the town square, many stalls are set up like a bazaar, with goods laid out directly on the ground.

There are also many food stalls.

“I will go buy food!”

《Dora too!》

“Eh, you are still eating? I get Sera-chan, but even Dora-chan?”

Surprised, Mio, who is also interested in food, followed Sera and Dora.

Do those two have bottomless stomachs?

Since I no longer had any appetite, the three of us left behind looked over the stalls.

“When there are a lot of people, you also get a lot of rare items.”

“Indeed… that is… a dogu…?”

Some people sell ordinary accessories, while others sell things that look like incomprehensible antiques.

What Sakura is looking at is dogu… no, that is a haniwa.

A large number of haniwa are lined up next to ordinary merchandise.

No, if you look closely, there is also dogu. Just one, but there is a goggle-eyed dogu.

Why are there haniwa in another world? A Hero? Wait, a Hero making haniwa?

I know there was a Hero who liked potatoes, but haniwa? That is quite a stretch?

It bothered me too much, so I went over to the haniwa vendor.

The shopkeeper was a middle-aged man you could find anywhere.

“Welcome.”

“Shopkeeper, what is this?”

I asked while pointing at a haniwa.

“Ah, that is the work of an artist from a farming village in the seventh layer. It does not sell at all, but I cannot just brush him off, so I am selling them on consignment.”

The seventh layer is the lowest level in this country’s class system. It refers to the towns and villages at the very outer edge of the country.

There are layers one through seven, with the first layer being the highest status and located at the center of the Crimson Empire.

“He goes around claiming he has memories of a previous life, and that he made these based on those memories. Well, nine times out of ten it is nonsense.”

Oh, so he is a reincarnator. I see.

…Even so, the reasoning that led him to making haniwa is still a mystery.

“Sounds interesting. I would like to meet the creator. Can you tell me where he is? Oh, and I will buy one of those.”

If he is a reincarnator, I would like to at least do a status check.

Even if I do not take him in as a subordinate, reincarnators are always good for conversation.

“You are a strange one… unfortunately, he was taken away by an upper-layer noble a little while ago.”

“Taken by a noble? What did he do?”

“No idea. But it happens sometimes in this country. Lower-layer residents get taken to the upper layers by nobles. Some come back, but they generally do not talk about what they were doing.”

So a reincarnator was taken to the upper layers.

What on earth is going on?

“I see. Thanks for the interesting story. Then sell me one.”

“Information fee? For a story like that, you do not have to buy anything.”

“No, I just wanted to buy one.”

“Seriously…? You really are a strange one. You are my first customer. He will be happy. If he comes back, that is.”

And so, I bought one haniwa.

“You really bought it…”

“Yeah. I am going to decorate my room with it.”

“Eh…?”

Sakura was left speechless.

L: It is just creepy. I do not like it.

I am not listening to the opinion of a freeloader.

I am decorating with it.

This is a completely unrelated story, but later, a mysterious group of women bought up all the haniwa.

Another completely unrelated story, but apparently haniwa are now displayed in the rooms of my maid subordinates.

Matching… is seems that’s what they are going for…

We left the haniwa stall and regrouped with Sera, Dora, and Mio.

“We bought a lot. Please eat as well.”

《Eat!》

Sera is holding a large amount of food. Even though it is stacked up, it is not collapsing.

Impressive sense of balance. One could also call it a useless skill.

“…Master, what is that?”

Mio shows interest in the haniwa.

“It is pottery. Is it tableware?”

《Cute!》

Dora’s sense of aesthetics worries me a bit.

Even I do not think it is cute.

“It is a haniwa. Apparently made by a provisional reincarnator.”

“Huh… there really are reincarnators who do strange things.”

“Mayo…”

“Guh… please stop bringing that up…”

Mio, the reincarnator who blew herself up trying to make a play with mayonnaise, groans.

Which is better, making haniwa or that?

“I will think about it.”

“Jin-kun, you never make a firm statement, do you…”

“Well.”

If I do not commit, I am free to do whatever later.

“Also, that provisional reincarnator was apparently taken to the upper layers, so his whereabouts are unknown.”

“…Come to think of it, the emperor of this country is also a reincarnator, right? Do you think there is some connection?”

The emperor of the Crimson Empire, Scarlet Crimson, is a reincarnator.

“It is possible, but with the information we have now, the accuracy would be too low to even speculate.”

“That is true. In that case, we can just ask him directly…”

“Yeah, that is the fastest way.”

“If you need an interrogation, leave it to me.”

This Hero is dangerous (as usual).

“You always say things so casually about questioning the top of a country.”

“That is Jin-kun for you…”

《That is him!》

After that, we wandered around the town for a while longer, and then decided to end the sightseeing.

We will stay one night in ‘Tokiwa Town’ and depart tomorrow morning.

Rouge and the others have already booked the inn.

It is the most luxurious inn in the town, built in the city center on prime land.

Since we are nominally acting as guards, we are staying at the same inn as Rouge and the others.

With a total of fourteen people, we split into three rooms of five, five, and four.

If we split up too much, it defeats the purpose of being guards.

“I am tired…”

As everyone gathered in the largest room, Rouge said this while looking completely exhausted.

“Did you really do anything that tiring? You just went to greet the lord, right?”

“That was the plan, but it seems the lord’s desire for advancement was stronger than expected…”

Let me explain the class structure of this country as I heard it from Minerva.

In addition to being classified as commoners or nobles, the residents of this country have seven ranks of status.

For commoners, the seven ranks correspond to the layer they are allowed to live in, and they cannot enter towns in layers above their own status. The same applies to foreigners.

Nobles can enter towns in all layers, but their authority weakens in towns above their own status.

This status can be raised through achievements and is passed on to children.

The town lord is a noble, and his status is generally several ranks higher than the status of the town he governs.

The lord of this town corresponds to the fourth layer. Seeking even more power, he apparently tried to cozy up to Rouge, a member of the imperial family at the very top. With everything he had…

“He seems capable as a lord, as my brother chose him, but he is a bit too persistent. Does he not understand that going too far can lower his evaluation instead?”

“Hm? What do you mean by Scarlet choosing him?”

More Scarlet information I did not know is coming out.

It is not like I interrogate them, so it cannot be helped…

“Another punishment might be coming…”

“No, it is not that important. Just tell me.”

“Yes…”

The previous declaration of “I will punish you if you forget something important related to Scarlet” is still in effect, so Rouge is trembling.

“Brother, Scarlet became emperor about eight years ago. At that time, there was a large-scale purge. Those who did not meet my brother’s standards were demoted to commoners at best, and executed if they had committed crimes.”

“Even great nobles who held power second only to the emperor were executed without mercy.”

According to Minerva’s supplement, it was truly a massive purge.

However, no one received punishment exceeding the severity of their crimes, and it was thoroughly fair.

“Most of the current lords, those whose territories have not changed hands, were all chosen by my brother. As far as I know, they are all capable. Ambition is another matter, of course.”

This town’s lord must have been particularly ambitious.

And it also became clear that all previous lords had been punished.

“To be honest, there are many incomprehensible points in Scarlet-sama’s rule. He purged corrupt nobles and greatly stabilized the country. On the other hand, he provokes skirmishes with neighboring countries and invites unnecessary trouble. I have no idea what he is thinking.”

Minerva tilts her head.

“Exactly. If only Brother Vermilion were here…”

Even his own sister cannot understand his true intentions. The absence of his greatest understanding ally is significant.

I do not think he is acting without thought, but I have no idea what he is thinking.

All that happened is that Scarlet became even more of a mystery.

“So in the end, there is no way to be certain without talking to Scarlet himself. He is quite secretive.”

“I do not think he is more secretive than Master. …He might be like Master. Not that he does not want to say it, but that he cannot.”

Even if he said it, no one would believe him.

Saying it would shatter the current common sense.

…That is possible.

Scarlet also seems to have knowledge about the final trial and the Heroes of this world…

“I am looking forward to meeting him more and more…”

“You already met him once.”

Mio makes an unrefined retort.

“That does not count. I was a Queen’s Knight then.”

Honestly, we barely even talked, so I hesitate to say we met.

“As always, you are thorough with your role-playing.”

I put my all into having fun.

After all, the mysterious knight Gene has become famous.

The next day, as we were about to depart by carriage, we had a visitor.

It was the lord of this town (as expected).

“Rouge-sama, our town’s soldiers will escort you to the imperial capital, so please refrain from using such unknown individuals as guards.”

Without much in the way of greetings, the lord (a slightly chubby man in his thirties) said this to Rouge.

Well, I understand what the lord is getting at.

To be honest, we do look suspicious for guards. High ratio of young girls, light equipment.

“Even if it is just one man, traveling together could lead to bad rumors. What do you plan to do then? We have gathered skilled female soldiers, so please remove that man and have them accompany you.”

What the lord says is reasonable.

Rouge is a woman of marriageable age, after all.

“Ignore the rumors. He is one of the people I trust most. Removing him is unthinkable.”

Rouge shoots back firmly.

It is less that she trusts me and more that she has no other choice.

After all, I hold the power over her life or death.

“Mm… If Rouge-sama insists that strongly, I will not say to remove him. But at least take the female soldiers with you. They are not as strong as Rouge-sama, but they can stand watch through the night and keep an eye on the surroundings.”

Ah, right, Rouge was introduced as a capable fighter.

I forgot because she leaves such an airhead impression…

“That will not be necessary. They are stronger than me. Anyone weaker than me would only be a hindrance.”

“What!? Stronger than Rouge-sama!? …Rouge-sama, forgive me, but has your perspective not narrowed somewhat? I cannot believe that a man with no intimidating presence whatsoever is stronger than Rouge-sama.”

Intimidating presence? Oh, I am deliberately suppressing that.

Rouge? Oh, I could kill her with just my little toe.

《Jin-sama, did you just think of something scary? I cannot stop sweating…》

Rouge’s telepathy.

《I was thinking a bit about how to kill you.》

《Hii!?》

《Just kidding. I was thinking about how big the gap in our strength is.》

《I-It is fine then…》

Even as she says that, I can see Rouge’s legs trembling.

“Rouge-sama. If you permit, may I measure that man’s strength? I wish to confirm whether he is a guard worthy of being entrusted with Rouge-sama.”

At the lord’s proposal, Rouge sends another telepathic message.

《Jin-sama, please forgive me! This was not intentional!》

《I will take the punishment! Please forgive Rouge-sama!》

Rouge and Minerva are panicking because this is a noble-related trouble involving me.

However, this is less trouble and more an event that was bound to happen.

《In this case, the lord’s argument is not wrong. What I hate are unreasonable noble demands. If it is not that, I have no intention of complaining.》

《《Phew…》》

Ever since I decided to act together with Rouge, this is not an unreasonable event I could not have foreseen.

Complaining about it would be unreasonable in itself.

“Can I accept that request?”

“Yeah. It is a hassle, so call as many soldiers as you like. I will take them all on at once.”

I declare this calmly and confidently to Rouge and the lord.

An appeal as a top-class adventurer!

“That is what he says. Call anyone you think can handle him.”

“I hope you do not regret such boastful words.”

The lord then gathered nineteen female soldiers.

Fighting in public did not seem appropriate, so we decided to fight in the courtyard of the lord’s residence.

“Is this enough? And they are all women…?”

“It is fine. These are the soldiers we were considering for Rouge-sama’s guard. If you can defeat all of them, then Rouge-sama’s words that anyone weaker would be a hindrance will be proven correct.”

“I see. That is logical.”

Rouge nods in agreement.

That is unexpected. …Honestly, I thought that if I provoked him like that, he might mobilize all his soldiers out of spite.

But that lord calmly focused on confirming what he needed to confirm.

Does that mean Scarlet’s judgment was correct?

He is more sensible than Rouge was when she first became my subordinate?

“Surrounding one person with many is not something I like, but since we are to entrust the princess to you, we cannot hold back. Our swords have blunted edges, but a solid hit will not end lightly.”

Says the female soldier who seems to be the leader.

“No need to worry. I have no intention of getting hurt or hurting anyone.”

“What? You will fight dressed like that? Where is your armor? Your weapon!?”

The leader (temporary) is surprised that I am unarmed and not wearing even light armor.

“Unnecessary.”

“…So you are serious. Very well. We will make you regret underestimating us.”

And then, at the lord’s signal, the match began.

“\<Fear>”

Do we need a detailed explanation of the match format?

It is already over.

“‘Area Purification’.”

This is its first public appearance.

It is ‘Area Purification’ from Daily-Life Magic LV3.

As the name suggests, it purifies the specified area all at once. The MP cost depends on the size of the specified area.

…Yes, that is the situation the female soldiers are in.

And so, we left ‘Tokiwa Town’ without incident.

The lord acknowledged my strength and said, “W-with this… I can rest assured entrusting Rouge-sama to you…” and when the female soldiers regained consciousness, they tearfully refused to accompany Rouge… or me.

Female soldiers, I think it is questionable for soldiers to tremble and collapse just because I approach them?

“Master, can I ask you one thing?”

“Sure.”

“Master, have you been using the ‘Heroic Spirit Blade Incomplete’ recently?”

“No.”

Mio’s question was something I would rather not have been asked.

“So you finally noticed. That I have barely used the ‘Heroic Spirit Blade Incomplete’ recently…”

“When you fight strong opponents, you fight barehanded, and it stands out, so you usually do not carry it where it can be seen, right? Not just that duel earlier. I thought I had not seen you use it lately…”

That is exactly right.

To be blunt, I am better at fighting barehanded than with a sword, so when it really counts, I choose bare hands.

The ‘Heroic Spirit Blade Incomplete’, which has grown in presence after reaching mythic class, is too conspicuous for everyday use. As a result, the opportunities to use it have drastically decreased.

I might even be using it less than the Queen’s Knight equipment, the Ultimate Holy Sword Ultimesia, made by the Saint Demon Blacksmith.

“I do use it when training in places without people around.”

“Yes, I sometimes spar with it during mythic-class training.”

“Indeed. I have seen it as well.”

In places where safety is secured, Maria and Sera also join in mock battles.

If you do not watch the training, you would never see me use it.

“Oh, so you do use it.”

“This is news to me…”

It is natural that Mio and Sakura, who do not watch my personal training, did not know.

《Dora knows!》

Dora sometimes comes to watch.

…Or rather, it might be more accurate to say she follows me around.

“However, I have not used it at all in actual combat. It is not strong enough against calamity dragons, and there are no just-right opponents, so there has been no timing to use it.”

“It is more surprising that you are not lacking in strength when fighting calamity dragons barehanded.”

That is old news.

“Alright, I have decided. I will use the ‘Heroic Spirit Blade Incomplete’ against the next monster we encounter. I just want the record that I have used it in real combat recently.”

“You decided that rather casually. No matter how you look at it, it is guaranteed overkill.”

《Master, there it is!》

As soon as she said it, a monster appeared relatively nearby.

Even though the imperial army is exterminating monsters, it is difficult to completely eradicate monsters that appear periodically.

Goblin

LV3

\<Physical Enhancement LV1> \<Staff Technique LV1>

Notes: Green imp. Among monsters, it is top-class weak.

“Eh? Of all times, a goblin!?”

“Normally speaking, it is not an opponent you would use a mythic-class weapon on.”

“How nostalgic…”

Come to think of it, the first monster I defeated in this world was also a goblin.

“I have come a long way.”

“Eh? Why are you getting all sentimental? Are you going to defeat it or not?”

“I am.”

I draw the ‘Heroic Spirit Blade Incomplete’ and leap toward the goblin.

“Gugya!?”

Ignoring the surprised goblin, I use \<Holding Back> and knock it into the air with the flat of the blade.

“Goge!”

I jump after the goblin, which flew nearly one hundred meters.

My leap is faster than the goblin’s flight, so I quickly overtake it.

Then, using the skill \<Sky Run> to run through the air, I change direction midair and face the goblin head-on.

“Haa!”

I swing the Heroic Spirit Blade Incomplete at the flying goblin.

“Gugyaaa…”

The death scream does not last long and vanishes along with the goblin’s evaporation.

Ah, the magic stone… I do not need it.

“I am back.”

After finishing the fight, I return to the carriage.

“That was overkill to a refreshing degree.”

“You even deliberately used \<Holding Back> on the first strike. It was clearly unnecessary.”

《Master amazing?》

Dora, you do not have to force yourself to praise me.

“Now the problem of not having used the ‘Heroic Spirit Blade Incomplete’ in real combat has been resolved.”

“Has it…?”

Mio tilts her head.

Just let it count.

“…I want to give it more opportunities to shine.”

“I think that is a good idea.”

Is there a convenient boss character somewhere?

“And I want to give Sera some opportunities to shine as well.”

“Me!?”

“Sera, you have not really fought lately either, right?”

Originally, I bought her as a slave to serve as combat power, but lately she has not done much beyond being a big eater.

Maria handles small fry, and I handle big ones.

“No, when I am not acting with Master, I fight various opponents.”

“Really?”

“Among this group, I am the one most active as an adventurer, and I have defeated monsters with rare skills. Like this, and this…”

“I did not know. You got these, Sera…”

I have a large number of rare skills, but more than half of them were gathered by my subordinates.

Occasionally, I enjoy looking over the rare skills that have increased without me noticing. If something looks interesting, I sometimes try using it.

“I thought you were eager for opportunities to shine in the beginning…”

When I first enslaved Sera, she was eagerly waiting for her chance to prove herself.

“That is in the past. Now our combat power has become excessive, so I have half given up on shining in front of Master. However, I do not neglect my training so that I can fight at any time.”

“Sorry about that.”

At this point, it seems difficult to give Sera a place to shine.

“That is it! If we have Sera fight using the ‘Heroic Spirit Blade Incomplete’, which also lacks opportunities to shine, would that not kill two birds with one stone?”

“Master, the ‘Heroic Spirit Blade Incomplete’ is equipment exclusive to you, you know? Its effects would be nullified.”

Right.

Having her fight with a weapon she does not normally use, with all its unique abilities nullified, would not really count as either of them shining…
