## **176: The Miasma Spirit and the Second-Layer City**

**AN:** At long last, I’ve finished writing Volume 12.

I’ll keep Volume 13 on the shorter side and build up a stockpile of chapters.

---

After finishing the Spirit Contract with the miasma spirit, we decided to clean up the abandoned mine.

The source of the miasma was gone, but the monsters that had spawned were still there.

It would be a bit too cruel if someone wandered in, thinking it was safe now, only to be killed by the monsters that remained.

According to Alta, there were no more events, so we unlocked the map and cleared things out efficiently.

Mio’s bow with its auto-tracking function was a huge help.

El’s \<Dragon Arts> also have auto-tracking, so they were useful too.

“I feel like I’m always stuck with roles like this…”

“Huh? But Mio-chan is perfectly satisfied, you know?”

And then there was one more person who was doing amazingly well: our newest addition, Eclipse.

“…!”

When Eclipse beckoned with her hand, the surrounding monsters staggered over toward her.

It seemed she could manipulate miasma and guide monsters that reacted to it to some extent.

“…(smile)”

And watching Eclipse with a gentle smile was Rain.

Seeing her little sister doing her best apparently warmed her heart.

“…(smile)”

By the way, Rain was just watching and not doing anything.

Me? I wasn’t doing anything either.

Well, if I were allowed to wipe out the entire mine, it would be easy, but…

“Please, I’m begging you to stop.”

Rouge stopped me.

With nothing else to do, I resigned myself to quietly watching.

We dashed through the abandoned mine at a brisk pace and wiped out all the monsters in a little over ten minutes.

Come to think of it, is there a full-clear bonus for this mine area?

A: There is none. Due to the emergence of Eclipse, the miasma within the area has already dissipated, so no bonus will occur.

No luck, huh.

In that case, we really don’t have any business left in the abandoned mine.

…Or maybe I’ll try one more thing.

“Would it be alright if I looked into Eclipse’s abilities a bit?”

“Do you think anyone here would say no to a decision made by Jin-sama?”

At Rouge’s words, everyone nodded.

Well then, I’ll take you up on that…

“Eclipse, could you produce some miasma?”

When I asked, Eclipse raised her hand on the spot.

Miasma welled up over her palm.

It was extremely dense miasma.

“Can you create monsters directly from this miasma?”

“…(shake shake)”

Eclipse shook her head.

As expected, it seems monsters won’t spawn unless the miasma density across the entire area is raised to a certain level.

“Can you raise the miasma density across the whole area?”

“…(nod). …?”

Eclipse asked, “Do you want me to raise it?”

“No, I don’t want you to raise it. I was just wondering whether, if you wanted to, you could freely cause monsters to spawn.”

Strictly speaking, they’re not exactly the same, but if she can manipulate miasma, then wouldn’t she also be able to manipulate monster generation?

According to Eclipse, she can interfere with monster spawning to some extent.

However, it’s a fairly forceful method, and there’s a high chance it would affect the environment.

As expected, forcibly twisting the laws of nature isn’t a good thing.

…Yeah, well, I can freely cause earthquakes, volcanic eruptions, and gusts of wind, and completely mess with the laws of nature.

Also, even if you can control the spawning of monsters, you can’t control the monsters themselves once they’ve spawned.

Once they exist, they become individuals unrelated to the miasma, so that’s only natural.

“Master, if you could control monster generation and even place the monsters you create under your dominion, wouldn’t that basically make you a Demon King?”

“The Demon King is the king of demons, not the king of monsters, you know?”

Mio, if you say things like that, the real Demon King might get mad, you know?

“In some works of fiction, the king of monsters is called the Demon King too, so it’s a trivial detail.”

“I suppose that’s true, but…”

“And for that matter, aren’t you already doing something like that in your labyrinth?”

“Well, that’s true too, but…”

A Labyrinth Ruler places all monsters that spawn within the labyrinth under their control, so calling them the king of monsters wouldn’t be wrong.

By that logic, am I already a Demon King?

“Mio-chan, you mustn’t lump Jin-sama together with something as trivial as a Demon King. Jin-sama is not merely the master of monsters. Rather, he governs all things… no, it’s nothing.”

“I, uh, wasn’t prepared for that kind of counterattack…”

Before the real Demon King, a believer had reacted.

She was definitely about to say, “the god who rules all things”, at the end there.

Wait a second. She’s a spirit who governs miasma, right…?

“What would happen if I performed ‘Spiritization’ with Eclipse? Can I even ‘Spiritize’ with her in the first place?”

A: You can. However, because you will absorb a large amount of miasma, your body will temporarily turn black. Once you cancel ‘Spiritization’, it will return to normal.

“Hm. So basically, ‘Dark Spiritization’. Miasma isn’t related to the dark attribute, though…”

It’s an easy mistake to make, but being a dark attribute and having stagnated magic like miasma are different things.

Miasma isn’t an attribute. It’s stagnant magic, or in other words, poison.

“Master can finally transform into a dark form!”

《Show me, show me!》

Dora, you can transform on your own, right?

Ah, you want to see my transformation…

If you say that, I can’t very well not transform.

“Please tell us the advantages and disadvantages of that ‘Spiritization’.”

Maria seemed more interested in performance than appearance.

More precisely, she was concerned about my safety.

A: Physical ability enhancement is about the same, and you gain flight capability. The advantage is that you can manipulate miasma. The disadvantage is that your magic power does not increase. The load is slightly greater than normal ‘Spiritization’, but it is within a range that does not affect Master.

So I’ll be able to handle miasma myself.

Since there doesn’t seem to be a problem, I’ll go ahead with ‘Dark Spiritization’. …Maybe ‘Miasma Spiritization’ sounds better?

“I see. That’s good to hear.”

From Maria’s perspective, it was within the safe range, so she didn’t try to stop me.

“Come, Eclipse!”

“(nod)”

And then, fusion.

My entire body turned black, and miasma flowed through me.

“That’s completely a dark-side skill.”

“If you’re not careful, you’d look like an enemy character…”

《So cool!》

“You look very strong.”

The reactions are pretty positive.

So how about Maria, who reveres me as something sacred?

“This is also… acceptable.”

Apparently, it’s fine.

Then Rain, who had been watching, asserted herself.

She hugged my head to her chest…

“…!”

“Huh? Rain wants to Spiritize too? More importantly, can you even do that!?”

A: Normally, it would not be possible. However, due to the combination of factors that both are spirits based on master’s magic, that Eclipse is not a normal spirit but a miasma spirit, and that Rain does not possess a specific attribute, it has become miraculously possible.

“Come, Rain!”

“(nod)”

And then, fusion.

My blackened body partially regained its original color and began to glow.

This is ‘Double Spiritization’!

Maybe I should come up with a cooler name?

-Gogogogogo-

“Something’s making the air tremble…”

“What an overwhelming presence.”

“The surrounding animals are fleeing…”

《Super cool!》

“Splendid.”

I can feel it myself, overflowing with energy.

It’s like releasing the power of the calamity dragon that I normally keep sealed away.

“At this moment, I feel like I could even turn this entire country into an eternally barren wasteland.”

“Master, why are you making remarks like an evil god just to check a new companion’s power?”

Mio asked, sounding a bit put off.

“I figured I should say something that fit the mood…”

I’d transformed into a form you’d normally only reach in the final battle, and in a situation that wasn’t even an event.

It felt wrong not to say a line worthy of a final form.

“Jin-sama, please, just stop. No, seriously, I’ll do anything.”

Rouge’s desperate plea came in.

No, obviously I’m joking.

Why would I destroy a country I came to visit as a tourist before even seeing the capital?

“Cancel!”

I cancel ‘Double Spiritization (tentative)’.

Rain and Eclipse reappeared.

“That’s more tiring than normal ‘Spiritization’.”

It seems the burden increases in proportion to the boost in abilities.

“Jin-sama, are you alright?”

“Yeah, I’m completely fine at this level. …Even I get tired despite having good compatibility with Rain and Eclipse, so there’s no way an ordinary person could handle it.”

I can see why Alta called it ‘miraculous’.

“For now, we’ve checked everything we wanted to check, so let’s get going.”

We exited the abandoned mine, summoned the carriage, and climbed aboard.

Then I suddenly remembered something and checked the map.

“Crap. I overdid it…”

Just like Sakura said earlier, animals had vanished from the surrounding area.

They must have fled after being startled by ‘Double Spiritization (tentative)’.

In no time at all, the second-layer city, ‘Shion City’, came into view.

Come to think of it, the name Ange had before was Shion. Not that it matters…

“There really won’t be any problems, right?”

“Yeah. Personality-wise, there were no issues, and my relationship with him was good.”

Rouge answered my question with confidence.

According to the map, one of the imperial family members, the Third Prince, was in Shion City.

I considered passing through the city to avoid trouble like with Carmine, but since Rouge said there wouldn’t be any problems, we decided to stop by.

Here is the Third Prince’s status.

Name: Ash Crimson

Gender: Male

Age: 15

Race: Half-elf

Title: Prince of the Crimson Empire

Skills:

Surprisingly, he’s a half-elf.

Even more surprising is that his name isn’t a red-based color.

And even more surprising than that is that he doesn’t have a single skill.

Being surprised by someone having many skills is one thing, but being surprised by having few is rare.

But when it hits zero, it becomes surprising in its own way. After all, if you live ten-plus years, you usually gain at least some skills.

“As far as I know, he should have been a fairly capable child…”

According to Rouge, four years ago he achieved excellent results in martial arts and academics.

However, among Scarlet’s children, he wasn’t particularly outstanding.

“Skills are just modifiers. They’re not absolutely necessary.”

“I’ve heard that before, but it still doesn’t quite sit right with me…”

Skills are a kind of modifier.

The easiest example is \<Cooking>.

You can cook without the skill. If you have the skill, you’re less likely to fail, and it adds a bonus to flavor.

But it’s not absolutely necessary to be adept at things.

“Also, can someone other than a human become emperor of the Crimson Empire? He’s a half-elf, right?”

“There’s no rule saying they can’t, but as far as I know, there’s no record of a non-human becoming emperor.”

If it’s not a rule but an unspoken understanding, that could get troublesome.

Breaking it, that is…

“This might not be related to your question, but although Ash is the Third Prince, his claim to the throne is quite low. His mother is unknown.”

“His mother would be… an elf, right?”

“No, that’s not what I mean…”

Apparently, Ash was a child Scarlet suddenly brought back one day.

Scarlet never spoke of who the mother was and simply forced the issue, saying he would be raised as a prince.

Most people assumed he was born to a mistress somewhere, but since Scarlet didn’t raise the children of his other mistresses as royals, there was considerable conflict over why only Ash was treated differently.

In the end, he was raised as royalty, but without backing from maternal relatives, his succession rights were lowered.

Still, it’s apparently not an insurmountable gap…

“Though honestly, among my brother’s children, there are fewer who seriously aim for succession. Most of them are of the mindset that whoever wants it can have it.”

Given that it’s the Crimson Empire, I imagined it would be a blood-soaked pit of power struggles, but it doesn’t seem to be like that.

“Ash is the leading figure of the moderate faction. …And Carmine is the leading figure of the radical faction.”

“I see.”

That faction division makes perfect sense.

“He sounds like an interesting person, but I don’t feel like going out of my way to approach him, so I’ll leave the response to Rouge.”

Even if he’s a moderate, I’m not going to proactively meet with royalty.

“Yeah. We’ll have to greet the local lord in this city anyway, so you’ll probably meet him then.”

And with that, we arrived at ‘Shion City’.

First, we headed to the inn and left the carriage there., Rouge and the others went to see the lord.

Those of us left behind relaxed at the inn.

“So basically, since it’s mostly nobles who come and go, there’s no such thing as anything other than a high-class inn?”

The inn we chose was a luxury inn frequented by nobles.

Only a limited number of people can enter second-layer cities, so there aren’t many inns, and almost all of them are high-end.

“Seems that way. Only upper-class people with clear backgrounds come to this city, so it makes sense.”

Mio replied (while munching) on rice crackers she’d brought with her.

“We’re able to enter as an exception because we’re accompanying Rouge-san as her escorts, but normally it’s quite difficult just to get in, isn’t it?”

《If you fly, it’s easy to get in, right?》

How many cities in this world could actually prevent Dora from infiltrating?

“N-no, that’s not what I meant. I meant through proper procedures.”

《Oh. That’s too bad.》

“Excluding brute force, there’s no way for foreigners to enter this city, right…”

It is impossible to for us to enter the second-tier city by any means other than accompanying the royal family.

As Sakura said, unless you use brute force.

And with the strength of this country’s soldiers, they can repel a certain amount of brute force.

“At this point, there are no foreign spies left at all.”

“The defense mechanisms seem to be functioning properly. Impressive.”

Mio admired the situation after hearing Maria’s explanation.

“It’s good for the country that there are no spies, but since there are no tourists either, the lack of sightseeing spots is a minus for me. Well, it can’t be helped…”

Yes, at this point, there’s finally no room left for tourism.

There are no novel attractions. It’s a city that relies solely on luxury, making it boring from a tourist’s perspective.

There’s still some potential when it comes to food, though…

“That’s why we’re lazing around in the room.”

“It’s nice to have days like this sometimes…”

《Relaxing.》

“It’s still a bit early for dinner. I’ll have some rice crackers to tide me over.”

“Jin-sama, would you like a refill of tea?”

“Ah, I’ll take some.”

So that’s why we’re spending our time relaxing at the inn until mealtime.

Mio’s homemade rice crackers are delicious. The tea is great too.

Just to be clear, it’s not a Japanese-style room or anything.

Relaxing, I sip my tea.

“Still, I never expected Scarlet to be absent…”

Actually, ‘Shion City’ is within three areas of the capital, the Imperial Capital.

That means I can check information about the capital via the map.

However, the key person, Scarlet Crimson, was not in the Imperial Capital.

I had Alta check the situation there, but no one knew where Scarlet had gone.

Eavesdropping on the ministers revealed that he would be absent for about a month. Even those involved only knew that much.

Moreover, Scarlet isn’t anywhere within the currently observable range, including the Imperial Capital.

“If we go now, we’ll be held up for two or three weeks at least. I really don’t want that…”

“For you, Master, this is… really rare. Truly rare timing.”

It’s rare for the person I’m looking for to be absent.

“For now, should we head to the Imperial Capital, then go look for Scarlet?”

“Wouldn’t it be better to wait rather than searching blindly?”

Sera said something reasonable, but I shook my head.

“I have the map, so searching blindly is faster.”

Since I can check in three-area units, if he’s not there, I can quickly move to another area. Finding someone is easy.

Normally, I don’t use that method because spoilers make sightseeing less fun, but…

“…That’s true. Your ‘blind searching’ is completely different in accuracy from a normal person’s.”

“Sera-chan, you still have common sense? You should throw that away.”

“I thought I had, but it seems some was still left.”

Isn’t that a bit rude?

Of course, I won’t deny it. I can’t.

At that moment, a message came from Alta.

A: Master, Rouge has received a request from Ash to meet you.

What?

A: During Rouge’s conversation with Ash, your name came up. Ash reacted strongly and asked Rouge to arrange a meeting. She hasn’t answered yet, but since Ash is making a sincere appeal, she wants you to consider it.

Hmm…

From what Alta heard, is this Ash guy decent?

A: Based on the information at present, he would fall under what Master considers “decent.”

I see. Just like Rouge said, he’s a decent guy.

Alright. Tell Rouge that if he comes to see us, I’ll allow the meeting.

A: Understood.

“So, we’re going to meet the Third Prince.”

“Is that alright? There’s a chance it could turn into one of those ‘noble troubles’ you dislike, Jin-sama…”

“There’s a chance, sure, but Alta says he’s decent, and if he’s coming to us, it’s not worth refusing outright.”

I understand Maria’s concern, but I did think he sounded a bit interesting to begin with.

Going to meet him myself is a no, but if he comes to me, that becomes a yes.

“By the way, how did the conversation even lead to him wanting to meet Master?”

Mio’s question was probably directed at Alta, not me.

A: The topic turned to Rouge’s return home, then to her companions. Master’s name wasn’t concealed, so when it was mentioned, Ash reacted to the name ‘Jin.’

“Ugh…”

“That reaction definitely sounds like what happens when someone connected to me gets involved…”

As far as I know, there are no famous people named ‘Jin’ in this world.

If he’d reacted to ‘Gene’, that’d be one thing, but reacting to ‘Jin’ makes it highly likely he’s directly connected to me.

And within the Crimson Empire, the only person who could plausibly have a connection to me is the reincarnated emperor, Scarlet Crimson. As for connections from before reincarnation, no one comes to mind at all.

Well, same as with Sharon. Trying to imagine someone’s pre-reincarnation connections with no hints is basically impossible.

Yeah, thinking about something that can’t be understood is just a waste of time.

So I decided to stop thinking about it. I’ll find out when we meet.

“By the way, do all of Master’s acquaintances reincarnate as royalty by default? If I’d known you in a previous life, maybe I wouldn’t have become a slave and could’ve lived a carefree royal life?”

“And then you’d make mayo and get executed for poisoning the royal family, right?”

Mio trembled with watery eyes.

Mio only ended up as a criminal slave because the person she gave mayo to was just a normal villager.

If it had been royalty, even if they were relatives, an attempted poisoning of the royal family might not have ended so lightly.

“T-that’s scary because it feels possible… Even if I’d been royalty, I definitely would’ve meddled with cooking…”

“I believe mayonnaise is safe in small amounts, but becomes poisonous if eaten in large quantities, correct?”

“Putting it bluntly, it would be an ideal poison for royalty.”

“Ah…”

Under the follow-up attacks from Sera and Maria, Mio collapsed.

Yeah, she probably would’ve messed up.

Oh, another message from Alta.

A: Master, would tomorrow morning be acceptable for the meeting with Ash?

Yeah, that’s fine.

Honestly, even right now would be fine, but…

A: Normally, Rouge cannot contact Master, so it would be safer to set a time slot that is absolutely problem-free.

That’s true.

Objectively speaking, Rouge is in a position where she was suddenly asked to arrange a meeting with her companion.

Without knowing my schedule, she couldn’t just say, “Can we come right now?”

Besides, it’s about time…

“It’s almost dinner time.”

《I’m getting hungry!》

Time passed, and it was about right to call it dinnertime.

It seems Rouge and the others will be eating elsewhere, and meeting after dinner doesn’t really appeal to me.

“Alright then, let’s go to a recommended restaurant.”

《Yay!》

“As we go up layers, the food gets gradually more refined, so there’s still something to look forward to. My research into Chinese cuisine will make progress.”

“Please do your best, Mio-san.”

There are no sightseeing spots, so I’m not keen on wandering around aimlessly, but food is a different matter.

Since we’re in a foreign city, we should eat as much of the local cuisine as possible.

Just like Mio said, it does feel like the level is gradually rising…

---

**AN:** Ash-kun is a decent guy (sudden spoiler).

Actually, now that I think about it, there don’t seem to be any decent men around Jin’s age appearing in the main story.

The Hero is just a punching bag, most slaves are women, and Claude, one of the few male slaves, is hard to call the same age.

+++

## **177: The Third Prince and Arrival at the Imperial Capital**

**AN:** As the title says, we arrive at the Imperial Capital. At last, the name of the Imperial Capital is revealed!

---

The next day, Rouge, who had stayed at the lord’s manor, came to the inn where I was staying, accompanied by Ash.

It seemed Ash had come alone, without any guards.

As usual, Rouge had seven attendants with her… no, one of them had returned to the inn to announce (or rather, pretend to announce) Ash’s visit, so there were six accompanying her.

As always, it felt like Rouge alone had an excessive number of attendants.

Apparently, Ash only wanted to speak with me, so I planned to ask everyone except Maria to wait in another room. Maria could not be helped. Rouge would also be present.

I had already told Rouge this, but I had no intention of being deferential to royalty in the Crimson Empire.

To begin with, this was the royal family of a country that was planning a war with Estea. I held almost no respect for them.

I did not dislike Scarlet as a person, but depending on the reason, I was fully prepared to oppose him.

– knock knock –

“It’s Rouge. May we come in?”

“Yeah. Come in.”

After the knock, I allowed Rouge and the others to enter.

“Excuse us.”

“Excuse me.”

When Maria opened the door, Ash entered the room after Rouge.

Despite calling himself Ash, the boy had red hair befitting royalty.

He had gentle features and seemed soft-spoken as well.

“Pleased to meet you. I am Ash Crimson, Third Prince of the Crimson Empire.”

A polite greeting, and unmistakable respect in his eyes.

“The pleasure is mine. My name is Jin. Welcome.”

I had no intention of being deferential, but I also did not plan to act arrogant right from the start.

Since it was clear the other party held respect, I had to return at least the minimum level of respect.

Simply put, Ash passed my internal evaluation.

We promptly sat down to talk.

Ash and I sat facing each other across the table, Rouge sat next to Ash, and Maria stood behind me, wearing her maid outfit and standing in the proper maid position.

“So, what business brings you here today?”

I had no intention of dancing around with indirect phrasing or probing each other.

“Yes… if you do not mind, may I first explain some background?”

“Of course. Go ahead.”

Ash made a preface, so I allowed it.

“You may or may not be aware, but at present, my father, Scarlet Crimson, is not in the Imperial Capital, Guren. At the very least, he will not return for another two weeks.”

As an aside, the name of the Crimson Empire’s capital is “Imperial Capital Guren.” It is also called simply “the Imperial Capital”, or “The City of Guren.” At last, a place name containing a word meaning red appeared.

Presumably, no city other than the capital is allowed to use a name containing “red”.

“…Is that something you can tell a foreigner like me?”

“Yes, it is fine.”

Just as I thought, it was going to be about Scarlet.

“Naturally, before leaving, my father made various preparations, so that the nation could continue functioning without issue during his absence.”

“If it was scheduled, that makes sense.”

Even Sakuya made all sorts of preparations before the summit.

She seemed to rely quite heavily on maid power, too…

“With that as the premise, one of those preparations involves you, Jin.”

Well, of course it does.

“My father gave the following instruction to the upper echelons of the Crimson Empire: ‘If someone calling himself Jin enters the Crimson Empire, entertain him in the Imperial Capital until I return.’”

“…”

Apparently, I was to be entertained.

“It is understandable that you would be bewildered. We were as well. He originally wanted to make it known throughout the entire country, but that would have made things too large-scale, so he changed it to: ‘If it comes to the ears of the upper echelons’.”

“…”

Apparently, I had nearly been entertained on a nationwide level.

“I would very much like you to stay in the Imperial Capital. What do you say? For the approximately two weeks until my father returns, all expenses will be covered by the Crimson Empire. We will also assign personnel to you.”

“…If you know the reason for that order, may I ask?”

“Unfortunately, my father did not explain that far. He only said, ‘If you do anything unnecessary, I will cut you down’.”

Is he a tyrant?

“My father does nothing without reason, and that look in his eyes was absolutely serious. Since the matter has reached the ears of the upper echelons under those circumstances, ignoring it is not an option.”

“…”

Now then, which was it…?

Like Sharon from the Regalia Beastman Kingdom, was this a friendly acquaintance from my previous life who wanted to meet me?

Or was it a hostile acquaintance from my previous life who wanted me dead?

Not to brag, but I had a fair number of enemies in my original world.

The probability felt about fifty-fifty, but either way, nothing would progress unless I met him.

For now, I would at least go.

“I will accept your offer and head to the Imperial Capital. However, I will cover my own expenses. I do not like to incur debts to others…”

If it were a friendly, give-and-take relationship, that would be one thing, but casually taking on debts toward someone who might be an enemy was not good for my mental health.

“I see… but would you at least accept the minimum level of hospitality? From our position, we cannot invite you and make a request of you, and then do nothing.”

“I understand. In that case, that is fine.”

Well, that much could not be helped.

Perhaps it could be considered compensation for the act of “waiting for Scarlet”.

“Thank you very much. When would you like to depart?”

“Rouge, do you have any remaining business in this city?”

I could not act based solely on my own schedule, so I asked Rouge.

“No, everything was finished yesterday. I have nothing in particular.”

“Got it. Once we finish some light preparations, we can depart immediately.”

I answered Ash again.

“No, there is no need to rush. I apologize, but I have obligations on my end, so departure will be tomorrow. If you were to leave immediately, I was considering writing a letter for you.”

“Wait. I am here. Do you think I would let him be inconvenienced?”

It seemed Rouge felt she was being told she was insufficient, and stopped Ash.

“Rouge-neesan, you have been away from the Imperial Capital for over three years, so you are out of touch with the current situation, right? Can you really invite Jin without issue? Besides, you have quite a few enemies, do you not?”

“Ugh…”

Given Rouge’s former personality, it was easy to imagine that not everyone around her was an ally.

“I think a letter would be better.”

“…Very well. Do as you wish.”

In the end, Rouge was the one who yielded.

Looking at it this way, her lack of influence was rather apparent.

“Here you are. With this, you should have no trouble in the Imperial Capital. It is effectively the same as having backing greater than most nobles.”

“What exactly is ‘minimum hospitality’ supposed to mean…?”

The influence of that letter was far greater than I had imagined…

Ash said “I apologize”, and continued.

“It is also necessary to protect you. We do not know what might incur my father’s wrath.”

“…I see. It clearly states, ‘If you lay a hand on him, be prepared to face the royal family.’ I hope I never have to use that backing.”

“Yes. Truly.”

That kind of situation would make no one happy.

Regardless of power or authority, I still found noble-related trouble unpleasant and unacceptable…

“Oh, and this is rather late to mention, but just because I am royalty, you do not need to use honorific language with me. You are my father’s guest, and to begin with, I am not fond of being spoken to that way.”

“If you dislike it, I will stop. But I am not using honorifics because you are royalty. I only use them for those I respect. As proof, I am not using them with Rouge, am I?”

“Rouge-neesan…”

“D-do not look at me like that! A lot happened!”

Rouge made a meaningless rebuttal as Ash looked at her with pity.

“Ahem. Then I will stop using honorifics.”

“Please do. …Though on my end, it is a habit, so I will continue speaking this way.”

Hey, if I stopped, you should stop too?

I thought that, but did not say it aloud.

And so, after finishing our meeting with Ash, we obtained a bit of authority and headed for ‘Imperial Capital Guren’.

I was getting tired of sightseeing in the Crimson Empire, and the Imperial Capital might offer something different, so we might as well head there quickly.

‘Imperial Capital Guren’ and the ‘City of Shion’ are within three map areas of each other, so by carriage, it is a distance of one to two hours.

Due to the centralized structure of the Crimson Empire, the closer one gets to the center, the shorter the distances between cities become, and there are also relay villages.

Near ‘Guren’, the only first-layer city, there are many second-layer cities.

In other words, the ‘City of Shion’ is also one of the cities near ‘Guren’.

And exactly one hour after we departed the City of Shion.

“Arrived at ‘Imperial Capital Guren’!”

Our carriage and horses are custom-made, so a distance that normally takes one to two hours can be comfortably covered in one hour.

As it happens, the Advance Trading Company also handles carriages.

Thinking about it, it is obvious. There is no way the maids who support my travels would not get involved with carriages, which could be called “travel equipment”. And once they get involved, there is no way they would compromise.

At present, I am using the Advance Trading Company’s highest-grade carriage (it looks plain).

In addition, the carriage horses are special as well.

They were the first horses I bought after coming to this world, and of course, I have raised their stats.

They could probably be hit by a thrown spear and not even suffer a scratch.

On top of that, even at high speed, the carriage hardly shakes, thanks to both the carriage’s mechanisms and the horses’ skill.

Well, if it did shake, I could just retreat into the ‘Room’…

“As expected, the outer walls are impressive. It really is a military nation.”

“Indeed. Among all the countries we have visited, it is the most impressive.”

As Mio and Sera said, the outer walls surrounding ‘Imperial Capital Guren’ were thick, tall, and on the largest scale we had seen so far. …If I punched them and broke them, would I get scolded?

There were eight gates in total: one in each of the cardinal directions, plus four in between. This time, we entered through the southwest gate.

In a typical capital, there would be lines to enter, but because the Crimson Empire has layer rules, only those recognized by the state can enter. As a result, there are no lines.

That said, security is extremely strict. There are nearly twenty soldiers at each gate, with at least one noble soldier stationed there at all times. It shows how much importance the Imperial Capital places on its walls and gates.

“Identification confirmed. Princess Rouge, please proceed.”

The gate soldiers were all high level (at least over 30), and even when dealing with royalty, they did not waver, fawn, or slack in their duties. High marks.

As companions, we followed behind, but the way the soldiers appraised us left an impression. Suspicious individuals!

The Imperial Capital has extremely wide, well-maintained roads, with separate carriage roads and pedestrian walkways.

The carriage roads are separated by direction of travel to prevent collisions. Yep, left-side traffic.

“Japanese?”

“Probably Japanese…”

“Definitely Japanese.”

The otherworlders unanimously agreed it was the work of Japanese people.

While there was a non-zero chance Scarlet himself was an otherworlder, it was hard to believe such large-scale construction was completed after he became emperor.

In other words, old Japanese people. Most of them were probably heroes.

Incidentally, even heroes cannot visit the Imperial Capital without an appointment these days.

The gate guards would not let them in.

“So then, Jin-sama, where do you plan to stay? I will likely return to my own room in the Imperial Castle. According to Ash, it seems you could also stay in the Imperial Castle.”

“I really do not want that… If there is an inn reasonably close to the Imperial Castle, that would be ideal…”

A: There is.

“I will leave it to Alta.”

《Leave it to Alta!》

When in trouble, use Alta Selection. Some say it is a form of decadence.

For the record, we are not heading to the inn immediately. First, we will be paying a visit to the Imperial Castle.

In other cities, Rouge alone was sufficient, but this time, I am being dragged along as well.

…What a pain.

“Master, your face clearly says you find going to the castle annoying.”

Mio seems able to read my expressions.

“Such a pain…”

“You said it out loud.”

Maybe I should not have accepted Ash’s request after all.

No matter how I think about it, I cannot imagine a future where this ends without trouble.

Dealing with Scarlet is one thing, but there is no need to get involved with other nobles and have unpleasant experiences.

But since I promised Ash, I cannot back out now.

I am Shindo Jin, a man who keeps his promises.

“If any trouble happens, I will stand in front, so you can rest easy.”

Rouge said confidently.

“No, I will kick them aside. You handle the cleanup.”

“Please do not do that!”

Kicking them aside would be faster, though?

“…Seriously speaking, since my brother has issued a clear directive, I think few nobles will do anything foolish. In this country, the emperor’s word carries that much weight.”

“The leadership, sure. But there is always a chance some idiot who does not know the situation will do something, right?”

There are always idiots whose actions are unpredictable.

“That cannot be said to be zero. But once you enter the castle, someone will likely be assigned to prevent such idiots. Normally, the fact that I am beside you should be enough to deter them, but…”

“You were out of the country for four years, and your recognition was low to begin with, so you are not much of a breakwater…”

“Ugh… yes, that is true…”

Rouge, you are less reliable than expected for a local.

Would waiting for Ash have been the correct choice?

Conclusion: it was mostly fine.

When we went to the Imperial Castle, we were promptly greeted by an elderly man who looked important (in status, not attitude).

Since word had already been sent from the ‘City of Shion’, preparations were likely complete.

As expected, the Imperial Castle had the atmosphere of a Chinese-style palace.

I lack the vocabulary to describe it well, but unlike Western castles, it does not have great height, instead spreading horizontally. Seen in silhouette, it resembles a trapezoid.

And of course, it is red. China also has a strong association with red, so it fits.

“Pierre, it has been a while. Have you been well?”

“Yes. It is good to see you well, Lady Rouge. And I am surprised to see you accompanied by the rumored Jin-dono.”

The elderly man seemed to be on relatively good terms with Rouge.

His map marker was green as well, so he did not seem to be a problematic individual.

Incidentally, the fact that he knew about Jin confirmed he was part of the leadership.

“Indeed. He has helped me greatly. I also asked him to escort me to the Imperial Capital.”

“Oh! For Lady Rouge to ask for escort, he must be quite formidable.”

That is why it feels strange that Rouge is viewed as the formidable one.

“Yes. At the very least, he is certainly stronger than I am.”

“That much, huh… If His Majesty Scarlet knew that, he might even challenge him to a duel.”

“Since Vermilion-brother passed away, he has been starving for battles against strong opponents.”

“Indeed… We truly lost a remarkable man.”

Pierre wore an expression of regret.

“Now then, Jin-dono, I would like to take some of your time.”

“Understood.”

Pierre consciously ended the conversation and guided me to a reception room in the Imperial Castle.

We sat facing each other on luxurious-looking sofas.

“I believe you have already heard from Prince Ash, but allow me to explain the situation once more.”

And so, Pierre repeated what he had heard from Ash.

After that, he moved to the main point.

“It was written in Prince Ash’s letter, but is it true that you do not wish for hospitality, Jin-dono? It said, ‘Only to the extent that it does not lower noble dignity’.”

“Yes. I do not feel comfortable receiving hospitality without knowing the reason, so I would like to decline it. At the very least, I have no intention of accepting financial preferential treatment.”

Money is the clearest form of debt, after all.

“Understood. Then, preferential treatment in terms of rights, such as the backing Prince Ash wrote about, would be acceptable?”

“Depending on the degree, but I do not intend to refuse it entirely.”

If I am invited and given some rights, it is easier to offset what I receive.

“Pierre, may I say one thing?”

“Of course, Lady Rouge.”

“He enjoys sightseeing. Rights related to moving around the city would be a good choice.”

There, Rouge provided an unexpectedly good assist.

“I see. In that case, granting passage rights seems appropriate. If hospitality cannot be used to occupy his time, letting him occupy it with sightseeing is reasonable.”

“Even if our Imperial Capital does not focus on tourism, it is not as if there is nothing to see, correct?”

“Yes. We have theaters and museums, but nothing that would particularly appeal to martial types. We cannot allow passage into military facilities, after all.”

“I am not interested in military facilities. Theaters and museums are preferable.”

And so, I obtained the right to sightsee in the Crimson Empire’s Imperial Capital.

Military facilities? Those are completely exposed the moment they enter the map.

Oh, so they are focusing on anti-dragon equipment now.

The discussion continued.

“So, you will be staying at a hotel near the Imperial Castle. Invitations to meals… you would like us to refrain as much as possible. Understood. Meetings with other royals… we will also refrain. Only Prince Ash is acceptable, correct? May we inform the hotel of some of the circumstances? Thank you.”

After that, we continued discussing necessary matters in a businesslike manner.

As expected, Pierre is competent. His character is also fine, making him worthy of polite speech.

With everything covered, we concluded for the day.

We were told it was fine to go sightseeing immediately.

All right!

It was about lunchtime, so we needed to decide where to eat first.

Since this was her home turf, it would have been nice to ask Rouge for recommendations, but she had various duties to attend to in the Imperial Castle, so we parted ways for the time being.

Pierre escorted us to the Imperial Castle’s main gate and our carriage.

With Pierre accompanying us, the likelihood of unpredictable idiots getting involved was low.

However, besides ‘idiots’ there are two other types of unpredictable beings.

Those are ‘elderly’ and…

“Take this!”

…’children’.

A red-haired girl around ten years old, wearing a dress and holding a dagger, leapt at us.

Of course, I knew she was there.

“Ah!”

Even I panicked.

The girl’s legs were unexpectedly fast, and she was about to enter Maria’s kill zone.

《Maria, I will handle this.》

《Understood.》

Even if she is a child, once a blade is drawn, it is no joke.

If I did not declare it beforehand, Maria would show no mercy.

I activated the composite skill \<Fear> on the girl for just an instant, but strongly.

As a result, her consciousness was cleanly cut off.

She then performed a head-first slide.

I gracefully dodged.

“Who is this?”

I grabbed the limp girl’s collar and turned toward Pierre.

I knew from her status, but I had to ask.

“That would be the Seventh Imperial Princess, Ruby…”

“Is it normal in this country for an imperial princess to attack the emperor’s guest?”

Pierre held his head and looked up at the sky.

“It is not normal… I am deeply sorry. And thank you for restraining Princess Ruby without injuring her.”

Thanks to the head-first slide, her dress and skin are pretty scraped up, though.

“If you know the reason for this violent act, may I ask?”

This should be something I am allowed to ask.

I am involved, after all.

“This will be speculation. Is that acceptable?”

“Yes, that is fine.”

I can ask her directly for the truth later.

“The objective was likely to prove her martial prowess. Princess Ruby is close with First Princess Carmine and Second Princess Strawberry, and she wishes to become a martial princess like them.”

Indeed, both are martial princesses.

“She has sufficient aptitude, and recently, her training has begun to show signs of talent. However, due to her age, she has been told it is still too early for real combat. Princess Ruby was dissatisfied with that.”

That much made sense.

“She likely heard of Jin-dono somewhere, and thought that defeating you would earn her recognition. …She probably heard that you are a powerful individual.”

“And that resulted in that ambush. She could have been killed by a counterattack.”

Utterly careless! Utterly reckless!

“Yes, exactly. That is why we are grateful that you restrained her without injuring her.”

“If she had been a bit stronger, I might not have been able to hold back.”

Because she was weak, I could stop Maria. If she had been somewhat stronger, it is entirely possible Maria would have cut her down before I could intervene.

“I am sorry to say this, Jin-dono, but this was a case of good fortune. A blessing in disguise, one might say… What were Princess Ruby’s attendants doing…”

“Found her! Princess Ruby!”

Before Pierre could finish, people who seemed to be searching for Ruby appeared.

“L-Lady Ruby…”

Five men and women gathered.

One of them, a maid, turned pale upon seeing Ruby in my arms.

“Lord Pierre, what is the meaning of this situation…?”

“Princess Ruby attacked Jin-dono, the emperor’s guest, with a dagger. Immediately afterward, she was overcome by Jin-dono’s killing intent and lost consciousness.”

“When I thought she had vanished, to think she would do such a thing…!”

A man carrying a sword, likely a guard, clutched his head.

It seemed Ruby had shaken off her attendants and come here alone.

“Your failure to keep track of Princess Ruby is also your fault.”

“We understand that. But to think she would defy His Majesty’s command…”

“Yes. That is the biggest problem.”

Pierre and the five attendants all wore grim expressions.

Apparently, disobeying the ‘Emperor’s Command’ was a bigger issue than attacking me.

One of the attendants turned toward me.

“You are Jin-dono, correct? I know this is an impertinent request, but could you possibly treat Princess Ruby’s attack as if it never happened? We cannot formally apologize if we do that, but we will provide compensation.”

It seemed this was genuinely a dangerous matter if it was not made to “not have happened.”

“I cannot do that.”

“W-why not!?”

I refused the offer.

“There are two reasons. First, without knowing the circumstances, I cannot accept being asked to pretend the attack never happened.”

“C-circumstances…”

Apparently, it was very difficult to say.

Even so, I could not accept pretending it never happened without hearing them.

“Second, even if a formal apology cannot be made, an apology itself is still necessary. And it must come from the person herself, not from those around her.”

“T-that is…”

I presented Ruby, still in my grip.

No matter how much those around her argued, I could not forgive it unless the person herself apologized.

“…Sigh. Jin-dono’s position is the correct one.”

At that point, Pierre spoke in an admonishing tone.

“But, Lord Pierre!”

“However, the fact remains that it must be treated as if it never happened. We have no choice but to proceed as Jin-dono wishes.”

“T-then…”

“That is the best course.”

“…Yes.”

The attendant slumped their shoulders in resignation.

“Jin-dono, I apologize, but could you come to the reception room again? This is not a matter I wish to discuss in public. Of course, Princess Ruby will also apologize.”

“Understood.”

Led by Pierre, who had persuaded the attendants, we headed back to the reception room once more.

## **178: The Imperial Family’s Circumstances and a Request**

**AN:** The future predictions for Ruby-chan in the comments section are way too cruel.

---

After returning to the reception room, we listened to an explanation from Mr. Pierre and Ruby’s attendants.

“The reason we wish for the earlier attack to be treated as if it never happened is because, if things continue as they are, there is a very high possibility that Her Highness Ruby will be executed by His Majesty Scarlet.”

Mr. Pierre suddenly began with an extremely ominous statement.

“This time, regarding how to deal with Jin-dono, His Majesty Scarlet said, ‘If she does anything unnecessary, cut her down’. This means that the maximum punishment for disobeying an order is execution. And Her Highness Ruby has very clearly done something ‘unnecessary enough to be cut down’.”

“Even if she is an imperial princess, it is natural for her to be punished if she disobeyed the emperor’s orders. But execution as punishment for his own young daughter… isn’t that a bit extreme?”

He did not seem like a tyrant so bloodthirsty…

“Certainly, under normal circumstances, it would not go as far as execution. However, in the past, His Majesty the Emperor executed his own wives, his consorts, on charges of treason.”

Oh, this ominous talk is starting to get downright bloody.

“This is something many people in the imperial capital know, but it is an unspoken agreement not to spread it outside the capital. About ten years ago, His Majesty the Emperor executed nearly all of his consorts, including the then First Consort. The charge was treason. To explain it in a bit more detail, it was attempted poisoning of a member of the imperial family.”

Again, ten years ago. Just what happened back then?

“The truth is known only to His Majesty the Emperor and the executed consorts themselves, so I do not know any further details. As it was determined that the children bore no guilt, only the consorts were executed. However, His Majesty’s anger at the time was intense, and he accepted no pleas for clemency whatsoever regarding the consorts.”

“In other words, even if they are blood relatives, there is a high possibility that he will not compromise when it comes to punishment?”

Mr. Pierre nodded with a bitter expression.

“That is correct. …The consort who was Her Highness Ruby’s mother was also executed at that time. Leaving behind Her Highness Ruby, who had just been born… Considering that, we cannot estimate the probability of Her Highness Ruby being executed as low.”

I see.

Ruby-chan’s life is literally hanging by a thread.

“In order to save Her Highness Ruby’s life, we humbly ask that Jin-dono please treat the earlier incident as if it never happened. We beg you.”

“We beg you.” x4

Mr. Pierre and Ruby’s attendants bowed their heads.

One attendant is currently in another room caring for Ruby.

“For now, I understand the situation. There is still one more condition that has not been met, so I cannot make a definitive promise, but I am satisfied.”

“That alone is more than enough. Thank you very much.”

Until Ruby apologizes herself, I will not say that I forgive her or that it never happened. However, I was at least able to meet the first condition, which was ‘being satisfied’.

I also learned about Scarlet’s hidden past, so I am glad I heard this.

“However, as I said earlier, I will not forgive her without an apology from Ruby herself, so please understand.”

“…I understand it is a selfish request, but could you at least refer to her with ‘Her Highness’?”

One of the attendants voiced a complaint because I had referred to Ruby without honorifics.

“Sorry, but I cannot do that. I will not compromise beyond the respect I have decided on myself.”

The reason I use polite speech with Mr. Pierre but not with Ruby’s attendants is the same.

The moment they failed to admonish Ruby and instead tried to silence things without explanation, they fell outside the scope of my respect.

For the record, I will act appropriately while playing a role.

Right now, I am default Shindo Jin.

“…Hmph.”

He shows his dissatisfaction openly, but since he is the one asking for a favor, he seems unable to push the matter further.

Yes, Ruby’s fate is in my hands. Hah hah hah. (Evil grin.)

“Is that all for now?”

Ignoring Ruby’s attendant, I ask Mr. Pierre.

“…Yes. It seems Her Highness Ruby has not yet regained consciousness, so would it be acceptable if the apology came later? Until then, we also ask that you do not speak of this to anyone.”

“Yes. As long as it does not become a matter of me explicitly not forgiving her, I will not speak of it.”

Conversely, that means if I do not forgive her, I will speak of it.

“Thank you.”

And with that, we concluded our discussion and left the imperial castle once more.

“Jin-san, we meet again. It seems your business at the castle has concluded.”

However, we ran into Ash along the way.

Just how long will it take before I can finally leave this place?

I am starting to get hungry…

《Food…》

As you can see, Dora also looks a bit dissatisfied.

《Hold out a little longer.》

《Okay.》

Since I am making Dora endure, I cannot take too much time.

“It looks like you are back as well, Ash-san. We are planning to do some sightseeing in the imperial capital now.”

“I see. It is not particularly well-suited for sightseeing, but please do enjoy yourselves.”

We parted surprisingly easily.

Surely we will not meet anyone else now.

Since we probably will not meet anyone, it is fine not to look at the map, right?

A: …..

“Hey, you are Rouge’s bodyguard! What are you doing in the imperial castle!?”

Contrary to my expectations, the one who appeared was the First Imperial Princess, Carmine.

It seems she had returned from the Withered Leaf City.

This is really starting to get troublesome…

“My name is Jin, that’s why.”

“Y-you are!?”

I did not introduce myself when I met Carmine before, so of course she would not know.

I do not know what would have changed if she had known, but…

“Pierre, is this true?”

“Yes, Princess Carmine. It seems his name is Jin. Whether or not he is truly the one His Majesty awaits is unknown, but we are acting on that assumption.”

“…”

After confirming with Mr. Pierre, Carmine looked down as if thinking for a while.

If you have no business, I am in a hurry, so I am leaving now?

“Y-you, no, Jin. Do you have time right now?”

As I started to walk away, Carmine looked up and asked.

“I do not. I am about to eat lunch in the imperial capital.”

“Then I will treat you to lunch. So please, listen to what I have to say.”

There was none of the barbed tone she had when speaking with Rouge. She asked quite normally.

This sudden change is a bit interesting. I suppose I will hear her out.

“I do not intend to be treated. I will listen, so introduce me to a good restaurant.”

“Is that fine? Understood. Leave it to me.”

And so, for some reason, we ended up being led by Carmine to eat lunch.

After being seen off by Mr. Pierre and leaving the imperial castle, we entered a building located a short distance away under Carmine’s guidance.

There was no signboard out front, and at a glance, it did not look like a place to eat.

“This is a completely referral-only restaurant. They say the food is better than at the castle, but the prices are no joke either. What will you do? Stop? Or let me treat you?”

Carmine asks in a slightly provocative manner.

She would prefer to treat me if possible.

No matter what kind of discussion it is, being the one who treats puts you in a psychologically advantageous position, making it easier to talk.

“No, I am fine.”

According to Alta, I have ‘leeway’.

She says the prices are low enough that I would get change back even if I paid with a ‘Limb Restoration Medicine’.

I heard that thing fetched a ridiculous price at auction, though?

Is that really an appropriate comparison?

“Is that so? If you come up short, feel free to say so at any time.”

At a glance, I probably do not look like I have much money.

Setting that aside, I do not often go to places like this, so I am a little excited.

Was this place on Alta’s list of recommendations?

A: No. It was not. At present, establishments that require power beyond our subordinates are filtered out in advance. If Master desires, I will accommodate this in the future.

Ah, it is not that I am dissatisfied.

If anything, being able to enter places like this due to unexpected events has a stronger element of chance, which I enjoy…

There was a front desk like a hotel. After Carmine checked in, we were guided to a private room.

“It is completely private and soundproofed, which makes it perfect for upper-class people to have confidential discussions. Of course, the food is also delicious.”

Carmine explained after we entered the room.

We decided to order the course that Carmine recommended.

Carmine herself did not order anything, as she had already eaten lunch.

“Then, while we wait for the food, may I tell you my story?”

“Sure.”

She guided us here, so listening as promised is no problem.

“I do not know what kind of position you are in, or what kind of relationship you have with my father. So I will probably tell you things you already know, and things you do not.”

Carmine prefaced her story that way before continuing.

“But there is one thing I want you to keep in mind. I am aiming to become the next emperor. Everything I say from here on is based on that premise.”

“Understood.”

It seems the premise is that Carmine is aiming to become emperor.

“Within this country, it would not be an exaggeration to say that I am in the position closest to becoming the next emperor. I am confident that my ability and achievements put me ahead of the other candidates. Are you aware of this?”

“Sorry, but I am not. I am not a resident of this country.”

This is not mere boasting.

“That is fine. Then you probably do not know this either, but are you aware that my father intends to step down from the throne in a few years?”

“That is news to me. Is that something any citizen of this country would normally know?”

“No. I believe it is something he has only told the imperial princes and princesses who have succession rights. Well, Ruby is still young, so she probably has not been told.”

That is top-class national secret information.

Is it really okay to casually tell me something like that?

“…May I ask the reason?”

“Yes. Apparently, there are things he wants to do that he cannot do while holding the position of emperor. He also said that he has finished what he needed to do as emperor. …It seems he did not intend to explain the details.”

As I thought, Scarlet seems to be acting with some clear objective in mind.

For that purpose, does he consider even the position of emperor unnecessary?

If that is true, what happens to the plan to attack the Kingdom of Estea?

“That is why I am working to accumulate as many achievements as possible within the next few years, to become the next emperor.”

And then Carmine let out a sigh.

“And yet, Rouge returning at this timing is nothing short of a nightmare.”

“Did something happen with Rouge?”

“…There was one thing I said earlier that was false, or rather, inaccurate.”

She did not answer my question, instead gazing off into the distance.

“Within this country, I may be the closest to becoming the next emperor. But including outside the country, the one closest is Rouge. At least, that is what I believe.”

“Rouge? Even though she has been away from the country for over three years and does not have much domestic support?”

That would be a baffling personnel decision.

Even I would hesitate to make Rouge the emperor if Scarlet were to be removed?

“Yes. Do you know the factor that ignores all logic like ability and achievements?”

I do know.

“Emotion.”

“Correct. Rouge is my father’s favorite. So much so that if Rouge were in the country, he might say he would entrust the next emperor’s role to her…”

Something feels off.

From everything I have heard about Rouge so far, was there anything that indicated Scarlet favored her?

“I have never heard anything like that from Rouge?”

“He never expressed it openly. But I can tell. The atmosphere when my father interacts with us is clearly different from when he interacts with Rouge… Of course, Rouge herself has probably not noticed.”

She would not have noticed. It is Rouge, after all.

“That is exactly why I hate Rouge! Rouge, who is loved by our father yet does not even realize it! Rouge, who has something I can never obtain no matter how much I want it, right from the start!”

Carmine raises her voice.

I see. That is the reason Carmine dislikes Rouge.

From Rouge’s perspective, she would have no idea why she is being treated as an enemy.

“…I am sorry for raising my voice.”

Carmine seems ashamed of having gotten emotional.

“No, that is fine. However, what I find puzzling after hearing all this is why you told us this in the first place. This must be where the real point begins, right?”

“Yes, exactly. Everything up until now was my general situation. The real point starts now.”

She had us listen to her side first, then moved on to what she wanted to know.

My first impression of her was not great, but is Carmine actually quite capable?

She said she was getting to the main point, but the food arrived, so priorities changed.

“Sorry. I do not think it is appropriate to have a serious discussion while eating, so wait until I finish.”

I do not want to have a serious discussion while eating, and it is bad manners.

Of course, food takes priority over Carmine’s story, so this is now mealtime.

“I understand. It does feel like my momentum was cut a bit, but we came here to eat in the first place, so I will not complain.”

So, unfortunately for Carmine, she had to wait until we finished eating.

《Delicious!》

“Hmm, not bad.”

“Yes, it seems it truly deserves its reputation as having the highest level of skill in this country.”

It is still categorized as Chinese cuisine, but the flavors are clearly more refined.

According to Carmine, it is top-tier cuisine even within the imperial capital.

I took a peek discreetly. The head chef of this restaurant had a Cooking skill level of 7.

It is no wonder Mio and Sera approve.

“I am glad you enjoyed it. If you want a letter of introduction, I will give you one. Rouge cannot introduce you to this place, after all.”

Her rivalry with Rouge runs deep.

“I do not need it right now. If I ever want it, I will ask then.”

It is delicious, but I do not plan to come here often enough to become a regular.

It is just a travel memory, after all.

And then, mealtime ended.

Apparently, you can stay for a while even after finishing your meal here.

The high price likely includes a seating fee of sorts.

“Then, shall we continue our conversation?”

“Sure.”

I listen to Carmine while resting after the meal.

For me, it is nothing new, but this is hardly the way one should treat an imperial princess.

“I said earlier that I want to become emperor, but that does not mean I want to push my father aside. I respect and admire him. If he wishes to continue as emperor, that is fine. But if he steps down, I want to be his successor.”

Her rivalry with Rouge is likely the flip side of her love for her father.

“My father does not tell anyone what is truly important to him. He probably will not tell Rouge either. So no one knows where his true intentions lie. And I want to know.”

The ‘clear objective’ of Scarlet that I have vaguely sensed.

Carmine wants to know it.

“I do not think it is a coincidence that Rouge returned at this timing, and that you, Jin, whom my father ordered us to detain even if we had to entertain you, came to this country. I believe your existence is close to my father’s true intentions.”

As far as intentions go, I think the timing is just coincidence.

“If you have information that brings you closer to my father’s true intentions, I want you to tell me.”

I want to know that myself.

“Of course, I am not asking for free. I am prepared to pay for information. The reason Rouge returned to this country, my father’s destination when he leaves, the reason he is stepping down as emperor, whether he truly intends to make Rouge emperor, and what he wants to do after that. I will pay one million per item of information on these topics. The price may change, but even fragmentary information is fine, and I will pay a fair price for any other information as well. What do you say?”

In other words, Carmine’s goal is to have me, someone who seems likely to know something, sell her information.

“Even if you say that, I hardly know anything. I have never even met His Majesty the Emperor.”

At least, not in the official record.

Officially, I have nothing to do with the Queen’s Knights.

Also, the only thing I really know is why Rouge returned.

If I said, ‘Depending on the situation, I may remove Scarlet’, what kind of face would Carmine make? It is a bit tempting, but obviously I cannot say that.

“…Well, I did not expect to learn my father’s true intentions right here. This is not a one-time conversation, you know.”

Even Carmine did not seem to expect information to start flowing immediately.

“You will likely have an audience with my father when he returns. If you hear anything like what we are discussing now at that time, I want you to tell me. Even if it is something you cannot tell anyone else, there is a possibility he will tell you, whom he wishes to meet… This is my greatest request.”

I see. This is laying the groundwork for the future.

Ah, that is why Carmine wanted to talk as soon as she learned my name was Jin.

It was something better asked sooner rather than later.

“My ideal scenario is that I become emperor while fulfilling my father’s wishes. The next best is that someone else becomes emperor while fulfilling his wishes. It is unfortunate, but acceptable if Rouge becomes emperor and fulfills my father’s wishes. In any case, what matters most is that my father’s wishes are fulfilled.”

It seems Carmine’s primary goal is for Scarlet’s wishes to be fulfilled.

Very filial.

“But is it really okay? What you told me could also reach Rouge.”

Even though she says the first is ideal, telling me increases the third possibility.

“I do not mind. The information reaching Rouge increases the chance of her becoming emperor. That is certainly disadvantageous for me. But on the other hand, it increases the overall chance of my father’s wishes being fulfilled. That is more important to me.”

She continues.

“If Rouge becomes emperor, I will leave this country, though.”

She apparently does not want to serve under Rouge.

“I accept that information may reach Rouge. And you do not have to say you will accept. So if you ever feel like it, please tell me as well.”

She does not force me in any way, conveys what she wants to say, and chooses the path that increases the chance of achieving her greatest goal, even if only slightly.

And she even says it does not have to be her who accomplishes it.

…I do not dislike that attitude.

For now, the Rouge Emperor Plan can be considered effectively nullified.

My first impression was not great, but after hearing her out, Carmine’s nature is quite upright.

At this point, Ash and Carmine have both passed my internal approval line. Ruby, on the other hand, fails by a wide margin.

Rather than placing an unreliable Rouge on the throne, I think it would be better to have a fundamentally upright prince or princess become emperor.

The only merit of making Rouge emperor would be creating a puppet emperor.

“Understood. I do not plan to promise anything definitively right now, but I understand your story.”

“Is that so? Then it was worth having you listen.”

My impression of her really changed from the first meeting.

If Carmine becomes the next emperor, it might be better for Rouge not to approach the Crimson Empire. It would be dangerous in many ways.

After finishing our conversation with Carmine, we paid and left the restaurant.

Hmm, it is quite expensive, but not so much that I cannot afford it.

“Then, I will return to the castle. If you ever need to talk, feel free to come see me. At least until my father returns, I plan to stay in the imperial capital.”

“Alright.”

“I look forward to working with you in various ways.”

With that, Carmine headed back toward the castle.

After parting with Carmine, we set out to sightsee the Imperial Capital of Crimson.

Our first destination for sightseeing was the museum.

Since it was the first stop, we chose a place everyone could enjoy.

Next would probably be free exploration.

Perhaps because it is an important facility, it was not far from the imperial castle.

In this country, important things tend to be placed closer to the center.

The museum was a wide, two-story building.

It was not as large as the imperial castle, but it would be quite difficult to see everything in a single day.

Well, there is no need to see it all in one day. We can skim it today and come back during free time.

There are apparently several conditions normally required to enter the museum, but we were able to enter easily just by showing the letter of recommendation from Mr. Pierre.

The main exhibits are ‘History’, ‘Art’, and ‘Folklore.’

We started with the ‘History’ section.

The founding of the country seems to have been about 700 years ago.

There is a story that a Hero was involved, but the Hero’s name does not appear.

The name of the first emperor was Scarlet Crimson. It seems there are limits even to red-themed names, so they appear to loop on a certain cycle.

The second emperor was Vermilion, and the third was a woman named Rouge… In other words, Scarlet’s siblings stole the names of the first through third emperors.

The national treasure passed down since the founding is the ‘Royal Sword: Divine Bestowal’. According to one theory, it is a treasured sword given directly by the goddess.

Ah, there is a sword on display that looks familiar. Naturally, it is a replica, but it is a sword of decent quality.

…The details are different, but it is clearly related to the ‘Royal Sword: Divine Curse’ that Scarlet had, right?

A: It was enhanced by clearing the final trial. Whether it was cleared by Scarlet is unknown.

…What has to happen for ‘Divine Bestowal’ to become ‘Divine Curse’?

Well, it is not hard to imagine something like ‘cursing the gods’ happened…

From there, history progressed smoothly.

Just as Rouge said, ‘self-dependence’ has been a policy since the founding, and glimpses of that can be seen here and there in the nation’s governance.

As evidence of that, though I am not sure it counts, the country has never once been a summoning nation for Heroes.

However, it seems they have supported Heroes before. That must be considered a separate matter.

Also, when the neighboring Atto Confederation was still in its warring states era before becoming a confederation, this country participated in wars and opportunistically expanded its territory.

Old maps and relatively new maps are displayed side by side. Oh wow, they took quite a lot.

The domestic stratified structure is relatively recent, only about 200 years old. Naturally, there was much dissatisfaction, but it began when the emperor at the time pushed it through, saying it was essential for national defense.

Despite having a class system, there are no major negative effects domestically. Balancing that must have been quite difficult.

Oh, the city layout and class divisions are displayed in an easy-to-understand, color-coded map.

…Hm? What is this ‘Unexplored Region’?

Part of the map, in the northeast, is labeled ‘Unexplored Region’, and there seems to be no information at all.

A: That is the forest where the Elf village is located. There is a barrier that repels ordinary humans, so investigation has not progressed.

I see.

…By the way, based on my experience so far, when there is a barrier, it is usually a dungeon. Could it be that the Elf village is a dungeon?

A: It is not a dungeon, but it uses a similar existence.

What is that?

A: The World Tree.

SEKAIJU!!!

Wait, calm down, Shindo Jin. The World Tree Alta refers to does not necessarily match the World Tree I am imagining. After all, in fiction, it is no exaggeration to say there are as many interpretations of a World Tree as there are stories.

Depending on the interpretation, there are even things that barely deserve to be called a World Tree. In other words, there is a possibility of being prematurely excited.

So let us take it slow and ask about the important things first.

Alta, is this World Tree an actual tree?

A: Yes. It is a great tree that grows with roots in the ground. It absorbs resources, so if you ask whether it is the same as an ordinary plant, the answer would be no.

Okay. That much is not a problem.

It does not seem to be a gimmicky World Tree like ‘it was actually metal’ or ‘it is a conceptual existence with no physical form.’

That is a relief.

Alright then, let us listen a bit more carefully.

---

**AN:** Repost: Top 3 Things I Absolutely Wanted to Include If I Ever Wrote Fantasy

1st: World Tree -> Reserved

2nd: Floating Castle -> Done

3rd: Dungeon -> Done
