## **179: Failed Apology and Evolution**

After spending half the afternoon touring the museum, we ate dinner outside and returned to the inn.

When we entered, the receptionist who saw us spoke up.

“Jin-sama. A guest is waiting for you. May I announce you?”

“Who is it?”

“They said they are a messenger of Princess Ruby.”

“Ah, that’s fine.”

I already knew who it was from the map, but I asked anyway and gave my consent.

While we waited in the lobby, one of Ruby’s attendants (a man) emerged from another room.

As the word “messenger” suggested, Ruby herself was not present.

“I am one of Princess Ruby’s attendants. Do you remember me?”

“Yeah, I remember.”

We hadn’t really exchanged formal greetings back then.

“I see. I have a message from Princess Ruby. ‘I will apologize tomorrow at ten, so please come to the Imperial Castle.’ That is all.”

“Are you screwing with me?”

I lowered my voice and glared at him with eyes that looked like they could kill.

No, seriously, no way.

“W-Why are you looking at me like that!? Is there some problem!?”

“…You really seem serious.”

The attendant showed no sign of understanding just how unreasonable what he said was.

If an attendant of the imperial family is like this, isn’t that a bit of a problem?

“Why should I, the one receiving the apology, have to go to the one apologizing? No matter how you look at it, the one apologizing should be the one to move. Even if I concede a hundred steps and say you’d apologize the next time I happened to come to the Imperial Castle, specifying a time and making the apologizing side do that is ridiculous. Stop messing with me.”

“B-But Princess Ruby is a princess. She cannot just move about so lightly…”

“Does Mr. Pierre know about the contents of that message?”

I cut him off before he could finish his excuse and asked.

“N-No. Mr. Pierre should not know. Princess Ruby asked me directly, and I came here straight away.”

“Thought so…”

If Pierre had been involved, there’s no way he would have allowed something this stupid.

A: Pierre is currently rushing over here at full speed.

Ah, so he realized it was bad after all.

But he was a bit late.

“I’ve decided. I’m not going to forgive Ruby.”

“W-Why!? She will apologize! Didn’t you say you’d forgive her if she apologized!?”

“I never said that.”

An apology is the bare minimum. It does not mean I will forgive her just because she apologizes.

An apology without even a shred of sincerity is nothing but a waste of time.

“Excuse me!”

“Mr. Pierre!? Why are you here!?”

At that moment, Pierre opened the inn’s door and came inside. The attendant looked shocked.

I crossed my arms in front of me and showed Pierre an X sign.

Pierre pressed a hand to his head and looked up at the heavens.

That alone seemed to let him grasp the situation to some extent.

Competent, but you can tell he’s had a hard life. Unfortunately, this isn’t something I can be considerate about.

“It seems I was too late…”

“Yes. After having something like that said right in front of me, I don’t even feel like forgiving her anymore.”

“…Is there truly no way?”

From Pierre’s position, he couldn’t just give up easily.

“P-Pierre-sama, what are you saying!?”

“You, be quiet for a moment!”

“Y-Yes!!!”

And with that, he silenced the attendant who still didn’t understand.

“Without sincerity from the one apologizing, there is nothing to forgive. Words spoken by someone who does not understand the meaning of an apology have no value.”

“I am aware of that. However, Lady Ruby is still young and has room for reform. I beg you, would you please reconsider?”

If this were something that directly led to execution, it might be questionable to cut it off due to momentary emotion.

However, “room for reform” alone is not worth considering. At the very least, I’d want something like “certain reform.”

Let’s see. There is something I want to test anyway, so perhaps…

“Then I have one proposal.”

“What would that be?”

“Entrust Ruby to Rouge. Separate her from her attendants and re-educate her at Rouge’s side. She may even have to leave this country for a while.”

Entrusting her to Rouge, or rather to me, means re-educating her under the maids.

If that’s the case, reform can be said to be certain. In a sense.

“T-That is… We would need Lady Rouge’s consent, and if this is education, we cannot avoid informing His Majesty the Emperor. I cannot decide this on my own…”

“Rouge is someone I’ll convince myself. You can think of an excuse for His Majesty.”

Alta.

A: Yes.

《Master Jin, I am fine with it. Leaving relatives who would be rude to you alone is far too frightening.》

When I asked Alta, a telepathic reply immediately came back from Rouge. Yes, persuasion complete.

I have no desire to persuade Scarlet.

The effort of coming up with a fake story for Ruby would be wasted.

“…Understood. To be honest, the current educational environment and the state of the attendants are not favorable for Lady Ruby. This may be a good opportunity to rethink everything from the ground up.”

“Pierre-sama!?”

“Didn’t I tell you to be quiet?”

Pierre glared sharply at the noisy attendant.

“Y-Yes!”

Pierre has quite an intimidating gaze himself.

Status-wise too, he looks like he’s been through a fair number of battlefields.

“I will explain everything to His Majesty the Emperor. Originally, His Majesty has not been particularly enthusiastic about the education of his sons and daughters, so with a certain level of persuasiveness, it should not be impossible.”

As expected, competent.

“The issue will be how much we can correct her before His Majesty returns. We cannot simply entrust her to Lady Rouge in her current state. Someone suitable as an educator would be…”

And a hard worker.

It seems he’s seriously thinking about an education plan.

“Jin-sama, please excuse me for today. I will do my utmost to correct Lady Ruby as much as possible and have her apologize with the proper meaning.”

With those words, Pierre left.

It is certain that the personnel around Ruby will be completely overhauled.

And then night.

We chatted aimlessly in our room at the inn.

“Today was packed with events. Both good and bad…”

“Um, the Third Prince visited, we were invited to the Imperial Capital with VIP treatment, we were attacked by the Seventh Princess, the First Princess asked us a favor, we toured the museum, and the Seventh Princess’s training was decided, right?”

Mio counted the day’s events on her fingers.

Most of them involved the imperial family, but aside from the Seventh Princess-related ones, none were particularly unpleasant.

“So it’s training, not education, for the Seventh Princess. Well, I can’t deny it…”

“The starting point is too low to call it education. Training an animal is closer, right?”

The Seventh Princess did not even get treated as human.

“Pointing a blade at Jin-sama is absolutely unforgivable. Training by the maids will be harsher than ever before.”

“Maria-chan calls it training too, huh…”

Sakura gave a wry smile at Ruby’s treatment being fixed as “training.”

《Tame her?》

“Dora-san, she is human. Even if she were to become a slave, taming is not possible.”

《Oh, okay.》

In Dora’s mind, training seems to equal taming.

I don’t recall ever doing anything like training to Dora, though…

“No, I don’t intend to make her a slave either.”

“Huh? Really?”

“Rather, I don’t want to.”

Hearing my statement, Mio tilted her head.

“Mio, didn’t you look at her skills? Interestingly, most of Scarlet’s children have at least one Unique-class skill.”

“I knew that, but I didn’t look at the details. My mistake… Oh, interesting.”

Yes. In fact, most of Scarlet’s children possess rare skills that could be called Unique.

And this is Ruby’s Unique skill.

\<Self-Made Royal Path>

Depending on the owner’s position, bonuses are applied to their status. The higher the rank, the greater the bonus.

It’s a type of skill you don’t see often, and it seems its effect changes based on one’s standing.

I’m curious what would happen if she were trained. That’s why I decided to take Ruby in.

If it leads to interesting results, I plan to make her a subordinate through \<Bond of Contract> rather than \<Slave Arts>.

To return and add context, Strawberry, whom we met before, also had a Unique skill.

As far as we know, the only exception is Ash-kun. A shocking no-skill.

A: No, Master. Ash is not Scarlet’s son.

Huh?

A: According to the detailed information confirmed by \<Clairvoyance>, strengthened through \<Extended Interpretation>, it lists his parents’ names. It seems Ash’s father is Vermilion Crimson.

Huh, first I’ve heard of that…

But that made sense.

Scarlet deciding to raise Ash as his own child must have been because he was the orphan of his deceased younger brother.

By the way, what about the mother?

A: The name is known, but the details are unknown.

I see.

Even with that skill, it’s not possible to chase down information that far.

…Wait? I recall that Vermilion possibly had the \<Hero> skill and title.

A hero whose skills are nullified by \<Seal> having a child without skills? Coincidence?

A: The skill itself has no such effect, but under certain conditions, it is possible for a child without skills to be born.

What conditions?

A: If both parents possess the \<Hero> skill and title. In that case, there is a low probability that a child without skills will be born.

Ash was a half-elf.

If the father was a “human Hero” and the mother an “elf Hero”, then Ash being born a half-elf without skills would not be unnatural.

A: That is a possibility.

The Scarlet family, including Ash, has way too many mysteries and new revelations.

In the sense that it’s never boring, it’s a very wonderful family.

Well, even such a wonderful family has exceptions…

But that’s a story for later…

The next morning, we decided to split up for sightseeing.

Sakura, and Maria and I went to continue yesterday’s museum tour. …Rather than going to the museum, it’s more accurate to say Maria came along with me, but that’s nothing new.

Meanwhile, Mio, Sera, and Dora went on their usual food tour. This, too, can be called a staple by now.

“Alright then, today we start from where we left off yesterday, the middle of ‘Art’.”

Yesterday, we finished ‘History’ and part of ‘Art’, so today we’ll see the rest of ‘Art’ and then ‘Ethnicities’.

We can’t help moving at a slightly brisk pace.

“Will we be able to finish everything today…?”

“If not, we can come again, but I’d like to avoid three days in a row. Let’s do something else tomorrow.”

“I’d be fine with three days in a row, though…”

Sakura might be fine, but I’d get bored after three days straight.

And today’s museum visit is only planned for the morning…

“We’ll probably split up again tomorrow, so I won’t stop Sakura from going…”

“Going alone would be a bit… I’ll stick with Jin-kun after all…”

“Me too.”

For Maria, that’s the default.

“So this afternoon, we meet up with Mio-chan’s group for lunch and then head to the theater, right?”

As Maria said, we planned to enjoy a stage performance at the theater in the afternoon.

Despite being a military superpower, the Crimson Empire has surprisingly many cultural facilities.

By the way, the performance is an original play called ‘Lion King’.

Yet another sudden Japanese element.

Now then, while chatting, we arrived at the museum.

We started touring from where we left off yesterday.

We resumed from the middle of ‘Art’.

Yesterday had many three-dimensional works like sculptures and statues, but today is mainly paintings.

Landscapes, portraits, even if the world changes, there isn’t much difference in art.

There are quite a few motifs I remember seeing in Japan.

Art has various trends and fads, and in the end, it settles where it settles. …Given that this is a world heavily influenced by Japan, it might make sense that it settles into something close to Japan.

From here on are portraits of successive emperors.

They are apparently painted at the time they ascend the throne, so they depict relatively young appearances.

There is already a portrait of Emperor Scarlet. It feels about ten percent cooler.

Speaking of Scarlet, I learned yesterday that the first emperor had the same name, so I took a look at that portrait.

A dignified middle-aged man is depicted.

I read the explanatory text below. Let’s see, it says this portrait was painted shortly after the founding of the nation, and since there were no famous painters in the country at the time, it was painted by someone with some basic knowledge, so it is said to lack accuracy.

Hey, you don’t need to make excuses in a place like this.

…But somehow, it feels like he resembles someone.

Hmm…

There’s no point in spending time on something I don’t understand, so I moved on.

“Is this okay?”

I tilted my head at a painting of a large tree that I saw a little further on.

The title of the painting was ‘World Tree’. The artist was ‘Lion Vermis’.

A work from about fifteen years ago.

Vermilion-san, what are you doing!?

And at this moment, it was confirmed that Vami-san (nickname) had been to the elf village.

Alta knew, didn’t you?

A: Yes. I used it as reference when considering matters related to Ash and Vermilion.

Why is important information about this country just popping up at the museum?

There weren’t any more amusing topics beyond that.

After thoroughly enjoying the museum as a normal museum, we finished ‘Art’, entered ‘Ethnicities’, and before long, the promised time was approaching.

“This is as far as we go.”

“Yes… As expected, we couldn’t finish everything today…”

Sakura said a little regretfully.

“Want to come again the day after tomorrow?”

“If possible, I’d like to…”

“I will accompany you.”

And so, we decided to come again the day after tomorrow.

We’ll probably be able to finish everything by then.

‘Ethnicities’ doesn’t have that many exhibits, so half a day should be enough.

However, since it displays lifestyles and such, the area is large. If you really wanted to look carefully, it might take the longest time.

Sorry, but we don’t plan to look that carefully.

After leaving the museum, we reunited with Mio’s gourmet group.

“Now then, it’s lunchtime.”

《Food!》

The two big eaters are energetic.

“You were going around food places until now, right?”

“Yeah, they really have bottomless stomachs.”

Even Mio, who was with them, seemed put off.

Especially Dora. She’s been eating an awful lot lately.

She eats almost as much as Sera, to the point that she’s also eating some ration balls.

Is there some reason for it?

A: Yes. That reason is because Dora’s ‘Evolution’ is approaching.

…..!?

…Let’s calm down a bit.

Alta, please explain one thing at a time.

A: Yes.

Is ‘Evolution’ the kind of evolution that appears in games from my world?

A: Yes. It refers to ‘strengthening accompanied by a change in race’.

I recall that Mio said her familiar Myao would also evolve.

I haven’t heard about it at all until now, but is the concept of ‘Evolution’ common in this world?

A: No, it is not a common concept. This phenomenon is limited to only a very small number of monsters. One of them is the draconian race with the form of a Feather Dragon.

????

A: To clarify, among the draconian race, a Feather Dragon refers to the juvenile form of a certain race. That race is called the Origin Dragon.

I’ve never heard of it… or maybe I have somewhere.

A: It is the transformed appearance of the guardian of the ‘Dragonkin Sanctuary’ labyrinth, the Dragonite Origin Replica.

Ah, that! I do remember thinking it looked like a Feather Dragon, and that it also looked like a grown Feather Dragon. I even remember having that conversation.

A: When draconian Feather Dragons grow, their form and name change. That is the transformed appearance of the Dragonite Origin Replica, and the name Origin Dragon.

You’ve been specifying draconian race this whole time. Does that mean that Feather Dragons of the ‘Race: Dragon’ do not ‘Evolve’?

A: Correct. They do not ‘Evolve.’ They remain Feather Dragons for their entire lives.

I didn’t know that.

Dora was a pretty special dragon.

I feel both happy and sad.

I’m glad for Dora’s growth, but it also means the end of my life using Dora as a body pillow.

Origin Dragons are large and not suitable as body pillows. That makes me very sad.

A: Origin Dragons can also take on the Feather Dragon form.

Yessssssssssss!!!!!!!!!!

I raised my clenched fist to the heavens.

“Huh? What? What’s wrong!?”

Since this conversation was one-on-one with Alta, Mio was very surprised.

Since it’s a good opportunity, I had Alta explain it to the other members as well.

“Dora-chan was a race that could evolve. I’m jealous. And now I understand her recent appetite.”

《Eat lots, get strong!》

“Do your best.”

Mio’s interest seems to be in the concept of ‘Evolution’. As expected of my kindred spirit.

“So that dragon really was Dora-san’s grown form.”

“And you defeated such a dragon… I feel a bit conflicted…”

Hearing that the guardian she defeated was Dora’s grown form, Sakura frowned.

That was just a guardian and different from a real living creature, so I don’t think she needs to worry too much…

“Sakura-sama, there is no need for you to concern yourself.”

《Sakura, don’t worry!》

“That’s right. That was a fake.”

Maria, Dora, and Sera comforted Sakura.

“Thank you… I’m fine… It’s just a little…”

Sakura seems to understand that thinking about it is pointless.

Still, it probably made her feel a little unpleasant.

According to Alta, ‘Evolution’ is not immediate and will take months.

And after the ‘Evolution’ is complete, Dora will be able to speak human language.

“Huh? I thought draconians start being able to talk around age ten?”

I remember hearing the same thing Mio mentioned.

A: She seems to be precocious.

Yeah, that’s a very simple answer.

Apparently, it’s just individual variation.

《When Dora gets big, will Master ride me? Like a mount?》

As far as I remember, Origin Dragons were a size that could be used as mounts.

It wouldn’t be impossible to ride her.

“No, my mount is Blue. Does Dora want me to ride her?”

《Nope. Just saying you can if you want.》

It doesn’t seem like she’s aiming for the mount position.

“If Blue says it’s okay, I might ride you once.”

《Okay.》

When I asked Blue, she tearfully begged me not to abandon her.

She said that while she could tolerate a carriage, a mount was absolutely NG.

If the mount doesn’t like it, I have no intention of forcing it.

Dora doesn’t particularly want to be ridden either…

After having lunch at a restaurant Mio recommended and taking a good rest, we headed to the theater.

The tickets were bought in advance, so there’s no problem even if we take it slow.

In this world, Japanese people have done various things, but as expected, movies still don’t exist.

So when you say theater, it equals stage performance.

In addition to regular plays, there are also musicals.

Today, we’re watching the musical ‘Lion King’.

There is also a regular play version. Apparently, it has even been published as a book.

And then we arrived at the theater.

We finished the reception, and before entering the hall, we bought popcorn and something like cola.

…Why is that part modeled after movie theaters?

《Next to Master!》

When we sat in our reserved seats, Dora immediately sat in the seat next to me.

On the other side, Maria silently took a seat.

“I was too slow again…”

It seems Mio also wanted to sit next to me.

– crunch crunch crunch crunch crunch –

With twenty minutes until the show starts, we finished all the popcorn.

At the popcorn stand, they told us, “Please do not eat popcorn during the performance as it will be noise”, so it couldn’t be helped. Drinks were okay.

That makes no sense.

And then the show began.

To be honest, I wasn’t expecting much.

The main reason we came was to do something touristy.

However, it was more enjoyable than I expected.

Since coming to this world, I’ve lived a life mostly unrelated to background music.

It made me realize that the synergistic effect of visuals and music is not something to be underestimated.

The theme is also a success story that would appeal to the masses.

It’s apparently a work that has been loved for over ten years.

Satisfied, I even bought a pamphlet at the shop on the way out.

First of all, I was surprised that pamphlets even existed.

However, what surprised me the most was what caught my eye as I flipped through the pamphlet…

Original Concept: ‘Red Scarlet’, Composition: ‘Lion Vermis’.

Vami-san, you shouldn’t have any skills, yet you’re quite versatile.

And also, what is His Majesty the Emperor doing?

## **180: Evidence Erasure and the Mastermind**

**AN:** The title sounds ominous, but Jin-kun does not end up in a pinch.

For the record, this is a fairly rare battle chapter.

---

After leaving the theater and heading toward our next destination, a group of around twenty people wearing red robes that concealed their faces blocked our path.

At the front, the one who looked the most important opened his mouth (his face still hidden).

“You’re Jin, right? Sorry about this, but you’re going to die here.”

This man made a declaration of murder on a busy public street in broad daylight, just before evening. His map indicator was red. Who exactly was he?

Name: Jonathan Crimson  

Gender: Male  

Age: 16  

Race: Human  

Title: Second Prince of the Crimson Empire

To my surprise, he was the (second) prince of the Crimson Empire.

This attack… no, assassination. Its motive can be summed up in a single phrase: “To protect Princess Ruby.”

Some of you may have already noticed from the name, but Jonathan is Ruby’s full sibling by the same mother.

Apples and gemstones are both written as “red jewel” in kanji, after all.

Scarlet probably named them.

Jonathan learned about Ruby’s attack incident and chose to assassinate me in order to cover it up and pretend it never happened.

At that point, Jonathan was already immediately guilty.

Knowing his sister was in the wrong and harming someone else to conceal it is beyond the pale.

If he truly cared about his sister, he should have brought her along and apologized in person.

Whether I would have forgiven them is a separate matter.

Instead of choosing to apologize together and show sincerity, he unhesitatingly chose assassination as a last resort.

I mean, even if this assassination succeeded, did he really think he would get away with it?

There are a lot of witnesses, you know?

A: No, he was prepared for the worst case of being executed by the emperor himself.

If he was prepared for that, then why didn’t he at least try apologizing first…?

By the way, Jonathan’s assassination plan was, of course, completely leaked from the planning stage.

“Die!”

With that shout, the red-clad group rushed at us.

They were Jonathan’s subordinates, a combat unit with fairly respectable levels.

In other words, this was an extremely rare group battle between humans (for me), and in the middle of a city at that.

Large-scale extermination battles with many enemies (like bandit hunts) are a different category.

As the party leader, I issued the most appropriate command for this situation.

《Handle it.》

If everyone has the strength, then not micromanaging and letting each person do what they believe is best is the optimal solution.

If you can predict what someone will do even without instructions, that is perfect.

I decided to personally deal with Jonathan, the leader.

As for the rest, it was just a simple job of each person defeating four opponents.

“Hah!”

Jonathan swung his greatsword with force.

It looked like the same type of greatsword his father used, but it was hardly a weapon suited for assassination.

To avoid being identified, he was using a lower-quality weapon than his usual one. A clever little trick…

-CLANG-

I caught his slash with my sword.

That sword was not the ‘Heroic Spirit Blade: Incomplete’.

The ‘Heroic Spirit Blade: Incomplete’ has too many issues for everyday use.

…In fact, that makes me not really qualified to criticize Jonathan for being crafty.

“What!? You stopped my slash!?”

Don’t be that surprised just because your attack was blocked.

Even if your full-power strike with a Unique Skill activated was stopped with one hand…

\<Greatsword Technique>

A large attack power bonus when using greatswords. Reduced weight burden. Grants a weapon destruction effect.

The name suggests it’s a derivative of \<Sword Technique>, but it’s still a Unique-class skill.

Specialization always leads to strength in games.

Still, since he’s Scarlet’s son, I had expected more, but he’s no good.

He doesn’t fall into my category of “decent”. At that point, my handling of him becomes rough.

-SLASH-

Without saying a word, I severed Jonathan’s right arm from the shoulder.

“Guaaaaaaah!!!”

Jonathan screamed.

There was a reason I wasn’t planning to kill him here, but he still needed to pay a price.

Once you lose an arm, you can never effectively use that Unique Skill again, right?

In that case, I’ll take it without hesitation.

I took \<Greatsword Technique> from Jonathan.

It’s not a particularly amazing skill, and I don’t desperately need it, but he clearly opposed me, so this is like a consolation prize.

Sera uses a greatsword, so I’ll probably give it to her.

“Guh… you bastard… you did this… I’ll kill you… I swear…”

“What can you even do in that state? More importantly, it’s about time I saw your face.”

I reached for the robe concealing his face.

Someone who loses a fight has no right to hide their identity.

“S-Stop…”

Jonathan tried to retreat, but the pain prevented him from moving properly, and he ended up crawling on the ground.

“All right, reveal.”

Without hesitation, I exposed Jonathan’s face.

I deliberately made sure passersby could see it.

“Isn’t that Prince Jonathan, the second prince?”

“It is! What!? The second prince carried out an attack!? An attempted assassination!?”

As expected, the area erupted into an uproar.

Of course they’d be shocked. A prince of their own country committing attempted assassination would do that.

“I-It’s not true!”

You’ve already shown your face. What do you mean, it’s not true…?

I said I wouldn’t kill him here, but I have no intention of considering his future position or standing.

“Now then, what about the others…”

When I looked around after taking my eyes off Jonathan, the other battles were already over.

They were all instant victories.

For the record, I had instructed everyone not to kill them (that doesn’t mean they’re unharmed).

I am fundamentally unforgiving toward those who choose assassination as a method.

Both the perpetrators and the masterminds must receive retribution.

There are two main patterns of retribution. The first is killing them directly. The second is stripping them of everything except their lives.

The first is often chosen when the opponent’s power allows them to conceal the truth (for example, the ringlet-haired noble of the Kingdom of Eldia, or the priest of the Divine Nation of Elgant).

The second is chosen when, for some reason, it is easy to take everything from them (for example, Duke Garfelt of the Kingdom of Estea).

This time, Jonathan disobeyed Scarlet’s orders and carried out an attack in public.

Once his face was revealed, there was no room for excuses, and everything could be taken from him easily.

Additionally, I was curious whether Scarlet would truly punish a son who defied her orders, so this would also serve as confirmation. A good deal.

“That being the case, Rouge, can I leave the rest to you?”

I spoke to Rouge, who had approached along with her attendants.

At this point, there was absolutely no room left for excuses.

“Yeah, leave it to me.”

“Y-You bastard, Rouge! Why are you here!?”

Jonathan asked through his pain, having adjusted slightly.

“Because I was originally scheduled to meet up with them.”

This was actually true.

Since arriving in the imperial capital, Rouge and I had often acted separately, so we had planned to have a meal together as a show of goodwill.

We were just on our way to the meeting place when an idiot attacked us.

“If I come because it’s noisy, and this is what you’re doing… Do you not feel ashamed as royalty, committing acts like an assassin?”

“S-Shut up! I have to protect Ruby!”

This is hopeless.

“Trying to solve things through assassination isn’t what you call protecting someone.”

“What would you know!?”

“I don’t know, and I’m not interested. At the very least, you can no longer protect Princess Ruby.”

With one arm, he can’t protect her in terms of combat power, and his position will likely deteriorate as well.

Depending on Scarlet’s decision, execution is even possible.

He won’t be in a position to talk about protecting Ruby anymore.

“Dinner’s going to be a bit late.”

“Yeah. Go on ahead. I have to take these people back to the castle.”

Under Rouge’s instructions, her aides bound the assassins.

If you’re going to attack, could you at least avoid dinner time? It’s a hassle.

We had a late dinner with Rouge and the others, then returned to the inn.

“For something that was supposed to be hospitality, we’re getting attacked as usual.”

“And this time with royalty themselves, no less.”

As Mio and Sera pointed out, despite the Emperor’s orders, we were being attacked more than usual.

And by completely abnormal members, one prince and one princess.

It vaguely reminds me of the Regalia Beastman Kingdom.

Even after the Queen issued an Imperial decree, people kept poking at me…

By the way, Rouge told me during dinner that Jonathan and his subordinates would be confined until Scarlet returned.

Once he comes back, they’ll explain everything and await his judgment.

As an aside, Pierre apparently silently gazed at the heavens upon hearing that.

Even Pierre had no way to intervene.

He didn’t even come to plead for leniency with me, which shows he’s completely given up.

The only unfortunate thing is that Ruby’s training plan will likely fall through.

Since the motive for the attempted assassination lies with Ruby, her own attack incident can no longer be concealed.

Once Scarlet learns about Ruby’s attack, there’s a chance Ruby will be punished.

And since the hush-up itself is gone, the opportunity for training is gone as well.

The ironic part… or rather the unfunny part, is that Jonathan claimed he was protecting Ruby, yet he personally crushed her future.

If he hadn’t done anything unnecessary, the damage could have been minimized…

“I don’t feel like putting up with this farce any longer, so I plan to finish it today.”

I have no intention of continuing to entertain an uninteresting play.

“I’ll accompany you.”

《Dora too!》

“Dora-chan is staying here with us…”

Maria coming along is business as usual, but Dora is not allowed.

It’s bad for her education.

“By the way, Master, it wouldn’t have been strange for you to move to eliminate things after the first incident, right? Why did you wait for a second one?”

“Strictly speaking, I hardly did anything to the second one. Something similar would have happened sooner or later anyway, so I judged it was fine to wait.”

Rather than preventing incidents, I often clean things up after they happen.

Especially when the cause of the incident isn’t me…

The reason is usually that it becomes more interesting that way.

And since it’s not my responsibility, I can approach it in a somewhat irresponsible manner.

“That said, I won’t allow a third one.”

This is where it ends.

“That makes sense. The fuse was already lit.”

“Even if you put out the spark, the bomb won’t stop.”

Waiting for the bomb to explode and then extinguishing the spark is not a problem.

Mio’s metaphor is quite accurate.

By her logic, tonight we’re going to put out the spark.

A: Ash has made his move regarding that matter.

That surprised me. Ash is really capable.

Even though I wasn’t exactly slow, I didn’t expect him to beat me to it…

I don’t know how far he’s gone, but I’d better hurry too.

“Apparently that’s the case. I’m heading out for a bit.”

“Master, your face looks a little scary.”

“…Really? I guess I’m more irritated than I thought.”

Maybe because I’ve never bothered to hide my expressions, my irritation is showing.

The place I’m going has the kind of people I really hate.

I force a smile onto my face.

“I don’t think Jin-kun needs to worry, but please be careful…”

《See you.》

“Yeah. I’m off.”

In a room of the imperial castle, two members of the imperial family sat facing each other.

“Rose, it was you, wasn’t it? You were the one who incited Ruby and Jonathan to attack Jin-san.”

“Ash, what are you talking about all of a sudden? Did you come here just to ask something so incomprehensible?”

One was Ash Crimson, the third prince of the Crimson Empire, the other was Rose Crimson, the third princess.

Ash wore a stern expression, while Rose smiled gently in contrast.

Rose Crimson had red hair like other royals, extending down to around her waist.

Her gently wavy, glossy hair and bewitching face exuded an allure that didn’t seem befitting of a fifteen-year-old.

Her chest was large.

“If you truly don’t know, then that’s fine. I didn’t come here to condemn you. But if you continue to trouble Jin-san or harm our siblings, I will become your enemy. Please remember that.”

“You speak as though I’m some kind of criminal. That’s not a pleasant accusation.”

Rose’s face twisted slightly in displeasure.

“If that’s not the case, then how did Ruby know about Jin-san? We decided to give Ruby only minimal information. She shouldn’t have known his appearance or the fact that Father had a strong interest in him. Unless someone deliberately told her and guided her actions, I can’t believe Ruby would attack Jin-san.”

“Are you saying that was me? Did Ruby say so?”

When Rose asked provocatively, Ash shook his head.

“No. Ruby doesn’t remember who she heard about Jin-san from.”

“Then please don’t treat me as the culprit. It’s unpleasant.”

“The moment Ruby said she didn’t remember, I suspected you. You’re the only one I can think of who could do something like that and choose to act on it.”

“I don’t understand what you’re saying. Why don’t you explain it more clearly?”

Rose spoke without showing the slightest hint of agitation on the surface.

Her expression didn’t betray it, but her body did.

According to Alta, sweating and eye movement clearly show her impatience.

Apparently, sweat was pooling between her large breasts.

“You can manipulate Ruby’s thoughts and even alter her memories. That’s what I’m saying.”

“…”

Rose barely endured it.

But the sweat increased.

“The same applies to Jonathan. He learned about Ruby’s incident too quickly, and some of his actions were unnatural. More than anything… there were gaps in his memory.”

The sweat increased further.

“I truly have no intention of condemning you here. This is starting to turn into real condemnation, so I’ll excuse myself here.”

With that, Ash stood to leave.

As he opened the door, he turned back to look at Rose.

“I’ll say this just in case. That won’t work on me.”

“…”

The door closed with a bang, and Rose remained motionless for a while.

After a full two minutes, she finally let out a sigh.

“…Nothing ever goes smoothly. I thought it was a good chance to eliminate both a nuisance and an anomaly at once. And I didn’t expect that mixed-in element to notice before things concluded. It seems I’ll have to deal with the mixed-in element first.”

Rose crossed her arms and began thinking.

Her crossed arms emphasized her chest. The sweat had subsided.

“It was unexpected that my ‘Eyes’ didn’t work, but even if they don’t work on him directly, there are plenty of other methods, so it’s not a problem.”

The power Ash mentioned is Rose’s Unique Skill.

Its name is \<Hollow Eyes>, a skill that manipulates memories and emotions.

And it’s the kind of skill I hate the most.

“Unfortunately, that won’t be happening.”

“Who’s there!?”

Startled by an unseen voice, Rose looked around.

When she turned back to face forward again, I appeared in the seat where Ash had been sitting, directly in front of her.

“You are…”

“My name is Shindo Jin. The anomaly you’re talking about.”

“Guards! Someone help! There’s an intruder!”

Rose shouted, but the guards who should have been outside showed no reaction at all.

“It’s useless. The sound won’t reach them.”

This is the effect of Maria’s \<Barrier Technique>, which blocks sound and light from inside the barrier to the outside.

It looks like nothing has changed, but from the outside, nothing can be perceived.

Rose’s guards won’t enter the room unless she permits it, so they won’t notice anything.

“What are you planning? Even if you’re Father’s guest, sneaking into the imperial castle at night without permission and threatening an imperial princess… Do you really think you’ll get away with this?”

She glared at me coldly, but there’s no way I’d be intimidated at this point.

“You won’t get away with it is my line. What you did is instigation of murder. No, it’s equivalent to commissioning murder.”

Jonathan aside, Ruby probably didn’t intend to kill me.

But during the attack, Ruby’s movements were clearly aimed at killing.

There was a discrepancy between her thoughts and actions. This was the result of \<Hollow Eyes> guiding her consciousness and subconscious.

Jonathan also seemed to have been guided to some extent, but the influence was weaker than with Ruby.

In other words, regardless of guidance, the attack would have happened anyway. The timing was just accelerated a bit.

That’s why Jonathan deserves no leniency.

“That again? I have no idea what you’re talking about.”

“Don’t play dumb now. I heard everything. …This room was where you incited Ruby and Jonathan, right?”

“…..”

I heard everything from before the first attack.

This woman is a natural-born mastermind who’s been causing all sorts of trouble using \<Hollow Eyes>.

Her ultimate goal is to become emperor, and she’s been working behind the scenes to eliminate her siblings.

At first, her motives weren’t entirely clear, but after hearing about Scarlet’s retirement from Carmine, it made sense. She’s already in the final phase.

Then Rouge returned, which was a complete miscalculation.

And Scarlet is searching for someone accompanied by Jin.

So Rose decided to eliminate me by inciting Ruby and Jonathan, even if it failed, two royals would be eliminated.

And with \<Hollow Eyes>, there was a guarantee that her own existence wouldn’t come to light.

How unpleasant.

If someone like her is going to be the next emperor, Rouge would still be better.

“You’re free to scheme, but I especially hate the way you twist the principle of high risk, high return, pushing all the risk onto others. Someone I hate used assassination to involve me. Don’t think I’ll go easy on you.”

I’m not going to say something as crude as eliminating someone just because I don’t like them when they have nothing to do with me.

But when someone I don’t like involves me first, there’s no reason to treat them kindly.

Like I said earlier, this ends today.

“It seems there’s no point in pretending anymore. Yes, I was the one who sent those two after you.”

Rose gave up easily.

“Why?”

“To become emperor, of course. Since I was born into the imperial family, why not aim for the throne? For that, my siblings are just in the way.”

She just repeated exactly what I explained earlier.

No new information at all…

“You’d kill your own siblings without hesitation. You’re truly despicable.”

“I have no interest in my siblings in this life. It’s my second run, after all. What’s wrong with living freely?”

From that casual line, it’s clear that this woman is a reincarnator.

A reincarnator giving birth to another reincarnator… there’s something karmic about that.

Name: Rose Crimson  

Gender: Female  

Age: 15  

Race: Human (Reincarnator)  

Title: Princess of the Crimson Empire

“So you really are Japanese. Are you a Hero?”

“No, just a transmigrator. Fellow reincarnator.”

“Oh? You know that much? Do you have Eyes that see through things, like Father?”

Unfortunately, I don’t have such convenient ‘Eyes’.

All I have is \<Clairvoyance>.

“Then can you see through this as well?”

-SLAP-

I knocked aside the knife Rose threw.

The next moment, Rose vaulted over the table, drew the rapier at her waist, and began thrusting.

I avoided it by shifting my head slightly while remaining seated on the sofa.

Rose didn’t pursue deeply and instead created distance again.

“I’m often misunderstood by my appearance, but I’m actually quite strong.”

She said this while maintaining her guard.

Indeed, the thrust was refined enough that it was hard to imagine from her noble appearance.

“I know you’re strong. I didn’t know how, but I see now. Fencing, huh.”

I knew the general direction from her high-level \<Sword Technique>, but fencing was unexpected.

“You can tell just from that? I was quite a well-known fencer over there, you know.”

“I see. That means you’re at least around thirty in total.”

If she was famous in fencing, she must have been a certain age.

Unless she was some prodigy who died in her early teens, she must have lived at least fifteen years in her previous life.

So fifteen years then, fifteen years now, that adds up to around thirty.

“Mind your own business!”

“And despite playing sports, it seems you failed to gain a healthy mindset.”

There’s no guarantee that athletes are good people.

A healthy mind doesn’t always reside in a healthy body.

Fencers don’t normally throw knives as feints.

“That’s why I said mind your own business!!!”

A rapier is classified as a one-handed sword.

You can do other things with the free hand if you want.

But using a sub-weapon for harassment like this is questionable.

“Hah!”

There, another throwing knife came flying.

I caught it between the index and middle fingers of my left hand.

Then, just like before, but incomparably faster, a thrust was unleashed.

This is probably Rose’s best surprise tactic.

During the first attack, both of us were seated on the sofa.

A surprise from that position inevitably takes time.

So she deliberately discarded the precious first attack.

She intentionally used a slower attack to make me misjudge her maximum speed.

Then, on the next attack, she repeated nearly the same sequence while drastically increasing speed, aiming to catch me off guard with the difference.

“Well thought out.”

I muttered while catching the tip of the rapier between the index and middle fingers of my right hand.

“Go on, try again.”

I tossed away the knife in my left hand and pushed the rapier back.

The force was too strong, causing Rose to stumble.

“What ridiculous strength… But don’t underestimate me!”

This time, the attack was even faster.

The second strike had the same motion as the first. It wasn’t full power, but prioritized surprise.

This seems to be her true full effort.

The tip of the rapier was aimed straight at my forehead.

I didn’t dodge.

I caught it with my forehead while still seated on the sofa.

The tip stopped without even scratching my skin.

This is the pure violence of a difference in stats.

“Y-You really are a monster…”

Even Rose couldn’t hide her cold sweat. Chest sweat.

“Is that it? Then it’s my turn.”

The overwhelming strong-person move!!

---

**AN:** A true mastermind is one whose existence is never known.

Rose, the true mastermind, never appeared at all from the reader’s perspective.

She shows up suddenly and exits next time.

+++

## **181: The Curtain Falls, and an Invitation**

**AN:** Lately, due to various mental circumstances, my writing has barely been making any progress.

There is a possibility that I will enter a stockpiling period once this volume ends (this volume itself is already written).

I know it would be a shame to stop consecutive updates, but I am not the type who can run on a self-perpetuating schedule, so I ask for your understanding.

If I recover and my writing progresses before this volume ends, I will continue the serialization.

---

“Ku…”

Rose faltered at my overwhelming pressure (self-praise), trying to put distance between us.

However, I raised one hand faster than she could move.

“It’s useless.”

At that moment, Rose’s body floated into the air as if seized by an invisible force.

Ah, this is an application of the wind-manipulation power of the Wind Catastrophe Dragon.

“W-what is this!?”

I did not answer Rose’s question, lightly clenching the hand I had raised.

“Guh!?”

At that instant, invisible pressure bore down on Rose’s body, forcing a groan from her.

Ah, this is an application of the wind-manipulation power of the Wind Catastrophe Dragon (second time).

“G-ghah…”

“It’s not over yet.”

“S-stop…”

I snapped my clenched hand open.

“Gyaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaah!!!”

At that moment, Rose’s body was carved apart by invisible blades.

Ah, this is an application of the wind-manipulation power of the Wind Catastrophe Dragon (third time).

When I say carved apart, all I did was rake something like countless wind blades along the surface of her body, so the damage amounted to her clothes being shredded until she was naked and her suffering numerous cuts.

There were many wounds, but she was not bleeding to death, nor were there any deep injuries.

Earlier, I said I would show no mercy, but in truth I am applying full restraint.

As you may have noticed, at the point of the second pressure, I could have killed Rose if I truly wanted to.

In other words, I have no intention of killing Rose.

…To put it another way, I intend to make this the kind of “retribution” that does not involve killing.

After confirming that Rose was completely battered, I released the wind binding.

“Guh…”

With a dull thud, the naked body collapsed to the floor.

“Kuh… A-are you planning to kill me…?”

Even though she put on a frightened face, could she not hide the fact that her hostility had not disappeared at all?

You can tell just by looking into her eyes.

Those eyes are thinking about seizing an opening to escape or counterattack.

“Ah, relax. I have no plans to kill you. …That said, I have no intention of forgiving you either. So I decided that you will end here.”

After saying that, I stood up from the sofa.

“E-end? W-what exactly are you going to do to me…?”

“You can find that out with your own body.”

I walked over to where Rose lay and reached out toward her head.

“Well then, goodbye.”

“S-stop! No, noooooo!!!”

Her dying scream was blocked by the barrier and reached no one but me and Maria.

Two days passed from the day I completely ended Rose.

With the mastermind dealt with, there have been no attacks on me since then.

So we have been leisurely continuing our sightseeing in the imperial capital. The other day, we finally completed all the museums.

There were also requests for meetings from people connected to Jonathan and Ruby, but of course we declined them all.

According to Alta, they were apparently pleas for mercy, so there is no need to worry about them.

And today, we were invited by Ash to have lunch at the Imperial Castle.

This is one of the “minimum hospitality” measures he mentioned at the very beginning.

Because of the Jonathan and Ruby incidents, I naturally hesitated. Ash bowed his head without the slightest hesitation. I was swayed and agreed. Ash vowed that he would not make me uncomfortable.

That is about how it went.

“Thank you for inviting me today.”

“No, thank you for coming.”

I got out of the carriage and exchanged greetings with Ash, who was waiting in front of the Imperial Castle.

Since this is a public place, we are using polite speech.

Only I was invited, so aside from Maria, who has turned invisible, no one else came along.

Maria cannot be helped.

Following Ash’s guidance, I proceeded through the Imperial Castle.

Ash has subordinates directly under him, and through their efforts together with Mr. Pierre, members of the Jonathan and Ruby factions are prevented from approaching us.

Which is to say, they are trying to approach.

And then the luncheon began.

“My siblings have caused you trouble this time.”

Saying that, Ash bowed his head.

He had apologized when he invited me, but this was now a formal apology in an official setting.

“That’s not something you need to apologize for, is it Ash?”

“They are my siblings, after all. I cannot say it has nothing to do with me.”

“I suppose that’s one way of thinking… But unfortunately, I cannot say that I ‘forgive’ the two of them.”

If Ruby or Jonathan themselves had been the ones to apologize, there might have been room to consider it.

The fact that the first apology came from a sibling is just no good.

“That is understandable. What they did cannot be forgiven. So in a sense, this apology is little more than self-satisfaction. I am sorry to have involved you in it.”

He does not seem to think it has much meaning himself.

“On top of that, I would also like to apologize again for making Jin deal with the aftermath on our behalf.”

Ah, it seems he has noticed what happened with Rose.

Given the timing, it is only natural that he would find out.

“Whatever could you mean?”

For now, I decided to play dumb.

Ash formed a slight smile at the corner of his mouth and continued as if it were nothing.

“No, it is nothing. More importantly, how is the food? Rather than dishes from the Crimson Empire, I had dishes from the land where my mother’s family comes from prepared.”

It seems Ash also intends not to pursue the Rose matter too deeply.

This sense of distance is excellent.

The dishes served were apparently from the elf village.

No wonder the meal centers on light vegetable dishes without the strong flavors characteristic of the Crimson Empire.

The chef, like Ash, is a half-elf and apparently from the elf village.

That said, it is not as though there is no meat.

The elves of this world eat meat normally. I know this because I have some among my companions.

《Elven regional cuisine, I’m jealous!》

《How enviable!》

Those were telepathic messages from Mio and Sera.

Do not butt in while someone is eating.

《Pi!?》

《Kya!? Me-e as well…》

For now, I silenced the two of them with remote \<Fear>.

“It’s very delicious. May I ask where this cuisine is from?”

I am genuinely interested, so I asked.

Well, I did not think he would actually tell me…

“Yes. It is from the ‘Uncharted Region’ to the northeast of here. It is the regional cuisine of the elf village located there.”

You are not hiding it!?!?

Is that okay? Really?

“…Is that something you can make public?”

“It would be troublesome if it became public, so I would appreciate it if you kept it secret. …Personally, I think it might be better to make it public outright.”

Ash seemed to have some thoughts about the way the elf village exists, letting a hint of displeasure show.

“That said, even if it were made public, there is the Fog of Confusion, so it is not as though anyone could reach it…”

“…Why are you telling me about the elf village?”

To be honest, I cannot think of a reason why Ash would talk to me about the elf village.

“That is because I would like to take you to the elf forest, Jin.”

Once again, the conversation veered in an unexpected direction…

Be that as it may, there is one thing I absolutely have to ask.

“…Is this mandatory?”

“No, of course it is voluntary. If you do not want to go, I will not force you.”

Ash answered readily, then continued.

“This is something only I know, but my father is currently in the elf village. …When I say only I know, I mean that since I am the only one from the elf village, I am the only one who can speak of it.”

New information keeps coming one after another.

This relates to what the Second Princess wanted to know, ‘Scarlet’s true feelings’, does it not?

There was someone by your side who seemed to know even more than I do.

“The original purpose of my father’s order to ‘entertain him at the castle’ was to have you wait in the Imperial capital until he calls for you. And my role is to take you to the elf village when you arrive.”

“As expected, is this a countermeasure for the Fog of Confusion?”

“Yes, exactly.”

Those from the elf village seem able to deal with the Fog of Confusion.

…I will keep it a secret that it would probably be fine even without them.

“I originally planned to tell you after my father’s messenger arrived. However, given the many troubles we have caused you in such a short time, I thought there was a chance you might return before then, so I decided to explain it to you now. Honestly, I did not expect our plans to fall apart this much…”

Looking at Ash’s expression, he seems somewhat exhausted.

Apparently, this is an attempt to prevent me from leaving by explaining things ahead of schedule.

“I understand the circumstances. I swear that I will not return home at this point. However, I ask that you also understand that if problems continue beyond this, I may retract that.”

I cannot promise to stay no matter what.

“Yes, that is more than enough. Thank you for your understanding. The messenger should arrive within a few days…”

That messenger is Scarlet’s dragon knight, the dragonkin, right?

They will probably arrive in about thirty minutes. I know because I saw it on the map.

After that, the luncheon ended over the course of about thirty minutes.

Following Ash’s guidance, I exited through a different entrance from the one we used to enter.

Why? Because there are people connected to Jonathan and Ruby lying unconscious in front of the original entrance.

Ash’s direct subordinates beat down those who tried to rush toward me.

Ash’s consideration in showing me a different route under the pretext of giving me a tour of the castle so as not to make me uncomfortable should be appreciated.

Pretext or not, Ash did properly show me around the castle.

While that was happening, one of Ash’s subordinates approached and whispered something to him.

“Jin, the messenger I mentioned earlier has arrived. Would you come with me?”

“That was faster than expected. Understood.”

Since we were already outside the room and could not know who might be listening, Ash avoided using words that explicitly referred to Scarlet.

Naturally, I already knew that Kroa had arrived.

Together with Ash, I headed to the courtyard.

It seemed to have been cleared out, as there was no one else there.

The only person present was the black dragonkin woman I had seen before. That was Kroa.

Her attire was the same as before, a black dress.

“Ash, it has been a while.”

“Yes, it has been a while, Kroa.”

The two exchanged greetings in a familiar manner.

“Is that the person in question?”

Ash nodded at Kroa’s question.

“Yes, this is Jin. Jin, this is Kroa, my father’s dragon knight, a dragonkin… does that make sense to you?”

“Yeah. A race with both human and dragon forms, right?”

“So you are familiar with them…”

Information about dragonkin has been gradually spreading thanks to Castal’s intelligence.

That said, since Kroa is the only dragonkin whose whereabouts are currently known, investigations have not progressed very far.

“Kroa, what time did my father say?”

“He said three days from now. I can make the trip in two hours one way.”

The two continued a conversation that I could not quite follow.

“Jin, including a buffer day, we are thinking of heading to that place within two days. Would you decide by then whether you will accompany us?”

“In that case, I have already decided. I would very much like to accompany you.”

Ash seemed a little surprised that I answered immediately.

“I am grateful, but are you sure?”

“Yeah. An opportunity to enter a place that is normally off-limits openly. There is no reason to let that pass.”

That is my honest feeling.

If I am going to enter anyway, it is preferable to do so openly.

“Heh, I see.”

Ash let out a small chuckle, apparently amused by my response.

“Understood. Kroa, can you fly with the two of us on your back?”

“It will be fine. Scarlet is probably heavier than the two of you combined.”

Because of the \<Proof of the Hero>, Scarlet is heavy. Including his armor, he likely exceeds 200 kg with ease.

If Kroa can fly while carrying that, transporting two teenage boys should be no problem.

“May I ask something?”

“What is it?”

“I am sorry, but I cannot ride on her.”

Ash tilted his head.

“Why is that?”

“Because I have my own dragon mount. She would get jealous, so I cannot ride another dragon.”

My dragon mount dislikes me riding other living creatures. At present, carriages are truly the absolute limit of what she can tolerate.

A dragonkin would definitely not be allowed.

She would probably start crying in earnest if I did.

“That dragon mount could not be…!?”

Ash, who seems sharp, looked startled.

“That is a secret.”

I cannot say she is a dragonkin.

What? It is basically saying it anyway? As long as I do not say it outright, it does not count.

“I will call her, so is it okay if we depart tomorrow?”

“E-eh, yes. That is fine, but call…?”

“I can call her.”

“Ah, I see.”

I forced it through.

If I wanted, I could call her right now and depart immediately, but this is about creating an alibi.

“Kroa, is tomorrow fine for you?”

“Yes, I have no problem with that.”

“Then let us depart tomorrow morning.”

Ah, right.

Before we finish talking, I should ask this as well…

“Also, can I bring companions with me?”

“Yes. My father said that as long as they are people Jin acknowledges, you may bring them.”

I am surprised at how readily he agreed.

“However, you cannot bring anyone connected to the Crimson Empire, so you cannot bring Sister Rouge.”

So we cannot bring the most important person, Rouge.

Well, the information will reach her anyway, so it is not a problem…

“And please limit the number of companions to as many as can ride on Kroa and Jin’s dragon mounts. Excluding us, that would probably be at most two or three people…”

It is natural to have limits based on capacity, but this time it is not something I need to worry about.

“That will be fine. If necessary, I will increase the number of dragon mounts. Also, is there any capacity limit on the village side?”

“N-no, there is no limit on entering the village. …More importantly, you can increase the number of dragon mounts?”

I can.

And so, we decided that tomorrow morning, I would head to the elf village together with Ash.

After finishing the luncheon with Ash plus a bit extra, I returned to the inn and began a strategy meeting.

“Who wants to accompany me to the elf village?”

First, confirming the companions.

“Me!”

The one who raised her hand energetically was Mio.

She is probably interested in elven cuisine.

《Dora wants to go too!》

“I will go as well.”

“I would like to go too…”

“Naturally, I will accompany you.”

All right, everyone is going.

“Next is the dragon mounts. Alta, did you ask them already?”

A: Yes. They are already on the move.

For the sake of creating an alibi, I had Blue fly from the Kingdom of Estea to the imperial capital of the Crimson Empire under her own power. She will probably arrive in about an hour.

I will also call the Deep Green Dragon and the Crescent Moon Dragon, but since it is impossible for them to keep up with the Sky Dragon’s flight speed, I plan to have them use a ‘Portal’ around the point where they enter the Crimson Empire.

As an aside, this time I decided to give Blue and the others a bit of a disguise.

I had Sakura create a magic called ‘Camouflage’ that changes coloration.

With that, I changed Blue from sky blue to ultramarine, Leaf from young leaf green to deep green, and Mikazuki from yellow to ocher, gradually shifting them toward darker tones.

Their forms themselves have not changed at all.

Will they get found out? Maybe they will?

Well, in the worst case, I can just force it by saying ‘They are different dragons’…

From now on, I plan to use the default colors when acting as the Queen’s Knight, and the darker colors when acting as Jin’s party.

This will probably continue until we reveal the true identities of the Queen’s Knight.

To be clear, revealing the identity of the Queen’s Knight is something I am considering for the future.

There is no plan at the moment, but there is a possibility that I myself will step onto the public stage someday.

The Queen’s Knight will serve as groundwork for that time.

The important thing is that it is ‘revealed’, not ‘found out’. That point is non-negotiable.

Now then, back to the main topic.

An hour later, the three dragon girls arrived safely.

They landed outside the imperial capital, and Ash had the gates let them in after explaining the situation.

Blue and the others were to be held at the gate as dragon familiars.

Of course, I will absolutely not tolerate any improper behavior. Anyone who lays a hand on them will atone with their life.

And then, the next day, we headed to the meeting place, the north gate of the imperial capital.

It is the closest to the Uncharted Region.

Even though it was before the meeting time, Ash was already standing by.

As expected, he is a diligent man.

“Good morning.”

“Good morning. So those are your dragon mounts, Jin. They are beautiful dragons.”

When I greeted him, Ash looked at Blue (in dragon form) and said so.

That is right, that is right. They are beautiful dragons.

“Yeah. This one is my proud beloved dragon.”

As I praised her while petting her, Blue looked extremely happy.

“And you really do have multiple dragon mounts…”

“I increased them.”

“Hahaha…”

Looking at Leaf (dragon form) and Mikazuki (dragon form), Ash gave a wry smile.

“Ash, let us depart at once.”

Kroa, already in black dragon form, urged us on.

Although there seems to be time to spare, she probably wants to get going as soon as possible.

“Yes. Jin, is that fine with you as well?”

“Yeah, no problem.”

We each mounted our dragons and departed.

As usual, Maria and I are on Blue, Sakura and Dora on Leaf, Mio and Sera on Mikazuki. Sera has been made lighter with the ‘Float’ spell.

Ash had his subordinates come to see him off, but no one came for me.

Naturally so, since I did not tell Rouge and the others anything publicly.

And then, an aerial journey.

Led by Ash and Kroa, we headed toward the elf village.

To be honest, Kroa is slow…

It is only natural that she cannot match the flight-specialized Blue, but is she not only about as fast as an ordinary Lesser Wind Dragon?

As a dragonkin, that is a bit questionable.

A: Black dragons are suited for combat and do not have high top speed. Instead, they have high load capacity and defense, making them suitable for armored dragon knights.

In that sense, they are just right for heavyweights.

I knew she was slow before, but experiencing it firsthand really makes her feel slow.

Riding a flight-specialized Blue probably makes it feel even slower…

《Honestly, I want to just overtake them.》

《Stop it. Then we would not know what the guide is for.》

《I know. I am just saying it because I am bored.》

Blue also looks bored due to the low-speed flight.

As the aerial journey continued, the area changed, updating adjacent areas, and various things became visible on the map.

I see, so that is how it is…

There are quite a few interesting things.

World Tree Core

Notes: The center of the World Tree and the source of its energy. By fulfilling certain conditions, one can become its master.

The description is basically a dungeon core.

Alta said the World Tree resembles a labyrinth, but it is similar enough that calling it a subspecies would be more accurate.

Let us see…

It appears that the position equivalent to a labyrinth ruler is currently vacant.

Could be a good opportunity?

Name: Lily

Gender: Female

Age: 65535

Race: High Elf

Titles: Elf Princess Shrine Maiden, Elf Royalty, Elf Storyteller, Guardian of the World Tree

Next is likely the person who is the purpose of this invitation.

She is the elf storyteller we were planning to meet eventually.

Despite being called an elf storyteller, she is clearly a high elf. Moreover, she is a ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’.

It feels like she is outside the naming rules for ‘Princess Shrine Maidenes’ since there is no ‘Yuri’ attached, but since Lily refers to the lily flower, maybe that counts.

Furthermore, like a labyrinth guardian in a dungeon, she also bears the role of preserving the World Tree.

Without a doubt, she has far too many attributes.

According to Alta, she is currently in a deep sleep and will not awaken for another two days.

More precisely, she was originally in a deep sleep, but it has grown considerably shallower, and she seems likely to awaken in two days.

This also matches what Kroa and Ash said about three days (as of one day ago).

According to Alta’s investigation, she began sleeping about nine years ago.

The fact that this lines up with events involving Scarlet about ten years ago does not feel like a coincidence.

That is precisely why I judged it to be the reason for the invitation.

Even without the Scarlet matter, it is someone I want to hear from. No, someone I will hear from.

Name: Claire

Gender: Female

Age: 120

Race: Elf

Title: Elf Hero

Skill: \<Seal LV10>

Since we are here, let me introduce one more elf.

As usual, someone is sealed, and that someone is the ‘Elf Hero’, Claire.

Incidentally, she is Ash’s mother (stated definitively).

---

**AN:** As for how Rose ended up, I will leave that to your imagination.

Jin is at least better about choosing his targets, but what he does is pretty extreme either way.

+++

## **182: The Mist of Confusion and the Elf Village**

**AN:** Rose is not dead. Her body is unharmed. Her mind has not broken yet.

What kind of ‘ending’ it turned into is already decided in the author’s mind, but it is too brutal, so there are no plans to make it public.

One thing can be said for certain: it is not something the protagonist would normaly do.

---

After a sluggish flight, we arrived at the forest where the elf village is located.

Before us spread a forest shrouded in mist.

This is the Mist of Confusion.

“From here on, you have to enter on foot to reach the elf village.”

Ash, who had landed ahead of us, explains.

If we really wanted to, we could probably get there without doing that, though?

Also, Kuroa has turned into humanoid form (completely naked) and is in the middle of getting dressed.

As expected of the dragonkin, her sense of shame is weak.

“By the way, Jin-san, what will you do about your riding dragons? They’ll be staying inside for several days, so you can’t exactly leave them here, right?”

“Is it okay to bring them inside?”

“Ordinary dragons are not allowed. Dragonkin are apparently fine, though…”

Huh? Dragonkin are okay?

“Do you want to come along?”

When I ask, Blue, Leaf, and Mikazuki all nod together.

“Then you can change into humanoid form. Ah, here.”

Before Blue turns humanoid, I pull a tunic over her head.

Sakura does the same for Leaf, and Mio does it for Mikazuki.

Blue and the others also lack shame, but I have no intention of having them strip naked in front of Ash.

“Phew… then we can go in too, right?”

“Seems like it.”

Blue quickly turns humanoid and straightens her clothes.

“As I thought… But is it really okay? Telling me who they really are?”

“Ash-san isn’t the kind of person who would spread it around, right? And even if it did spread, there wouldn’t really be that much disadvantage anymore…”

Since we’re planning to make information about dragonkin public anyway, aside from me standing out a bit and people suspecting a connection to the Queen’s Knight, it’s fair to say there’s no real downside.

Come to think of it, what kind of position am I in right now, when I’m not acting as a Queen’s Knight?

A: An adventurer and explorer who appeared in Castal and Estea. The mentor of Claude and the other S-rank adventurers. The owner of the first conqueror of the Estea Labyrinth. Probably something like that.

Yeah… that actually checks a lot of boxes for standing out.

Honestly, it’s strange that I’m not more famous.

A: That is because you rarely appear in public, and because the Queen and princess have been working to keep matters from becoming a big deal. Cattleya, in particular, made great efforts during the labyrinth conquest.

I see.

Now that I think about it, there was also potential trouble regarding the identities of Cynthia and the others who conquered the labyrinth.

Since nothing ever came to me, I hadn’t worried about it, but Cattleya must have worked hard behind the scenes.

A: In the end, a policy of “non-interference” was adopted. A connection to the Advance Trading Company was also suspected, and it was judged dangerous to meddle carelessly.

So it’s not like I’m unnoticed, exactly.

Maybe it’s about time I seriously step onto the main stage…

But if I do, I feel like I’ll just get saddled with pointless responsibilities. Like becoming the Demon King or something…

Of course, I’d refuse with all my might if it came to that, but even the trouble of refusing would be annoying.

Well, I’ll think about that later.

“I have no intention of spreading it. I will take this as a sign of trust.”

“Yeah, do that.”

Honestly, I like Ash quite a bit.

That aside, what’s with Kuroa spacing out over there?

“Kuroa-san? Is something wrong?”

Tapped on the shoulder by Ash, Kuroa snaps back to her senses.

“Hah! N-no, it’s just… for some reason, when I looked at that girl, my heart started to feel unsettled…”

Kuroa stares intently at Blue.

《Blue, do you have some kind of connection with this dragonkin?》

《…I do. She was one of the attendants from the Tenri era who went missing four years ago during a battle with a dragon. I heard there was no body found, but to think she was alive…》

That’s closer than I expected.

Come to think of it, after seeing Kuroa in the Elgant Theocracy, I never did tell Blue about it.

Blue looks at Kuroa (formerly Yoiyami) with nostalgia.

Kuroa, too, though she has no memories, seems to feel a sense of familiarity.

Even if it’s amnesia, it probably isn’t at the level where everything is irretrievably lost.

“Could it be that she has something to do with Kuroa-san’s lost memories…?”

“No comment.”

Blue completely shuts him down.

《Is that okay?》

《It’s fine. If she remembers on her own, that’s one thing, but I don’t intend to say anything myself. Both of them are in different positions now, after all…》

Even if she regains her memories, things can’t just go back to the way they were.

At this point, no one except my subordinates can come and go from the “Dragonkin Sanctuary”.

If we were to bring Kuroa back to the Dragonkin Sanctuary, we’d have to explain things to some extent.

But I can’t give that level of special treatment unconditionally.

If Blue seriously begged me, I’d probably think about it. Conversely, Blue must have thought she couldn’t ask me that much.

In the first place, we don’t even know whether Kuroa, with her memories restored, would want to go back…

“Let’s get going already. That’s why we came here, right?”

At Blue’s words, Ash nods, looking a little disappointed.

“…Yes, that’s right. Then everyone, please follow me. If you stray more than 20 meters away from me, you will be affected by the Mist of Confusion, so please be careful.”

Saying that, Ash enters the forest.

At that moment, the mist clears only around Ash. About a 20-meter radius.

“As you can see. If your visibility worsens along the way, that means you’re being affected by the Mist of Confusion, so just keep moving. Eventually, you’ll make it out of the forest.”

So it’s not one of those forests where you can never get out once you enter. It kindly sends you back, apparently.

“However, you can only exit the forest once per day. The second time, you’ll wander the forest until you die.”

Looks like you get one chance per day.

Well, since you can retry after a day passes, I guess you could say it’s merciful?

A: To begin with, only those involved know that rule. Outside, it’s well known that you can enter once and come back, but there is no second time, and no one tries entering again on another day.

That makes sense.

Not many people would risk their lives to test something like that.

“If we get separated, I’ll come to pick you up, so please wait at the entrance. In that case, let’s enter again tomorrow, just to be safe.”

“Got it.”

Even though I answered that way, getting separated from a 20-meter radius doesn’t seem very likely.

We’re not children, after all.

“Then let’s depart.”

It took less than ten minutes to realize that this was a flag.

Guided by Ash, we proceed through the forest.

There don’t seem to be any markers, but Ash’s steps show no hesitation.

Simply clearing the mist doesn’t automatically lead you to the elf village, it seems.

Me? If I used the map and various other things, I could probably get there easily.

《Jin-sama…》

《Yeah, I know. But it’s not really my place to say anything.》

I’d noticed even before Maria spoke up.

That there was an enemy approaching us right now…

World Tree Guardian

LV200

\<Flight LV5> \<Gatekeeper LV10>

Notes: A guardian that protects the World Tree. Eliminates external enemies.

Looks like we’ve completely tripped the security system.

What did we do wrong, I wonder?

A: When forces related to Labyrinth Rulers, Calamity Dragons, Spirits, Miasma or Miasma Spirits, or the Final Trial enter the forest, the guardian activates.

Yeah, that’s not something you can fix with a little effort.

Spirits, Miasma Spirits, the Final Trial, a Labyrinth Ruler with the power of a Calamity Dragon. I’m Shindo Jin. Nice to meet you.

Leaving it alone probably isn’t an option.

“Huh? This presence, could it be!?”

Before I can say anything, Ash notices.

Ash, you really don’t have any skills, right?

“Everyone, run! An enemy is coming. At the very least, we have to get out of the Mist of Confusion!”

“Yeah!”

We run, careful not to stray more than 20 meters from Ash.

“Just a little more!”

Ah, yeah, this won’t make it.

The World Tree Guardian will attack before we get out of the Mist of Confusion.

Keeping everyone within the 20-meter radius in that situation might be difficult.

So, I casually throw a small pebble.

It hits the World Tree Guardian directly and sends it flying. That buys us some time.

Huh? The Mist of Confusion? I don’t know about that.

And so, we passed through the Mist of Confusion (lol).

The mist and forest are gone, replaced by open plains.

We still have to go a bit farther to reach the elf village.

“Huh? The guardian is down? It looks kind of beaten up?”

The World Tree Guardian lies there, not getting back up.

“That is the guardian that protects this elf village. It seems you were recognized as enemies. Do you have any idea why?”

“I might… have a few ideas.”

About five of them.

“So you do… I see. In that case, there’s nothing we can do. You can’t reason with that thing, so the only way to protect ourselves is to defeat it. Jin-san, I’m very sorry, but could you lend us a hand? Even weakened, it’s a bit much for me alone.”

Ash’s level is 50.

Abnormally high for his age, but taking on a level 200 guardian would be tough.

“Of course. Rather, Ash-san, you can step back if you like.”

I’m probably the target anyway, so that would be safer.

“I can’t do that. This is our mistake.”

He seems to think it wouldn’t be right to leave dealing with it entirely to me, the guest.

This is fundamentally different from how the Ruby siblings think.

That said, it would be hard to assume I met this many NG conditions, so I don’t blame Ash either. It’s not something you could check in advance…

“Kuroa-san, please step back.”

“My apologies.”

Kuroa, who is actually a non-combatant despite her cool dragon form, withdraws.

“The others… seem fine.”

Everyone besides me is ready for battle.

Ash also draws his sword and takes a stance.

Me? I don’t. Free hands.

Ah, the World Tree Guardian is getting up. It’s trembling.

If I had to describe the World Tree Guardian in one phrase, it would be “a wooden winged mannequin”.

Somehow, it has a lazy, labyrinth-like design.

Its weapon is a wooden sword, but it cuts better than most metals.

It can fly. Its top speed is decent, but it’s not very agile.

As the World Tree Guardian stands, it points its sword at us.

“Here it co-…”

In the middle of Ash’s line, the World Tree Guardian collapses into pieces.

“…mes.”

Yeah, unfortunately, it didn’t come.

I didn’t think a single pebble would completely wipe its HP.

A: A critical hit landed. It’s the type of guardian that dies instantly if its core is destroyed.

That’s kind of a pathetic way to go…

“Jin-san, did you do something?”

“I made a preemptive attack.”

Since there’s no need to hide it, I nod and answer Ash’s question.

I said preemptive attack, but it was more like a warning shot.

That warning shot just happened to erase its HP…

Incidentally, there are no remains of the World Tree Guardian.

Seems it uses the same specifications as labyrinth guardians.

“I knew you were strong, but to this extent…”

I’m glad to have exceeded Ash’s expectations.

“Jin-san, after coming all this way, I hate to say it, but now that the guardian has been defeated, going to the elf village may be dangerous. This information will certainly reach the village. If things go badly, the entire elf village might become your enemy.”

That’s certainly possible.

But after coming all this way, I don’t want to be turned back…

“I will head to the elf village to explain things. Jin-san, please use the mist to leave the forest. I will make this up to you later…”

“Then we’ll come along for that explanation. And if the elves tell us to leave, we’ll leave. It would be far too wasteful to come all this way and go back without doing anything.”

We tripped the guardian’s security, but we haven’t been told to leave yet.

In that case, it’s not too late to hear them out.

“It’s dangerous, you know?”

“What is?”

Honestly, I don’t feel threatened by the elves of the elf village.

“…All right. I’ll try to persuade them as much as I can, but please don’t expect too much.”

“Please do. Also, is there a possibility of fighting?”

“I want to believe there isn’t, but it is possible. …If it does come to a fight, could you leave it to me alone? I’ll incapacitate everyone.”

He says something incredible so calmly.

Even though there are plenty of elves in the village with level 100 or higher.

“I’m fine with leaving the fight to you, but if danger approaches, I’ll retaliate, okay?”

“That can’t be helped. I’ll do my best to make sure it doesn’t come to that. And in the unlikely event something happens, I would appreciate it if you didn’t kill anyone who attacks you. They’re my compatriots…”

“Understood. I’ll make the effort.”

I’m not saying I can. I’m not saying I will. But I’ll make the effort.

“Thank you.”

And so, we once again head for the elf village.

“From here, we’ll proceed again on riding dragons, but there is one point of caution. Please don’t gain too much altitude. Make sure you stay below 20 meters.”

So the Mist of Confusion has a hitbox in the air too?

I just asked Alta about that.

“In fact, the Mist of Confusion spreads not only through the forest, but also through the air. From above, this area also appears to be covered in mist. And if you fly above a certain altitude, about 20 meters as I mentioned, you’ll get caught in the mist even from inside.”

Yep, that was it.

Looking at the sky from here, there’s no mist.

But that doesn’t mean the effect of the Mist of Confusion is gone… it’s hard to understand.
