“If you get caught in the mist while in the air, you won’t be able to see your surroundings, which is dangerous. If that happens, descend immediately and walk through the forest to exit.”

This, too, seems to be allowed once.

We proceed while consciously maintaining low altitude.

The least stable flyer is Kuroa, which I laugh about internally.

After about twenty minutes, the elf village comes into view, so we land on the ground.

“There are armed people gathering.”

“When the guardian moves, it’s that serious of a matter.”

Near the entrance of the elf village, there is a group of armed elves. About twenty of them.

As you’d expect of elves, many are equipped with bows or dressed like mages.

All of them are over level 100. The top 20 levels in the elf village. In other words, elites.

Judging it an emergency due to the activation of the World Tree Guardian, they hurriedly prepared for battle.

They can probably see us too, but the tense atmosphere hasn’t dissipated.

To avoid provoking them, we decide to proceed on foot from here.

Once we get close enough, the armed elves head toward us as well.

And then, the two groups come face to face.

“Stop.”

The expressionless, imposing elf at the front says so.

Imposing… or rather, he really is important.

Name: Gosh

Gender: Male

Age: 1111

Race: High Elf

Title: Chief of the Elf Village, Protector of the World Tree

So he’s the chief.

At a glance, he looks like a man who’s just reached adulthood, but that’s just because high elves age slowly in appearance. Within the village, excluding the storytellers, he is the oldest.

So the chief is also a high elf and a protector of the World Tree.

Since he’s male, he doesn’t have the “Princess Shrine Maiden” title.

“Ash, these are the guests Scarlet mentioned, correct?”

“Yes, they are Jin-san and his party.”

Jin and his merry companions.

“I trust you’ve noticed. Someone seems to have met the conditions, causing the guardian to activate.”

“Indeed, the guardian came to us.”

“And judging by the situation, you defeated the guardian… I suppose I should say ‘as expected of Ash’.”

Huh? Does he think Ash defeated the guardian?

“But the guardian exists to protect the elf village. Since it recognized these individuals as external enemies, we must eliminate those enemies.”

Excluding the chief, the elves’ displays turn red. Enemies.

Huh? Instead of expelling us, they’re going straight to elimination? And by elimination, do you mean killing?

“Please wait! They are not external enemies! They have no intention of attacking this village! They merely happened to meet the guardian’s elimination criteria by accident!”

Ash raises his voice in defense.

Huh? …Well, yeah, the village, right? Probably… I think we won’t attack it?

“Intent is irrelevant. Reasons are irrelevant. Once elimination targets have passed through the forest, there is no option but elimination.”

That’s what you call having no room to maneuver.

“Then at least exile them outside the forest! We were the ones who invited them! Killing them for that is far too unreasonable. You gave permission to let them enter, didn’t you, Chief!”

“Indeed, I was persuaded by Scarlet and allowed them to enter the village. However, that was on the premise that they were not elimination targets. Now that they are elimination targets, that promise no longer has any meaning.”

The chief replies flatly, without expression.

“I do not know which factor caused them to be deemed external enemies, but once one sets foot in the elf village, elimination targets are permitted no end other than death.”

This is definitely heading toward combat.

“Ash, you alone are excluded. Without you, these individuals would pose no threat. Obey us quietly and assist in their elimination.”

Huh? Aren’t we being seriously underestimated?

A: He is estimating your strength based on the resources he can observe.

According to Alta, like a labyrinth, the World Tree can obtain more resources from those who are stronger within its domain.

The chief is in a position akin to a labyrinth guardian for the World Tree, and has the authority to confirm the amount of resources obtained within the domain.

Since the resources obtained from your group were extremely small, he judged you to be no threat.

Incidentally, no resources can be obtained from a Labyrinth Ruler, so the amount from you is zero.

Most of the resources from your other companions are diverted to the Estea Labyrinth due to the effect of \<Bond of Contract>, so almost none flow to the World Tree.

Regarding resources, since it is unclear who would benefit, you deliberately avoid letting them flow to other labyrinths and the like.

As mentioned earlier, rather than “not releasing”, it is more accurate to say “changing the destination”.

This policy was decided around the time we left the Dragonkin Sanctuary, so in fact, we were not releasing resources even in the Mermaid Kingdom.

There is a huge difference between “zero” and “a small amount”.

“Small” alone would indicate weakness, but “zero” implies some underlying reason.

The chief is at fault for not knowing or considering that.

“I refuse. Turning my blade on guests I personally guided here is something my pride will not allow.”

“Foolish.”

The foolish one is the chief.

“So be it. Everyone, ignore Ash and annihilate them.”

At the chief’s command, the twenty elite elves ready their weapons.

“Jin-san.”

“Leave it to you.”

“Thank you.”

We step back, leaving the fight to Ash.

“Here I go.”

Saying that, Ash draws his sword from its sheath and dashes forward.

We also keep our distance so as not to interfere.

“Take this! ‘Fireball’!”

“Now! ‘Thunder Bullet’!”

“‘Ice Ball’!”

The elves fire off level 1 spells, the fastest to cast.

Unfortunately, elite or not, they don’t have \<Chantless>.

It doesn’t feel like it because we use it so casually, but \<Chantless> is actually a very rare skill.

The spells fly toward the charging Ash.

But Ash doesn’t dodge them. He swings his sword and erases them.

It doesn’t look like he cut them down. They seemed to vanish just by touching the blade.

Ash’s sword is a good one, but it has no effect that erases magic.

And Ash has no skills. …Could it be a “Trait”?

“Trait” refers to individual characteristics with various effects.

Unlike skills, they don’t change easily, and since they are information engraved into the soul, they don’t appear on the status screen.

To learn someone’s ‘Trait’, you have to touch them.

I haven’t touched Ash, so I don’t know his ‘Trait’.

Still, few ‘Traits’ have an influence on the level of skills.

If he has an effect similar to \<Hostile Magic Nullification>, it would be extremely rare.

“Magic won’t reach Ash! If you’re going to target with magic, aim at the external enemies, and point your bows at Ash!”

At the chief’s command, the mages change their targets.

The waiting archers aim at Ash, while the mages aim at us.

The five armored front-liners appear to be guards for the back-line.

Arrows fired by the archers fly at Ash.

But Ash dodges them by a hair’s breadth.

“Tch, so close!”

The archer groans in frustration.

No, it wasn’t close.

It’s true he dodged by a “hair’s breadth”, but more accurately, he dodged so that it would be a “hair’s breadth”.

He just didn’t move any more than necessary.

Ash then closes in on the back-line.

“Don’t let him!”

“You’re too slow.”

“Wha!?”

A front-liner with a shield steps in front of the back-line, but Ash at top speed sidesteps around the shield.

To the front-liner, it must have looked like Ash suddenly vanished.

Ash then kicks one of the front-liners away.

“Guh!?”

Ash easily sends a larger elf flying.

Next, Ash targets the mages.

The mages had begun chanting level 2 or higher spells.

Since there’s distance between the mages and us, level 1 spells would be easy to dodge or have little effect.

Ash pulls knives from his item box at his waist.

Then he throws them at the mages in the order their chants are about to complete.

“What!?”

“Gah!”

“Tch!”

Whether they dodged or got hit, the chants were interrupted either way.

Since none of them have \<Chant Interruption Resistance>, once the chant stops, they have to start over from the beginning.

“Uoooh! What!? Guh!”

A front-liner with a sword charges at Ash while he’s in his throwing posture.

The next moment, a leg sweep plus heel drop slams him onto his back, knocking him unconscious.

After that, the elves fall one after another.

Attacks on us are also shut down as they occur.

Though he carries a sword, Ash mainly uses martial arts to defeat opponents. The weapon is used only to clash with other weapons. For long-range attacks, it’s knives…

Ash’s fighting style feels specialized for combat against people. He can handle many opponents at once if they’re human.

Conversely, he would struggle against stat monsters that can’t be dealt with through tricks.

“Haa!!!”

Little by little, the front-line thins, the back-line even more so, and the final front-liner collapses from a palm strike.

That one’s handy since it deals damage through armor.

And so, the elite elves are wiped out, leaving only the old man chief.

Ah, the elves aren’t dead. They’re all just cleanly unconscious.

---

**AN:** What will become of the chief!?

From next time on, there will be consecutive reveal chapters. About one-third of this work’s mysteries and foreshadowing will be made clear.

+++

## **183: The Storyteller and the Emperor**

**AN:** It looks like I am going to have to take a break in terms of progress after all. I have barely been able to write for almost a month.

---

“With this, we cannot eliminate them. Chief, please give up on elimination.”

After knocking out the elite elves, Ash declared this to the chief.

“I will take responsibility and escort them outside the elven village.”

In this situation, there was no way to say we were going to sightsee the elven village.

It was unfortunate, but we should probably give up this time.

“No! There can be no option other than elimination of outside enemies!”

Even so, the chief did not abandon his hardline stance.

And then, the chief chose his final measure.

“I can no longer afford to choose my means! ‘I, Gosh, a vassal of the World Tree, command this! Guardians, manifest yourselves!’”

As the chief chanted something like a spell, numerous magic circles appeared in the air.

Passing through those circles were, just as the chant said, the guardians of the World Tree.

Uh… there are only fifteen of them.

Alta, what kind of function is this?

A: It is a function that consumes a massive amount of resources to create guardians of the World Tree, a privilege granted only to the “Protector of the World Tree”. It is one of the last-resort measures that ignores proper procedure.

It seems the chief really wants to eliminate me at all costs.

If he goes that far, then I suppose we have to accept it.

“W-What!? He summoned the guardians!? I did not know such a thing was possible…”

If Ash is surprised, then it must be a little-known ability.

“Ash. This is my trump card. How long do you think you can fight against this many guardians?”

“Ugh…”

Ash probably understands that he is at a disadvantage… that this is a hopeless situation.

Well, it is hopeless for Ash alone, anyway…

I walked over to Ash at a leisurely pace.

“Ash-san, it is fine to destroy those, right? No need to hold back, correct?”

“Y-Yes. But with those numbers…”

“Then can you leave it to us this time? While we are at it, I would like to clear up the chief’s misunderstanding.”

The misunderstanding that we are weak should be corrected here.

“…Understood. I will leave it to you.”

Ash seemed to think things over, but in the end, he entrusted it to us.

“Alright then, this time everyone fights. Match your levels to the opponent at around 200, and each of you take down at least one. The dragon-rider group can handle something like that too, so you are participating. Time limit is one minute. There is no penalty, but if you go over, I will wipe out the rest myself.”

We could annihilate them instantly with overwhelming power, but this time I want to show that everyone is strong.

Hearing my instructions, everyone took up a combat stance.

“Hmm. So you intend to fight yourselves. In that case, I am spared the trouble of eliminating Ash. Very well. Do it, guardians!”

At the chief’s command, the guardians of the World Tree charged at us.

Incidentally, since the guardians of the World Tree have no ranged attacks whatsoever, all of them flew in to close the distance.

It is a waste that they have wings and can fly, but cannot make use of it due to having no ranged means of attack.

Since this is an elven village, they could at least have given them bows…

The scattered companions faced off against the guardians of the World Tree.

There are fifteen guardians, and eight companions excluding myself. If each person defeats two, that is enough.

Their stats are lowered to around level 200, but their skills and equipment remain unchanged, so they should not struggle.

Maria pierces a vital point in a single thrust, Sera cuts one clean in half, Sakura burns one away, Mio shoots one down, and Dora smashes one flat.

The three dragon-rider girls, not used to solo combat, each defeat one using \<Dragon Magic> in dragon form.

Dora’s \<Dragon Magic> is excessive firepower, so I have told her not to use it in group battles. Sakura’s magic is also restricted to low-tier spells.

Although I said the time limit was one minute, the fight ended in less than thirty seconds.

Guardians without intelligence are about this much.

Naturally, I never had to step in.

All the guardians vanished, and the chief was left dumbfounded.

“I-Im-Impossible… The guardians… completely wiped out…”

Ash and Kuroa also looked as if they had seen something unbelievable.

“To think they were this strong… I still have much to learn…”

“Could they possibly be stronger than Scarlet…?”

A: Master, they are here.

Oh, that was earlier than expected.

“S-So the guardians were not enough… If only, if only I could manifest more guardians…”

The chief muttered something dangerous with trembling, half-mad eyes.

If he were to summon more guardians of the World Tree, it would consume most of the World Tree’s resources. Naturally, the mist of confusion would disappear, and the chief himself would not escape unscathed.

Because it would clearly exceed the authority of the “Protector of the World Tree”.

-DOOOOOON!!!-

However, the chief’s desperate final move ended in failure due to an impact that struck immediately afterward.

Something heavy fell nearby, the shock spread, and a cloud of dust rose.

“Stop it, Gosh!”

From within the rising dust, a woman’s voice rang out.

“L-Lady Lily!? Why are you here!? You should not awaken yet!”

“If you go on a rampage while consuming that much resource, I will wake up whether I like it or not.”

When the dust cleared, standing there were two people: the Crimson Empire’s emperor, Scarlet Crimson, and the elven storyteller, Lily.

To put it simply, Scarlet had made a huge jump and landed while carrying Lily.

“Looks like we made it in time.”

“Indeed. It was fortunate that you were nearby.”

Despite her manner of speech, Lily looked no more than about ten years old.

She looked even younger than Dora, who is growing rapidly.

The silver hair common to “Princess Shrine Maidenes” was so long it reached the ground… no, it clearly extended beyond her height. Scarlet seemed to be holding it gathered up.

Overall, she shared the common impression of a “Princess Shrine Maiden”, but she also had distinct traits.

Yuria is “serious”, Ulysses is “gentle”, (Yuri) Suzu is “valiant”, Yuriela is “fierce”, and Lily is “fragile.”

“Gosh. You should stop doing anything further, it’s meaningless.”

“Why should I stop!? Outside enemies must be eliminated!”

“I am telling you that it is meaningless. What I asked of you was not that. It was the peace of the elven village and its people. Your role was to choose the best course according to the situation instead of relying on inflexible guardians, yet you ended up just as inflexible yourself. How regrettable…”

“I-I am terribly sorry…”

From the chief’s earlier behavior, it did not look like he was responding flexibly to the situation at all.

“Even if they met the conditions for rejection by the World Tree, they were guests of Letto-boy and judged acceptable by Ash-boy. If you had not interfered unnecessarily, it would not have become such a big matter…”

To begin with, the guardians of the World Tree are not automatic interception devices. They do not deploy without the approval of the “Protector of the World Tree”.

In other words, things were escalated from the very first move.

“Now then, we cannot leave our guests unattended forever.”

“Should I put you down?”

“Please.”

Scarlet set Lily down on the ground.

Standing on the ground, Lily wobbled slightly, then sat in seiza on the ground without caring that her clothes would get dirty.

“On behalf of the elven village, I apologize for Gosh’s discourtesy. I am truly sorry.”

And then she performed a perfect prostration.

Do high elves have a culture of prostration? Suzu did a naked prostration before too…

Come to think of it, she is representing the village while ignoring the chief. Is that okay?

Isn’t the chief the only one who can represent them?

A: Lily’s authority over the World Tree is higher. Gosh’s role is essentially to act as Lily’s proxy.

I see.

So although she is usually asleep, Lily is actually the highest authority in the elven village.

“Please stop! You are the most precious person in the village! You must not prostrate yourself!”

“A subordinate’s misconduct is a superior’s responsibility. It will not be settled unless I apologize. More importantly, Gosh, you should prostrate yourself as well.”

“B-But…”

“Quickly!”

When spoken to so forcefully, even the chief could not resist.

Reluctantly, the chief lined up beside Lily and prostrated himself.

“Jin-san, I know it is not my place to say this, but please. Could you forgive the chief?”

Ash spoke apologetically, but I was a bit troubled as well.

“Um… I was not particularly angry to begin with.”

“Huh?”

Ash blinked in confusion.

“I understand that I look suspicious, so it cannot be helped if guardians were sent after me. Before coming here, I had already accounted for the possibility of combat and being caught up in it. We both accepted that, so there is no reason for me to be angry.”

If anything, I do think the chief’s actions were a bit excessive, but after everything was over, he apologized with a prostration, even if reluctantly.

With no fuel to feed the flames of anger, there is nothing to ignite.

“I see. That is a relief.”

“By the way, there is one thing I would like to ask. Should we leave this place?”

I asked Lily.

Incidentally, Lily, the chief, and Scarlet are not objects of respect to me at present, so I have no intention of using honorific language.

I cannot let myself be killed, but if they tell us to leave, leaving is not a problem.

I also told Ash that “if the elves tell us to leave, we will leave”.

That declaration is still valid, so it is better to confirm first.

“Then, you should lea-“

The chief’s words were cut off when Lily drove an elbow into his solar plexus.

The chief writhed in agony.

“No, I would like you to come into the village if possible. You came all this way, and to send you back after only discourtesy would reflect poorly on us. We cannot do much, but at least allow us to entertain you as guests. If you truly dislike it, I will not force you to stay…”

“No, I would love to accept the invitation.”

“Very well.”

In that case, I will gratefully accept the hospitality.

“Looks like everything is settled. Man, for a moment there I wondered how this would turn out.”

With things calming down, Scarlet, who had been quiet until now, joined the conversation.

“Sorry about that, granny. Caused you trouble.”

“There is no need for you to worry, Letto-boy. It was good experience for Gosh as well, and… considering the outcome, it was resolved peacefully.”

“Well, the other side looks like corpses everywhere.”

Where Scarlet looked, the bodies (not dead) of elves defeated by Ash were lying around.

“Still, from what I can see, none of them seem seriously injured.”

It seems she grasped their condition with just a glance.

“That is good to hear. Ash-boy has grown stronger.”

“No, I still have a long way to go.”

“Do not be modest. I never expected you to brush aside the elite elves so easily. Oh, right. Ash, Kuroa, good work. You helped a lot. Were there any other problems?”

“You are welcome. Please ask Ash about that.”

“There were problems. It would be awkward to say here, so later…”

Ash seemed reluctant to speak.

It is a royal scandal, after all. You would not want to say it out in the open.

“So there were problems after all… Well, it cannot be helped.”

Scarlet seemed to have expected it.

Then he turned his gaze toward me.

“So, since Ash brought you here, you must be Jin and company. Wow, you are lined up with nothing but monsters.”

“Hm? Do you not already know who I am?”

From the information so far, I thought he had called me here due to a connection from before reincarnation, like Sharon of the Regalia Beastman Kingdom, but Scarlet’s manner of speaking did not sound like he was addressing an acquaintance.

“No, I do not know the current you. What I know is my past life. Even then, I do not have all my memories, so it is debatable whether ‘know’ is the right word.”

Scarlet said this without hiding anything.

In other words, Scarlet is a reincarnator of the type whose memories did not fully carry over.

So far, there seem to be two types of reincarnators: those like Mio and the demon Naruse mother and daughter, who retain all their memories, and those like Tiramisu, whose memories are fragmented.

Tiramisu barely remembered her previous self at all. Considering that she remembered much of the common sense of her previous world, there must be memories that fade easily and memories that remain.

“You are not surprised?”

“Do you want me to be surprised?”

When I asked, Scarlet shook his head.

What the heck. If you wanted me to be surprised, I would have made a big show of it.

“No, I am relieved. Just like the fragments of my memory said, Jin really is a genuine monster.”

Is that really something to be relieved about?

Anyway…

“There is one thing I want to ask.”

“What is it?”

“Do you have any intention of invading the Kingdom of Estea?”

There are many things to discuss.

But to decide future policy, this is something I have to ask first.

“Hm? …Ah! Information via Rouge, huh! If she told you that much, it is safe to assume Rouge has submitted to you. Well, in a way, that is the safest place for her, so I guess it is fine.”

With just that one line, Scarlet seemed to grasp a lot.

He muttered to himself for a while, then looked at me as if he had realized something.

“Ah, sorry, sorry. To get to the point, I have no intention of invading the Kingdom of Estea. What Rouge told you is just a pretext to drive her out of the empire.”

Once again, he said it plainly. It seemed to be his true intention.

With this, it is probably safe to say there is no reason to eliminate Scarlet.

We will ask for details later, but for now, it is a relief.

“Hm? That means Rouge is back too, right?”

“She has returned.”

“Ugh, what a pain…”

When Ash confirmed it, Scarlet made a very displeased face.

“Letto-boy, Jin-dono, standing around talking is not ideal. Why not enter the elven village? I cannot sit on the ground in thin clothing forever.”

After the prostration, Lily had remained seated on the ground.

Her outfit is a priestess-like white robe, relatively thin.

“That is true. Then let us head into the elven village for now.”

“Gosh, gather people and tend to the elves who are unconscious.”

“Understood.”

Looks like we can finally enter the elven village.

We followed Lily, who was being carried by Scarlet (due to her weak legs), and set foot into the elven village (the residential area).

《It really looks exactly like an elven village, just like you would imagine.》

《Yeah, it is easy to understand.》

As Mio said through telepathy, the elven village was extremely close to the image one would expect.

All the buildings are wooden, with none taller than two stories.

There are many log cabins, but also treehouses built on top of trees.

There are even wonderful houses where a huge tree is hollowed out and used as a dwelling, something you only see in fiction.

The residents wear simple clothes, and neither men nor women wear any accessories.

There are no shops; everything is basically bartered.

All the elves are watching us from a distance, but perhaps because Lily is with us, none of them approach or speak to us.

Incidentally, we have not seen the ‘World Tree’ itself on the way here.

When I asked Alta, she said that it is “concealed and not visible”.

“We passed through in a hurry earlier, but it has not changed in nine years.”

“Of course it would not. There is no way an elven village changes in just ten years.”

Scarlet retorted to Lily.

“This is my home. Though, it has been nine years since I last entered it.”

We arrived at the second-largest house in the elven village.

The largest one belongs to the chief.

“We clean it regularly, and since we were told that Lady Lily would awaken, we have been cleaning every day for the past few days, so it should be quite clean.”

“I am sorry even though I barely use it. Perhaps it is time I relinquish this house.”

“Please do not say that. The cleaning staff consider it an honor.”

As seen from the chief’s attitude, Lily is treated with great respect.

“If you say so, then I will keep it as is. Come in.”

Scarlet, not Lily, opened the door, and we entered Lily’s home.

“Then, I will take my leave.”

The chief went off to gather people, so we parted ways.

Inside the house, Scarlet seated Lily in a wooden rocking chair.

The storyteller vibe intensifies.

“It seems this will be a long story. Are there enough chairs?”

“We have simple chairs.”

We sat on stump-like chairs handed out by Ash.

The elven village vibe intensifies.

“Now then, where should I start…”

Scarlet folded his arms and thought.

“I want you to start with the reason you called us here.”

“Yeah, that makes sense. I will skip the details for now and give you the conclusion.”

At last, it seems we will learn Scarlet’s objective.

“I want Jin to help me punch the goddess.”

Scarlet’s goal was precisely an act of rebellion against the god of this world.

Judging from his eyes, he did not seem to be joking.

“That alone does not explain much. Let me explain step by step.”

“Please do. Honestly, I still cannot see the whole picture.”

“If you could, you would be a monster.”

Scarlet chuckled.

“Granny Lily here is the storyteller of this village. She has lived an absurdly long time and knows tons of things nobody else knows.”

She looks like a little girl, though…

Oh right, our former calamity dragon was similar.

“Most of what I am about to tell you is what I learned from granny. And there is still a lot I do not know. Jin, I want you to listen to this together with me and then decide whether you will cooperate with my goal.”

Listening to the elven storyteller and hearing Scarlet’s true intentions were both on the agenda, so getting it done at once is honestly convenient.

Though the story is likely to be very long…

“First, about the goddess who created this world. You may have noticed already, but she actually has a pretty awful personality.”

“If the Goddess Church heard that, they would come after you. Though, I did expect it…”

Based on her actions so far, you really cannot say she has a good personality.

“You are not surprised, are you, Jin? Then do you also know about skills?”

“Yeah, I know about those too.”

There is no point talking to someone ignorant about skills, and no reason to hide it from someone who knows.

“Man, this is fast. I am glad I can skip the annoying explanations. …The goddess gave certain skills disadvantages. Disadvantages that can be life-threatening if you are unlucky.”

So it really was the goddess who added the disadvantages.

Scarlet’s \<Proof of the Hero>.

That is a skill with an obvious life-threatening disadvantage. If you are poor, you go bankrupt from food expenses, or you starve to death.

And \<Hero> is probably the same.

“You know about this too, huh… This damn disadvantage. Do you know why it was added?”

“No, I do not know that much. But I assume it is for some rotten reason.”

Given the goddess’s personality, it is easy to imagine.

“You are right. It is a rotten reason. ‘Because it is a skill that could threaten me, I gave it a disadvantage so the holder would not grow.’ …That is why the goddess added disadvantages.”

“If she is going to add disadvantages, why not just erase the skill? Or better yet, why create such skills in the first place?”

“That is impossible. The goddess can create things, but she cannot erase them. All she can do to naturally occurring skills is add disadvantages afterward.”

Important information just keeps coming out.

This is something even Alta does not know, right?

A: I am sorry. It is almost impossible to obtain information related to the goddess.

No, I am not blaming you.

I came here precisely to fill that gap.

“Do skills naturally occur?”

“Yeah. Even if the goddess created this world, there are many parts she leaves to natural generation. Skills are the same. …To add disadvantages after the fact just because she does not like something that formed on its own is beyond childish.”

Scarlet spat it out in utter disgust.

Seeing this, Maria and Sera nodded slightly in agreement.

They are both victims of skills with disadvantages, just like Scarlet.

“It is the same for the dragonkin.”

At that point, Lily, who had not spoken until now, interjected.

“Hm? What do you mean, granny?”

“Dragonkin are not a race prepared by the goddess. They are a naturally occurring race.”

“…What about the disadvantage?”

“Simple. They are socially treated as monsters and targeted for extermination.”

Lily answered Scarlet’s question calmly.

I suddenly thought of something and asked.

“Could it be that monsters without magic stones…”

“All of them are creatures that fall outside the goddess’s intentions. Most of them have bodies constructed no differently from humans. By deliberately treating them as monsters, she obstructs their interaction with humans. Though, under certain conditions, some are apparently treated as human…”

That explanation made sense.

Why are dragonkin treated as monsters instead of people?

Why can Dora become an adventurer when other monsters with magic stones cannot?

Simply put, the goddess insists they are monsters, but biologically they are no different from humanoid races.

“Dragonkin are especially unfortunate, though… She even prepared dragons as their natural enemies.”

“Seriously? Dragonkin existed before dragons…?”

Normally, you would think dragons came first, and dragonkin came later.

Well, in this world, there does not seem to be a biological connection between the two, so maybe it is not that strange… probably.

“She implanted hostility toward dragonkin into dragons, and at the same time made dragons enemies of humans, thereby forcing dragonkin into the position of being enemies of humans as well. …As harassment, it is nearly perfect.”

“Dammit…”

Both Lily and Scarlet did not hide their displeasure.

I had imagined it to some extent, but she really is a terrible goddess.

“…By the way, Scarlet, it seems Jin-dono’s group also has dragonkin. Has the barrier of the ‘Hidden Land’ been lifted?”

Lily asked while looking at Dora, Blue, Leaf, and Mikazuki.

Oh? Does she have something to do with the ‘Dragonkin Hidden Land’?

“On my end… it seems Kuroa does not know anything. She was found near ruins in the Crimson Empire with amnesia, so that is understandable…”

“Those ruins must be the ‘Dragon Gate.’ It connects to the distant ‘Hidden Land.’ If something has happened, I would like to know…”

It seems she is quite deeply involved.

It would be a shame to send her on a wild goose chase, so I should give a brief explanation.

“It would be pointless to go. The gate is already closed.”

“What!? What on earth happened…?”

I see. Lily knows a lot about the past, but she does not grasp the entire current situation.

In that regard, I might have an overwhelming advantage.

“Can we leave that story for later? It feels like we are getting off track.”

“Y-Yes. Please tell me later.”

“I want to hear it too. If it concerns Kuroa, I cannot ignore it.”

“Understood. For now, let us continue.”

I nodded in response to their requests.

“To get back on topic, as you heard, the goddess spreads various disadvantages… malice. One of them caused someone to die. The goddess did not directly do it herself, but the cause lies with her. …That is unforgivable, right? You cannot be satisfied without punching her at least once, right?”

Could the person caught up in it be Vermilion?

“That is why I decided to punch the goddess. I will absolutely make her take responsibility.”

Scarlet clenched his fist.

“Until now, I planned to do it alone. But recently, the situation changed. And following my past life’s memories, I decided to ask you, Jin, to help.”

It looks like next we will be hearing about Scarlet’s past life.

**AN:** The truth keeps getting revealed one layer at a time.

If anything contradicts previous information, assume it was a reflexive mistake.

I should have decided the content of this chapter first, after all.

## **184: Memories of a Past Life and the Truth**

**AN:** Explanatory chapters continue.

I am going to reveal, without mercy, the things I have been dragging out until now.

---

“Before that, could you tell me about those past-life memories of yours?”

“I do not mind, but before that, I want to ask you one thing. Do you need an explanation about past lives?”

“I know about them, but I would rather you explain. I do not want any differences in understanding.”

If there are differences in understanding at important points, things get troublesome later, so it is necessary to align our perceptions at key moments.

“Got it. In this world, reincarnators like me, who are born with memories of another world, a past life, are extremely rare. As far as I know, all of them were originally Japanese. Apparently, even the old lady does not know the details.”

“Even I have many things I do not know.”

Lily is a storyteller, not a sage.

She probably was not originally focused on gathering knowledge.

“The problem is that not everyone retains all of their past-life memories.”

“I know someone who remembers common sense and such, but forgot most proper nouns.”

That refers to the dinosaur girl.

“I am close to that pattern. I have memories of common sense and such, but I can hardly remember individual episodes. On the other hand, useless bits of knowledge sometimes remain. So I do not know who I was in my past life.”

That is a relatively severe case.

“But you remembered me, right?”

“Rather than remembering, it would be more accurate to say I recalled it. On the way back from the Elgant Theocracy, when I was thinking about Queen’s Knight Gene, the name Jin came to mind first. From there, my memories returned in a chain.”

As expected, he has figured out that ‘Gene equals Shindo Jin’.

Not many people know that I use the name Jin.

They might make the association, but very few could be confident about it.

With that in mind, let us think this through.

…Based on Scarlet’s demeanor and skills, there is one person who comes to mind.

“Even so, I still cannot remember myself. And remembering Jin more clearly than myself feels strange…”

“There is one person who comes to mind. Someone who was close to me in that world, knew the information Scarlet knows, and…is probably already dead.”

“Who is it? Tell me.”

Scarlet asks with a serious expression.

“My best friend, Asai Yoshinobu. A man who was once summoned to this world as a Hero, and who is thought to have died in this world.”

I cannot say for certain that he died, because I did not witness it.

Common sense would say he must be dead, but common sense is often shattered.

“…No good. I cannot remember. But that name sounds familiar. Am I Asai Yoshinobu? And wait, if a Hero dies in this world, can they reincarnate?”

“Considering the role of a Hero, the goddess should never allow such a thing. However, if you ask whether it is an absolute rule, I cannot say for certain.”

After all, spontaneous occurrences, in other words, random events, are built into the rules.

That is practically the same as permitting all kinds of exceptions.

Although, the goddess usually handles such exceptions by assigning penalties…

By the way, Lily just said something interesting again.

What is the role of a Hero?

“For now, we will be satisfied with having identified my possible past life.”

Scarlet does not seem to be thinking that he absolutely must remember.

Probably because he is living his current life to the fullest.

As for me, even if Scarlet were Asai’s reincarnation, I have no intention of treating someone who reincarnated and lived for decades without Asai’s memories as Asai.

I will treat him as another person who happens to have memories.

“At the very least, there must have been a connection between my past life and Jin. Even I am surprised at how naturally Jin’s presence fits.”

I also feel a sense of nostalgia when I talk with Scarlet.

I do not know whether that is because it reminds me of talking with Asai.

“Throughout my life so far, my past memories, and the intuition and impulses they bring, have always been on my side.”

“What are you suddenly talking about?”

Are you bragging about your intuition? I am not planning to lose either.

“Just listen. This is not completely unrelated to what I am about to explain.”

If you put it that way, I have no choice but to listen.

“Normally, you would not trust someone you have never met. Of course, you would not reveal a plan like ‘punching the goddess’ either. But my intuition screamed at me, strongly, to trust Jin and ask for his cooperation. Faced with choosing between common sense and intuition, I chose intuition without hesitation.”

Unlike Sharon, who has clear memories, he summoned a stranger based only on fragmentary memories and revealed a plan on a world-upending scale.

…That would normally be impossible.

“Originally, punching the goddess is a reckless thing to begin with. Honestly, the chance of success is low. If you are going to gamble with bad odds anyway, why not add another gamble of trusting Jin? If that gamble pays off, the odds of the main plan succeeding increase. There is risk, but the return is big.”

Scarlet grinned and continued, “And besides…”

“According to my past-life memories, ‘If you are going to gamble, do whatever it takes to get Jin on your side’.”

I see. If someone knows me, that would be the obvious conclusion.

When the conversation reached a stopping point, it happened to be a good time, so we decided to have lunch.

That said, only we actually ate.

Lily had just woken up and was not hungry, and said she would use the free time to greet the villagers.

Scarlet was outside the house listening to Ash talk about what happened in the Crimson Empire. Of course, Kuroa was with them.

“Finally, elf food!”

Seeing the dishes brought out by the elves of the village, Mio said happily.

Like what Ash served us, it was mainly vegetable-based.

There were also dishes with meat, like stir-fried vegetables.

There are many fields around the elf village, wild animals in the forest, and they also practice animal husbandry, so they do not seem to lack food.

There are no monsters, so monster meat is unavailable.

《I’m looking forward to it!》

“Indeed.”

“I am glad we could join Master this time.”

“If we had stayed behind, we would not have been able to eat this.”

The gluttons (Dora, Sera, Mikazuki, and Leaf) are also happy.

…Come to think of it, Scarlet also has a Mark of the Hero like Sera, so as a drawback, he needs to eat a lot, right?

How does he deal with hunger?

A: He had ration balls in his inventory, the same kind that exist in the elf village. He probably procures them from the elf village.

Ration balls are not the “ration balls” made by Sakura’s magic, but actual emergency food rations.

According to Alta, they are highly nutritious and filling, but taste extremely bad.

So bad that you absolutely need a palate cleanser afterward…

Once all the dishes were laid out, we started eating.

“The seasoning is light, but the flavor is good, so it is easy to eat… It suits me…”

Sakura praised the food, which is rare.

“It is rare for Sakura to praise food.”

“Well, food in tourist areas tends to be heavily seasoned, so it often does not suit Lady Sakura’s tastes. Lady Sakura usually eats lighter dishes at the mansion, you know?”

“Now that you mention it, that is true.”

I nod in agreement with Mio’s explanation.

At food stalls, they need to attract customers with smell, so strong seasoning is the norm.

At the mansion, there are several menu options, and Sakura often chooses lighter dishes.

Meanwhile, the hungry group focuses on meat.

“Is something wrong?”

I look at Leaf, who is eating the vegetable dishes happily.

Leaf has a plant-type dragon form, but eats both vegetables and meat.

“Leaf, which do you like better, meat or vegetables?”

“I like meat better. Most dragonkin like meat.”

《Dora too!》

“Naturally, I am the same.”

“Well, I do not dislike vegetables, but meat gives me more strength.”

It seems unanimous that dragonkin like meat.

Regardless of what their dragon form is, it has nothing to do with their diet.

As Blue said, they do not dislike vegetables either, and everyone is eating happily.

Apparently, Japanese children often dislike vegetables, but Dora does not.

“So, Mio. Do you think you can recreate this?”

The food was highly rated overall, and I would love for her to recreate it.

“Perfectly!”

“Well done!”

If I take Mio to various places, she can learn the local cuisine.

The scary part is that it often ends up tasting better than the original.

If the local chefs found out, they would probably cry.

“The pickles seem unique to the elf village. We hardly saw any until now, but there seem to be many kinds here.”

“Pickles, huh. Come to think of it, I have not eaten them since coming here.”

“Pickles are deep. I never really tried them seriously over there. Maybe I should give it a real shot?”

“Then please start with fukujinzuke. I am a fukujinzuke-with-curry person.”

Mio also has curry in her repertoire, but there is no side dish.

It is not enough to complain about, but if she is motivated, I would like to ask.

“What are you talking about?”

《Tell us!》

“I’m talking about a type of cooking that I haven’t tried before.. It’s basically a sour type of food.”

Mio starts explaining pickles to those who do not know them.

When she mentions that curry becomes even tastier, Dora’s eyes light up.

《Dora wants to eat it too!》

“Having a sour accompaniment… I am interested as well.”

The culture of placing a different type of flavor alongside a dish is not very common in this world.

“Fukujinzuke is recommended.”

“I prefer rakkyo…”

“Either way, it is pickles. All right, I will try it!”

Since Sakura is in the rakkyo camp, Mio’s motivation finally ignites.

For the record, I am a moderate fukujinzuke person, so I will eat rakkyo too.

“Mio-chan, please teach me how to make that ‘fukujinzuke’ that Jin-sama likes.”

“Ah, yes.”

Since I showed strong interest, Maria would not let it go.

By the way, is making pickles covered by the Cooking skill?

A: No.

In this world, pickles are not considered cooking.

After finishing our meal, we rejoined Scarlet’s group and Lily, and resumed listening.

Scarlet was the first to speak.

“I heard from Ash that my brats caused you trouble in the imperial capital.”

He looks displeased, though not as much as when talking about the goddess.

“Well, it was troublesome, yes.”

“I cannot do it here and now, but I will apologize later without fail. I will execute everyone involved. I will make sure they never act on their own again within my reach, so rest assured.”

He says he will execute his own children without changing his expression.

Asai from my original world would not go that far.

“Father, could you please reconsider at least the execution?”

“No. Those who make light of the emperor’s orders have no right to live as royalty.”

Ash pleads for leniency, but Scarlet does not listen.

The same exchange apparently occurred when Ash explained the events of the capital.

“In the first place, ‘do not do anything unnecessary to the emperor’s guest’ should go without saying, right? Why do they not understand that this is an important matter?”

He is absolutely right.

Laying a hand on someone the emperor personally declared as his guest is the act of a complete idiot.

“It is unpleasant to say, but is this blood at work? Using power without restraint, yet looking down on authority above them. They really resemble those women.”

“Father, not everyone is like that.”

Ash admonishes Scarlet, who spits it out.

“Those women” probably refers to Scarlet’s wives who were executed.

“I know. That is why I want to entrust the next emperor to someone even slightly better.”

“Is it true that you plan to step down as emperor?”

“Yeah. There is no way someone planning something like punching the goddess should be emperor, right? Once I have prepared to a certain extent, I plan to abdicate and do things my way.”

Unintentionally, most of what the First Princess wanted to know has been revealed.

If I recall correctly, Carmine had one more thing she wanted to ask.

“By the way, who are you going to hand the throne to? Rouge, now that she is back?”

“Huh!?”

Scarlet looks like he heard something unbelievable.

“Are you serious about making Rouge emperor? No matter how you look at it, she is not suited for it.”

“Ah, yes.”

Even from Scarlet’s perspective, Rouge is no good.

“It is not strictly by age, but Red or Carmine would be appropriate. Carmine has a slight edge.”

Oh, Carmine would be happy to hear that.

Whether I will tell her or not is undecided…

“What about Ash?”

“I have no intention of making Ash do something that trivial. Ash does not want it either.”

Ash nods at Scarlet’s words.

“Yes, I plan to travel the world someday. Sorry, Father, but this is something I decided long ago.”

“Yeah, Vermilion asked me too. I will keep my promise.”

“Um…”

Ash looks a bit awkward.

“Hm? Ash, have you not explained your parents?”

“No, I have not.”

“Ash’s parents are my younger brother Vermilion and an elf from this village. He wanted to travel, so I took him in as my own child to teach him common sense and such. Any questions?”

“No.”

Thanks to Scarlet’s simple explanation, there is nothing I want to ask.

Well, there are things, but this does not feel like the right timing.

Still…

“You have been leaking a lot of confidential information about the Crimson Empire, have you not?”

State-level secrets keep pouring out.

“Compared to the plan to punch the goddess, a nation’s secrets are nothing.”

“Well, that is true, but…”

“Besides, when it comes to Jin, my past-life memories are screaming that it is better to speak without holding back. So if there is anything else you want to ask, go ahead. I will answer most things.”

It does make you feel like cooperating when someone is that honest.

I sense no lies or malice in Scarlet’s words.

All right. While we are at it, I will ask this too.

“Do you remember killing a fox monster that had taken human form about ten years ago?”

Needless to say, that refers to the golden fox, parent of Tokoyo, killed by Scarlet.

Honestly, I am not unwilling to cooperate with Scarlet.

But if I do not understand Scarlet’s stance regarding the golden fox, I cannot commit to cooperation.

I will not put Tsukiyo and Tokoyo in danger.

“…”

Scarlet looked deeply regretful.

“…I did not expect that topic to come up here. …Of course, I remember.”

“What do you think about it?”

“I regret it. It is one of the greatest regrets of my life. Those two should not have been killed. …Who did you hear that from, Jin?”

He deliberately said “those two” instead of monster.

“A friend of that fox. They talked about Scarlet before dying.”

“I see… What happened to their child?”

“That friend is raising them. …More importantly, did you know the child was hidden?”

I had heard that Tokoyo’s parents hid Tokoyo so she would not be found.

“I realized it at the very end. …Back then, I mistakenly believed all monsters were inherently evil. If I had known there were monsters who cared for their children, I would never have thought of killing them.”

For Scarlet, ten years ago must carry significant meaning.

If possible, I want to know about it.

“There are too many prerequisites to explain that properly. …May I tell you about my past? I think it would be easier to understand if I explained it chronologically.”

“Please do.”

I am also very interested in the life story of a man who was isekai-reincarnated and became emperor.

“All right. But it will take time, so I was thinking of leaving it for later. Is that fine?”

“Yeah.”

“Now then, what were we talking about… Oh right, it was about the brats. I said I would apologize later, but do you have any demands, Jin? If you want to kill the three yourself, I will accept that too.”

Scarlet casually says something extreme.

The three are probably Ruby, Jonathan, and Rose.

From his words, I sense indifference toward his own children.

Yet, I can see consideration for relatives who are not his children, like Ash and Rouge.

“No, I found them annoying, but I do not hold enough of a grudge to want to kill them myself. …Rather than killing them, why not give them to me? Especially Ruby and Rose.”

Jonathan already had his unique skill stolen, so his priority is low. Or rather, I do not want him.

“What? You want women? Come to think of it, all your companions are women.”

“No, I want skills rather than women. Those two have rare skills.”

I deny Scarlet’s amusing misunderstanding.

As for those two, just stealing their skills would be enough, but I somehow felt it would be better to keep them alive. Jonathan is different.

“…So you really can grasp the details of skills, Jin.”

Scarlet says it like it is someone else’s problem.

“Scarlet, can you not see skills too?”

“I can, in a sense, but for others’ skills, I can only tell the rank and rough direction. I can tell a bit more about my own skills, though…”

According to him, Scarlet’s eyes show skill levels and effects in a very rough manner.

That is one of the effects of Scarlet’s Heavenly Eye skill.

“When it comes to knowledge about skills, the old lady Lily knows more.”

“I only have knowledge. I cannot see people’s skills. Do not lump me together with you.”

“I can vaguely see them. The old lady has knowledge. What about you, Jin?”

I generally keep my abilities hidden, but explaining what I can do should be fine.

“I can see detailed skill information for both myself and others. I can see rank, that is, level, as numbers, and I can confirm effects as clear descriptions.”

“Seriously? That is a complete superior version…”

When skills and special abilities do similar things, there is an incomparable difference.

In most cases, special abilities are a complete superior version of skills.

“Jonathan’s skill does not matter, but Ruby and Rose’s skills are too valuable to waste, so I want to keep them with me. As an apology, I will make them apologize themselves.”

“…Wait, how exactly do you plan to ‘take’ them? Make them your wives?”

“Eh, no.”

I immediately reject that.

Now that you mention it, saying that to their father would be like asking for his daughters.

“I can also use \<Slave Arts>, so owning them as slaves would be best.”

“It’s coming from me, but telling a parent to hand over their children as slaves is quite something, is it not?”

“Normally, I would not say that. But the parent himself is saying he will execute them and leave the decision to us. I am just saying I would like to take them as slaves.”

I have never enslaved children by forcibly separating them from their parents (though I have taken parent and child together).

If Scarlet does not want that, I will not force it, but if he did not want it, he would not talk about execution in the first place.

“Externally, we will need to say they were executed, so you will not be able to use their status as princesses, but if you are fine with that, I do not mind handing them over to you as slaves.”

“That is fine. I have no intention of using their status as princesses.”

“All right. I will hand them over once we return to the capital.”

Secured two slaves with unique skills!

Even so, Scarlet really has no interest in his children.

After thinking for a moment, Scarlet asked another question.

“You met Carmine in the capital too, right?”

“Yeah. There was nothing unpleasant in my interactions with Carmine.”

Aside from her treatment of Rouge, Carmine had no issues.

“Yeah, she is one of the more balanced ones among my brats. Like I said, she is one of the candidates for next emperor.”

Scarlet paused there.

“So then, Jin. Do you have any intention of taking Carmine as your wife?”

“What are you suddenly talking about?”

Scarlet suddenly says something strange.

“It is not that strange, is it? I recognize Jin’s power. I have decided to trust you and ask for your cooperation. If so, I would want to bring you into the family, right?”

“I refuse. I do not want to marry someone I am not particularly close to, and I do not want to get involved in power struggles. I do not want to call you father-in-law, and I have no intention of spending my life in this world, so I do not want to marry.”

Just off the top of my head, that many reasons not to marry came out.

“Jin, do you plan to return to your original world?”

However, what Scarlet was concerned about was a different part.

“Yeah. At least once, I plan to return to my original world. One of my reasons for coming to the elf village is to ask the elven storyteller about how to return.”

“I see. Old lady, do you know how to cross to the other world?”

“Hmm…”

When Scarlet asks, Lily groans thoughtfully.

“There is a way, but it is extremely difficult.”

“Really? Since there are reincarnators like me and transmigrators like Heroes, reverse travel does not seem like it should be that difficult…”

As Scarlet says, normally it would not seem that hard, but even Sakura’s \<Magic Creation> has not achieved it.

That is why we came all the way to the elf village.

“To explain conceptually, this world is positioned below your original world. Transmigration and reincarnation are, in other words, like falling down a waterfall. Climbing up a waterfall would be nothing but ‘quite difficult’, would it not?”

It was the first time I heard that worlds have positional relationships, but Lily’s explanation was very easy to understand.

If there is a height difference, it makes sense that going against it would be difficult.

“But there is a way, right? Otherwise, you would not say ‘quite difficult’ from the start.”

Lily said it was not impossible, but ‘quite difficult’.

When I ask, Lily nods.

“Yes, it is not impossible. It simply means you cannot move directly. In other words, if there is an intermediary location, it is not impossible.”

So instead of climbing the waterfall directly, you take a detour to the top.

The ‘quite difficult’ part is probably passing through that intermediary location.

“The name of that intermediary location is the Goddess’s Domain. This also relates to Scarlet’s story, but the goddess is not strictly in this world. She resides in a space different from the two worlds.”

That the goddess is not in this world was, in a sense, expected.

If she were easily reachable, she would be more widely known.

“I came here to ask how to reach the Goddess’s Domain, and how to punch the goddess.”

To punch the goddess, Scarlet needs to go to the space where the goddess resides.

To return to my original world, I also need to go to that space.

You could say that Scarlet’s and my goals, or rather, our means, align.

However, in my case, I also have to consider returning here afterward.

Come to think of it…

“Scarlet, what do you plan to do after punching the goddess? In the first place, you keep saying ‘punch’, but it is safe to assume you do not intend to kill her, right?”

Scarlet consistently says “punch the goddess”.

He has never once said “kill”.

If the goddess is alive after being punched, will she forgive Scarlet?

It may be an extreme way to put it, but would killing her not leave fewer loose ends?

“Well, it is natural to wonder about that. To give you the conclusion first, I do not plan to kill the goddess. And the odds are high that I will be able to return safely after punching her.”

“Explain.”

I cannot understand why that would be the case.

What I understand least is the goddess’s stance.

“I do not know the details either. But apparently, once you reach the Goddess’s Domain, your right to punch the goddess and your right to return safely are guaranteed.”

Saying something incomprehensible again, Scarlet looks toward Lily.

“Yes, that should be the case. Furthermore, when returning safely, you should also be able to choose your original world.”

That means that ‘punching the goddess’, ‘Scarlet returning safely’, and us ‘returning to our original world’ can all be satisfied at the same time.

That is truly killing three birds with one stone.

It sounds great, but what concerns me is…

“You are being unusually vague. Can you not say for sure?”

“Hmm. It seems that memories related to that have been erased.”

Lily says something quite unsettling.

“In fact, my memories have also been tampered with by someone. Therefore, there is no guarantee that everything I say is correct. I have knowledge, but the source of that knowledge has been erased. That is why I can only tell ‘stories’.”

There is no guarantee that the stories told by the ‘storyteller’ are true.

The ‘storyteller’ herself acknowledges that.

“Actually, the ‘bad-odds gamble’ I mentioned includes the credibility of Lily’s ‘stories.’ Evidence of memory manipulation is a significant risk.”

“Even so, you wish to hear the story if there is a possibility.”

Manipulating memories means there was a truth inconvenient to someone.

That inconvenient truth could very well harm us, but it is not certain.

Scarlet decided to take that gamble.

“I knew the risks from the start. That is why I want Jin.”

“Hey, I am not interested in being proposed to by an old man…”

“That is not it! It is to increase the odds of the gamble!”

“So you are only after my body.”

“Stop it!”

Seeing this exchange, the possibility that Scarlet was Asai in his previous life increases a little.

“You make such tasteless jokes…”

Despite saying that, Scarlet seems to be enjoying the banter.

“Anyway, my plan requires Jin’s cooperation. At first, I planned to accomplish everything alone, but considering the information I gathered afterward, that is probably impossible.”

“Indeed. If it were just you alone, Red boy, it would be extremely difficult. No, we can say clearly that it would be impossible. Of course, with Jin-dono’s cooperation, it is a different story.”

I am being rated quite highly.

“It is about time. May I finally tell you my past?”

“What do you mean ‘about time’?”

“To get Jin’s cooperation, my past is necessary, right? There is also the matter of the fox monster. …It is about time I want a firm commitment of cooperation.”

Up to now, I have not explicitly said “I will cooperate”.

If he wants a commitment, then yes, it is indeed about time.

---

**AN:** Next time will be Scarlet’s oral history (a standalone story).

It is connected to the main story’s timeline, but Scarlet’s past will be told in a digest format.

I judged that writing it in the normal story format would be close to a full volume.

**Editor’s Note:** It’s as long as normal chapter, so expect it tomorrow.

+++

## **184.5 – Oral Tradition, Chapter 4: Scarlet’s Circumstances**

**AN:** As announced, this is Scarlet’s oral tradition.

Though it’s called an “oral tradition”, I think it’s fair to say it’s basically part of the main story.

The format is the same as Sera’s oral tradition. I’m not sure anyone still remembers that, though.

---

From the moment I was born, I had knowledge from my previous life and a clear sense of self.

And along with that came an abnormal level of hunger.

I only realized it after learning about Skills, but that hunger was a drawback of one of my Skills.

…You knew that?

What, that woman has the same Skill as me? Seriously…?

…Yeah, I can’t see Jin and the others’ Skills.

I can tell they have a lot of Skills, but the individual details feel like they’re hidden behind something like fog.

That’s Jin’s power too, huh. At this point, nothing surprises me anymore.

Anyway, back to the story.

Those days were hell, plain and simple.

Imagine being constantly starving, fully self-aware, and only able to cry.

There weren’t enough wet nurses with just one. I think there were over ten of them.

A baby sucking from one woman after another, lined up side by side. That’s a pretty horrifying image, right?

On top of that, I had awareness and knowledge, but no memories.

I couldn’t even understand who I was, and I had to keep living as a baby, stewing in frustration.

If only my mind had been that of a baby too, how much easier it would have been…

She wasn’t a reincarnator, right? I envy her.

My twin younger brother, Vermilion… Leon, unlike me, was a completely normal baby.

I checked a few times just in case, but he never showed any signs, so I quickly concluded he was different and used him as my model for “proper baby behavior”.

Since we were twins, we were naturally raised together except during feeding times.

I had troublesome knowledge and troublesome Skills, but sometimes I thought things balanced out.

One of the advantages of my Skill was heightened physical ability.

Normally that’s a benefit, but a child with excessively high physical ability is dangerous in more ways than one.

Because I had knowledge and self-awareness from my previous life, I could avoid mistakes in controlling my strength.

I even suspected that my past-life knowledge existed specifically to control my high physical ability.

According to Lily, it was apparently just pure coincidence.

By the way, what was that woman… Sera, was it? Like?

I see. Always hungry and unable to exert strength…

That’s one solution in its own way, but I wouldn’t call it enviable.

Despite the constant hunger, I grew up more or less smoothly, but as twins, Leon and I were constantly compared.

I had past-life knowledge and high physical ability.

Leon, on the other hand, due to the drawback of a certain Skill, couldn’t learn other Skills.

…Yeah, the \<Hero> Skill. Of course you knew.

And you’d already predicted Leon was a \<Hero> even before coming here?

I really won’t be surprised anymore.

That girl has the \<Hero> Skill too!? You say you won’t surprise me and then pull this…

Still, it makes sense that you could predict the \<Hero> Skill just from what Rouge told you.

Seriously, you people are like a jack-in-the-box.

At the time, I didn’t know about Skills, but I at least understood that I had the advantage.

That’s why I felt bad for Leon, who was constantly being compared to me. …In hindsight, that was completely unnecessary.

Because Leon exceeded my expectations and remained my equal.

Yeah, he didn’t have talent in the sense of Skills.

He lacked the “talent to gain Skills”, but in exchange, Leon had the “talent to think”.

That’s on a completely different level from Skills.

Even as a child, Leon was someone who thought deeply about things.

When something didn’t go well, he’d thoroughly analyze what went wrong and how to make it work next time.

Then he’d make up for whatever was lacking through relentless effort.

“If you push thought and effort to their limits, they can rival talent.”

That was Leon’s creed.

He really was an incredible guy.

I took inspiration from his way of thinking in a lot of areas too.

But even thought and effort have limits.

The most obvious example was ‘martial arts’ …in other words, combat.

In the Crimson Empire, individual martial strength is valued, and it’s something an imperial prince can’t avoid.

Because of my Skills, my physical ability grew at an abnormal rate as I aged.

Leon, due to his Skill, had slow physical growth.

Naturally, Leon learned a combat style focused on technique rather than physical power, but martial arts are heavily influenced by Skills.

It didn’t take long for Leon’s approach to hit its limits.

Even so, the fact that he stayed evenly matched with me until we were past ten years old was amazing…

At the time, about eighty percent of the soldiers couldn’t beat us. In other words, we were at least on par with the elite of the military.

After we passed ten, the win rates gradually started to skew.

By the time we were eleven, I won over ninety percent of the matches. Every so often, I’d lose to some outrageous trick, but still…

Once the gap formed, Leon didn’t try to push himself recklessly to compete.

He kept training, but the number of mock battles clearly dropped.

Instead, he put more weight on academics, which could be called his strong suit.

“If Let is going to master ‘martial prowess’, then I’ll master ‘scholarship’. I think you’re better suited to be emperor, Let, so I’ll do my best to support you.”

I wasn’t bad at studying either, but I couldn’t match Leon’s thinking.

We both had our biases, but together we were a perfectly balanced pair of brothers.

By the way, art was Leon’s specialty.

He loved drawing, and whenever he traveled, he’d always draw at least one picture of where he’d been.

What, you went to the museum?

Yeah, I was the one who had Leon’s works exhibited under a pseudonym.

“I’m a bit embarrassed to have people see my immature paintings, but I think art that’s never seen has no reason to exist. Someday, if there’s a chance, I’d like people to see them…”

He said something like that once.

Displaying them under his real name would’ve been a hassle, so I pushed to have them exhibited without revealing it was Leon.

Apparently, they’re pretty well received?

Oops, I got sidetracked.

Anyway, a few years later, when I was twelve, our third sibling was born. Our younger sister, Rouge…

Hey, I want to ask one thing. Did that guy Asai, who’s a candidate for my past life, have a younger sister?

Ah, so he did.

When Rouge was born, I felt a strange sense of nostalgia.

It wouldn’t be strange if I’d had a sister in my previous life, right?

But if I really did have a sister, that just makes Asai even more likely to be my past life.

Even though I felt that nostalgia, I was already in the military by then, going out to subjugate monsters, so I didn’t interact with her much.

Leon, who was also in the military but studying administrative work, had more contact with her.

She was the youngest and probably doted on.

It seems our parents spoiled Rouge quite a bit.

I heard Leon sometimes voiced concerns, but they rarely listened.

A few years after that, it was finally time for me to take wives.

Yeah, of course it was a political marriage.

Given my birth, I understood it logically, but because I still had a Japanese mindset, I couldn’t accept it easily.

That’s probably why I couldn’t love my wives.

You’re saying I had a lot of kids for someone like that?

That wasn’t my choice. It was the country’s.

The number of royals was declining, so they decided it was time to replenish them.

Political marriages plus being treated like breeding stock, there’s no way love would grow in that situation, right?

And the same applied to my wives.

What they wanted was seed and power, not me as a person.

Naturally, I never felt any affection from them.

Even if I was told a child was born between us, there was no way I could love that child.

The fact that their upbringing was handled almost entirely by their mothers’ families, leaving me little involvement, was another problem.

If I’d had frequent contact from birth, maybe affection could’ve grown…

No, Leon didn’t have a wife in the Crimson Empire.

Probably because it was almost certain I’d become emperor. There were no nobles willing to marry their daughters to Leon.

In this country, there’s a huge gap between the emperor and everyone else.

Even now, I think they were fools with no eye for talent.

As you know, I have a Skill that lets me see Skills.

At the time, I didn’t know about Skills, but I could see that something ‘bad’ was clinging to Leon.

I researched all kinds of things, trying to remove it.

I even thought that if I could remove that ‘bad thing’, it’d be fine for Leon to become emperor.

Yeah, I had no interest in the throne even back then.

Leon said I was better suited to be emperor, but I thought Leon was the better choice.

I’m emperor now out of necessity, not because I wanted it.

Then, twelve years ago, I finally found a way to remove Leon’s ‘bad thing’.

You could call it hiding in plain sight?

It was the Crimson Empire’s national treasure, a treasured sword passed down through generations.

Its name was “King Sword: Divine Bestowal.” Yeah, this sword. Or rather, its original form…

As the next emperor, I was to use the treasured sword.

In our country, even a national treasure is used if it’s a useful weapon.

When this sword cut a monster, the monster’s Skill… at the time it was a more ambiguous concept, would sometimes disappear.

At first I didn’t understand, but after testing it, I realized the sword had the ability to transfer Skills.

It steals the Skill it cuts and gives it to another target. A terrifying effect.

There’s a reason I say it cuts Skills rather than cutting the target’s Skills.

If the part you cut doesn’t contain a Skill, you can’t steal it.

To my “eyes”, Skills look like they’re constantly moving around the body. Only by cutting in sync with that movement does the effect activate.

If you can’t see Skills, this sword is no different from an ordinary blade.

At the time, I was thrilled, thinking it was a weapon made just for me.

By the way, it can only store one Skill at a time, and the next target you cut is forcibly given that Skill.

This comes up later, so remember it.

To my ‘eyes’, Leon’s Skill looked like it was wrapped in something “bad”.

If I could steal the “bad thing” with the King Sword, great. Even if I failed and stole the harmless Skill instead, it was useless anyway, so no problem. Then I could just try again.

See? There was no reason not to do it?

I talked it over with Leon, and we decided to remove his Skill.

He refused the idea of becoming emperor if it worked, though.

In hindsight, that decision was a failure.

Immediately after we succeeded in removing Leon’s “bad thing”, the final trial appeared before us.

The final trial… you know what that is, right?

Yeah. That.

It called itself “Reaper: Mold.”

What’s with that look? Oh, you fought an adventurer with a similar alias?

“Reaper: Mold” said this:

“I am a reaper who hunts those who defy the laws. I never thought I’d be assigned a job. Unfortunately for you, you’ve gone against the rules created by the goddess. This is my first memorable assignment. Sorry, but you’ll have to die.”

Apparently, the goddess doesn’t intend to forgive those who resist the drawbacks she gives.

Naturally, we resisted.

“Reaper: Mold” was absurdly strong, fitting for a final trial meant to hunt those who defy the goddess’s will.

Thankfully, it was humanoid and wielded a scythe, so its attack range was limited, and the damage didn’t spread too widely.

If it had used area magic, I’d have been fine, but the surroundings would’ve been in serious trouble.

With my fully developed body and Leon, who’d further refined his techniques, our teamwork was never inferior to “Reaper: Mold.”

We couldn’t land a decisive blow, but neither could it.

Yeah. If we’d fought head-on, we shouldn’t have lost.

…After a while, Leon’s movements gradually worsened.

There was no way he’d lose stamina that easily, so I asked him why during a lull in the fight.

It was a ridiculous story.

My wives had been poisoning Leon.

To make me emperor… or rather, to eventually make their own children emperor, they wanted to weaken Leon, who was in the way.

But that wasn’t all…

Leon knew it wasn’t lethal poison, so he deliberately accepted it.

He wanted me to be emperor too.

“I never thought it would backfire like this. Please forgive them. I share the blame for not stopping it.”

Leon never spoke a word of resentment until the end.

Even for me, fighting “Reaper: Mold” alone was too much.

But if this continued, it was only a matter of time before Leon fell, then me.

“I won’t last much longer… I’ll create an opening, so I leave the rest to you.”

With that, Leon launched a reckless charge at “Reaper: Mold.”

No, he attacked in a way that made it look reckless.

…At that point, Leon must’ve already resolved himself to die.

Ignoring my attempts to stop him, Leon’s assault continued.

And the moment Leon lost his balance badly, “Reaper: Mold” didn’t miss it.

…The butt of its scythe pierced Leon’s heart.

“…Take care of Ash.”

Those were Leon’s last words.

I didn’t understand them at the time.

Leon died.

But Leon used his body to give me a chance.

I thrust at “Reaper: Mold”, Leon’s corpse included.

Leon adjusted the positioning, using his own body to create a blind spot.

The “King Sword: Divine Bestowal” pierced “Reaper: Mold.”

It was far from fatal, but it definitely struck.

At that moment, the “bad thing” that had tormented Leon transferred to “Reaper: Mold.”

Yeah, from the start, if we’d landed even one hit, we would’ve won.

“Reaper: Mold” panicked.

Most of the Skills it had been using were suddenly unusable.

After that, there’s no story worth telling.

I just killed the pathetic, begging “Reaper: Mold.”

Even after defeating it, Leon didn’t come back to life.

There was no way to call it a victory.

I couldn’t forgive my own inadequacy, and I wanted to curse the goddess to death.

After defeating the final trial, the “rank” of both me and my weapon increased.

I must’ve been raging with fury.

The “King Sword: Divine Bestowal” became the “King Sword: Divine Curse.”

Yeah, it’s read the same.

“Bestowed by the gods” turned into “cursing the gods.”

I couldn’t see it, but I understood the change.

Even after Leon’s funeral, my anger didn’t subside.

At Leon’s request, I let my wives go unpunished.

I didn’t even know how to meet the goddess.

So my anger turned toward the final trial, in other words, monsters.

I hunted every monster around the Crimson Empire.

Even I think I was out of control.

I wasn’t satisfied with just within the country. I even went into neighboring nations.

Oh right.

This was when I killed Ginko.

More precisely, killing Ginko marked the end of that violent period.

That was about ten years ago.

I found the infamous Ginko and attacked without a word.

Since it was a humanoid monster like the final trial, I was especially unhinged then.

Ginko and his wife were strong. Even after realizing magic didn’t work, they didn’t give up.

They used magic as bait and toyed with me in close combat.

But as the fight went on, their movements started to show strain.

That was because they were desperately trying to draw me away from where they’d hidden their daughter.

I only realized they were protecting a child after I’d inflicted near-fatal wounds on both of them.

I felt empty about my actions.

What meaning was there in killing one of the few monsters who cared for their child, just to vent my anger?

…Of course, there was no meaning.

If I could, I would’ve liked to heal them, but I couldn’t use \<Recovery Magic> back then.

Yeah, I learned it later. I worked pretty hard at it.

In any case, faced with two people on the brink of death, there was nothing I could do.

They understood that I’d noticed their child and begged me to save her.

By then, my killing intent was gone, so I agreed.

But if I left the child there, she’d eventually die.

I considered taking her in and raising her, but that would’ve gone against reason too.

I agonized over what to do.

The mother seemed to realize something and told me to leave the area.

I left, uneasy, but followed her words.

According to Jin, someone they knew came and took the child.

Yeah, I’d always wondered. When I went back later, there was nothing left.

And I truly believe I did something unforgivable.

At the very least, I can’t let myself be killed until I punch that goddess.

But I’m prepared to be punched myself.

Same thing as the goddess. It’s about settling accounts.

Yeah, if the chance comes, call me.

After that, I stopped hunting monsters indiscriminately.

Of course, I still kill harmful monsters, but I stopped seeking out harmless ones just to kill them.

And I came to accept Leon’s death in my own way.

First, I started by sorting through Leon’s belongings, which I’d left untouched at my own orders.

During that, I noticed something.

Among Leon’s paintings was one of a tree I didn’t recognize.

Leon never drew from imagination, so there was no doubt he’d seen it in person.

Curious, I began investigating the time when that painting was made.

Leon was meticulous and stored his paintings in order of creation, so it was easier than expected.

During that investigation, I learned of a plan.

My wives were planning to poison Rouge as well.

Rouge had begun to show strength at the time.

Their policy was probably to crush anything that could become a threat.

…I did warn them, you know.

After Leon died, I confronted my wives with the fact they’d poisoned him and told them never to do it again.

Maybe not punishing them, in accordance with Leon’s wishes, was a mistake.

They might’ve mistaken the lack of punishment for forgiveness.

I didn’t forgive them, but if they’d stopped there, there might’ve been hope.

But they tried to do it again.

That was the limit.

I found no value whatsoever in letting them live.

There was evidence too, so I had them all executed.

To be honest, I even found myself envying Ginko and his wife.

Not that I have the right to say that, after destroying them…

That’s why I don’t love my wives or my kids.

Even if they share my blood, they also share those women’s blood, expecting me to love them would be unreasonable.

Like I said before, I barely had any involvement with them anyway.

The kids themselves weren’t guilty, so I didn’t punish them, but I lost all interest.

I left their education to people with no ties to their mothers and kept my mouth shut as much as possible.

I figured I’d just let the least terrible one inherit.

Honestly, I didn’t expect much, but it seems a decent number turned out passably well.

Unfortunately, some didn’t…

Enough about my wives and kids. Back to Leon.

As a result of my investigation, I learned that Leon regularly went into the uncharted region.

Obviously, I had to go?

So I headed into the uncharted region myself.

I nullified the Mist of Confusion with my Skill and quickly arrived at the elf village.

The elf village was full of surprises.

Yeah, the elves were surprised too.

I know, I know. No need for the old lady to tell me.
