The biggest surprise was Ash’s existence.

I never imagined Leon had a child in the elf village.

And on top of that, that the mother had the same Skill as Leon… who could’ve predicted that?

Still, knowing Leon had someone he loved and a child was a relief to me.

That’s when I remembered Leon’s final words.

He must’ve been certain I’d eventually come to the elf village.

When I heard that Ash’s dream was to travel, I decided to teach him about the outside world in the Crimson Empire.

It would’ve been a hassle if people found out he was Leon’s child, so I brought him back as “my” child.

Of course, his mother agreed.

And there, from old lady Lily, I heard many things about the truth of this world… About the goddess’s malice.

…No, it wasn’t possible to hear everything at that point.

Old lady Lily sleeps for nine years and wakes for one.

It’s a system to ensure stable survival as a storyteller.

I arrived right before she went to sleep.

So I only heard the most important things then.

And I decided to punch the goddess, and to prepare over the nine years until the old lady woke again.

Those nine years were spent on preparation, just as I said, so a brief digest explanation should be fine.

First, I became emperor to solidify my base of operations.

I was originally the next emperor anyway, so that wasn’t difficult.

Next, I purged the rot within the country so I wouldn’t get stabbed in the back.

There were more corrupt nobles than I expected. It was exhausting…

After that, I started small conflicts with neighboring nations.

It was to instill a sense of crisis both domestically and abroad.

With the current system, all Demon-related problems would be dumped on the Hero otherwise.

I also raised food self-sufficiency, in case the Crimson Empire ended up ostracized.

The groundwork to sustain the nation independently was already there, so it was easy.

Anything else worth mentioning…?

Hm? Reincarnators in the Crimson Empire?

Oh, you know about that too.

Yeah, besides me, reincarnators are born there from time to time.

I gather them and collect Japanese knowledge.

It’s hard to make effective use of it, though.

…I didn’t mention that yet, did I?

Sending Rouge to the Estea Kingdom’s labyrinth was to protect her.

The goddess’s power doesn’t reach inside labyrinths.

Yeah, she’s a bit dumb, but she’s my precious little sister.

Given the possibility of being dragged into a fight with the goddess, it’s only natural I’d want her somewhere safe, right?

…At that point, the only ones I wanted to protect were Rouge and Ash.

Our parents were already dead, and Ash would probably have left the country by then, so Rouge was the only one I needed to worry about.

To protect Rouge, who knew nothing, the easiest way was to send her into a labyrinth with some plausible excuse.

Attacking the Estea Kingdom was that “plausible excuse”.

I wasn’t serious about it, the miscalculation was that Rouge was far more enthusiastic about labyrinth conquest than I expected.

She understood how dangerous labyrinths are, so I’d hoped she’d take it slower. But she kept charging ahead, and that worried me.

Since the pretense was “labyrinth conquest”, I couldn’t exactly tell her to slow down.

In any case, I’m glad Rouge is safe.

…What? She wasn’t safe?

She ran into one of the Demon King’s Four Heavenly Kings and got turned into minced meat? I don’t understand…

I see, I see. Wow…

…She’s really lucky Jin picked her up.

He enslaved her to heal that state? I don’t get the logic, but I understand.

Well, yeah… just spoil her appropriately.

That’s about it for the nine-year preparation period.

Lastly, let’s talk about recent events.

After seeing many reincarnators, I’ve come to be able to tell whether someone is one.

It’s hard to explain concretely, but I can just kind of tell.

Yeah, of course I noticed Rose.

I also thought it was a dangerous combination.

I went too far when I was unhinged, but normally I don’t like eliminating someone just because they’re dangerous.

So I left her alone until she actually did something.

But once she did, I showed no mercy.

Recently, by coincidence, I encountered one of the Demon King’s Four Heavenly Kings.

That’s when I realized the Four Heavenly Kings are reincarnators.

I got curious and came to the elf village to hear the chief’s story.

No, the chief actually knows a fair amount.

Even if he’s not a storyteller, he’s lived long and heard things from old lady Lily.

What? He knows about twenty percent of the whole picture?

Hard to tell if that’s a lot or a little.

According to the chief, the Demon King can only be defeated by the Hero.

The Four Heavenly Kings are based on souls summoned from other worlds.

If someone other than the Hero defeats a Four Heavenly King, a new one can be summoned.

I figured there was no way to defeat the Demon King without the Hero, so as much as I disliked it, I chose to become a Hero-supporting nation.

You already know this part, right?

And since nine years had passed, I was waiting in the elf village for the old lady to wake up.

That got pretty long, but that’s the end of my story.

If you have questions, I’ll take them.

---

**AN:** If Scarlet and the others hadn’t defeated them, then when Maria’s \<Seal> was removed, “Reaper: Mold” would have appeared.

It would’ve been a tough opponent for Jin at the time, but he probably would’ve beaten it somehow.

And the equipment he had back then, the “Goblin General’s Sword (Rare)”, would have ranked up to Legendary. What a waste…

+++

## **185: The World Tree and the Goddess’s Domain**

After hearing Scarlet’s life story, I understood that many of the questions and uneasy feelings I had, both before and after coming to the Crimson Empire, had been resolved.

In particular, hearing explanations I could accept regarding the “invasion of the Kingdom of Estea” and the “murder of the Golden Fox couple”, which were crucial factors in deciding whether or not to cooperate with Scarlet, was a big deal (whether I forgive the killing of the Golden Foxes or not is a separate matter).

That said…

“For starters, haven’t your actions backfired way too often?”

The \<Sealing> incident, the matter with his wives, the matter with his children, the matter with the Golden Foxes.

“Hah, you’re absolutely right! …Well, most of it was my own fault, so I can’t complain. Especially when it comes to my wives and kids, one of the biggest reasons was that I just didn’t put in enough effort. As for the Golden Foxes, there’s no excuse for that.”

Scarlet said regretfully.

Certainly, depending on how Scarlet had acted, many of the tragedies could probably have been avoided.

Whether he could have predicted those tragedies in advance is another question entirely, though…

Still, there is one thing that bothers me.

Scarlet’s story is, naturally, told from Scarlet’s own perspective.

And in order to keep it short, he likely skipped over quite a few details.

Scarlet said he had no interest in his children and hardly interacted with them, but I don’t think that’s entirely accurate.

For someone who claims he had no interest, Scarlet knew a lot about his children’s personalities and circumstances, and he was even able to talk about them from the standpoint of succession.

For someone who claims he barely interacted with them, Carmine genuinely adored Scarlet, and as far as I know, none of the children ever spoke badly of him.

…Well, there’s no point in digging into things he chose not to talk about.

“I think I’ve heard just about everything I was curious about, so I’m satisfied.”

“So, will you cooperate with me?”

Scarlet immediately asked.

“Honestly, it’s a little hard to decide based only on what I’ve heard so far. What exactly do you need help with? That never came up.”

I can’t promise cooperation if I don’t even know what I’m being asked to do.

It wasn’t directly related to his backstory, so I didn’t ask at the time, but…

“Ah, that part was intentionally left out. It’ll be easier if you hear it together when we talk to old lady Lily. So for now, you don’t need to make a firm promise. Could you at least tell me where you’re leaning?”

“I think I can give you a pretty positive answer. As long as the cooperation doesn’t involve demanding extreme disadvantages, I should be able to say yes.”

“Alright! That’s more than enough for now!”

Scarlet made a small fist pump.

He must really want my cooperation.

“Then next up is old lady Lily’s ‘story’. Personally, the thing I most want to know is how to get to the ‘Goddess’s Domain’, but Jin, what do you want to ask first?”

“Yeah… Lily-san, just who exactly are you?”

What I want to know first is Lily’s true identity.

Given her title of “Princess Shrine Maiden”, she’s clearly connected to the Calamity Dragons, but beyond that, there’s almost no information, making it hard to grasp what kind of being she actually is.

“This time it’s my life story, eh. If I had to put it into one phrase, ‘one of the Primordial Princess Shrine Maidens’ would be the most accurate.”

I had a pretty good idea already.

“In this world, there are calam-“

“Ah, I already know about that part. The ‘Princess Shrine Maidens’ who seal the Calamity Dragons. You’re saying you were one of the first, right? There are four Calamity Dragons, so which one were you the shrine maiden for?”

I cut off the storyteller’s tale.

“W-water…”

Lily answered, looking a bit dejected.

“Jin, wasn’t that a bit harsh?”

“If we skip what I already know, it’ll go smoother, right?”

“Well, that’s true, but still…”

I mean, she’s a ‘storyteller’?

It’s obvious each story would get long, right?

Let’s skip what we can.

“By the way, there are a few things I’d like to ask. Is that alright?”

Ignoring Scarlet’s awkward expression, I continued.

“…Very well.”

“Then first question. Lily-san, did you have parents?”

When someone says ‘primordial’, you can’t help but wonder about their lineage.

“I did not. I appeared in the land where the Calamity Dragon was sealed, already in this form. The knowledge I possess was also there from the beginning. However, I do not know who gave it to me.”

No parents, no change in appearance since birth, and knowledge from the very start.

Hmm…

“Based on the content of that knowledge, I once considered that I might have been created by the Goddess. However, among my knowledge are things that would be inconvenient for the Goddess. I cannot believe the Goddess would deliberately create a being that puts herself at a disadvantage. Thus, the most likely candidate at present is ‘something equivalent to the Goddess’.”

“Yeah, I can’t imagine someone petty enough to intentionally add downsides to skills doing something like that.”

“Agreed.”

“The Goddess is petty and ill-natured” has already become common understanding.

I can’t imagine someone like that creating something that would work against her.

“Second question. What happened to the other three ‘Primordial Princess Shrine Maidens’?”

“They took their own lives long ago. Even with immortality, it seems eternal loneliness was too much to bear. I chose to live on as a storyteller, stabilizing my mind through the World Tree in this land.”

So when Scarlet talked about ‘stable survival’, he was mainly referring to mental stability.

“To be precise, I lost at rock-paper-scissors and ended up becoming the storyteller.”

“You pushed it off on each other, huh…”

Scarlet muttered, apparently hearing this for the first time.

The ‘Primordial Princess Shrine Maidens’ understood that they would eventually choose death, unable to endure the loneliness.

Despite there being four of them, they still felt lonely because the ‘Primordial Princess Shrine Maidens’ shared knowledge and memories.

Though they had individual differences in personality, their sense of being separate individuals was weak, and the loneliness was never eased.

After many events, they arrived at the World Tree, where they left one behind as a storyteller and ended their own lives.

“That ties into what you just said, but what exactly is the World Tree?”

“The World Tree and dungeons are naturally occurring entities, unrelated to the Goddess’s will. What sets them apart is that they possess the property of rejecting the Goddess’s interference.”

“That’s why you sent Rouge into a dungeon.”

Scarlet must have decided to send Rouge into a dungeon after hearing this from Lily.

“Do you know about dungeons?”

“Yeah, I should know them pretty well.”

After all, I am a dungeon ruler.

“Then it will be quicker to explain by comparing them. Both place a specific area under their control, but the conditions differ greatly. Dungeons have a high degree of freedom. They can create spaces underground, or designate territory by placing barriers above ground.”

Though Lily didn’t mention it, dungeons can also be created by placing barriers on the seafloor.

They really are flexible.

“In contrast, the World Tree’s territory is limited to ‘the forest centered around the World Tree’.”

“Hearing that, it sounds like dungeons are superior. Doesn’t the World Tree have any advantages?”

At Scarlet’s question, Lily nodded.

“Of course it does. To begin with, dungeons and the World Tree serve fundamentally different roles.”

“Yeah, if their roles were the same, there’d be no point in having both.”

“Precisely. Though they share similar abilities, their roles are complete opposites. Jin-dono, do you have any idea what those roles are?”

Lily asked me.

Unfortunately, I already had an idea.

And Lily’s words just now confirmed it.

“The direction they head, right? Dungeons generally go underground, downward. The World Tree grows upward. Like you said, the directions are completely opposite.”

“…Correct.”

Lily looked dejected again.

She probably hadn’t expected me to get it right.

Maybe she wanted to explain it proudly herself.

“The original purpose of dungeons is ‘to distance oneself from the Goddess’. The World Tree is ‘to head toward the Goddess’.”

“Ah, so that’s why you said the World Tree’s power is needed to reach the Goddess’s Domain.”

Scarlet said, sounding convinced.

“Indeed. In fact, the Goddess’s Domain is located on the moon. That is why the World Tree grows upward, toward the moon.”

That’s some major new information.

And there’s one thing that stands out.

“If there’s a way to reach the moon, does that mean the World Tree isn’t necessary?”

“No. Even if you went straight to the moon, you would not reach the ‘Goddess’s Domain’. The moon itself is part of this world. In other words, what’s on the moon is merely an entrance. The World Tree has the power to connect this world and the ‘Goddess’s Domain’… the power to open that entrance.”

So just reaching the moon isn’t enough. Figures.

“In short, the way to reach the ‘Goddess’s Domain’ is to grow the World Tree until it reaches the moon.”

At last, the storyteller delivered a shocking truth.

“I see. So that’s how it works. …Then what does the World Tree need in order to grow? Nine years ago, I barely managed to hear that a being outside the Goddess’s intent was the key.”

“Yes. There are two main things needed for the World Tree’s growth. Nutrients called ‘resources’, and beings outside the Goddess’s intent, known as ‘Abnormal individuals.’”

I like the sound of “Abnormal individuals.”

“And these abnormal individuals become the source of the power that connects this world to the ‘Goddess’s Domain’.”

“Tell me one thing. What do those abnormal individuals have to do?”

I raised my hand and asked Lily.

I have plenty of candidates in mind, but how they’re treated matters.

“If you tell me they need to be buried as nourishment for the tree, I’ll have to refuse.”

“What do you take the World Tree for…?”

A “pleasant object”, maybe?

“Simply touching the main body of the World Tree is enough. The goal is for the World Tree to take in the factors of the abnormal individuals. There is no disadvantage to them.”

“Then that shouldn’t be a problem.”

Let’s hope it doesn’t eat things like a carnivorous plant.

Scarlet raised his hand as well.

“I’ve got a question too. How many abnormal individuals do we need? And what kind?”

“There are several conditions for the abnormal individuals. …That said, while the abnormal individuals are important, the more immediate problem is the resources.”

Lily looked extremely uncomfortable.

“I got so focused on the abnormal individuals that I missed it. What exactly are these resources?”

Scarlet asked, apparently unfamiliar with the concept.

“Resources are like nutrients needed to maintain and grow dungeons and the World Tree. When people exist within the territory, resources are generated in proportion to their strength.”

“From the way you’re saying it, resources decrease when you use them, right?”

“Yes, and that’s the problem. …That idiot Gosh just used a massive amount of resources to try to eliminate Jin-dono and the others. As a result, the World Tree is barely able to maintain itself, with no leeway to grow at all.”

Gosh summoning the World Tree’s guardians to drive us out really did a number on things.

Summoning the guardians is equivalent to consuming massive resources.

And because he used an improper method, the consumption was even higher.

“Seriously…”

“Seriously… We used up in an instant the resources we’d painstakingly saved up.”

As with dungeons, if a barrier system relies solely on residents for resources, it often struggles just to maintain itself, let alone save up reserves.

The ‘Dragonkin Sanctuary’ is a perfect example. Lacking resources, cracks formed in the barrier, allowing dragons to slip in.

Creating a system that draws people in and stabilizes resource acquisition, like the Estea Labyrinth, is likely the proper form of a dungeon.

Meanwhile, the Mermaid Country maintains its barrier solely through residents by keeping the barrier small and implementing several cost-saving measures.

“From what you said earlier, resources build up if strong people stay inside, right? Wouldn’t I be enough?”

“At the rate of Red-boy, if you stayed in the village for 1,000 years, it would build up.”

“Seriously…? I was pretty confident in my strength, you know…”

“Even so, that’s still extraordinary. To match the existing reserves in just 1,000 years.”

The problem is that Scarlet won’t live for 1,000 years.

“Then what about Jin and the others? They’d probably generate more than me, right?”

“For some reason, no resources are generated from Jin-dono and his companions.”

Lily tilted her head in confusion.

She probably doesn’t know dungeon mechanics in that much detail.

“Jin, what did you do?”

“I changed where the resources go. All of our resources are going to another dungeon.”

Lily clutched her head.

“You say outrageous things so casually… I’m sorry, but could you share your resources with the World Tree?”

“If cooperation is confirmed, I don’t mind sharing.”

“…So once again, Jin’s cooperation is indispensable.”

Scarlet also clutched his head.

There’s nothing Scarlet can do about this.

“Based on what I’ve heard, I’m not opposed to cooperating. Assuming the resource issue is resolved, tell me what’s needed.”

“Very well. What we need are the types and numbers of abnormal individuals. At least 10 types, and at least 100 individuals. Additionally, for those with the \<Hero> skill, we need factors from five individuals.”

“Just hearing that, I can tell it’s insane… Sounds worth doing, though.”

Scarlet smiled wryly, but the conditions don’t seem that harsh to me.

“There are three major categories of abnormal individuals. The first is skills. The second is race. The third is origin. I’ll explain each.”

With that, Lily stood up and brought out a blackboard from the corner of the room.

The storyteller is well prepared.

“First, skills. This includes \<Hero> and Red-boy’s \<Proof of Heroism>. These are generally innate skills. There are others, such as \<Holy Magic Blacksmith> and \<Branch of the Genealogy Tree>, but since they are not easy to find, I’ll skip the detailed explanations.”

We’ve already found them, actually…

“Second, race. This refers to new races generated by \<Branch of the Genealogy Tree>. Dragonkin and merfolk… Hmm? It seems a new race called angels has been born while I was unaware. These should be relatively easy to find.”

Already found those too…

More importantly, how does she know about angels that were born just recently?

Does her knowledge auto-update or something?

“Third, origin. This includes otherworld reincarnators like Red-boy, otherworld transmigrators without blessings, and those who manage dungeons.”

Ah, that’s ten types.

Numbers won’t be an issue either, since there are plenty of dragonkin.

That just leaves the \<Hero> skill holders.

Beastman, human, hobbit, and an elf hero in the elven village makes four.

We need one more to reach five.

“Now then, where should we start… For now, \<Hero>, \<Proof of Heroism>, dragonkin, and reincarnators are all in this village, so that leaves six types.”

At that, Scarlet shook his head.

“No, that’s wrong. Jin is a transmigrator without blessings, right? That makes it five remaining types. What about the numbers?”

“If we can go to the ‘Dragonkin Sanctuary’, the numbers can be gathered immediately.”

“That place you mentioned earlier… So that ends up being Jin’s job again. The real problem is gathering five Heroes. That’s probably the hardest part. We still need three more.”

Scarlet and Lily continued discussing.

“…No, we only need one more \<Hero>.”

“What? You know where two \<Heroes> are? Impressive… Then that leaves one \<Hero>, five types, and 100 abnormal individuals. If Jin helps, we’ll need to divide roles.”

Ah, there’s a misunderstanding.

“Sorry, but I can’t leave this place. I can’t help directly.”

“I know. I wasn’t planning to ask that much of you.”

“No, I mean, we only need one more Hero…”

“?”

Question marks appeared over their heads.

“I can gather the five types and 100 individuals immediately. I can also gather three Heroes. Adding the one in this village makes four. We just need one more.”

“”…””

The two stared blankly.

“Specifically, I can gather all the examples of abnormal individuals Lily-san mentioned earlier. As for numbers, just like Lily-san said, I can call over 100 dragonkin. For Heroes, we have beastman, human, and hobbit.”

“Seriously…?”

“This day just keeps surprising me… I’ll never forget it…”

It’s an honor to be told that by a storyteller.

I wonder if she’ll tell stories about me someday?

“By the way, may I ask about the ‘Dragonkin Sanctuary’ you said we’d talk about later? If you can gather 100 individuals, does that mean most of them have left the sanctuary?”

“Yeah, I want to know too. What’s going on with Kuroa’s homeland?”

“Even if you call it my homeland, I don’t really remember it…”

Kuroa spoke up for the first time in a while.

“I don’t mind answering, but before that, could you tell me about Lily-san’s relationship with the ‘Dragonkin Sanctuary’?”

I was actually pretty curious.

The ‘Dragonkin Sanctuary’ never mentioned the elven village, but the elven village talks about the ‘Dragonkin Sanctuary’. What’s the connection?

“I had interactions with the progenitor of the dragonkin who created the ‘Dragonkin Sanctuary’. That progenitor was the first dragonkin generated by \<Branch of the Genealogy Tree>.”

So she interacted with Dora’s ancestor.

It may have been so long ago that Lily’s information didn’t remain.

Dragonkin don’t seem like the type to understand the importance of information…

“Long ago, that individual visited this land and interacted with me. They told me of the hardships of being a new race… I shared a great deal of my knowledge with them. Later, that individual created the dungeon known as the ‘Dragonkin Sanctuary’.”

“Hey! The ‘Dragonkin Sanctuary’ is a dungeon?!”

Scarlet shouted.

Information about dragonkin has been spread to some extent, but information about the ‘Dragonkin Sanctuary’ has been completely classified, so there’s no way Scarlet would know.

“Yes, it is a dungeon. To protect the dragonkin, who are abnormal individuals, a dungeon outside the Goddess’s intent was used. Quite ironic, wouldn’t you say?”

The same applies to the Estea Labyrinth and the ‘Mermaid Country’.

“If Jin hadn’t been able to help, we could have looked for dungeon-related abnormal individuals there. It would have been easier than conquering the Estea Labyrinth…”

“Not necessarily. There’s a barrier, and you can’t even enter without dragonkin. And according to Jin-dono, even dragonkin can’t enter now.”

“So what happened?”

The conversation turned to me.

“Simply put, some dragonkin defected from the ‘Dragonkin Sanctuary’. Since it would be a problem if people could come and go freely using existing methods, I made it so no one can enter or leave.”

“That was unavoidable…”

“Then Kuroa can’t return home… Wait, then which of these does the nearly 100 dragonkin Jin mentioned fall under?”

Scarlet noticed the inconsistency.

“Obviously, the 100-plus dragonkin still remaining in the ‘Dragonkin Sanctuary’. It’s a dungeon I control. Bringing them over is easy.”

It’s still a secret that I’m controlling the Estea Labyrinth.

For now, I will just reveal that I am the labyrinth ruler of the “Dragonkin Sanctuary”.

“Seriously…”

“I see. That clears up several questions. No wonder the guardians were activated.”

Ah, sorry. That’s not just because I’m a dungeon ruler.

I satisfy a bunch of other conditions too…

“So that means Jin can return Kuroa to her homeland, right?”

“If you’re asking if I can, then yes, I can. But I have no intention of letting those I haven’t tamed come and go freely.”

The ‘Dragon Gate’ is currently inactive, so travel is basically done via ‘Portal’ or ‘Summoning’.

That’s within the domain of Special Powers, so even Scarlet isn’t going to learn it.

“Haa… Well, I guess knowing what happened to Kuroa’s homeland is good enough.”

Deciding that persuasion was pointless, Scarlet said with a sigh.

“I don’t really mind that much myself…”

Kuroa doesn’t seem particularly attached.

“If your memories come back, tell me. I’ll beg Jin if I have to to send you back.”

“Yes, I’ll do that when the time comes.”

If it’s just one way, I can open the ‘Dragon Gate’ for you.

Just not back and forth.

“Knowing the sanctuary is safe is a relief for now.”

I should correct Lily’s misunderstanding.

“By the way, the reason Kuroa ended up leaving through the Dragon Gate was because she was injured fighting a dragon that entered through a crack in the barrier. She probably got caught up in the chaos and was transferred.”

“So that’s where that injury came from… The memory loss too.”

“It was not as safe as I thought…”

Without exaggeration, the sanctuary would have been destroyed by the invading dragon if I hadn’t taken control.

They said the pace of incursions was increasing.

“It’s fine now, right?”

“Of course. I trained the dragonkin inside and stabilized resource supply, so it won’t fall so easily.”

“…Perhaps the elves of the village should train more too.”

Please decide that within the elven village.

Alright, I think that’s everything that needed to be said.

“Is there anything else you want to ask about the dragonkin?”

“No.”

“Me neither.”

Both shook their heads.

“Jin, isn’t it about time you told us whether you’ll cooperate? I think we’ve pretty much covered everything we needed to hear from old lady Lily.”

“Indeed. Now that it’s clear your cooperation is indispensable, it would help if you decided quickly.”

That’s true. There probably isn’t any more information coming.

And from what I’ve heard so far, there doesn’t seem to be any problem with cooperating.

“Alright. I’ll cooperate in going to the Goddess’s Domain.”

“Yes!”

Scarlet pumped his fist with all his might.

“That brings us one step closer to punching the Goddess.”

“The growth of the World Tree is favorable to me as well. Resolving the resource shortage is a great relief.”

Scarlet was happy, but Lily seemed even more relieved.

The World Tree’s resource shortage must have been extremely serious.

“Then let’s talk about finding the remaining Hero.”

Since I’ve decided to cooperate, I’ll give it my all.

“Jin-dono, you can gather the beastman, human, and hobbit Heroes, correct?”

“Yeah. And there’s one Hero in this village too, right?”

“Yes, the elven Hero. Therefore, the remaining Hero must be of another race. The most populous would be dwarves or oni.”

So other humanoid races like dwarves and oni also have \<Hero> holders.

“The problem is that there may not be any \<Hero> skill holders at all. At worst, it’s possible there are no other Heroes in this era.”

The \<Hero> skill is inherited, but there are periods when it doesn’t exist.

There is no pattern to those periods, and it’s not uncommon for an era to lack five Heroes.

Cynthia was born after Vermilion’s death and possessed the \<Hero> skill.

That gap being so short was an extremely rare case.

“We’ll probably need to take our time.”

“Yes. There’s nothing we can do if it hasn’t been born yet.”

“No, I don’t think that’s a concern.”

“”?””

Had they already forgotten that I said I’d cooperate?

“If I’m cooperating, there’s no way we’d end up one short.”

By pure coincidence, I had met the conditions for going to the ‘Goddess’ Realm’ to the point where there was only one condition left.

There is no way that the last one will end up being ‘a state that can not be satisfied’.

“You’re saying something incredible…”

“Indeed. Normally, no one could say that with such confidence.”

I’m Jin Shindo, a man confident in his luck.

“Give me one month. I’ll find them.”

If I’m looking, I don’t think it’s possible that they don’t exist (this is the most important part).

That means there’s a pretty high probability (laugh) that I’ll find them.

In the worst case, I’ll mobilize all my subordinates and do a full sweep.

---

**AN:** Everyone’s favorite final battlefield, TSUKI!

I also love absurdly tall towers.

If you think about the World Tree scientifically, it’s saying some pretty crazy things, but it all gets resolved with one word: “fantasy”.

+++

## **186: Choosing the World Tree and Returning Home**

I had declared that we would find the last person with a \<Hero> skill within one month, but even if we failed to do so in that time, nobody would really lose anything. So we did not set any penalties or the like.

It was merely a declaration that we would search on our own for one month.

After finishing our discussion about searching for the \<Hero>, we decided, guided by Lily, to visit the World Tree.

Scarlet said that just in case, he wanted to give the World Tree the abnormal individual factor while we still had the chance.

“It is here.”

Where we arrived was an unnaturally open space, far from the elf settlement.

It was roughly a circular area about one kilometer in diameter.

“It looks like there is nothing here, but the World Tree is right here.”

“Normally it is in an invisible, non-interfering state. Only those involved with the World Tree, that is, myself or Gosh, can make it visible.”

“You can touch it, but there is no sense of resistance. It is a strange feeling.”

Scarlet placed his hand on empty space and took a posture that would be impossible if there were nothing there.

I tried touching it as well.

…Yeah, it is a strange sensation. I can feel that I am touching something, yet there is no impression of what I am touching.

Incidentally, on the map, I can recognize the existence of the World Tree.

If I wanted to, it seems I could even cancel the non-interference.

“Then I shall make the World Tree visible.”

As she said this, Lily also touched the space where the World Tree was.

The next moment, a gigantic tree appeared before us.

A great tree brimming with vitality, its leaves a vivid green.

At present, it does not give the impression of suffering from a lack of resources.

Since we are looking up at it from below, it is hard to tell how tall it is, but judging from the thickness of the trunk, it is certain that it far exceeds one kilometer.

“As always, it is a magnificent tree. You think so too, Jin?”

“Yeah. I have never seen a tree this huge before.”

Ah, though I did see an even bigger tree in a dream…

“That is so, that is so. This World Tree was much smaller at first as well. Over a long span of years, it grew to this extent.”

And now it is in trouble due to a lack of resources…

“However, it is regrettable. If only it had resources, I could have granted you skills…”

“Ah, so that thing does require resources after all.”

Lily said something that could not be overlooked, and Scarlet nodded as if he understood.

“What do you mean?”

“One of the World Tree’s functions. The World Tree can grant one suitable skill to those who possess a soul from another world. It consumes a fair amount of resources, so it is impossible right now.”

“When I came here before, I received a skill from the World Tree. In terms of knowledge from my previous life, it would be called a unique skill.”

Scarlet possesses several unique-class skills.

In addition to the clearly sourced \<Proof of the Hero> and \<Hostile Magic Nullification>, he also has \<Heavenly Eye Sight> and \<Soul Sublimation>.

From Scarlet’s life story, if \<Heavenly Eye Sight> was something he was born with, then \<Soul Sublimation> must be what he received.

“Could it be that at that time, it also incorporated my abnormal individual factor?”

“That is correct. At present, the World Tree possesses three factors: the elf \<Hero>, the \<Proof of the Hero>, and the reincarnator.”

“Does it not have the factor of the Dungeon Master?”

I had just heard that they were acquaintances. Did it not receive that factor?

It was such a rare existence that could have satisfied two factors at once.

“It does not have that factor. After he created the labyrinth, I was the one who visited him, you see.”

“Granny Lily, were you able to leave the elf village?”

“Indeed. Recently I have not gone out, and it is difficult to do so now, but in the past I went out fairly often.”

To be honest, I had imagined her as being shut in all the time.

《Master, I have a request.》

At that point, Mio sent me a telepathic message in a very formal tone.

《I know. You want a unique skill, right?》

《Please.》

She begged earnestly, without any teasing.

She really seems to want it.

“If it has resources, can it grant that skill?”

“Yes. Ah, I did not mention this earlier, but anyone who has received a Blessing even once is excluded.”

Skills that were formerly Blessings separated from the ‘Remnants of Blessings’ should be fine.

“Then, if we direct our resources to the World Tree, could you give us skills in return?”

“That would be most welcome, but can you switch it right here?”

“Yeah, I can. …All right, I have switched it.”

I changed the settings so that resources would be sent to the World Tree.

“O, ooooooooooh…”

Lily let out a sound like a broken toy.

Her legs trembled violently, and her head swayed unsteadily.

“W-what happened? Granny, did you finally go senile?”

“D-do not say such rude things. A-a large amount of resources suddenly flowed in, so I was merely confused.”

Lily is still swaying her head.

“I see… This would indeed resolve the World Tree’s resource shortage in no time.”

“Seriously? Jin, that is insane…”

“Of course, it would also be possible to grant skills to everyone.”

“A give-and-take situation, huh.”

Ah, that is the nature of my Special Power.

“Then, who will receive a skill first?”

In response to Lily’s question, Mio smoothly raised her hand. Her eyes were serious.

“Is this girl acceptable?”

“Yeah, please grant this girl a skill.”

“Then she should touch the World Tree. After incorporating the factor, she will obtain a skill immediately.”

Urged by Lily, Mio touched the World Tree.

Then she made a small fist pump.

\<Automatic Transcription>

Transfers one’s knowledge onto paper. Activates by imagining the knowledge one wishes to leave on blank paper. Reads the deep psyche and automatically turns it into written text.

Just as Lily said, it is a skill well-suited to Mio.

It is also a skill that solves Mio’s troubles.

She had said before that writing cooking recipes on paper was difficult, and she also bears the role of conveying Earth knowledge to Maria and the others, which has apparently been quite a burden.

Mio is good at explaining things, so we tend to rely on her.

You might say that Sakura could create that level of magic?

However, even if Sakura tried to do something similar with her magic, it would probably not work well.

In fact, magic created with Sakura’s \<Magic Creation> has one drawback… or rather, a characteristic: the target of the magic’s effect must be clearly defined.

Originally, the conditions for creating magic derive from the caster’s image, and it likely has a nature that does not allow ambiguity.

If she were to create a similar magic, she would probably need to verbally speak every single line of text to be written onto the paper.

The latter half of the description, “reads the deep psyche and automatically turns it into written text”, is particularly strong.

“Thank you very much.”

Mio bowed her head in thanks toward the World Tree.

She looked so happy when leaving the World Tree that she seemed like she might start humming.

It is her long-awaited “unique skill for herself”, after all.

“Who is next?”

The ones present here who possess “souls from another world” are me, Sakura, and Mio, three people.

“Sakura, do you want to go?”

“Is it all right for you, Jin-kun…?”

“Since we have the chance, I will go last.”

“Understood… You will probably surprise us when it is your turn, right?”

Yeah.

I do not know what will happen, but I think it probably will be surprising.

“Excuse me…”

Sakura also touched the World Tree and obtained a skill.

\<Magic Proficiency>

When using magic, MP consumption decreases in proportion to the number of times that magic has been used. However, MP consumption will not become zero.

Another interesting skill has appeared.

MP consumption decreasing based on usage count is a fairly common system in games.

In this world, while MP consumption can increase when using things like \<Chantless Casting>, I have never seen a skill that reduces it.

A: There are such skills.

Apparently, there are.

…In any case, there is no doubt that it is a rare and valuable skill.

And in a sense, it is not uncharacteristic of Sakura.

Specifically, in that it interferes with fundamental principles, and…

《Sakura, is it all right if I share this skill via \<Contract Bond>? If everyone under my command uses this skill, I think MP consumption will decrease very quickly.》

It has extremely good compatibility with my ability.

By sharing this skill through \<Contract Bond>, the count of magic usage can be advanced collectively by all subordinates.

And all subordinates can receive the benefit of reduced MP consumption.

However, those who are in positions where they interact with people outside of my subordinates will be set so that they do not receive the benefit.

I want to eliminate, as much as possible, the risk of my special ability or Special Powers being exposed.

《Of course, I do not mind… I am happy if I can be of help to you and everyone, Jin-kun…》

Sakura readily agrees.

Actually, the one that has the best compatibility with this skill is the \<Unique Magic> created by Sakura’s \<Magic Creation>.

Originally, \<Unique Magic> consumes a lot of MP and is used often, so it gains the greatest benefit.

I see, it really is true that one obtains a skill that has synergy with one’s own abilities.

Naturally, my expectations for the skill I will obtain also rise.

“Is Jin-dono last?”

“No, before that, let us prioritize incorporating the other factors.”

“Is that all right?”

“Yeah, I am fine going truly last.”

Since I do not know what will happen, we should finish what needs to be done first.

After that, the incorporation of factors proceeded smoothly.

Maria, Sera, Dora, Blue, Leaf, and Mikazuki touched the World Tree in that order.

“At last, it is Jin’s turn. I wonder what kind of skill he will get?”

“There are exceptions, but normally it should be about the level of a Hero’s Blessing. Red-boy’s skill was one of those rare exceptions.”

“If I am an exception, then Jin will be one too.”

“That is an unpleasant kind of trust. …Though I cannot deny it.”

Now then, what will come out…?

I approached the World Tree and placed my hand on its trunk.

This time it is materialized, so I can feel the normal texture of a tree.

By the function of the World Tree, you have obtained \<蘚＆#[あLV >.

I see, so that is how it goes.

Due to the garbled text, I cannot understand the details at all.

Alta, please analyze it.

A: Understood.

“Huh?”

Lily stands there with her mouth agape.

“W-what happened? The World Tree’s resources are almost empty. They decreased by more than the amount that had just increased. It was really right on the verge of the barrier disappearing. Jin-dono, what kind of skill did you obtain?”

Just producing this \<蘚＆#[あ> skill seems to have drained the World Tree’s resources.

Just what kind of skill is it?

“It is \<蘚＆#[あ>.”

“What?”

“It is \<蘚＆#[あ>.”

“?”

I repeated it for Lily, who could not catch it the first time, but she still did not seem to understand the second time either.

So I had no choice but to write the characters on the ground.

“I-I do not understand at all…”

“It is bugged. It came from way below expectations.”

Hey, do not say “below expectations.”

“Well, things like this happen sometimes.”

“I have never heard of such a thing. Jin-dono, this is dangerous.”

Even a storyteller who has lived for ages is calling it dangerous.

Well, things like this happen sometimes.

After that, we had some minor discussions with Scarlet and Lily.

And after finishing everything we needed to do in the elf village, we departed and returned to the imperial capital of the Crimson Empire.

To be honest, I would not have minded sightseeing the elf village a bit more, but since we had set a one-month deadline for searching for the Hero, sightseeing had to be postponed.

Returning to the imperial capital was for retrieving Rouge and the others, and for going to receive the apologetic princess.

After arriving at the imperial capital, Scarlet parted from us for a while to handle important state matters.

We took lodgings again and waited leisurely.

The next morning, Ash was sent as an errand runner to summon us to the imperial castle.

And then, Scarlet’s office.

Only the members who had gone to the elf village were gathered here.

“You are going to search for the last Hero after this, right, Jin?”

“Yeah. I plan to find them within one month.”

I have also told Lily that I will come again in about a month.

“That is a lot of confidence… I also will not be leaving the imperial capital for a month, so when you come next time, stop by the capital first. Let us regroup and then go to the elf village.”

“Yeah, got it.”

By the way, since we have not told Scarlet and the others about ‘Portal’, I told them that when we come to the Crimson Empire next time, we will arrive on riding dragons.

“We have finally made it this far…”

Scarlet mutters with deep emotion.

“If Jin had not been here, just thinking about how much we would have had to do within the one year before Granny falls asleep again makes me shudder.”

Scarlet lets out a wry smile.

In the worst case, it might not even have been realized within Scarlet’s lifetime.

“Yeah… This time, I ended up owing you a huge debt, Jin. I want to repay it even a little. Do you have any requests?”

“Let me think…”

Since he is offering to hear a request, is there anything I want?

A: Master. How about requesting passage and residence rights within the Crimson Empire? You would be able to explore the Crimson Empire. If you can obtain them for your subordinates as well, you could also open branches of the Advance Trading Company.

All right, let us go with that.

“Then, could you grant us the rights to operate within the Crimson Empire? I do not know exactly what rights are necessary, but it would help if we could receive rights related to residence, passage, and commerce, for a number of people plus some extra. I want to wander around this country a bit more.”

“That is all you want? That is easy. If you tell me, I can prepare them for any number of people. Just make sure you ask while I am still emperor. I do not want to act all high and mighty after I abdicate.”

“That is only natural.”

When someone who has stepped down from power does as they please, it usually does not end well.

If I am going to ask Scarlet for favors, it is best to do so while he is still emperor.

“If my subordinates who are not present here receive those rights, we will probably open a branch of the Advance Trading Company within the Crimson Empire.”

“That was related to you too, Jin…? Shin-dou… progress… advance, I see…”

Do not analyze it so much!

“Fine. Just understand that due to this country’s nature, there is a possibility it will not be well received.”

“Yeah. In the first place, profit is secondary, so I do not mind.”

“Is that really fine for a trading company?”

“Probably…”

The primary purpose of the Advance Trading Company is to support my travels.

Of course, making a profit would be nice, but even without profit, it can still fulfill its purpose.

Due to how \<Clairvoyance> works, as long as even one subordinate is present, information about that land can be gathered.

“Well, if you say it is fine, Jin, then I have no complaints. I will not pry into the details, but let me ask you one thing.”

“What is it?”

“If I need to urgently contact you, should I get in touch with the Advance Trading Company?”

“Yeah, that will be fine.”

Scarlet really does have good instincts.

“Then we should also consider the reverse. Let us conduct direct transactions between the Advance Trading Company and me. That way, there will be fewer people who try to mess with the company, and the company side can also contact me directly.”

“Is that basically becoming a retainer merchant?”

“Then let us do that.”

“That is awfully casual, for the ruler of a country.”

And so, the Advance Trading Company became the Crimson Empire emperor’s retainer merchant.

Even though it does not even have a store yet…

After that, discussions with Scarlet continued.

Scarlet’s sense of distance is excellent. He does not pry deeply into areas we do not want to be questioned about, and only confirms the important points.

I did not explain my Special Powers, but I did tell him some of “what we can do”.

“You really are amazing, Jin. I know it is unreasonable, but let me ask one more time. Will you not live here?”

It seems he has given up on saying “marry my daughter”.

“I will pass. I would not mind having a vacation home, but I do not need a main residence.”

In my mind, my main estates are the two in Castal and Estea.

For example, the residential area of the labyrinth or the castle portion of the Sky Castle are like vacation homes to me.

Since I rarely use them, I do not assign many people to manage them.

Or rather, I make it so they can handle it alongside other work.

“Even so, that is fine! Along with the Advance Trading Company matter, I will give you prime land in the imperial capital!”

“Is that really fine? For the ruler of a country?”

Is that really something you can decide so easily?

“It is fine. I am the emperor right now. I am the law.”

“There is a tyrant here.”

“A tyrant is fine! With money and power, most unreasonable things can be pushed through.”

Scarlet continued with “Besides”.

“Think of it as payment for the items you gave me. If anything, I should be giving you change.”

It was not exactly a token of friendship, but I gave him several items I had.

They were things I took out at random, but he seemed more pleased than expected.

A: As Scarlet says, even if considered as payment for prime land in the imperial capital, it would be excessive.

Hmm. Could it be that my sense of money is off?

A: Rather than your sense of money, it seems your recognition of rarity is distorted.

I see. That is something I am aware of.

Surrounded by too many rare items, I probably cannot recognize their rarity properly.

“Well, do not worry about the land. I will sort it out by tomorrow.”

“Yeah, I will leave it to you.”

During the discussion, it was decided that we would depart from the Crimson Empire tomorrow.

According to Scarlet, he will finish handling everything related to me today.

Specifically, the rights, the land, and the princess.

With Scarlet beginning to handle matters related to me right away, the meeting came to an end.

After parting with Scarlet, we began our last sightseeing in the Crimson Empire.

Each of us merely resolved any lingering regrets from sightseeing before going to the elf village, so there was nothing particularly noteworthy to talk about.

And then, without incident, the next day arrived.

We received the rights, the land, and the princess from Scarlet.

“…I did say that how you use what I give you is up to you. But even so, this is beyond my expectations…”

So murmured Scarlet, who had come along with us, as he watched buildings being constructed at an abnormal speed before his eyes.

“They are my subordinate maids. I called them over yesterday. Ah, do not worry. They came here through proper procedures using the passage permits we had already received yesterday. Also, they are not employees of the Advance Trading Company, so I will be calling those separately.”

“There are too many things to comment on. I cannot keep up.”

Scarlet looks like he has given up on something.

“…Well, fine. I will just take it as a reconfirmation of how dangerous you are, Jin.”

That is a harsh way to put it.

“I am really glad that you are on our side, Jin.”

“If it had been true that you were going to attack Estea, you would have been classified as an enemy.”

“That was close!?”

“By the way, the Golden Fox incident was also a candidate for enemy classification.”

“I was walking a tightrope there, huh…”

There were many enemy flags with Scarlet.

Conversely, that means I broke every single one of those flags, and now he is standing beside me.

“In the original plan, we were going to eliminate Scarlet and make Rouge a puppet emperor.”

Since we have come this far, I decided to be frank.

“I can understand eliminating me, but could Rouge really handle being a puppet?”

“Honestly, I was not very confident.”

“Yeah, figures.”

Rouge continues to be treated as usual.

“Besides, since we would have had to forcibly seize the imperial throne, the country would inevitably have been thrown into chaos. I am just as glad that Scarlet is an ally as you are.”

“In a sense, everything wrapped up nicely.”

There were some troubles, like the attacks on the princess and prince, but it can be said that our objectives in coming to the Crimson Empire were fully achieved.

From Scarlet’s perspective as well, by gaining me as an ally, he must have been able to greatly shorten the time needed to reach his goals.

There was no notable damage to land or people, and everyone involved achieved their objectives.

This trip can safely be called a great success.

Even I can enjoy a peaceful trip once in a while.

“That is true. But Scarlet, your objective has not been achieved yet, has it?”

“Yeah, it is from here on. It is pathetic to rely on you again, Jin, but can I leave it to you?”

“Of course. It also aligns with one of my objectives, so I will devote my full effort to it.”

I am a man who does what he says, Shindo Jin.

“…Well then, construction seems to be going smoothly, so I suppose it is about time for us to depart from this country.”

Even as we talk, work is proceeding smoothly at the construction site before us.

Considering the abilities of the construction maids, the store and residential area should be completed within the day.

“You are leaving already?”

“Yeah. Next time we come, we will have the remaining Hero with us.”

“I will be looking forward to it. …Oh, right. Since we are allies now.”

Saying that, Scarlet held out his hand.

Once in a while, this kind of thing is nice.

I grasped his hand in return.

It is rare not to have a boss battle, but Scarlet is an ally, and he is not a battle-crazed person who would pick a fight with guests he invited.

What? His introduction scene in the Elegant Theocracy arc? That was because stress had built up from a long flight. He is not battle-crazed, but he does like moving his body. Also, it was a bit of presence assertion.

As mentioned before, updates to the main story will stop for a while.

It will probably be difficult to update in October. I apologize.

## **186.5: Scarlet’s Office**

**AN:** This is supplementary material related to Scarlet.

I had already finished writing the character introductions, but this piece, which I wanted to post at the same time, ended up taking longer.

---

That day, I summoned Rose, Ruby, and Jonathan to my office.

The three of them had defied my orders as emperor and laid hands on our guest, Jin, and were therefore imprisoned.

Even now, after being summoned, all three wore handcuffs and shackles, their freedom completely restrained.

Ruby looked sorrowful, and Jonathan looked frustrated, but Rose remained calm.

Not long ago, I was told she had been in a pitiful state to behold, and yet…

I fixed my gaze on Rose and Ruby and made my declaration.

“Rose, Ruby. You will become Jin’s slaves.”

“Understood.”

Rose answered immediately. There was not the slightest hesitation.

“Hey, Father! What are you thinking!? And Rose! Why are you agreeing to this!?”

As expected, Jonathan snapped back.

The punishment for Rose and Ruby and the punishment for Jonathan are separate matters, but Jonathan treasures Ruby, his sister by the same mother.

If told that Ruby would become a slave, there was no way he could stay silent.

“What do you mean, what am I thinking? It is obviously punishment for defying my orders and laying hands on Jin.”

“Then why does that turn into becoming that bastard’s slave!?”

“What, would you rather all three of you be executed? If you defy the emperor’s orders, execution is the natural outcome, right? Don’t tell me you don’t understand that.”

“Gh…”

Jonathan groaned.

This country grants the emperor extremely strong authority. It is a nation that functions well because of that.

Though I intend to step down from the throne eventually for the sake of my objective, I have no intention of diminishing imperial authority during my reign.

If I did that, I could not face Leon, who thought of this country until the very end.

Therefore, once I declare something as an “Imperial order”, not even I can overturn it.

Even if they are my own children, I cannot stop an execution.

The fact that I cannot prioritize my own children likely means I am unfit as a parent.

At this point, it does not seem like something I can change…

In this situation, the only one who can call for a halt is Jin himself, the victim.

Only if there is a proposal from the victim does a path other than execution open up.

If the guest who was wronged speaks, leniency can be granted.

To be honest, part of me had hoped Jin would make some kind of proposal.

Slavery was a bit unexpected, but compared to execution, it should be preferable.

“If Jin had not said he would take Rose and Ruby as slaves, I intended to execute all three of you.”

“…What happens to me?”

It seems his mind was so consumed with Ruby that he had not even thought about his own punishment.

“You will only be stripped of your right of succession. Other than that, things will basically remain as they were.”

“Then I’ll become a slave! So reduce Ruby’s punishment to losing her succession rights!”

Given how clearly lighter Jonathan’s punishment is, I can understand why he would say that.

But that is impossible.

“It is precisely because Ruby becomes a slave that your punishment is light. I cannot reverse that.”

“…What do you mean?”

“According to Jin, it is so that Ruby can become a slave without lingering concerns.”

Jin truly has quite the personality.

“Try imagining her state of mind after becoming a slave in the case where you are alive versus the case where you are executed.”

“So I’m basically a hostage…”

That is not far off.

Ruby becoming a slave is already decided, but whether her brother is alive or not makes a huge difference.

If her brother had been executed, the resentment would be enormous, but since he lives, she cannot harbor hatred over that point. That is precisely why Jonathan’s punishment is clearly lighter.

“…Why did Rose accept becoming a slave without a single complaint?”

At that point, Jonathan turned his attention toward Rose.

“I have no objections to becoming Lord Jin’s slave. Or rather, even without a slave crest carved upon me, I am already Lord Jin’s loyal servant. Absolute obedience.”

“Eh…?”

Jonathan was left speechless.

I do not think it showed on my face, but I felt the same way.

People really do change…

“Jonathan, a message from Jin. He says, ‘If both Jonathan and Ruby become upright people, I would be willing to let them meet.’ At the very least, Jin said he has no intention of tormenting Ruby without reason. I will not say you should feel at ease, but it is not without hope.”

“Is that true!?”

I silently nodded.

If anything, Jonathan’s conditions are likely the harsher ones, but there is no need to say that out loud.

Ruby will be reeducated as a slave under Jin.

Her authority as an imperial princess will vanish, and she will be educated as nothing more than a slave girl. She will grow into whatever Jin desires.

On the other hand, can Jonathan become the kind of person Jin would desire from here on out?

After all, the method he chose to protect his sister was an assault.

I think it will be difficult to reform his nature at this point.

“The punishment has already been decided. No matter what Jonathan says, it will not be overturned. …Once you leave this room, you will not be able to meet until the conditions are fulfilled, so say your farewells.”

Jonathan made a frustrated expression, lowered himself, and brought his eyes level with Ruby’s.

With his handcuffed hands, he grasped Ruby’s hand and spoke to her with a serious expression.

“Ruby, I know it will be hard, but do your best. I’ll work hard too, so that I can see you again.”

Ruby nodded.

After that, the two exchanged a few words, and then it was time to part.

Rose and Ruby were taken away by Jin’s subordinate maids, while Jonathan would spend some more time in prison. At least until Jin returns.

“Father, did you summon me?”

“Ah, come in.”

The one who entered my office was my eldest daughter, Carmine.

Since I summoned her right after her military duties ended, she was still in uniform.

I told her there was no need to hurry, so she could have changed, but…

“It has been a long time since you last summoned me, Father.”

Of all my children, Carmine is probably the one I interact with the most.

She had been unusually attached to me since she was young. Even I cannot treat a child who dotes on me poorly.

She was ambitious and said she was interested in the Emperor’s work, so when I had time, I would call her in and teach her various things.

Lately, I have been busy with many matters, so there have been fewer such opportunities.

“Yes. There is something I need to tell you, Carmine.”

Just as I said that, the office door opened again.

“Brother, I’m coming in.”

The one who entered without even knocking was my foolish younger sister, Rouge.

I had heard she was being educated under Jin, but perhaps I misheard?

“W-Why are you here!?”

“Hm, Carmine. If you ask why, it is obviously because Brother summoned me.”

It is good to see that they still do not get along.

“That may be so… but at least knock!”

“Since I was summoned, it is only natural to enter. Knocking would just waste time, would it not?”

Rouge said confidently.

“Rouge’s argument is correct in a sense, but as a lady, do you not think that is inappropriate?”

It may be rational, but it is not something a princess should do.

“Shall I consult Jin about this…?”

“Please don’t! I’m sorry!”

This is what has become of Rouge, who used to fear nothing.

People really do change.

“S-So, what did you call us here for?”

Rouge blatantly tried to change the subject.

She really is an idiot.

“I called you two here to talk about the next emperor.”

“!?”

Ignoring their shock, I continued.

“You already know this, but I will abdicate the throne in the not-too-distant future. At that time, I intend to hand the throne to the one most suitable.”

Hearing my words, Carmine timidly asked,

“Father… are you speaking about this directly?”

“Yes. After speaking with Jin, I thought it was time to convey this seriously.”

Thanks to Jin, various plans may be accelerating.

My abdication may come sooner as well. I should lay the groundwork so there are no problems when that time comes.

“He is that important a person to you, Father?”

“Yes. He is indispensable to my objective.”

“As expected…”

I have heard about the matter where Carmine asked Jin for a favor.

That is precisely why I decided to tell Carmine first.

“So then, who is planned to be the next emperor? Calling us here at this timing means it must be one of the two of us, correct?”

“!?”

Carmine looked extremely frustrated.

She probably thought I would choose Rouge.

“Obviously it’s Carmine. Don’t tell me, Rouge, you actually think you’re fit to be emperor?”

“Of course not. There is no way I could serve as emperor. At best, it would only result in a puppet emperor.”

“Eh?”

Carmine looked dumbfounded, as if she did not understand.

“At present, the one most suited to be emperor is you, Carmine.”

“Is that… truly the case…?”

“There is no reason for me to lie about something like this.”

Even after saying that, Carmine’s expression did not change much.

She still could not believe it.

“So Carmine has a high chance of becoming the next emperor. If that is the case, it may become difficult for me to return to this country.”

Rouge, who does not get along with Carmine, said this with a hint of regret.

The reason she did not seem very regretful is probably because her place is no longer in this country.

“That would be a problem. Rouge has deep ties with Jin as well. Considering Jin’s impression and the country’s interests, driving her out would not be a good move. Carmine, what would you do?”

“…I cannot give her a position of power in this country, but I would not do something like driving her out.”

When I asked, Carmine tightened her expression, thought for a moment, and answered.

“That is fine. Giving Rouge a position would not lead to anything good.”

“Isn’t that a bit harsh?”

“Reflect on your own actions before saying that.”

“…I have nothing to say.”

From my perspective, she has improved considerably, but she is still within the unacceptable range.

Caring about someone and granting them a position are separate matters.

“By the way, why did you only call the two of us here? Carmine aside, there is no need to call me, is there? On the contrary, it also bothers me that you did not call the other candidates.”

That was surprisingly perceptive of Rouge.

I had expected Carmine to bring that up…

“Because Rouge is the one who gets along worst with Carmine. I wanted to see both of your reactions. Since Carmine said she would not eliminate Rouge, that puts my mind at ease.”

“I dislike her, but I do not want to eliminate her.”

Carmine muttered quietly, “Because Father would be saddened”, but I pretended not to hear it.

“As for the other candidates, they are not as eager for the throne as Carmine, so I lowered their priority. …The two who were eager have dropped out due to this incident.”

Rose and Jonathan were the ones who sought the throne most strongly after Carmine.

It is their own fault, but losing those two is significant.

“I am not aware of it, but what is the stance of the other candidates?”

Having been away for several years, Rouge knows almost nothing about the current state of the Crimson Empire.

“The ones who say they do not want to be emperor are the Third Prince and the twin Fourth and Fifth Princesses. The twins are probably more suited to research.”

To be honest, it is not as though I have no desire to pass the throne to Ash… to Vermilion’s son. But I have no intention of forcing someone to do what they do not wish to do.

“The passive ones are the First Prince, the Second Princess, and the Sixth Princess. The two princesses lack confidence. Red says he will become emperor if there is no one else suitable.”

In a sense, Red may have inherited my blood most strongly.

“If Red acknowledges Carmine, then Carmine will unquestionably be the next emperor.”

“I see. Indeed, Carmine is the strongest candidate.”

“…Rouge would acknowledge me?”

Carmine looked surprised.

“…I have been through many things as well. Carmine’s ability and achievements are facts and cannot be denied.”

“So…”

Rouge said this while turning her face away from Carmine.

Hearing those words, Carmine looked just a little happy.

When someone you favor and someone you care about do not get along, it is rather taxing on the mind.

I do not expect them to get along, but it is better if there is no unnecessary friction.

“Excuse me.”

The one who entered, saying that, was my aide, Pierre.

“Did something happen?”

“Yes. We have received a letter regarding Lady Strawberry.”

“Oh?”

I asked Strawberry to apologize to the Regalia Beastman Kingdom regarding the matter of the Elgant Theocracy.

Considering the distance, she should be returning around now… Did something happen?

“It seems Lady Strawberry is currently in the Brown Wall Kingdom.”

“What? Why?”

The Brown Wall Kingdom lies in a completely different direction from the Regalia Beastman Kingdom.

“After reaching the Regalia Beastman Kingdom, she apparently got lost and ended up in the Brown Wall Kingdom.”

“I do not understand… What did Strawberry’s letter say?”

“No… the letter did not come from Lady Strawberry.”

Come to think of it, Pierre said, “regarding Lady Strawberry.”

He did not say it was from Strawberry.

“It came from the Advance Trading Company, Brown Wall Kingdom branch. They say they will send her by air.”

“Anything goes, with Jin… that bastard.”

Another debt to Jin has been added.

Seriously, would he not marry Carmine or Strawberry already?

---

**AN:** A short piece where the imperial family members appear only by name.

There was no room to give them proper scenes.

And Ruby-chan does not speak.

## **12 Characters**

**AN:** Posted simultaneously with a Scarlet-related short story.

---

As for the main story only, this list basically includes only people whose names are explicitly shown. Skills are excluded.

Any information that is not explicitly stated is excluded.

**Protagonist Side**

Name: Eclipse

Gender: Female

Age: 0 years old

Race: Great Spirit

Notes: Jin’s contracted Spirit and a Great Spirit who governs miasma. Miasma is stagnant magical power, and Spirits, which are originally aggregates of non-stagnant magical power, cannot normally come into existence from it. This is an abnormal situation that occurred due to Jin’s involvement. Having gained self-awareness by synchronizing with the Great Spirit Rain, she is treated as a younger sister. As a result of the synchronization, she has strongly inherited Rain’s nature, and her affection toward Jin is at the same level.

Name: Ruby

Gender: Female

Age: 10

Race: Human

Notes: The Seventh Imperial Princess of the Crimson Empire. After defying Scarlet’s orders and attacking Jin, events progressed to the point where she ultimately became Jin’s slave. Although the attack on Jin was the result of being manipulated by Rose, what Jin truly took issue with was her response afterward. If Jin had not enslaved her, she would truly have been executed. She has extremely few lines.

Name: Rose Crimson

Gender: Female

Age: 15

Race: Human (Reincarnator)

Title: Imperial Princess of the Crimson Empire

Notes: The Third Imperial Princess of the Crimson Empire. A reincarnator with a strong lust for power who schemes in the shadows to become Empress. However, laying a hand on Jin in order to eliminate obstructive siblings proved to be her undoing. She was defeated by Jin and brought to an end. She was revived when she became Jin’s slave through negotiations with Scarlet. After her revival, she obeys Jin completely. In her previous life, she was a fencer in her thirties who died after being run over by a tanker truck. How one manages to get run over by a tanker is unknown.

**Crimson Empire**

Name: Carmine Crimson

Gender: Female

Age: 17

Race: Human

Title: Imperial Princess of the Crimson Empire

Notes: The First Imperial Princess of the Crimson Empire. A closet father complex (severe). She notices Scarlet’s hidden consideration toward Rouge and burns with jealousy. As long as Rouge is not involved, she is generally excellent and has good judgment. She belongs to the military and has high command ability and solo combat power. She also has support from the populace, and it is no exaggeration to call her an upper-compatible version of Rouge. Of course, this is the result of her efforts driven by a desire not to lose to Rouge.

Name: Ash Crimson

Gender: Male

Age: 15

Race: Half-Elf

Title: Imperial Prince of the Crimson Empire

Notes: The Third Imperial Prince of the Crimson Empire. In reality, he is not Scarlet’s child, but the son of Vermilion and Claire. Being born between two Heroes, he gained the nature of having no skills and being unaffected by skills. His personality is serious and upright, so Jin likes him quite a lot. His dream for the future is to travel the world. In that respect as well, he gets along well with Jin. He has no skills, but is excellent, and if he set his mind to it, he could even aim for the throne. In fact, Scarlet thinks that would be acceptable as well.

Name: Pierre

Gender: Male

Notes: One of Scarlet’s close aides. Because his response was proper, Jin addresses him with the honorific “shi.” While Scarlet was absent, troubles related to Jin continued one after another, and he lived a life of constant stomach pain. When Scarlet returned, he was relieved because he understood the situation.

Name: Jonathan Crimson

Gender: Male

Age: 16

Race: Human

Title: Imperial Prince of the Crimson Empire

Notes: The Second Imperial Prince of the Crimson Empire. Ruby’s full-blooded older brother. A fool who moved to kill Jin in order to cover for Ruby’s blunder. As a matter of course, he was defeated in retaliation and lost one arm. Under normal circumstances he would have been executed, but due to Jin’s proposal, it was settled with only the stripping of his right of succession.

**Elf Village**

Name: Lily

Gender: Female

Age: 65535

Race: High Elf

Titles: Elf Princess Shrine Maiden, Elf Royalty, Storyteller of the Elves, Protector of the World Tree

Notes: A loli granny. The storyteller of the Elves, whose existence had been hinted at since Volume 1. It may have been forgotten, but meeting her was one of the purposes of Jin’s journey. She knows many important things, yet does not know the truly important parts, making her an unbalanced existence. She is considering choosing suicide if the World Tree reaches the realm of the Goddess and someone arrives at the Goddess.

Name: Claire

Gender: Female

Age: 120

Race: Elf

Title: Elf Hero

Notes: Ash’s mother. Does not appear in the main story. The \<Seal> has not been lifted.

Name: Gosh

Gender: Male

Age: 1111

Race: High Elf

Titles: Chief of the Elf Village, Protector of the World Tree

Notes: The chief who governs the Elf Village while Lily is sleeping. In essence, Lily’s proxy. He lacks flexibility and attacks Jin. The price of that was a shortage of resources, something that affected the survival of the World Tree. However, Jin somehow dealt with it. Jin internally calls him “old man.”
