## **187: Searching for the Hero and the Water City**

**AN:** The serialization has resumed.

However, I am still not fully back in shape, and because the writing pace is like that of a turtle, updates will be irregular (roughly every 10 to 20 days).

Honestly, it makes me uneasy to post while the chapter is not yet finished, but since I at least have something resembling a plot, I would like to continue posting.

**Editor’s Note:** About the above, that was written way back in 2019, so it does not really affect us until we catch up, though it does mean there are fewer chapters total.

---

The day after returning from our trip to the Crimson Empire.

After finishing a shorter-than-usual leisurely time, I gathered the party members to hold our final meeting for searching for the Hero.

“Huh…? Dora-chan and Maria-chan aren’t here…?”

Sakura asked with a puzzled look.

The two of them were currently resting in their rooms.

“Ah, it seems yesterday’s full-power fluffing is still taking its toll.”

During leisurely time, I almost always end up fluffing my beastman subordinates and beasts.

This time, since leisurely time was shorter than usual, I ended up going all out with the fluffing for the first time in a while.

As a result, every single participant in the fluffing session was unable to endure it and collapsed.

Even Maria and Dora were unable to get back up the next morning, so the other fluffing attendants probably would not be able to function properly until around tomorrow.

Yeah. Honestly, I went a bit too far.

Normally, the ones nearing their limit tell me themselves, but this time no one said anything, so I lost track of when to stop.

I asked Maria about it earlier, and apparently my full-power fluffing has an addictive quality, making it impossible for them to stop until they collapsed.

“Even those two couldn’t endure it… Just how powerful is Master’s fluffing?”

“If I imagine myself as a beastman, it makes my skin crawl.”

Mio and Sera shuddered in fear.

Naturally, if Sera were a beastman, she would have been one of the fluffing targets.

“Well, anyway, we’ll hold the meeting with just these members for now.”

With their stamina, leaving in the afternoon should be fine.

And the two of them probably would not have much to say about the destination anyway…

“So, um, we’re looking for the final holder of the \<Hero> skill, right…?”

“Master, do you have any leads?”

In response to Mio’s question, I nodded confidently.

“Yeah. I have an efficient search method that only I can use.”

“Efficient… Ah, I get it! Use flying subordinates to roll over the map and fill it in!”

That’s certainly not a bad idea. It’s not like I never considered it.

I won’t do it to avoid spoilers, but if I really wanted to, I could strip the entire world’s map bare.

If we were willing to use any means necessary to search for the \<Hero>, it would be effective.

“It’s a good move, but I wouldn’t call it ‘efficient’. The effort of the people who fail to find anything would be wasted.”

“I think it’s still better than searching blindly…”

“Yeah, searching blindly is no good. So then, don’t do it blindly. That’s where this comes in.”

I took out a map from \<Infinite Storage> and spread it out.

“It’s a map of this world.”

“And despite its rough accuracy, it’s surprisingly expensive.”

This world doesn’t have very detailed maps, but they do exist.

It’s the same type as on Earth, where a sphere is unfolded into a rectangle.

I pinned the map onto the corkboard hanging on the wall.

“Jin-kun, what are you planning to do…?”

“D-don’t tell me…”

It seemed Mio had realized something.

“And then, I use this.”

What I took out from \<Infinite Storage> next was a dart.

“Throw a dart at the map and go to wherever it lands.”

“I knew it! A dart journey!”

Mio shouted, her guess spot-on.

“I see, so you’re leaving it up to Master’s luck.”

“Indeed, only Jin-kun could do something so reckless…”

Sera and Sakura seemed to understand as well.

“Master, you know that if you throw a dart at a world map at random, most of the time it’ll land in the ocean, right?”

“Huh? I’ve never had that happen even once.”

“You’ve done this in your original world too?!”

Mio’s sharp retort.

Of course I’ve done it.

“It’s fine. This method actually has a decent track record.”

“It has a track record?!”

“Ancient ruins, buried treasure…”

Even without darts, I’ve always been good at finding things.

“…Master, sometime soon, please tell us about your original world again, okay? It has to be interesting.”

“If it’s about Jin-kun’s original world, I want to hear it too…”

“If Maria-san were here, she’d definitely want to listen.”

After Mio begged me, I ended up promising to tell some old stories eventually.

“Alright then, let’s throw it.”

“What if it lands in the ocean?”

Mio asked a strange question.

“Obviously, we go there.”

So far it’s never landed in the ocean, but if it did, going to that sea area would be the natural thing to do.

“Even though we’re searching for the \<Hero>?”

“You don’t have any proof that there’s no \<Hero> in the ocean, do you?”

“There’s no way…”

“It’s possible they’re traveling by ship.”

“Or they could be in a place like a merfolk kingdom…”

Nice follow-ups from Sera and Sakura.

“Exactly. Let’s throw it first and think later.”

I closed my eyes so I wouldn’t aim and threw the dart toward the world map.

After confirming the sound of it sticking, I opened my eyes.

“The ocean! …No, wait, if you look closely, it’s stuck on an island.”

“You hit an island that small, like a grain of rice. Impressive.”

The dart I threw had landed on a tiny island surrounded by ocean.

Alta, give me the information.

A: It is a maritime kingdom composed of multiple islands, the Kingdom of Pajel. The location struck is an island called Latis Island, famous as a tourist destination, also known as the “Water City.”

“The Water City! As someone who loves sightseeing, this is absolutely a place we have to go!”

“Master, you’re not forgetting the objective, are you?”

Seeing my excitement rise, Mio reined me in.

“Eh, sightsee… uh, yeah, we’re looking for the holder of the \<Hero> skill. Don’t worry, I remember.”

“You were definitely about to say sightseeing…”

“Of course not.”

Let’s quickly find the \<Hero> holder, then use the free time to sightsee.

“So then, how do we get to this country?”

Sera asked while looking at the map.

I looked at it too and considered our route.

“The closest country I’m connected to is the Izumo Wa Kingdom. Since it doesn’t share land borders with other countries, going through official channels would mean taking a ship.”

A: Ships depart regularly from the Izumo Wa Kingdom, but they are not direct, so it takes about a week.

“A week of travel with a one-month time limit is too long. Let’s go by unofficial means.”

“Flying?”

“That would be the easiest. The issue is immigration…”

In this world, traveling between countries usually requires paying a toll.

Entering unofficially means not paying that toll. Neglecting obligations to a country while enjoying sightseeing there feels a bit improper.

A: The Kingdom of Pajel does not generally charge tolls. Instead, a usage fee is collected when foreign ships use its ports. If you do not use a port, even foreign ships are not charged. However, you receive no guarantees.

I see. As an island nation, it’s inherently incompatible with toll systems.

From our perspective, that’s a relief.

“Sounds fine. Let’s head there on riding dragons.”

“Blue-chan will be happy.”

Will she?

《Blue. We’re going on an aerial trip this afternoon. Can you manage?》

《I’m definitely going! Yay!》

That’s not “can you”, that’s “I’m going.”

She’d probably cancel other plans if she had to.

And she’s really happy.

“She is happy.”

“Then I’ll let Leaf-chan and the others know…”

Sakura used telepathy to inform the others.

By the time all preparations were finished, it was afternoon.

Maria and Dora had recovered, so we transferred to the Izumo Wa Kingdom via ‘Portal’, then crossed the sea on riding dragons.

“This is the item you requested.”

“Please make good use of it.”

Before departing, we received identification documents from the royal twins of the Izumo Wa Kingdom, Tooru and Kaoru.

If we were to get into trouble in the Kingdom of Pajel, having identification from the allied Izumo Wa Kingdom would greatly change how things played out.

“I hope we never have to use it, since it’s for emergencies.”

This was trump card number one.

Trump card number two, by the way, is “merciless violence.”

“But did we really need to come all the way to the castle?”

“Please don’t say such sad things about our nation’s castle.”

“Ah, sorry. That’s not what I meant.”

This time, after transferring to End, the capital of the Izumo Wa Kingdom, we received the documents at End Castle.

What Mio meant was that we could have saved the trouble by exchanging them via \<Infinite Storage>.

“There are two reasons. First, if you’re receiving identification documents, you should go through proper procedures to some extent.”

After all, you can’t exactly tell people you received them via \<Infinite Storage>, right?

I want to be able to say clearly that they were “handed directly by royalty”.

“Ah, Master’s mysterious insistence.”

Don’t call it mysterious.

“And the other reason?”

“Please tell us.”

Perhaps because it involved their own country, the twins listened with interest.

“…After hearing that End was restored, I realized I hadn’t visited the Izumo Wa Kingdom even once. Since we had the chance, I figured I should at least see the castle and castle town.”

I could always go later, and it wasn’t a high priority, so I kept putting it off.

Once I put something off, I tend to delay it an absurd amount (example: the Crimson Empire trip). That’s why I want to seize opportunities when they come.

“Now that you mention it, we never heard that you visited our country.”

“How is our restored nation?”

“I think it’s good. The castle is more impressive than before…”

“That is thanks to the maids…”

Tooru looked slightly dissatisfied.

“No, we are grateful. Still, it’s frustrating, or rather…”

The maids work surpassed that of the nation’s own architects.

As the nation’s future leader, she probably couldn’t fully accept that.

“By the way, just how effective is this document?”

I held up the document and asked what I’d been wondering.

It was identification from the nation’s top figures. It should carry considerable authority.

“With that, you’ll receive hospitality equivalent to that given to Izumo Wa Kingdom’s senior officials.”

“It also carries the implication that if something happens to its holder, the Izumo Wa Kingdom becomes your enemy.”

“That’s beyond simple identification.”

I went to get an ID and received Lord Mitsukuni’s seal.

“Jin-dono, to be honest, this is neither excessive nor unnecessary.”

“That’s right. Jin-dono seems to underestimate his own importance, but in reality, you’re far more important than ordinary royalty.”

Maria nodded vigorously beside us.

《Master, are you important?》

“Honestly, I have no awareness of that at all.”

I’m not trying to belittle myself, but being called an important figure doesn’t really sink in.

Right now, I’m just a tourist living freely, you know?

“What a troublesome man…”

“I almost think it would be better if you held some form of official authority.”

“Yeah, I’ll pass on that.”

Gaining an official public position sounds like nothing but trouble.

Ah, role-playing like a Queen’s Knight is fine, though.

“So at least, please accept our full support.”

“Yes. Providing half-hearted support and having something happen to Jin-dono would be far more problematic.”

“You’d definitely get beaten half to death by the maids…”

That might not be impossible…

The maids get pretty violent when it comes to me.

“Alright. Then for your sakes, I’ll gratefully accept the document.”

“That would help us.”

“Please use it without hesitation.”

And so, having obtained the important item, “Lord Mitsukuni’s seal”, at End Castle, we set off through the skies toward the Kingdom of Pajel.

And then, the sky.

As usual, I rode the Sky Dragon with Maria and led the way.

The speed was kept slow enough not to leave Leaf and Mikazuki behind, which apparently left Blue slightly dissatisfied.

I’ll take her for a full-speed ride next time…

《It’s a promise!》

Even without going all out, draconic flight is not slow.

In no time, the Kingdom of Pajel came into view (on the map).

Just as I was about to hide the map, something outrageous caught my eye.

“Fah!?”

This is what it was.

Name: Ashley

Gender: Female

Age: 17

Race: High Elf

Titles: Elf Princess Shrine Maiden, Elf Royalty, Living Sacrifice

Skills:

Magic

\<Water Magic LV2> \<Spirit Arts LV10> \<Spirit Magic LV10> \<Sealing Arts LV >

Skill

\<Swimming LV4> \<Magic Tool Creation LV10> \<Forest Wisdom LV >

Other

\<Ageless LV > \<Shrine Maiden Succession LV > \<Flowing Water’s Thought LV >

As you know, a ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’.

No, it wasn’t surprising that there was a ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’.

The problem was her current situation.

Ashley-san was currently living a half-naked survival life on a deserted island.

More specifically, she was topless, wearing only panties, living in a hut made of wood and grass.

…What in the world happened?

《What could possibly lead a Princess Shrine Maiden to end up like that?》

Seeing what I saw, Mio commented.

《Did she get stranded…?》

《No, Sakura-sama. If she can use \<Spirit Magic>, she should be able to cross the sea, so that seems unlikely.》

What \<Spirit Magic> can do depends on the environment.

Near the sea, there should be water spirits present, so asking them should allow her to cross.

At the very least, it’s hard to imagine the Princess Shrine Maiden of the Water Calamity Dragon being stranded.

《This is bad… Ashley doesn’t seem to have noticed, but she’ll encounter a strong monster soon.》

On the island where the ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’ was, a large, unique-class monster lived.

She didn’t seem to have noticed it yet, but it was only a matter of time.

《That might be too much for the Princess Shrine Maiden to handle.》

《Master, are we going to help?》

《Hmm, we can’t exactly leave a ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’ alone. …Tamo-san, sorry, but could you guard her?》

《Understood.》

Going to the island ourselves to protect her or defeat the monster would be a hassle right now.

Without knowing her circumstances, I didn’t want to act unilaterally, so for now I decided to eliminate the risk to her life.

And when it comes to stable guarding, no one surpasses Tamo-san.

Never tires, never needs sleep, high-level presence concealment and camouflage for stealth, adaptability to exploit any enemy’s weakness. Truly the strongest guard.

《Then I’m counting on you.》

Saying that, I summoned a guard-use Tamo-san.

Just so you know, one is always attached to me.

“Go!”

I threw the Tamo-san I was holding toward the island where Ashley was.

Tamo-san flew off at incredible speed. Before long, he’d become a bird-type monster.

《Tamo-san flew away! Dora wants to do that too!》

Dora’s eyes sparkled.

《Do you think it’s okay to throw Dora?》

《I don’t think so…》

《Absolutely not. I mean, even with Tamo-san, it’s not exactly okay, but…》

《You should refrain. It would be quite the horrific sight…》

《If Jin-sama wishes it, I will not stop him, but I will prepare \<Healing Magic> and ‘Summon’ just in case.》

When I asked around, every sensible person rejected the idea.

Maria? Your perspective is different from everyone else’s, isn’t it?

《Dora, they say no.》

《Muu…》

Dora puffed out her cheeks. Cute.

Oh no. Since she’s riding a different dragon, I can’t pat her to cheer her up.

“‘Summon’.”

《Wah!? 》

Suddenly summoned, Dora blinked in surprise, and I immediately patted her.

《Ehehe.》

Her mood improved instantly.

《Jin-kun, suddenly summoning someone is bad for the heart…》

《Ah, sorry.》

Sakura scolded me from Leaf, whom she’d been riding with Dora.

Once her mood was fixed, Dora flew back to Leaf.

Yeah, since Dora can fly on her own, riding a dragon is basically pointless for her.

We continued our aerial journey, and Latis Island entered the map’s range.

After continuing further, Latis Island finally came into view.

Actually, after entering the Kingdom of Pajel and finding the ‘Princess Shrine Maiden’, we had kept the map hidden the entire time. Naturally, we weren’t searching for the \<Hero> either.

Even though I said “efficient search”, this time I wanted to leave encountering the \<Hero> to chance, without using the map.

《Thinking about it normally, that’s insane.》

Deciding the destination by throwing a dart at a world map, then searching for a single person with no hints. Objectively, as Mio said, it’s insanity.

《It has a track record.》

《It has a track record?!》

Back in my original world, it did, a few times.

《Who were you searching for…?》

《Well, let’s leave that story for another time… More importantly, look at that. It’s truly worthy of being called the Water City.》

I dodged Sakura’s question and pointed out Latis Island’s scenery.

Latis Island has very low elevation, making it look like it’s floating on the sea.

Canals run throughout the island, and Western-style buildings line those waterways.

Transportation along the canals is, of course, by gondola. A water city without gondolas would be unthinkable.

《It’s totally Venice.》

《I’ve never been, but I’ve seen it… Could it be a Hero…?》

《It’s possible, but considering the land, it’s not unnatural.》

It could be civilization warped by the Hero, but it could also be a natural development.

It’s hard to judge.

《Still, we’ve been doing a lot of real sightseeing lately. It’s nice.》

《Yeah, come to think of it, last time was China, and this time it’s Italy. It’s like an overseas travel brochure.》

《Overseas travel… I’ve never been…》

Sakura’s mood darkened slightly.

At our age, not having traveled abroad shouldn’t be strange…

《Sakura-sama, it’s okay. I haven’t either.》

《I have. The route wasn’t official, though…》

《Tell us more.》

《Another time.》

This time, I dodged Mio’s pursuit. While we were talking, we arrived at Latis Island in no time.

If you can see it, it’s close.

Once we got close enough, we turned invisible using \<Non-Attribute Magic> and landed in an uninhabited area in the northwest of Latis Island. From there, we headed toward the city on foot.

The three riding dragons returned home at this point.

“For now… let’s ride a gondola.”

That was my first line upon reaching the city.

“Master, you’re seriously consistent. Is it really okay to put the person we’re looking for on the back burner?”

Mio asked, already used to this.

Since there were people around, she didn’t use the word \<Hero>.

“Yeah, back burner. Isn’t it more of a problem to come to a water city and not ride a gondola? Or are you saying you don’t want to ride one, Mio?”

“No… I do want to, but…”

Even Mio couldn’t bring herself to say she didn’t want to.

“I want to ride one too…”

“If Jin-sama rides, I will as well.”

《Dora too!》

Sakura, Maria, and Dora were also in favor of the gondola tour.

Huh? What about Sera?

“‘Float’. …I will join as well.”

You just used weight-reduction magic, didn’t you?

I don’t know the gondola’s load limit, but putting heavy objects in one spot isn’t a good idea.

It was Sera’s quiet consideration.

“Sera-chan…”

“Mio-san, please don’t look at me like that!”

Sera protested after being looked at with pity.

“Seems no one is against it. Let’s ride the gondola.”

《Yeah!》

We immediately went to sign up for a gondola tour.

“A gondola tour, is it? I’m terribly sorry, but we operate primarily by reservation. We cannot accommodate you today. During this season, with many tourists, even cancellations are difficult.”

“What… did you say…”

I had completely forgotten.

That many tourist attractions require reservations…

Tourist Jin Shindo. A lifelong regret.
